::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Khuddakanikāye

## Jātakapāḷi

#### (Paṭhamo bhāgo)

### 1. Ekakanipāto

#### 1. Apaṇṇakavaggo

#### 1. Apaṇṇakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Apaṇṇakaṃ {pb:T:1.0001}{pb:V:1.0001}{pb:M:1.0001} ṭhānameke, dutiyaṃ āhu takkikā;
::

::gathalast
Etadaññāya medhāvī, taṃ gaṇhe yadapaṇṇakanti {note:taṃ gaṇheyya apaṇṇakaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Apaṇṇakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 2. Vaṇṇupathajātakaṃ

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Akilāsuno {pb:V:1.0002} vaṇṇupathe {note:vaṇṇapathe (ka.)} khaṇantā, udaṅgaṇe tattha papaṃ avinduṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ munī vīriya {note:muni viriya (pī.), muni vīriya (syā. ka.)} balūpapanno, akilāsu vinde hadayassa santinti.
::

::centre
Vaṇṇupathajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 3. Serivavāṇijajātakaṃ

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Idha {pb:T:1.0002}{pb:M:1.0002} ce naṃ {note:idha ce hi naṃ (sī. pī.)} virādhesi, saddhammassa niyāmataṃ {note:niyāmakaṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ tvaṃ anutappesi {note:anutapessasi (sī. pī.), anutappissasi (?)}, serivāyaṃva vāṇijoti.
::

::centre
Serivavāṇijajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 4. Cūḷaseṭṭhijātakaṃ

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Appakenapi medhāvī, pābhatena vicakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Samuṭṭhāpeti attānaṃ, aṇuṃ aggiṃva sandhamanti.
::

::centre
Cūḷa {note:culla (sī.), cullaka (syā. pī.)} seṭṭhijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 5. Taṇḍulanāḷijātakaṃ

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
{note:kimagghatī taṇḍulanāḷikā ca, bārāṇasī antarabāhirāni; assapañcasate tāni, ekā taṇḍulanāḷikāti; (syā.)} Kimagghati taṇḍulanāḷikāya, assāna mūlāya vadehi rāja {note:nāḷikā ca (sī.), nāḷikāya (ka. sī. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Bārāṇasiṃ santarabāhirato {note:bāhirantaṃ (sī.)}, ayamagghati taṇḍulanāḷikāti {note:kimagghatī vaṇḍulanāḷikā ca, bārāṇasī antarabāhirāni; assapañcasate tāni, ekā taṇḍulanāḷikāti; (syā.)}.
::

::centre
Taṇḍulanāḷijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 6. Devadhammajātakaṃ

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Hiriottappasampannā{pb:T:1.0003}, sukkadhammasamāhitā;
::

::gathalast
Santo sappurisā loke, devadhammāti vuccareti.
::

::centre
Devadhammajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 7. Kaṭṭhahārijātakaṃ

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Putto tyāhaṃ mahārāja, tvaṃ maṃ posa janādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Aññepi devo poseti, kiñca {note:kiñci (ka.)} devo sakaṃ pajanti.
::

::centre
Kaṭṭhahāri {note:kaṭṭhavāhana (ka.)} jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 8. Gāmaṇijātakaṃ

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:V:1.0003}{pb:M:1.0003} ataramānānaṃ, phalāsāva samijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Vipakkabrahmacariyosmi, evaṃ jānāhi gāmaṇīti.
::

::centre
Gāmaṇijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 9. Maghadevajātakaṃ

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Uttamaṅgaruhā mayhaṃ, ime jātā vayoharā;
::

::gathalast
Pātubhūtā devadūtā, pabbajjāsamayo mamāti.
::

::centre
Maghadeva {note:makhādeva (sī. pī.), devadūta (ka.)} jātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 10. Sukhavihārijātakaṃ

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Yañca {pb:T:1.0004} aññe na rakkhanti, yo ca aññe na rakkhati;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve rāja sukhaṃ seti, kāmesu anapekkhavāti.
::

::centre
Sukhavihārijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Apaṇṇakavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varāpaṇṇaka vaṇṇupatha serivaro, suvicakkhaṇa taṇḍulanāḷikassā;
::

::gathalast
Hiri puttavaruttagāmaṇinā, yo ca na rakkhati tena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Sīlavaggo

#### 11. Lakkhaṇamigajātakaṃ

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Hoti sīlavataṃ attho, paṭisanthāra {note:paṭisandhāra (ka.)} vuttinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Lakkhaṇaṃ passa āyantaṃ, ñātisaṅghapurakkhataṃ {note:purakkhitaṃ (syā.), purekkhitaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Atha passasimaṃ kāḷaṃ, suvihīnaṃva ñātibhīti.
::

::centre
Lakkhaṇamigajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 12. Nigrodhamigajātakaṃ

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Nigrodhameva {pb:T:1.0005}{pb:V:1.0004}{pb:M:1.0004} seveyya, na sākhamupasaṃvase;
::

::gathalast
Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo, yañce sākhasmi {note:sākhasmiṃ (sī. pī.)} jīvitanti.
::

::centre
Nigrodhamigajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 13. Kaṇḍijātakaṃ

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu kaṇḍinaṃ sallaṃ, purisaṃ gāḷhavedhinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dhiratthu taṃ janapadaṃ, yatthitthī pariṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Te cāpi dhikkitā {note:dhikkatā (?)} sattā, ye itthīnaṃ vasaṃgatāti.
::

::centre
Kaṇḍijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 14. Vātamigajātakaṃ

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Na kiratthi rasehi pāpiyo, āvāsehi va {note:vā (sabbattha)} santhavehi vā;
::

::gathalast
Vātamigaṃ gahananissitaṃ {note:gehanissitaṃ (sī. pī.)}, vasamānesi rasehi sañjayoti.
::

::centre
Vātamigajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 15. Kharādiyajātakaṃ

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhakkhuraṃ kharādiye, migaṃ vaṅkātivaṅkinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattahi {pb:T:1.0006} kālātikkantaṃ {note:sattahi kalāha’tikkantaṃ (sī.), sattakāleha’tikkantaṃ (syā.), sattahi kālāha’tikkantaṃ (pī.)}, na naṃ ovaditussaheti.
::

::centre
Kharādiyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 16. Tipallatthamigajātakaṃ

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Migaṃ {pb:M:1.0005} tipallattha {note:tipallatta (ka.)} manekamāyaṃ, aṭṭhakkhuraṃ aḍḍharattāpapāyiṃ {note:aḍḍharattāvapāyiṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ekena sotena chamāssasanto, chahi kalāhitibhoti {note:kalāhatibhoti (sī. syā. pī.)} bhāgineyyoti.
::

::centre
Tipallatthamigajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 17. Mālutajātakaṃ

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Kāḷe {pb:V:1.0005} vā yadi vā juṇhe, yadā vāyati māluto;
::

::gathalast
Vātajāni hi sītāni, ubhotthamaparājitāti.
::

::centre
Mālutajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 18. Matakabhattajātakaṃ

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ ce sattā jāneyyuṃ, dukkhāyaṃ jātisambhavo;
::

::gathalast
Na pāṇo pāṇinaṃ haññe, pāṇaghātī hi socatīti.
::

::centre
Matakabhattajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 19. Āyācitabhattajātakaṃ

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:T:1.0007} mucce {note:muñce (sī. syā. pī.)} pecca mucce {note:muñce (sī. syā. pī.)}, muccamāno hi bajjhati;
::

::gathalast
Na hevaṃ dhīrā muccanti, mutti bālassa bandhananti.
::

::centre
Āyācitabhattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 20. Naḷapānajātakaṃ

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā padamanuttiṇṇaṃ, disvānotaritaṃ padaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Naḷena vāriṃ pissāma {note:pivissāma (sī. syā. pī.)}, neva {note:na ca (ka.)} maṃ tvaṃ vadhissasīti.
::

::centre
Naḷapānajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Sīlavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha {pb:M:1.0006} lakkhaṇa sākha dhiratthu puna, na kiratthi rasehi kharādiyā;
::

::gathalast
Atibhoti vara {note:rasa (sabbattha)} māluta pāṇa, muccena naḷaavhayanena bhavanti dasāti.
::

#### 3. Kuruṅgavaggo

#### 21. Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Ñātametaṃ {pb:V:1.0006} kuruṅgassa, yaṃ tvaṃ sepaṇṇi siyyasi {note:seyyasi (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ {pb:T:1.0008} sepaṇṇi gacchāmi, na me te ruccate phalanti.
::

::centre
Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 22. Kukkurajātakaṃ

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Ye kukkurā rājakulamhi vaddhā, koleyyakā vaṇṇabalūpapannā;
::

::gathalast
Teme na vajjhā mayamasma vajjhā, nāyaṃ saghaccā dubbalaghātikāyanti.
::

::centre
Kukkurajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 23. Gojānīyajātakaṃ

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Api passena semāno, sallebhi sallalīkato;
::

::gathalast
Seyyova vaḷavā gojo {note:bhojjo (sī.), bhojjho (syā. pī.)}, yuñja maññeva sārathīti.
::

::centre
Gojānīya {note:bhojājānīya (sī. syā. pī.)} jātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 24. Ājaññajātakaṃ

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā yadā yattha yadā, yattha yattha yadā yadā;
::

::gathalast
Ājañño kurute vegaṃ, hāyanti tattha vāḷavāti.
::

::centre
Ājaññajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 25. Titthajātakaṃ

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Aññamaññehi {pb:T:1.0009}{pb:M:1.0007} titthehi, assaṃ pāyehi sārathi;
::

::gathalast
Accāsanassa puriso, pāyāsassapi tappatīti.
::

::centre
Titthajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 26. Mahiḷāmukhajātakaṃ

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Purāṇacorāna {pb:V:1.0007} vaco nisamma, mahiḷāmukho pothayamanvacārī;
::

::gathalast
Susaññatānañhi vaco nisamma, gajuttamo sabbaguṇesu aṭṭhāti.
::

::centre
Mahiḷāmukhajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 27. Abhiṇhajātakaṃ

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Nālaṃ kabaḷaṃ padātave, na ca piṇḍaṃ na kuse na ghaṃsituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi abhiṇhadassanā, nāgo snehamakāsi {note:sinehamakāsi (sī. syā. pī.)} kukkureti.
::

::centre
Abhiṇhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 28. Nandivisālajātakaṃ

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Manuññameva {pb:T:1.0010} bhāseyya, nāmanuññaṃ kudācanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Manuññaṃ bhāsamānassa, garuṃ bhāraṃ udaddhari;
::

::gathalast
Dhanañca naṃ alābhesi, tena cattamano ahūti.
::

::centre
Nandivisālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 29. Kaṇhajātakaṃ

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Yato yato garu dhuraṃ, yato gambhīravattanī;
::

::gathalast
Tadāssu kaṇhaṃ yuñjanti, svāssu taṃ vahate dhuranti.
::

::centre
Kaṇhajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 30. Munikajātakaṃ

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:M:1.0008} munikassa pihayi, āturannāni bhuñjati;
::

::gathalast
Appossukko bhusaṃ khāda, etaṃ dīghāyulakkhaṇanti.
::

::centre
Munikajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kuruṅgavaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kuruṅgassa {pb:V:1.0008} kukkuragojavaro, puna vāḷavassasirivhayano {note:sirivayano (sabbattha)};
::

::gathalast
Mahiḷāmukhanāmanuññavaro, vahate dhura munikena dasāti.
::

#### 4. Kulāvakavaggo

#### 31. Kulāvakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Kulāvakā {pb:T:1.0011} mātali simbalismiṃ, īsāmukhena parivajjayassu;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ cajāma asuresu pāṇaṃ, mā me dijā vikkulavā {note:māyime dijā vikulāvā (sī. syā. pī.)} ahesunti.
::

::centre
Kulāvakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 32. Naccajātakaṃ

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Rudaṃ manuññaṃ rucirā ca piṭṭhi, veḷuriyavaṇṇūpanibhā {note:vaṇṇūpaṭibhā (syā.), vaṇṇasannibhā (ka.)} ca gīvā;
::

::gathalast
Byāmamattāni ca pekhuṇāni, naccena te dhītaraṃ no dadāmīti.
::

Naccajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 33. Sammodamānajātakaṃ

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Sammodamānā {pb:M:1.0009} gacchanti, jālamādāya pakkhino;
::

::gathalast
Yadā te vivadissanti, tadā ehinti me vasanti.
::

::centre
Sammodamānajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 34. Macchajātakaṃ

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0012} maṃ sītaṃ na maṃ uṇhaṃ, na maṃ jālasmi bādhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yañca maṃ maññate macchī, aññaṃ so ratiyā gatoti.
::

Macchajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 35. Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Santi {pb:V:1.0009} pakkhā apatanā, santi pādā avañcanā;
::

::gathalast
Mātāpitā ca nikkhantā, jātaveda paṭikkamāti.
::

::centre
Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 36. Sakuṇajātakaṃ

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nissitā jagatiruhaṃ vihaṅgamā, svāyaṃ aggiṃ pamuñcati;
::

::gathalast
Disā bhajatha vakkaṅgā {note:vaṅkaṅgā (syā.)}, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayanti.
::

::centre
Sakuṇajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 37. Tittirajātakaṃ

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Ye vuḍḍha {note:vaddha (sī. pī.)} mapacāyanti, narā dhammassa kovidā;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭheva dhamme pāsaṃsā, samparāye ca suggatīti.
::

::centre
Tittirajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 38. Bakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Nāccantaṃ {pb:T:1.0013} nikatippañño, nikatyā sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Ārādheti nikatippañño {note:ārādhe nikatippañño (pī.)}, bako kakkaṭakāmivāti.
::

::centre
Bakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 39. Nandajātakaṃ

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Maññe {pb:M:1.0010} sovaṇṇayo rāsi, soṇṇamālā ca nandako;
::

::gathalast
Yattha dāso āmajāto, ṭhito thullāni {note:thūlāni (ka.)} gajjatīti.
::

::centre
Nandajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 40. Khadiraṅgārajātakaṃ

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ {pb:V:1.0010} patāmi nirayaṃ, uddhaṃpādo avaṃsiro;
::

::gathalast
Nānariyaṃ karissāmi, handa piṇḍaṃ paṭiggahāti.
::

::centre
Khadiraṅgārajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kulāvakavaggo catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sirimātali dhītara pakkhivaro, ratiyāgato mātāpitā ca puna;
::

::gatha1
Jagatīruha vuḍḍha sukakkaṭako, tathā nandakapiṇḍavarena dasāti.
::

#### 5. Atthakāmavaggo

#### 41. Losakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:T:1.0014} atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ajiyā pādamolamba {note:pādamolumba (sī. syā. pī.)}, mittako viya socatīti.
::

::centre
Losakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 42. Kapotajātakaṃ

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0011} atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kapotakassa vacanaṃ akatvā, amittahatthatthagatova setīti.
::

::centre
Kapotajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 43. Veḷukajātakaṃ

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Yo atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ so nihato seti, veḷukassa yathā pitāti.
::

::centre
Veḷukajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 44. Makasajātakaṃ

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Seyyo {pb:T:1.0015}{pb:V:1.0011} amitto matiyā upeto, na tveva mitto mativippahīno;
::

::gathalast
Makasaṃ vadhissanti hi eḷamūgo, putto pitu abbhidā uttamaṅganti.
::

::centre
Makasajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 45. Rohiṇijātakaṃ

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Seyyo amitto medhāvī, yañce bālānukampako;
::

::gathalast
Passa rohiṇikaṃ jammiṃ, mātaraṃ hantvāna socatīti.
::

::centre
Rohiṇijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 46. Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Na ve anatthakusalena, atthacariyā sukhāvahā;
::

::gathalast
Hāpeti atthaṃ dummedho, kapi ārāmiko yathāti.
::

::centre
Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 47. Vāruṇidūsakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0012} ve anatthakusalena, atthacariyā sukhāvahā;
::

::gathalast
Hāpeti atthaṃ dummedho, koṇḍañño vāruṇiṃ yathāti.
::

::centre
Vāruṇidūsakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 48. Vedabbajātakaṃ

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Anupāyena {pb:T:1.0016} yo atthaṃ, icchati so vihaññati;
::

::gathalast
Cetā haniṃsu vedabbaṃ {note:vedabbhaṃ (sī. pī.)}, sabbe te byasanamajjhagūti.
::

::centre
Vedabba {note:vedabbha (sī. pī.)} jātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 49. Nakkhattajātakaṃ

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Nakkhattaṃ {pb:V:1.0012} paṭimānentaṃ, attho bālaṃ upaccagā;
::

::gathalast
Attho atthassa nakkhattaṃ, kiṃ karissanti tārakāti.
::

::centre
Nakkhattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 50. Dummedhajātakaṃ

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Dummedhānaṃ sahassena, yañño me upayācito;
::

::gathalast
Idāni khohaṃ yajissāmi, bahu {note:bahū (sī. pī.), bahuṃ (ka.)} adhammiko janoti.
::

::centre
Dummedhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Atthakāmavaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha mittaka mātu kapotavaro, tathā veḷūka eḷamūgo rohiṇī;
::

::gathalast
Kapi {pb:T:1.0017} vāruṇi cetacarā ca puna, tathā tāraka yaññavarena dasāti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamo paṇṇāsako.
::

#### 6. Āsīsavaggo

::gathalast

#### 55. Pañcāvudhajātakaṃ

55\.

::

::gathalast

#### 58. Tayodhammajātakaṃ

#### 59. Bherivādakajātakaṃ

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::centre

#### 60. Saṅkhadhamajātakaṃ

60\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::centre

Tassuddānaṃ –

::

::gathalast

#### 7. Itthivaggo

#### 61. Asātamantajātakaṃ

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Asā lokitthiyo nāma, velā tāsaṃ na vijjati;
::

::gatha2
Sārattā ca pagabbhā ca, sikhī sabbaghaso yathā;
::

::gathalast
Tā hitvā pabbajissāmi, vivekamanubrūhayanti.
::

::centre
Asātamantajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 62. Aṇḍabhūtajātakaṃ

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Aṇḍabhūtā bhatā bhariyā, tāsu ko jātu vissaseti.
::

::centre
Aṇḍabhūtajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 63. Takkapaṇḍitajātakaṃ

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Brahmacariyaṃ cara bhikkhu, so sukhaṃ na vihāhasīti {note:pihāhisīti (sī. syā. pī.), vihāyasi (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Takkapaṇḍitajātakaṃ {note:takkajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.)} tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 64. Durājānajātakaṃ

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0021} su nandi icchati maṃ, mā su soci na micchati {note:na icchati (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Thīnaṃ bhāvo durājāno, macchassevodake gatanti.
::

::centre

#### 65. Anabhiratijātakaṃ

::hangnum
65\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre

#### 66. Mudulakkhaṇajātakaṃ

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Ekā icchā pure āsi, aladdhā mudulakkhaṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yato laddhā aḷārakkhī, icchā icchaṃ vijāyathāti.
::

::centre
Mudulakkhaṇajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 67. Ucchaṅgajātakaṃ

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Ucchaṅge deva me putto, pathe dhāvantiyā pati;
::

::gathalast
Tañca desaṃ na passāmi, yato sodariyamānayeti {note:sodariyaṃ naye (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Ucchaṅgajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 68. Sāketajātakaṃ

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Adiṭṭhapubbake pose, kāmaṃ tasmimpi vissaseti.
::

::centre
Sāketajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 69. Visavantajātakaṃ

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu taṃ visaṃ vantaṃ, yamahaṃ jīvitakāraṇā;
::

::gathalast
Vantaṃ paccāvamissāmi {note:paccāharissāmi (ka.)}, mataṃ me jīvitā varanti.
::

::centre
Visavantajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 70. Kuddālajātakaṃ

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Na taṃ jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ avajīyati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kho jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ nāvajīyatīti.
::

::centre
Kuddālajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Itthivaggo sattamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Mudulakkhaṇa sodariyā ca mano, visa sādhujitena bhavanti dasāti.
::

#### 76. Asaṅkiyajātakaṃ

::gathalast

#### 77. Mahāsupinajātakaṃ

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Usabhā {pb:V:1.0018} rukkhā gāviyo gavā ca, asso kaṃso siṅgālī {note:sigāsī (sī. syā. pī.)} ca kumbho;
::

::gathalast
Pokkharaṇī ca apākacandanaṃ, lābūni sīdanti silā plavanti.
::

::gatha1
Maṇḍūkiyo kaṇhasappe gilanti, kākaṃ supaṇṇā parivārayanti;
::

::gathalast
Tasā {pb:T:1.0025} vakā eḷakānaṃ bhayāhi, vipariyāso {note:vipariyāyo (syā. ka.)} vattati nayidha matthīti.
::

::centre
Mahāsupinajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 78. Illisajātakaṃ

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

#### 79. Kharassarajātakaṃ

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Yato {pb:M:1.0019} viluttā ca hatā ca gāvo, daḍḍhāni gehāni jano ca nīto;
::

::gathalast
Athāgamā puttahatāya putto, kharassaraṃ ḍiṇḍimaṃ {note:deṇḍimaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), ḍindimaṃ (ka.)} vādayantoti.
::

::centre
Kharassarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 80. Bhīmasenajātakaṃ

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ te pavikatthitaṃ pure, atha te pūtisarā sajanti pacchā;
::

::gathalast
Ubhayaṃ {pb:T:1.0026} na sameti bhīmasena, yuddhakathā ca idañca te vihaññanti.
::

::centre
Bhīmasenajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

#### 9. Apāyimhavaggo

#### 83. Kālakaṇṇijātakaṃ

::hangnum

::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ kathaṃ attasukhassa hetu, cirasanthutaṃ {note:cirasandhavaṃ (ka.), cirasatthunaṃ (pī.)} kāḷakaṇṇiṃ jaheyyanti.
::

::centre
Kālakaṇṇijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 84. Atthassadvārajātakaṃ

84\.

#### 85. Kiṃpakkajātakaṃ

#### 86. Sīlavīmaṃsakajātakaṃ

::gathalast

::centre

#### 87. Maṅgalajātakaṃ

::hangnum
87\.

#### 88. Sārambhajātakaṃ

::gathalast

::centre

#### 89. Kuhakajātakaṃ

#### 90. Akataññujātakaṃ

::gathalast

#### 10. Littavaggo

#### 91. Littajātakaṃ

::hangnum

::gathalast

::centre

#### 92. Mahāsārajātakaṃ

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::centre

#### 93. Visāsabhojanajātakaṃ

93\.

::centre

#### 94. Lomahaṃsajātakaṃ

::gathalast

::centre

#### 95. Mahāsudassanajātakaṃ

::hangnum
95\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Mahāsudassanajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 96. Telapattajātakaṃ

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Samatittikaṃ {pb:V:1.0022} anavasekaṃ, telapattaṃ yathā parihareyya;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ sacittamanurakkhe, patthayāno disaṃ agatapubbanti.
::

::centre
Telapattajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 97. Nāmasiddhijātakaṃ

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Jīvakañca {pb:M:1.0023} mataṃ disvā, dhanapāliñca duggataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Panthakañca vane mūḷhaṃ, pāpako punarāgatoti.
::

::centre
Nāmasiddhijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 98. Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu {pb:T:1.0032} kho paṇḍito nāma, na tveva atipaṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Atipaṇḍitena puttena, manamhi upakūḷitoti {note:upakūlitoti (sī.), upakuṭṭhitoti (syā.), upakuṭito (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 99. Parosahassajātakaṃ

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Parosahassampi samāgatānaṃ, kandeyyuṃ te vassasataṃ apaññā;
::

::gathalast
Ekova seyyo puriso sapañño, yo bhāsitassa vijānāti atthanti.
::

::centre
Parosahassajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 100. Asātarūpajātakaṃ

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Asātaṃ sātarūpena, piyarūpena appiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ sukhassa rūpena, pamattamativattatīti.
::

::centre
Asātarūpajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Littavaggo dasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Gilamakkhakutūhala {pb:T:1.0033}{pb:V:1.0023} mātukassā, muninā ca aniccata pattavaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhanapālivaro atipaṇḍitako, saparosahassaasātadasāti.
::

::centre
Majjhimo paṇṇāsako.
::

::gathalast

#### 103. Verijātakaṃ

#### 130. Kosiyajātakaṃ

::hangnum

#### 145. Rādhajātakaṃ

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0034} tvaṃ rādha vijānāsi, aḍḍharatte anāgate;
::

::gathalast
Abyayataṃ {note:abyāyataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), abyattataṃ (?)} vilapasi, virattā kosiyāyaneti.
::

::centre
Rādhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 146. Samuddakākajātakaṃ

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Api nu hanukā santā, mukhañca parisussati;
::

::gathalast
Oramāma na pārema, pūrateva mahodadhīti.
::

::centre
Samuddakākajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 147. Puppharattajātakaṃ

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Nayidaṃ dukkhaṃ aduṃ dukkhaṃ, yaṃ maṃ tudati vāyaso;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ sāmā puppharattena, kattikaṃ nānubhossatīti.
::

::centre
Puppharattajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 148. Siṅgālajātakaṃ

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Nāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0048} punaṃ na ca punaṃ, na cāpi apunappunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hatthibondiṃ pavekkhāmi, tathā hi bhayatajjitoti.
::

::centre
Siṅgālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 149. Ekapaṇṇajātakaṃ

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Ekapaṇṇo ayaṃ rukkho, na bhūmyā caturaṅgulo;
::

::gathalast
Phalena visakappena, mahāyaṃ kiṃ bhavissatīti.
::

::centre
Ekapaṇṇajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 150. Sañjīvajātakaṃ

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Asantaṃ {pb:V:1.0033}{pb:M:1.0035} yo paggaṇhāti, asantaṃ cūpasevati;
::

::gathalast
Tameva ghāsaṃ kurute, byaggho sañjīvako yathāti.
::

::centre
Sañjīvajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kakaṇṭaka {note:pāpasevana (ka.)} vaggo pannarasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sukhamedhati daṇḍavaro ca puna, lasi vāladhi pañcamarādhavaro;
::

::gathalast
Samahodadhi {pb:T:1.0049} kattika bondi puna, caturaṅgulabyagghavarena dasāti.
::

::centre
(Uparimo paṇṇāsako.) {note:( ) sīhaḷapotthakeyeva dissati}
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Apaṇṇakaṃ sīlavaggakuruṅga, kulāvakaṃ atthakāmena pañcamaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Āsīso itthivaruṇaṃ apāyi, littavaggena te dasa;
::

::gathalast
Parosataṃ haṃci kusanāḷi {note:haṃsi sarikkhaṃ (sabbattha)}, asampadaṃ kakaṇṭakavaggo.
::

::centre
Ekanipātamhilaṅkatanti.
::

::centre
Ekakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 2. Dukanipāto

#### 1. Daḷhavaggo

#### 151. Rājovādajātakaṃ (2-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Daḷhaṃ {pb:T:1.0050}{pb:V:1.0034}{pb:M:1.0036} daḷhassa khipati, balliko {note:malliko (sī. pī.)} mudunā muduṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sādhumpi sādhunā jeti, asādhumpi asādhunā;
::

::gathalast
Etādiso ayaṃ rājā, maggā uyyāhi sārathi.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Akkodhena jine kodhaṃ, asādhuṃ sādhunā jine;
::

::gatha2
Jine kadariyaṃ dānena, saccenālikavādinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etādiso ayaṃ rājā, maggā uyyāhi sārathīti.
::

::centre
Rājovādajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 152. Asamekkhitakammantaṃ, turitābhinipātinaṃ.

::gathalast
Sāni kammāni tappenti, uṇhaṃvajjhohitaṃ mukhe.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Sīho ca sīhanādena, daddaraṃ abhinādayi;
::

::gatha2
Sutvā sīhassa nigghosaṃ, siṅgālo {note:sigālo (sī. syā. pī.)} daddare vasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhīto santāsamāpādi, hadayañcassa apphalīti.
::

::centre
Siṅgālajātakaṃ {note:sigālajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 153. Sūkarajātakaṃ (2-1-3)

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Catuppado {pb:T:1.0051} ahaṃ samma, tvampi samma catuppado;
::

::gathalast
Ehi samma {note:sīha (sī. pī.)} nivattassu, kiṃ nu bhīto palāyasi.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Asuci {pb:V:1.0035} pūtilomosi, duggandho vāsi sūkara;
::

::gathalast
Sace yujjhitukāmosi, jayaṃ samma dadāmi teti.
::

::centre
Sūkarajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 154. Uragajātaka (2-1-4)

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Idhūragānaṃ {pb:M:1.0037} pavaro paviṭṭho, selassa vaṇṇena pamokkhamicchaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brahmañca vaṇṇaṃ {note:vakkaṃ (ka.)} apacāyamāno, bubhukkhito no vitarāmi {note:visahāmi (ka. si. syā. pī.)} bhottuṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
So brahmagutto cirameva jīva, dibyā ca te pātubhavantu bhakkhā;
::

::gathalast
Yo brahmavaṇṇaṃ apacāyamāno, bubhukkhito no vitarāsi {note:sabbatthapi samānaṃ} bhottunti.
::

::centre
Uragajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 155. Bhaggajātakaṃ (2-1-5)

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Jīva {pb:T:1.0052} vassasataṃ bhagga {note:gagga (sī. pī.)}, aparāni ca vīsatiṃ {note:vīsati (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mā maṃ pisācā khādantu, jīva tvaṃ sarado sataṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Tvampi vassasataṃ jīva, aparāni ca vīsatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Visaṃ pisācā khādantu, jīva tvaṃ sarado satanti.
::

::centre
Bhaggajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 156. Alīnacittajātakaṃ (2-1-6)

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Alīnacittaṃ nissāya, pahaṭṭhā mahatī camū;
::

::gathalast
Kosalaṃ senāsantuṭṭhaṃ, jīvaggāhaṃ agāhayi.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ nissayasampanno, bhikkhu āraddhavīriyo;
::

::gatha2
Bhāvayaṃ kusalaṃ dhammaṃ, yogakkhemassa pattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Pāpuṇe anupubbena, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayanti.
::

::centre
Alīnacittajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 157. Guṇajātakaṃ (2-1-7)

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Yena {pb:M:1.0038} kāmaṃ paṇāmeti, dhammo balavataṃ migī;
::

::gathalast
Unnadantī vijānāhi, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:V:1.0036} cepi dubbalo mitto, mittadhammesu tiṭṭhati;
::

::gatha2
So ñātako ca bandhu ca, so mitto so ca me sakhā;
::

::gathalast
Dāṭhini {pb:T:1.0053} mātimaññittho {note:maññivo (syā.), maññavho (ka.)}, siṅgālo mama pāṇadoti.
::

::centre
Guṇajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 158. Suhanujātakaṃ (2-1-8)

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Nayidaṃ visamasīlena, soṇena suhanū saha;
::

::gathalast
Suhanūpi tādisoyeva, yo soṇassa sagocaro.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Pakkhandinā pagabbhena, niccaṃ sandānakhādinā;
::

::gathalast
Sameti pāpaṃ pāpena, sameti asatā asanti.
::

::centre
Suhanujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 159. Morajātakaṃ (2-1-9)

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Udetayaṃ cakkhumā ekarājā, harissavaṇṇo pathavippabhāso {note:paṭhavippabhāso (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi harissavaṇṇaṃ pathavippabhāsaṃ, tayājja guttā viharemu divasaṃ.
::

::gatha1
Ye brāhmaṇā vedagū sabbadhamme, te me namo te ca maṃ pālayantu;
::

::gatha2
Namatthu buddhānaṃ {note:buddhāna (?)} namatthu bodhiyā, namo vimuttānaṃ {note:vimuttāna (?)} namo vimuttiyā;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ so parittaṃ katvā, moro carati esanā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Apetayaṃ {pb:T:1.0054}{pb:M:1.0039} cakkhumā ekarājā, harissavaṇṇo pathavippabhāso;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ nammassāmi harissavaṇṇaṃ pathavippabhāsaṃ, tayājja guttā viharemu rattiṃ.
::

::gatha1
Ye brāhmaṇā vedagū sabbadhamme, te me namo te ca maṃ pālayantu;
::

::gatha2
Namatthu buddhānaṃ namatthu bodhiyā, namo vimuttānaṃ namo vimuttiyā;
::

::gathalast
Imaṃ so parittaṃ katvā, moro vāsamakappayīti.
::

::centre
Morajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 160. Vinīlajātakaṃ (2-1-10)

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva nūna {note:nu (ka.)} rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Assā vahanti ājaññā, yathā haṃsā vinīlakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Vinīla {pb:V:1.0037} duggaṃ bhajasi, abhūmiṃ tāta sevasi;
::

::gathalast
Gāmantakāni {note:gāmantikāni (sī.), gāmantarāni (ka.)} sevassu, etaṃ mātālayaṃ tavāti.
::

::centre
Vinīlajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Daḷhavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varaballika {pb:T:1.0055} daddara sūkarako, uragūttama pañcamabhaggavaro;
::

::gathalast
Mahatīcamu yāva siṅgālavaro, suhanuttama mora vinīlaṃ dasāti.
::

#### 2. Santhavavaggo

#### 161. Indasamānagottajātakaṃ (2-2-1)

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0040} santhavaṃ {note:sandhavaṃ (ka.)} kāpurisena kayirā, ariyo anariyena pajānamatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cirānuvutthopi karoti pāpaṃ, gajo yathā indasamānagottaṃ.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ tveva jaññā sadiso mamanti, sīlena paññāya sutena cāpi;
::

::gathalast
Teneva mettiṃ kayirātha saddhiṃ, sukho have sappurisena saṅgamoti.
::

::centre
Indasamānagottajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 162. Santhavajātakaṃ (2-2-2)

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0056} santhavasmā paramatthi pāpiyo, yo santhavo {note:sandhavo (ka.)} kāpurisena hoti;
::

::gathalast
Santappito sappinā pāyasena {note:pāyāsena (ka.)}, kicchākataṃ paṇṇakuṭiṃ adayhi {note:adaḍḍhahi (sī. syā.), adaṭṭhahi (pī.), adaddahi (?)}.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Na santhavasmā paramatthi seyyo, yo santhavo sappurisena hoti;
::

::gathalast
Sīhassa byagghassa ca dīpino ca, sāmā mukhaṃ lehati santhavenāti.
::

::centre
Santhavajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 163. Susīmajātakaṃ (2-2-3)

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Kāḷā migā setadantā tavīme {note:tava ime (sī. syā. pī.)}, parosataṃ hemajālābhichannā {note:hemajālābhisañchannā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Te te dadāmīti susīma brūsi, anussaraṃ {pb:T:1.0057} pettipitāmahānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Kāḷā {pb:V:1.0038}{pb:M:1.0041} migā setadantā mamīme {note:mama ime (sī. pī.)}, parosataṃ hemajālābhicchannā;
::

::gathalast
Te te dadāmīti vadāmi māṇava, anussaraṃ pettipitāmahānanti.
::

::centre
Susīmajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 164. Gijjhajātakaṃ (2-2-4)

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nu gijjho yojanasataṃ, kuṇapāni avekkhati;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhasi.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
::

::gathalast
Atha jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhatīti.
::

::centre
Gijjhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 165. Nakulajātakaṃ (2-2-5)

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Sandhiṃ katvā amittena, aṇḍajena jalābuja;
::

::gathalast
Vivariya dāṭhaṃ sesi {note:sayasi (sī. syā. pī.)}, kuto te bhayamāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅketheva {note:saṅkateva (ka.)} amittasmiṃ, mittasmimpi na vissase;
::

::gathalast
Abhayā bhayamuppannaṃ, api mūlāni kantatīti {note:mūlaṃ nikantatīti (sī.)}.
::

::centre
Nakulajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 166. Upasāḷakajātakaṃ (2-2-6)

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Upasāḷakanāmāni {note:upasāḷhakanāmānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, sahassāni catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Asmiṃ padese daḍḍhāni, natthi loke anāmataṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Yamhi {pb:T:1.0058} saccañca dhammo ca, ahiṃsā saṃyamo damo;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ ariyā sevanti, etaṃ loke anāmatanti.
::

::centre
Upasāḷakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 167. Samiddhijātakaṃ (2-2-7)

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Abhutvā {pb:M:1.0042} bhikkhasi bhikkhu, na hi bhutvāna bhikkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvāna bhikkhu bhikkhassu, mā taṃ kālo upaccagā.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Kālaṃ {pb:V:1.0039} vohaṃ na jānāmi, channo kālo na dissati;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā abhutvā bhikkhāmi, mā maṃ kālo upaccagāti.
::

::centre
Samiddhijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 168. Sakuṇagghijātakaṃ (2-2-8)

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Seno balasā patamāno, lāpaṃ gocaraṭhāyinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sahasā ajjhappattova, maraṇaṃ tenupāgami.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ nayena sampanno, pettike gocare rato;
::

::gathalast
Apetasattu modāmi, sampassaṃ atthamattanoti.
::

::centre
Sakuṇagghijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 169. Arakajātakaṃ (2-2-9)

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve mettena cittena, sabbalokānukampati;
::

::gathalast
Uddhaṃ {pb:T:1.0059} adho ca tiriyaṃ, appamāṇena sabbaso.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Appamāṇaṃ hitaṃ cittaṃ, paripuṇṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ pamāṇakataṃ kammaṃ, na taṃ tatrāvasissatīti.
::

::centre
Arakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 170. Kakaṇṭakajātakaṃ (2-2-10)

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ pure uṇṇamati {note:unnamati (syā.)}, toraṇagge kakaṇṭako;
::

::gathalast
Mahosadha vijānāhi, kena thaddho kakaṇṭako.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Aladdhapubbaṃ laddhāna, aḍḍhamāsaṃ kakaṇṭako;
::

::gathalast
Atimaññati rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahanti.
::

::centre
Kakaṇṭakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Santhavavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha {pb:M:1.0043} indasamāna sapaṇṇakuṭi, susimuttama gijjha jalābujako;
::

::gathalast
Upasāḷaka bhikkhu salāpavaro, atha mettavaro dasapuṇṇamatīti.
::

#### 3. Kalyāṇavaggo

#### 171. Kalyāṇadhammajātakaṃ (2-3-1)

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Kalyāṇadhammoti {pb:T:1.0060}{pb:V:1.0040} yadā janinda, loke samaññaṃ anupāpuṇāti;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā na hiyyetha {note:hīyetha (sī.)} naro sapañño, hiriyāpi santo dhuramādiyanti.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Sāyaṃ samaññā idha majja pattā, kalyāṇadhammoti janinda loke;
::

::gathalast
Tāhaṃ samekkhaṃ idha pabbajissaṃ, na hi matthi chando idha kāmabhogeti.
::

::centre
Kalyāṇadhammajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 172. Daddarajātakaṃ (2-3-2)

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Ko nu saddena mahatā, abhinādeti daddaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ sīhā nappaṭinadanti {note:kiṃ sīhā nappaṭinadanti (sī. pī.), na sīhā paṭinadanti (ka.)}, ko nāmeso migādhibhū.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Adhamo migajātānaṃ, siṅgālo tāta vassati;
::

::gathalast
Jātimassa jigucchantā, tuṇhī sīhā samacchareti.
::

::centre
Daddarajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 173. Makkaṭajātakaṃ (2-3-3)

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Tāta {pb:T:1.0061}{pb:M:1.0044} māṇavako eso, tālamūlaṃ apassito;
::

::gathalast
Agārakañcidaṃ atthi, handa demassagārakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Mā kho tvaṃ tāta pakkosi, dūseyya no agārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Netādisaṃ mukhaṃ hoti, brāhmaṇassa susīlinoti.
::

::centre
Makkaṭajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 174. Dubbhiyamakkaṭajātakaṃ (2-3-4)

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Adamha te vāri pahūtarūpaṃ, ghammābhitattassa pipāsitassa;
::

::gathalast
So dāni pitvāna {note:pītvāna (sī. pī.)} kiriṅkarosi {note:kikiṃkarosi (sī. syā. pī.)}, asaṅgamo pāpajanena seyyo.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Ko te suto vā diṭṭho vā, sīlavā nāma makkaṭo;
::

::gathalast
Idāni kho taṃ ohacchaṃ {note:ūhacca (sī. pī.), ohaccaṃ (syā.), uhajjaṃ (ka.)}, esā asmāka dhammatāti.
::

::centre
Dubbhiyamakkaṭajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 175. Ādiccupaṭṭhānajātakaṃ (2-3-5)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbesu {pb:V:1.0041} kira bhūtesu, santi sīlasamāhitā;
::

::gathalast
Passa sākhāmigaṃ jammaṃ, ādiccamupatiṭṭhati.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
::

::gathalast
Aggihuttañca {pb:T:1.0062} uhannaṃ {note:ūhantaṃ (sī.), ūhanaṃ (syā.), ūhanti (pī.), uhadaṃ (ka.)}, dve ca bhinnā kamaṇḍalūti.
::

::centre
Ādiccupaṭṭhānajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 176. Kaḷāyamuṭṭhijātakaṃ (2-3-6)

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Bālo {pb:M:1.0045} vatāyaṃ dumasākhagocaro, paññā janinda nayimassa vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kaḷāyamuṭṭhiṃ {note:kalāyamuṭṭhiṃ (sī. pī.)} avakiriya kevalaṃ, ekaṃ kaḷāyaṃ patitaṃ gavesati.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva mayaṃ rāja, ye caññe atilobhino;
::

::gathalast
Appena bahuṃ jiyyāma, kaḷāyeneva vānaroti.
::

::centre
Kaḷāyamuṭṭhijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 177. Tindukajātakaṃ (2-3-7)

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Dhanuhatthakalāpehi, nettiṃ savaradhāribhi;
::

::gathalast
Samantā parikiṇṇamha, kathaṃ mokkho bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Appeva bahukiccānaṃ, attho jāyetha koci naṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atthi rukkhassa acchinnaṃ, khajjathaññeva tindukanti.
::

::centre
Tindukajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 178. Kacchapajātakaṃ (2-3-8)

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Janittaṃ {pb:T:1.0063} me bhavittaṃ me, iti paṅke avassayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ maṃ paṅko ajjhabhavi, yathā dubbalakaṃ tathā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi bhaggava, suṇohi vacanaṃ mama.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Gāme vā yadi vā raññe, sukhaṃ yatrādhigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ janittaṃ bhavittañca, purisassa pajānato;
::

::gathalast
Yamhi jīve tamhi gacche, na niketahato siyāti.
::

Kacchapajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 179. Satadhammajātakaṃ (2-3-9)

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Tañca {pb:V:1.0042} appañca ucchiṭṭhaṃ, tañca kicchena no adā;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ brāhmaṇajātiko, yaṃ bhuttaṃ tampi uggataṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0046} dhammaṃ niraṃkatvā {note:nirākatvā (?) ni + ā + kara + tvā}, yo adhammena jīvati;
::

::gathalast
Satadhammova lābhena, laddhenapi na nandatīti.
::

::centre
Satadhammajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 180. Duddadajātakaṃ (2-3-10)

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo durannayo.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā satañca asataṃ, nānā hoti ito gati;
::

::gathalast
Asanto {pb:T:1.0064} nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyaṇāti {note:parāyanā (syā. ka.)}.
::

::centre
Duddadajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kalyāṇavaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Susamaññamigādhibhū māṇavako, vāripahūtarūpādiccupaṭṭhānā;
::

::gathalast
Sakaḷāyasatindukapaṅka puna, satadhamma sududdadakena dasāti.
::

#### 4. Asadisavaggo

#### 181. Asadisajātakaṃ (2-4-1)

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Dhanuggaho asadiso, rājaputto mahabbalo;
::

::gathalast
Dūrepātī akkhaṇavedhī, mahākāyappadālano.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbāmitte raṇaṃ katvā, na ca kañci viheṭhayi;
::

::gathalast
Bhātaraṃ sotthiṃ katvāna, saṃyamaṃ ajjhupāgamīti.
::

::centre
Asadisajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 182. Saṅgāmāvacarajātakaṃ (2-4-2)

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅgāmāvacaro {pb:V:1.0043}{pb:M:1.0047} sūro, balavā iti vissuto;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ {pb:T:1.0065} nu toraṇamāsajja, paṭikkamasi kuñjara.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Omadda khippaṃ palighaṃ, esikāni ca abbaha {note:ubbaha (syā.), abbhuha (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Toraṇāni ca madditvā, khippaṃ pavisa kuñjarāti.
::

::centre
Saṅgāmāvacarajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 183. Vālodakajātakaṃ (2-4-3)

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Vālodakaṃ apparasaṃ nihīnaṃ, pitvā {note:pītvā (sī. pī.)} mado jāyati gadrabhānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imañca pitvāna rasaṃ paṇītaṃ, mado na sañjāyati sindhavānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Appaṃ pivitvāna nihīnajacco, so majjatī tena janinda puṭṭho {note:phuṭṭho (sī. syā.), muṭṭho (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Dhorayhasīlī ca kulamhi jāto, na majjatī aggarasaṃ pivitvāti.
::

::centre
Vālodakajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 184. Giridattajātakaṃ (2-4-4)

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Dūsito giridattena {note:giridantena (pī.)}, hayo sāmassa paṇḍavo;
::

::gathalast
Porāṇaṃ pakatiṃ hitvā, tassevānuvidhiyyati {note:nuvidhīyati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:T:1.0066} ca tanujo poso, sikharākāra {note:siṅgārākāra (syā.)} kappito;
::

::gathalast
Ānane naṃ {note:taṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} gahetvāna, maṇḍale parivattaye;
::

::gathalast
Khippameva pahantvāna, tassevānuvidhiyyatīti.
::

::centre
Giridattajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 185. Anabhiratijātakaṃ (2-4-5)

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Yathodake {pb:M:1.0048} āvile appasanne, na passati sippikasambukañca;
::

::gathalast
Sakkharaṃ vālukaṃ macchagumbaṃ, evaṃ āvilamhi {note:āvile hi (sī.)} citte;
::

::gathalast
Na passati attadatthaṃ paratthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Yathodake {pb:V:1.0044} acche vippasanne, so passati sippikasambukañca;
::

::gathalast
Sakkharaṃ vālukaṃ macchagumbaṃ, evaṃ anāvilamhi citte;
::

::gathalast
So passati attadatthaṃ paratthanti.
::

::centre
Anabhiratijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 186. Dadhivāhanajātakaṃ (2-4-6)

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Vaṇṇagandharasūpeto{pb:T:1.0067}, amboyaṃ ahuvā pure;
::

::gathalast
Tameva pūjaṃ labhamāno, kenambo kaṭukapphalo.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Pucimandaparivāro, ambo te dadhivāhana;
::

::gathalast
Mūlaṃ mūlena saṃsaṭṭhaṃ, sākhā sākhā {note:sākhaṃ (syā. ka.)} nisevare {note:nivīsare (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Asātasannivāsena, tenambo kaṭukapphaloti.
::

::centre
Dadhivāhanajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 187. Catumaṭṭhajātakaṃ (2-4-7)

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Ucce viṭabhimāruyha, mantayavho rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Nīce oruyha mantavho, migarājāpi sossati.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ suvaṇṇo suvaṇṇena {note:yaṃ supaṇṇo supaṇṇena (sī. syā. pī.)}, devo devena mantaye;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ tettha catumaṭṭhassa, bilaṃ pavisa jambukāti.
::

::centre
Catumaṭṭhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 188. Sīhakotthujātakaṃ (2-4-8)

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Sīhaṅgulī {pb:M:1.0049} sīhanakho, sīhapādapatiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
So sīho sīhasaṅghamhi, eko nadati aññathā.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0068} tvaṃ nadi rājaputta, appasaddo vane vasa;
::

::gathalast
Sarena kho {note:mā (ka.)} taṃ jāneyyuṃ, na hi te pettiko saroti.
::

::centre
Sīhakotthujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 189. Sīhacammajātakaṃ (2-4-9)

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Netaṃ sīhassa naditaṃ, na byagghassa na {note:byagghassa na ca (ka.)} dīpino;
::

::gathalast
Pāruto sīhacammena, jammo nadati gadrabho.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Cirampi {pb:V:1.0045} kho taṃ khādeyya, gadrabho haritaṃ yavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pāruto sīhacammena, ravamānova dūsayīti.
::

::centre
Sīhacammajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 190. Sīlānisaṃsajātakaṃ (2-4-10)

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Passa saddhāya sīlassa, cāgassa ca ayaṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāgo nāvāya vaṇṇena, saddhaṃ vahatupāsakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satañhi sannivāsena, sotthiṃ gacchati nhāpitoti.
::

::centre
Sīlānisaṃsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Asadisavaggo catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Dhanuggaha {pb:T:1.0069} kuñjara apparaso, giridattamanāvilacittavaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dadhivāhana jambūka sīhanakho, haritayava nāgavarena dasāti.
::

#### 5. Ruhakavaggo

#### 191. Ruhakajātakaṃ (2-5-1)

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:M:1.0050} {note:ambho (syā. ka. sī.)} ruhaka chinnāpi, jiyā sandhīyate puna;
::

::gathalast
Sandhīyassu purāṇiyā, mā kodhassa vasaṃ gami.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Vijjamānesu vākesu {note:vijjamānāsu maruvāsu (sī.), vijjamānāsu marūdvāsu (pī.)}, vijjamānesu kārisu;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ jiyaṃ karissāmi, alaññeva purāṇiyāti.
::

::centre
Ruhakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 192. Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ (2-5-2)

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Itthī siyā rūpavatī, sā ca sīlavatī siyā;
::

::gathalast
Puriso taṃ na iccheyya, saddahāsi mahosadha.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Saddahāmi {pb:V:1.0046} mahārāja, puriso dubbhago siyā;
::

::gathalast
Sirī {pb:T:1.0070} ca kāḷakaṇṇī ca, na samenti kudācananti.
::

::centre
Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 193. Cūḷapadumajātakaṃ (2-5-3)

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Ayameva sā ahamapi {note:ahampi (sī. syā. pī.), ahasmi (ka.)} so anañño, ayameva so hatthacchinno anañño;
::

::gathalast
Yamāha ‘‘komārapatī mama’’nti, vajjhitthiyo natthi itthīsu saccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Imañca jammaṃ musalena hantvā, luddaṃ chavaṃ paradārūpaseviṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imissā ca naṃ pāpapatibbatāya, jīvantiyā chindatha kaṇṇanāsanti.
::

::centre
Cūḷapadumajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 194. Maṇicorajātakaṃ (2-5-4)

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0051} santi devā pavasanti nūna, na hi nūna santi idha lokapālā;
::

::gathalast
Sahasā karontānamasaññatānaṃ, na hi nūna santī paṭisedhitāro.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Akāle vassatī tassa, kāle tassa na vassati;
::

::gathalast
Saggā {pb:T:1.0071} ca cavati ṭhānā, nanu so tāvatā hatoti.
::

::centre
Maṇicorajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 195. Pabbatūpattharajātakaṃ (2-5-5)

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Pabbatūpatthare {note:pabbatapatthare (sī. syā. pī.)} ramme, jātā pokkharaṇī sivā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ siṅgālo apāpāyi {note:apāpāsi (sī. syā. pī.)}, jānaṃ sīhena rakkhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Pivanti ce {note:pivanti ve (sī.), pivantiva (pī.), pivanteva (?)} mahārāja, sāpadāni mahānadiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tena anadī hoti, khamassu yadi te piyāti.
::

::centre
Pabbatūpatthara {note:pabbatapatthara (sī. syā. pī.)} jātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 196. Valāhakassajātakaṃ (2-5-6)

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Ye na kāhanti ovādaṃ, narā buddhena desitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Byasanaṃ te gamissanti, rakkhasīhiva vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:V:1.0047} ca kāhanti ovādaṃ, narā buddhena desitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sotthiṃ pāraṃ gamissanti, valāheneva {note:vālāheneva (sī. pī.)} vāṇijāti.
::

::centre
Valāhakassa {note:vālāhassa (sī. pī.)} jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 197. Mittāmittajātakaṃ (2-5-7)

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Na naṃ umhayate disvā, na ca naṃ paṭinandati;
::

::gathalast
Cakkhūni cassa na dadāti, paṭilomañca vattati.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Ete {pb:T:1.0072}{pb:M:1.0052} bhavanti ākārā, amittasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Yehi amittaṃ jāneyya, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍitoti.
::

::centre
Mittāmittajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 198. Rādhajātakaṃ (2-5-8)

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Pavāsā āgato tāta, idāni nacirāgato;
::

::gathalast
Kaccinnu tāta te mātā, na aññamupasevati.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Na kho panetaṃ subhaṇaṃ, giraṃ saccupasaṃhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sayetha poṭṭhapādova, mummure {note:mummure (syā.), maṃ pure (ka.) mummurasaddo thusaggimhi kukkuḷe ca vattatīti sakkatābhidhānesu} upakūthitoti {note:upakūsitoti (sī. syā. pī.), upakūlito (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Rādhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 199. Gahapatijātakaṃ (2-5-9)

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Ubhayaṃ me na khamati, ubhayaṃ me na ruccati;
::

::gathalast
Yācāyaṃ koṭṭhamotiṇṇā, nāddasaṃ iti bhāsati.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ gāmapati brūmi, kadare appasmi jīvite;
::

::gathalast
Dve māse saṅgaraṃ katvā {note:kāraṃ katvāna (sī. pī.), saṃkaraṃ katvā (ka.)}, maṃsaṃ jaraggavaṃ kisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appattakāle codesi, tampi mayhaṃ na ruccatīti.
::

::centre
Gahapatijātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 200. Sādhusīlajātakaṃ (2-5-10)

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Sarīradabyaṃ {pb:T:1.0073} vuḍḍhabyaṃ {note:vaddhabyaṃ (sī. pī.)}, sojaccaṃ sādhusīliyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brāhmaṇaṃ teva pucchāma, kannu tesaṃ vanimhase {note:vaṇimhase (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Attho {pb:V:1.0048} atthi sarīrasmiṃ, vuḍḍhabyassa namo kare;
::

::gathalast
Attho atthi sujātasmiṃ, sīlaṃ asmāka ruccatīti.
::

::centre
Sādhusīlajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Ruhakavaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Apiruhaka {pb:M:1.0053} rūpavatī musalo, pavasanti sapañcamapokkharaṇī;
::

::gathalast
Atha muttimavāṇija umhayate, ciraāgata koṭṭha sarīra dasāti.
::

#### 6. Nataṃdaḷhavaggo

#### 201. Bandhanāgārajātakaṃ (2-6-1)

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Na taṃ daḷhaṃ bandhanamāhu dhīrā, yadāyasaṃ dārujapabbajañca {note:babbajañca (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sārattarattā maṇikuṇḍalesu, puttesu {pb:T:1.0074} dāresu ca yā apekkhā.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Etaṃ daḷhaṃ bandhanamāhu dhīrā, ohārinaṃ sithilaṃ duppamuñcaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etampi chetvāna vajanti dhīrā, anapekkhino kāmasukhaṃ pahāyāti.
::

::centre
Bandhanāgārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 202. Keḷisīlajātakaṃ (2-6-2)

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca, hatthayo {note:hatthino (sī.), hatthiyo (syā. pī.)} pasadā migā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe sīhassa bhāyanti, natthi kāyasmi tulyatā.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva manussesu, daharo cepi paññavā;
::

::gathalast
So hi tattha mahā hoti, neva bālo sarīravāti.
::

::centre
Keḷisīlajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 203. Khaṇḍajātakaṃ (2-6-3)

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Virūpakkhehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ erāpathehi me;
::

::gathalast
Chabyāputtehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ kaṇhāgotamakehi ca.
::

::gatha1
Apādakehi {pb:V:1.0049}{pb:M:1.0054} me mettaṃ, mettaṃ dvipādakehi me;
::

::gathalast
Catuppadehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ bahuppadehi me.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0075} maṃ apādako hiṃsi, mā maṃ hiṃsi dvipādako;
::

::gathalast
Mā maṃ catuppado hiṃsi, mā maṃ hiṃsi bahuppado.
::

::gatha1
Sabbe sattā sabbe pāṇā, sabbe bhūtā ca kevalā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhadrāni passantu, mā kañci {note:kiñci (syā. ka.)} pāpamāgamā.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Appamāṇo buddho, appamāṇo dhammo;
::

::gatha2
Appamāṇo saṅgho, pamāṇavantāni sarīsapāni {note:sirisapāni (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ahivicchikasatapadī, uṇṇanābhi {note:uṇṇānābhi (sī. syā. pī.)} sarabūmūsikā.
::

::gatha1
Katā me rakkhā katā me parittā, paṭikkamantu bhūtāni;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ namo bhagavato, namo sattannaṃ sammāsambuddhānanti.
::

::centre
Khaṇḍajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 204. Vīrakajātakaṃ (2-6-4)

::hangnum

::

::gatha1
{note:abhidhāvathā ca patathā ca, vividhavinaditā ca dantibhi; vattatajja tumulo ghoso, yathā vijjutā jaladharassa gajjatoti; (sī. pī. ka.)} Abhidhāvatha {pb:M:1.0063} cūpadhāvatha ca {note:abhidhāvathā cuppatathā ca (syā.)}, vividhā vināditā {note:vināditattha (ka.)} vadantibhi;
::

::gathalast

#### 230. Dutiyapalāyitajātakaṃ (2-8-10)

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
Dhajamaparimitaṃ anantapāraṃ, duppasahaṃdhaṅkehi sāgaraṃva {note:sāgaramiva (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Girimivaanilena duppasayho {note:duppasaho (sī. pī. ka.)}, duppasaho ahamajjatādisena.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0088} bāliyaṃ vilapi {note:vippalapi (bahūsu)} na hissa tādisaṃ, viḍayhase {note:viḷayhase (sī. pī.)} na hi labhase nisedhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsajjasi gajamiva ekacārinaṃ, yo taṃ padā naḷamiva pothayissatīti.
::

::centre
Dutiyapalāyitajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kāsāvavaggo aṭṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varavatthavaco {pb:V:1.0057} dumakhīṇaphalaṃ, caturodhammavaraṃ purisuttama;
::

::gathalast
Dhaṅkamagadhā ca tayogirināma, gajaggavaro dhajavarena dasāti.
::

#### 9. Upāhanavaggo

#### 231. Upāhanajātakaṃ (2-9-1)

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi {pb:M:1.0064} kītā purisassupāhanā, sukhassa atthāya dukhaṃ udabbahe;
::

::gathalast
Ghammābhitattā thalasā papīḷitā, tasseva pāde purisassa khādare.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva {pb:T:1.0089} yo dukkulīno anariyo, tammāka {note:tamhāka (sī.), tumhāka (syā. pī.)} vijjañca sutañca ādiya;
::

::gathalast
Tameva so tattha sutena khādati, anariyo vuccati dupāhanūpamoti {note:pānadūpamoti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::centre
Upāhanajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 232. Vīṇāguṇajātakaṃ (2-9-2)

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
Ekacintito yamattho, bālo apariṇāyako;
::

::gathalast
Na hi khujjena vāmena, bhoti saṅgantumarahasi.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
Purisūsabhaṃ maññamānā, ahaṃ khujjamakāmayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Soyaṃ saṃkuṭito seti, chinnatanti yathā viṇāti {note:thuṇāti (sī.)}.
::

::centre
Vīṇāguṇajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 233. Vikaṇṇajātakaṃ (2-9-3)

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ yahiṃ icchasi tena gaccha, viddhosi mammamhi {note:mamasmi (ka.)} vikaṇṇakena;
::

::gathalast
Hatosi bhattena suvāditena {note:savāditena (sī. syā. pī.)}, lolo ca macche anubandhamāno.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi {pb:M:1.0065} lokāmisaṃ opatanto, vihaññatī {pb:T:1.0090} cittavasānuvattī;
::

::gathalast
So haññati ñātisakhāna majjhe, macchānugo soriva suṃsumāroti {note:susumāro (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Vikaṇṇajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 234. Asitābhūjātakaṃ (2-9-4)

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1
Tvameva {pb:V:1.0058} dānimakara {note:makari (syā.), makarā (ka. sī.)}, yaṃ kāmo byagamā tayi;
::

::gathalast
Soyaṃ appaṭisandhiko, kharachinnaṃva renukaṃ {note:rerukaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
168\.
::

::gatha1
Atricchaṃ {note:atricchā (sī. syā. pī.)} atilobhena, atilobhamadena ca;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ hāyati atthamhā, ahaṃva asitābhuyāti.
::

::centre
Asitābhūjātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 235. Vacchanakhajātakaṃ (2-9-5)

::hangnum
169\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhā gharā vacchanakha, sahiraññā sabhojanā;
::

::gathalast
Yattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, sayeyyātha anussuko.
::

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
Gharā nānīhamānassa, gharā nābhaṇato musā;
::

::gathalast
Gharā nādinnadaṇḍassa, paresaṃ anikubbato {note:anikrubbato (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ chiddaṃ durabhisambhavaṃ {note:durabhibhavaṃ (sī. pī.)}, ko gharaṃ paṭipajjatīti.
::

Vacchanakhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 236. Bakajātakaṃ (2-9-6)

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaddako {pb:T:1.0091} vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo kumudasannibho;
::

::gathalast
Vūpasantehi pakkhehi, mandamandova jhāyati.
::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
::

::gathalast
Amhe dijo na pāleti, tena pakkhī na phandatīti.
::

::centre
Bakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 237. Sāketajātakaṃ (2-9-7)

::hangnum
173\.
::

::gatha1
Ko {pb:M:1.0066} nu kho bhagavā hetu, ekacce idha puggale;
::

::gathalast
Atīva hadayaṃ nibbāti, cittañcāpi pasīdati.
::

::hangnum
174\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbeva sannivāsena, paccuppannahitena vā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ taṃ jāyate pemaṃ, uppalaṃva yathodaketi.
::

::centre
Sāketajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 238. Ekapadajātakaṃ (2-9-8)

::hangnum
175\.
::

::gatha1
Iṅgha {pb:V:1.0059} ekapadaṃ tāta, anekatthapadassitaṃ {note:padanissitaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kiñci saṅgāhikaṃ brūsi, yenatthe sādhayemase.
::

::hangnum
176\.
::

::gatha1
Dakkheyyekapadaṃ tāta, anekatthapadassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tañca sīlena saññuttaṃ, khantiyā upapāditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ {pb:T:1.0092} mitte sukhāpetuṃ, amittānaṃ dukhāya cāti.
::

::centre
Ekapadajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 239. Haritamaṇḍūkajātakaṃ (2-9-9)

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1
Āsīvisampi maṃ {note:āsīvisaṃ mamaṃ (sī. pī.)} santaṃ, paviṭṭhaṃ kumināmukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ruccate haritāmātā, yaṃ maṃ khādanti macchakā.
::

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
Vilumpateva puriso, yāvassa upakappati;
::

::gathalast
Yadā caññe vilumpanti, so vilutto vilumpatīti {note:viluppatīti (?)}.
::

::centre
Haritamaṇḍūkajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 240. Mahāpiṅgalajātakaṃ (2-9-10)

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbo jano hiṃsito piṅgalena, tasmiṃ mate paccayā {note:paccayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vedayanti;
::

::gathalast
Piyo nu te āsi akaṇhanetto, kasmā nu tvaṃ rodasi dvārapāla.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0067} me piyo āsi akaṇhanetto, bhāyāmi paccāgamanāya tassa;
::

::gathalast
Ito gato hiṃseyya maccurājaṃ, so hiṃsito āneyya puna idha.
::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
Daḍḍho vāhasahassehi, sitto ghaṭasatehi so;
::

::gathalast
Parikkhatā {pb:T:1.0093} ca sā bhūmi, mā bhāyi nāgamissatīti.
::

::centre
Mahāpiṅgalajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Upāhanavaggo navamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varupāhana khujja vikaṇṇakako, asitābhuya pañcamavacchanakho;
::

::gathalast
Dija pemavaruttamaekapadaṃ, kumināmukha piṅgalakena dasāti.
::

#### 10. Siṅgālavaggo

#### 241. Sabbadāṭhijātakaṃ (2-10-1)

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅgālo {pb:V:1.0060} mānathaddho ca, parivārena atthiko;
::

::gathalast
Pāpuṇi mahatiṃ bhūmiṃ, rājāsi sabbadāṭhinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva manussesu, yo hoti parivāravā;
::

::gathalast
So hi tattha mahā hoti, siṅgālo viya dāṭhinanti.
::

::centre
Sabbadāṭhijātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 242. Sunakhajātakaṃ (2-10-2)

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
Bālo {pb:T:1.0094} vatāyaṃ sunakho, yo varattaṃ {note:yo ca yottaṃ (ka.)} na khādati;
::

::gathalast
Bandhanā ca pamuñceyya, asito ca gharaṃ vaje.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhitaṃ {pb:M:1.0068} me manasmiṃ me, atho me hadaye kataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, yāva passupatū jano {note:pasupatujjano (syā. ka.)}.
::

::centre
Sunakhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 243. Guttilajātakaṃ (2-10-3)

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
Sattatantiṃ sumadhuraṃ, rāmaṇeyyaṃ avācayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ raṅgamhi avheti, saraṇaṃ me hohi kosiya.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ taṃ saraṇaṃ samma {note:ahaṃ te saraṇaṃ homi (vi. va. 328)}, ahamācariyapūjako;
::

::gathalast
Na taṃ jayissati sisso, sissamācariya jessasīti.
::

::centre
Guttilajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 244. Vigaticchajātakaṃ (2-10-4)

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ passati na taṃ icchati, yañca na passati taṃ kiricchati;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi ciraṃ carissati, na hi taṃ lacchati yaṃ sa icchati.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ labhati na tena tussati, yañca pattheti laddhaṃ hīḷeti;
::

::gathalast
Icchā hi anantagocarā, vigaticchāna {note:vīticchānaṃ (sī. pī.)} namo karomaseti.
::

::centre
Vigaticcha {note:vīticcha (sī. pī.)} jātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 245. Mūlapariyāyajātakaṃ (2-10-5)

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
Kālo {pb:T:1.0095}{pb:V:1.0061} ghasati bhūtāni, sabbāneva sahattanā;
::

::gathalast
Yo ca kālaghaso bhūto, sa bhūtapacaniṃ paci.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
Bahūni narasīsāni, lomasāni brahāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Gīvāsu paṭimukkāni, kocidevettha kaṇṇavāti.
::

::centre
Mūlapariyāyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 246. Bālovādajātakaṃ (2-10-6)

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
Hantvā chetvā {note:jhatvā (sī. pī.), ghatvā (syā.)} vadhitvā ca, deti dānaṃ asaññato;
::

::gathalast
Edisaṃ bhattaṃ bhuñjamāno, sa pāpamupalimpati {note:sa pāpena upalippati (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
Puttadārampi {pb:M:1.0069} ce hantvā, deti dānaṃ asaññato;
::

::gathalast
Bhuñjamānopi sappañño, na pāpamupalimpatīti.
::

::centre
Bālovādajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 247. Pādañjalījātakaṃ (2-10-7)

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā pādañjalī sabbe, paññāya atirocati;
::

::gathalast
Tathā hi oṭṭhaṃ bhañjati, uttariṃ nūna passati.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, atthānatthañca bujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Aññatra {pb:T:1.0096} oṭṭhanibbhogā, nāyaṃ jānāti kiñcananti.
::

::centre
Pādañjalījātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 248. Kiṃsukopamajātakaṃ (2-10-8)

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbehi kiṃsuko diṭṭho, kiṃnvettha vicikicchatha;
::

::gathalast
Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, sārathī paripucchito.
::

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ sabbehi ñāṇehi, yesaṃ dhammā ajānitā;
::

::gathalast
Te ve dhammesu kaṅkhanti, kiṃsukasmiṃva bhātaroti.
::

::centre
Kiṃsukopamajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 249. Sālakajātakaṃ (2-10-9)

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
Ekaputtako {pb:V:1.0062} bhavissasi, tvañca no hessasi issaro kule;
::

::gathalast
Oroha dumasmā sālaka, ehi dāni gharakaṃ vajemase.
::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1
Nanu maṃ suhadayoti {note:nanu maṃ hadayeti (sī. pī.)} maññasi, yañca maṃ hanasi veḷuyaṭṭhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Pakkambavane ramāmase, gaccha tvaṃ gharakaṃ yathāsukhanti.
::

::centre
Sālakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 250. Kapijātakaṃ (2-10-10)

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
Ayaṃ {pb:T:1.0097}{pb:M:1.0070} isī upasamasaṃyame rato, sa tiṭṭhati {note:santiṭṭhati (sī. pī.)} sisirabhayena aṭṭito;
::

::gathalast
Handa ayaṃ pavisatumaṃ agārakaṃ, vinetu sītaṃ darathañca kevalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ isī upasamasaṃyame rato, kapī ayaṃ dumavarasākhagocaro;
::

::gathalast
So dūsako rosako cāpi jammo, sacevajemampi {note:sace + āvaje + imampi} dūseyyagāranti {note:dūsaye gharanti (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::centre
Kapijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Siṅgālavaggo dasamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha rājā siṅgālavaro sunakho, tathā kosiya icchati kālaghaso;
::

::gathalast
Atha dānavaroṭṭhapi sārathinā, punambavanañca sisirakapi dasāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Daḷhañca {pb:T:1.0098} vaggaṃ aparena santhavaṃ, kalyāṇavaggāsadiso ca rūhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nataṃdaḷha bīraṇathambhakaṃ puna, kāsāvupāhana siṅgālakena dasāti.
::

::centre
Dukanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 3. Tikanipāto

#### 1. Saṅkappavaggo

#### 251. Saṅkapparāgajātakaṃ (3-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkapparāgadhotena{pb:T:1.0099}{pb:V:1.0063}{pb:M:1.0071}, vitakkanisitena ca;
::

::gathalast
Nālaṅkatena bhadrena {note:nevālaṅkatabhadrena (syā.)}, usukārākatena ca {note:na usukārakatena ca (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Na kaṇṇāyatamuttena, nāpi morūpasevinā;
::

::gathalast
Tenamhi hadaye viddho, sabbaṅgaparidāhinā.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Āvedhañca na passāmi, yato ruhiramassave;
::

::gathalast
Yāva ayoniso cittaṃ, sayaṃ me dukkhamābhatanti.
::

::centre
Saṅkapparāgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 252. Tilamuṭṭhijātakaṃ (3-1-2)

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjāpi me taṃ manasi {note:sarasi (ka.)}, yaṃ maṃ tvaṃ tilamuṭṭhiyā;
::

::gathalast
Bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna, laṭṭhiyā anutāḷayi.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Nanu jīvite na ramasi, yenāsi brāhmaṇāgato;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ maṃ bāhā gahetvāna, tikkhattuṃ anutāḷayi.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Ariyo anariyaṃ kubbantaṃ {note:kubbānaṃ (sī. pī.), kubbaṃ (syā.)}, yo daṇḍena nisedhati;
::

::gathalast
Sāsanaṃ taṃ na taṃ veraṃ, iti naṃ paṇḍitā vidūti.
::

::centre
Tilamuṭṭhijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 253. Maṇikaṇṭhajātakaṃ (3-1-3)

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Mamannapānaṃ {pb:T:1.0100} vipulaṃ uḷāraṃ, uppajjatīmassa maṇissa hetu;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te na dassaṃ atiyācakosi, na cāpi te assamamāgamissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Susū {pb:V:1.0064}{pb:M:1.0072} yathā sakkharadhotapāṇī, tāsesi maṃ selaṃ yācamāno;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te na dassaṃ atiyācakosi, na cāpi te assamamāgamissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Na taṃ yāce yassa piyaṃ jigīse {note:jigiṃse (sī. syā. pī.)}, desso hoti atiyācanāya;
::

::gathalast
Nāgo maṇiṃ yācito brāhmaṇena, adassanaṃyeva tadajjhagamāti.
::

::centre
Maṇikaṇṭhajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 254. Kuṇḍakakucchisindhavajātakaṃ (3-1-4)

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Bhutvā tiṇaparighāsaṃ, bhutvā ācāmakuṇḍakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ te bhojanaṃ āsi, kasmā dāni na bhuñjasi.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Yattha posaṃ na jānanti, jātiyā vinayena vā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuṃ {note:pahū (sī. pī.), pahuṃ (syā. ka.)} tattha mahābramhe, api ācāmakuṇḍakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Tvañca {pb:T:1.0101} kho maṃ pajānāsi, yādisāyaṃ hayuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Jānanto jānamāgamma, na te bhakkhāmi kuṇḍakanti.
::

::centre
Kuṇḍakakucchisindhavajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 255. Sukajātakaṃ (3-1-5)

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Yāva so mattamaññāsi, bhojanasmiṃ vihaṅgamo;
::

::gathalast
Tāva addhānamāpādi, mātarañca aposayi.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Yato ca kho bahutaraṃ, bhojanaṃ ajjhavāhari {note:ajjhupāhari (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tato tattheva saṃsīdi, amattaññū hi so ahu.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā mattaññutā sādhu, bhojanasmiṃ agiddhatā {note:agiddhitā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Amattaññū hi sīdanti, mattaññū ca na sīdareti.
::

::centre
Sukajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 256. Jarūdapānajātakaṃ (3-1-6)

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Jarūdapānaṃ {pb:M:1.0073} khaṇamānā, vāṇijā udakatthikā;
::

::gatha2
Ajjhagamuṃ ayasaṃ lohaṃ {note:ajjhagaṃsu ayolohaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, tipusīsañca vāṇijā;
::

::gathalast
Rajataṃ jātarūpañca, muttā veḷūriyā bahū.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Te ca tena asantuṭṭhā, bhiyyo bhiyyo akhāṇisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te tatthāsīviso {note:tattha āsīviso (ka.), tatthapāsīviso (syā.)} ghoro, tejassī tejasā hani.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā {pb:T:1.0102}{pb:V:1.0065} khaṇe nātikhaṇe, atikhātaṃ {note:atikhaṇaṃ (ka.)} hi pāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khātena ca {note:khaṇena ca (ka.), khaṇanena (syā.)} dhanaṃ laddhaṃ, atikhātena {note:atikhaṇena (ka.)} nāsitanti.
::

::centre
Jarūdapānajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 257. Gāmaṇicandajātakaṃ (3-1-7)

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ gharānaṃ kusalo, lolo ayaṃ valīmukho;
::

::gathalast
Kataṃ kataṃ kho dūseyya, evaṃdhammamidaṃ kulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Nayidaṃ cittavato lomaṃ, nāyaṃ assāsiko migo;
::

::gathalast
Siṭṭhaṃ {note:satthaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} me janasandhena, nāyaṃ kiñci vijānati.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Na mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā, bhātaraṃ bhaginiṃ sakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhareyya tādiso poso, siṭṭhaṃ dasarathena meti.
::

::centre
Gāmaṇicanda {note:gāmaṇicaṇḍa (sī. pī.)} jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 258. Mandhātujātakaṃ (3-1-8)

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Yāvatā candimasūriyā, pariharanti disā bhanti virocanā {note:virocamānā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva dāsā mandhātu, ye pāṇā pathavissitā {note:paṭhavinissitā (sī. pī.), paṭhavissitā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Na kahāpaṇavassena, titti kāmesu vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Appassādā dukhā kāmā, iti viññāya paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:M:1.0074} dibbesu kāmesu, ratiṃ so nādhigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhakkhayarato {pb:T:1.0103} hoti, sammāsambuddhasāvakoti.
::

::centre
Mandhātujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 259. Tirīṭavacchajātakaṃ (3-1-9)

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Nayimassa vijjāmayamatthi kiñci, na bandhavo no pana te sahāyo;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena vaṇṇena tirīṭavaccho {note:tirīṭivaccho (syā. ka.)}, tedaṇḍiko bhuñjati aggapiṇḍaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Āpāsu {note:āvāsu (ka.)} me yuddhaparājitassa, ekassa katvā vivanasmi ghore;
::

::gathalast
Pasārayī kicchagatassa pāṇiṃ, tenūdatāriṃ dukhasaṃpareto.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Etassa {pb:V:1.0066} kiccena idhānupatto, vesāyino visayā jīvaloke;
::

::gathalast
Lābhāraho tāta tirīṭavaccho, dethassa bhogaṃ yajathañca {note:yajatañca (sī. pī.), yajitañca (syā.)} yaññanti.
::

::centre
Tirīṭavacchajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 260. Dūtajātakaṃ (3-1-10)

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Yassatthā {pb:T:1.0104} dūramāyanti, amittamapi yācituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassūdarassahaṃ dūto, mā me kujjha {note:kujjhi (sī. pī.)} rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa divā ca ratto ca, vasamāyanti māṇavā;
::

::gathalast
Tassūdarassahaṃ dūto, mā me kujjha {note:kujjhi (sī. pī.)} rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi {pb:M:1.0075} te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
::

::gathalast
Dūto hi dūtassa kathaṃ na dajjaṃ, mayampi tasseva bhavāma dūtāti.
::

::centre
Dūtajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Saṅkappavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Usukāravaro tilamuṭṭhi maṇi, hayarāja vihaṅgama āsiviso;
::

::gathalast
Janasandha kahāpaṇavassa puna, tiriṭaṃ puna dūtavarena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Padumavaggo

#### 261. Padumajātakaṃ (3-2-1)

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Evaṃ rūhatu te nāsā, padumaṃ dehi yācito.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā sāradikaṃ bījaṃ, khette vuttaṃ virūhati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ rūhatu te nāsā, padumaṃ dehi yācito.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Ubhopi palapantete {note:vilapantete (syā. ka.)}, api padmāni dassati;
::

::gatha2
Vajjuṃ vā te na vā vajjuṃ, natthi nāsāya rūhanā;
::

::gathalast
Dehi samma padumāni, ahaṃ yācāmi yācitoti.
::

::centre
Padumajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 262. Mudupāṇijātakaṃ (3-2-2)

::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Mudupāṇijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 264. Mahāpanādajātakaṃ (3-2-4)

::hangnum
40\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
41\.

::centre

#### 265. Khurappajātakaṃ (3-2-5)

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ bhayasmiṃ maraṇe viyūḷhe, kasmā nu te nāhu chambhitattaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā khurappe dhanuveganunne, khagge gahīte tikhiṇe teladhote;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ bhayasmiṃ maraṇe viyūḷhe, vedaṃ alatthaṃ vipulaṃ uḷāraṃ.

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::centre

#### 266. Vātaggasindhavajātakaṃ (3-2-6)

::hangnum
46\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ayaṃ so āgato bhattā {note:tāto (sī. syā. pī.)}, kasmā dāni palāyasi.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {note:na kho (syā. ka.)} panādikeneva, santhavo nāma jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Yaso hāyati itthīnaṃ, tasmā tāta palāyahaṃ {note:palāyihaṃ (syā.), palāyitaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Yassassinaṃ kule jātaṃ, āgataṃ yā na icchati;
::

::gathalast
Socati {pb:T:1.0108} cirarattāya, vātaggamiva bhaddalīti {note:kundalīti (sī. pī.), gadrabhīti (syā.)}.
::

::centre
Vātaggasindhavajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 267. Kakkaṭakajātakaṃ (3-2-7)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅgīmigo {pb:M:1.0078} āyatacakkhunetto, aṭṭhittaco vārisayo alomo;
::

::gathalast
Tenābhibhūto kapaṇaṃ rudāmi, mā heva maṃ pāṇasamaṃ jaheyya {note:jaheyyā (pī.) jahā’yye (?)}.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Ayya na taṃ jahissāmi, kuñjaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ {note:kuñjara saṭṭhihāyana (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pathabyā cāturantāya, suppiyo hosi me tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Ye kuḷīrā samuddasmiṃ, gaṅgāya yamunāya {note:nammadāya (sī. pī.)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ tvaṃ vārijo seṭṭho, muñca rodantiyā patinti.
::

::centre
Kakkaṭaka {note:kuḷīra (ka.)} jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 268. Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ (3-2-8)

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0069} ve sabbasametānaṃ, ahuvā seṭṭhasammato;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva tuvaṃ brahme, anaññāya vinindasi;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ mūlaṃ adisvāna {note:kathaṃhi mūlaṃ aditvā (syā. pī.)}, rukkhaṃ jaññā patiṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 269. Sujātajātakaṃ (3-2-9)

::hangnum
55\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Nanu passasimaṃ kāḷiṃ, dubbaṇṇaṃ tilakāhataṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
57\.

Tasmā {pb:M:1.0079} sakhilavācassa, mantabhāṇī anuddhato;
::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Sujātajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 270. Ulūkajātakaṃ (3-2-10)

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbehi kira ñātīhi, kosiyo issaro kato;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaṇa samma anuññāto, atthaṃ dhammañca kevalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Santi hi daharā pakkhī, paññavanto jutindharā.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Na me ruccati bhaddaṃ vo {note:bhadante (ka.)}, ulūkassābhisecanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkuddhassa {pb:T:1.0110} mukhaṃ passa, kathaṃ kuddho karissatīti.
::

::centre
Ulūkajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Padumavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Padumuttama {pb:V:1.0070} nāgasirivhayano, sa-mahaṇṇava yūpa khurappavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha bhaddalī kuñjara rukkha puna, kharavāca ulūkavarena dasāti.
::

#### 3. Udapānavaggo

#### 271. Udapānadūsakajātakaṃ (3-3-1)

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Āraññikassa isino, cirarattaṃ tapassino;
::

::gathalast
Kicchākataṃ udapānaṃ, kathaṃ samma avāhasi {note:avāhayi (sī. pī.), apāhasi (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Esa dhammo siṅgālānaṃ, yaṃ pitvā ohadāmase;
::

::gathalast
Pitupitāmahaṃ dhammo, na taṃ {note:na naṃ (sī. pī.)} ujjhātumarahasi.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Yesaṃ {pb:T:1.0111}{pb:M:1.0080} vo ediso dhammo, adhammo pana kīdiso;
::

::gathalast
Mā vo dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, addasāma kudācananti.
::

::centre
Udapānadūsakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 272. Byagghajātakaṃ (3-3-2)

::hangnum

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Yena mittena saṃsaggā, yogakkhemo pavaḍḍhati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Etha byagghā nivattavho, paccupetha {note:paccametha (sī. pī.)} mahāvanaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Byagghajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 273. Kacchapajātakaṃ (3-3-3)

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ {pb:V:1.0071} kapismi dummedho, anāmāsāni āmasiṃ;

::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Kacchapajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 274. Lolajātakaṃ (3-3-4)

71\.

::centre
Lolajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 276. Kurudhammajātakaṃ (3-3-6)

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Tava saddhañca sīlañca, viditvāna janādhipa;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi {pb:V:1.0072} vo brāhmaṇā nāgametaṃ, rājārahaṃ rājabhoggaṃ yasassinaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::centre
Kurudhammajātakaṃ {note:kurudhammajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 277. Romakajātakaṃ (3-3-7)

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Vassāni {pb:M:1.0082} paññāsa samādhikāni, vasimha selassa guhāya romaka;
::

::gathalast
Asaṅkamānā abhinibbutattā {note:abhinibbutacittā (syā. ka.)}, hatthatta {note:hatthattha (syā.)} māyanti mamaṇḍajā pure.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Te dāni vakkaṅga kimatthamussukā, bhajanti aññaṃ girikandaraṃ dijā;
::

::gathalast
Na nūna maññanti mamaṃ yathā pure, cirappavutthā atha vā na te ime.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Jānāma taṃ na mayaṃ sampamūḷhā {note:na maya’masma mūḷhā (sī. pī.)}, soyeva tvaṃ te mayamasma nāññe;
::

::gathalast
Cittañca {pb:T:1.0114} te asmiṃ jane paduṭṭhaṃ, ājīvikā {note:ājīvaka (sī. syā.), ājīvika (pī.)} tena tamuttasāmāti.
::

::centre
Romakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 278. Mahiṃsarājajātakaṃ (3-3-8)

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Kimattha {note:kamattha (sī. pī.)} mabhisandhāya, lahucittassa dubbhino {note:dūbhino (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmadadasseva {note:duhasseva (sī. syā. pī.), rahasseva (ka.)}, imaṃ dukkhaṃ titikkhasi.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅgena nihanāhetaṃ, padasā ca adhiṭṭhaha;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyo {note:bhīyo (sī.)} bālā pakujjheyyuṃ, no cassa paṭisedhako.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Mamevāyaṃ maññamāno, aññepevaṃ {note:aññampevaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} karissati;
::

::gathalast
Te naṃ tattha vadhissanti, sā me mutti bhavissatīti.
::

::centre
Mahiṃsarājajātakaṃ {note:mahisajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 279. Satapattajātakaṃ (3-3-9)

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā {pb:M:1.0083} māṇavako panthe, siṅgāliṃ vanagocariṃ;
::

::gatha2
Atthakāmaṃ pavedentiṃ {note:pavadantiṃ (pī.)}, anatthakāmāti maññati;
::

::gathalast
Anatthakāmaṃ satapattaṃ, atthakāmoti maññati.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva idhekacco, puggalo hoti tādiso;
::

::gathalast
Hitehi vacanaṃ vutto, paṭigaṇhāti vāmato.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:T:1.0115}{pb:V:1.0073} ca kho naṃ pasaṃsanti, bhayā ukkaṃsayanti vā {note:ca (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tañhi so maññate mittaṃ, satapattaṃva māṇavoti.
::

::centre
Satapattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 280. Puṭadūsakajātakaṃ (3-3-10)

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi nūna migarājā, puṭakammassa kovido;
::

::gathalast
Tathā hi puṭaṃ dūseti, aññaṃ nūna karissati.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Na me mātā vā pitā vā, puṭakammassa kovido;
::

::gathalast
Kataṃ kataṃ kho dūsema, evaṃ dhammamidaṃ kulaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Yesaṃ vo ediso dhammo, adhammo pana kīdiso;
::

::gathalast
Mā vo dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, addasāma kudācananti.
::

::centre
Puṭadūsakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Udapānavaggo {note:araññavaggo (sī. pī. ka.)} tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Udapānavaraṃ vanabyaggha kapi, sikhinī ca balāka ruciravaro;
::

::gathalast
Sujanādhiparomakadūsa puna, satapattavaro puṭakamma dasāti.
::

#### 4. Abbhantaravaggo

::hangnum
92\.

#### 282. Seyyajātakaṃ (3-4-2)

::hangnum
94\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
{note:kasmā…pe… saggaṃ na gaccheyya (katthaci)} Tasmā sabbena lokena, sandhiṃ katvāna ekato {note:ekako (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pecca saggaṃ nigaccheyya {note:kasmā…pe… saggaṃ na gaccheyya (katthaci)}, idaṃ suṇātha kāsiyā {note:kāsayo (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ vatvā mahārājā, kaṃso bārāṇasiggaho;
::

::gathalast
Dhanuṃ kaṇḍañca {note:tūṇiñca (sī. pī.)} nikkhippa, saṃyamaṃ ajjhupāgamīti.
::

::centre
Seyyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 283. Vaḍḍhakīsūkarajātakaṃ (3-4-3)

::gathalast

::gathalast

::centre

#### 299. Komāraputtajātakaṃ (3-5-9)

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
