::

::gathalast
Karohare {note:karohi re (ka.)} makkaṭiyāni makkaṭa, na taṃ mayaṃ sīlavataṃ ramāma.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Sutā {pb:T:1.0126} hi mayhaṃ paramā visuddhi, komāraputtassa bahussutassa;
::

::gathalast
Mā dāni maṃ maññi tuvaṃ yathā pure, jhānānuyutto viharāmi {note:jhānānuyuttā viharāma (sī. pī.)} āvuso.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Sacepi selasmi vapeyya bījaṃ, devo ca vasse na hi taṃ virūḷhe {note:neva hi taṃ ruheyya (sī. pī.), na hi taṃ virūhe (?)};
::

::gathalast
Sutā hi te sā paramā visuddhi, ārā tuvaṃ makkaṭa jhānabhūmiyāti.
::

::centre
Komāraputtajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 300. Vakajātakaṃ (3-5-10)

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Parapāṇarodhā {pb:V:1.0080} {note:parapāṇaghāte (syā.), parapāṇarocaṃ (ka.)} jīvanto, maṃsalohitabhojano;
::

::gathalast
Vako vataṃ samādāya, upapajji uposathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa sakko vataññāya, ajarūpenupāgami;
::

::gathalast
Vītatapo ajjhappatto, bhañji lohitapo tapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva {pb:M:1.0092} idhekacce, samādānamhi dubbalā;
::

::gathalast
Lahuṃ karonti attānaṃ, vakova ajakāraṇāti.
::

::centre
Vakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kumbhavaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varakumbha {pb:T:1.0127} supattasirivhayano, sucisammata bindusaro cusabho;
::

::gathalast
Saritaṃpati caṇḍi jarākapinā, atha makkaṭiyā vakakena dasāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Saṅkappo padumo ceva, udapānena tatiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abbhantaraṃ ghaṭabhedaṃ, tikanipātamhilaṅkatanti.
::

::centre
Tikanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 4. Catukkanipāto

#### 1. Kāliṅgavaggo

#### 301. Cūḷakāliṅgajātakaṃ (4-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Vivarathimāsaṃ {pb:T:1.0128}{pb:V:1.0081}{pb:M:1.0093} {note:vivaratha imāsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} dvāraṃ, nagaraṃ pavisantu {note:pavisituṃ mayā; (ka.)} aruṇarājassa;
::

::gathalast
Sīhena susiṭṭhena, surakkhitaṃ {note:susatthena, surakkhitaṃ (sī. pī.), susiṭṭhena (ka.)} nandisenena.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Jayo kaliṅgānamasayhasāhinaṃ, parājayo anayo {note:ajayo (syā.), anvito (ka.)} assakānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Icceva te bhāsitaṃ brahmacāri, na ujjubhūtā vitathaṃ bhaṇanti.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Devā musāvādamupātivattā, saccaṃ dhanaṃ paramaṃ tesu {note:tathaṃ pemakaraṃ nu (ka.), tathaṃ paramaṃ karaṃ nu (syā.)} sakka;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te musā bhāsitaṃ devarāja, kiṃ vā paṭicca maghavā mahinda.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Nanu te sutaṃ brāhmaṇa bhaññamāne, devā na issanti purisaparakkamassa;
::

::gatha2
Damo samādhi manaso abhejjo {note:adejjo (sī. pī.), abhijjo (ka.)}, abyaggatā {pb:T:1.0129} nikkamanañca {note:nikkhamanañca (sī.)} kāle;
::

::gathalast
Daḷhañca viriyaṃ purisaparakkamo ca, teneva āsi vijayo assakānanti.
::

::centre
Cūḷakāliṅgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 302. Mahāassārohajātakaṃ (4-1-2)

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Adeyyesu dadaṃ dānaṃ, deyyesu nappavecchati;
::

::gathalast
Āpāsu byasanaṃ patto, sahāyaṃ nādhigacchati.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Nādeyyesu {pb:M:1.0094} dadaṃ dānaṃ, deyyesu yo pavecchati;
::

::gathalast
Āpāsu byasanaṃ patto, sahāyamadhigacchati.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Saññogasambhogavisesadassanaṃ, anariyadhammesu saṭhesu nassati;
::

::gathalast
Katañca ariyesu ca ajjavesu, mahapphalaṃ hoti aṇumpi tādisu.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Yo pubbe katakalyāṇo, akā loke sudukkaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pacchā kayirā na vā kayirā, accantaṃ pūjanārahoti.
::

::centre
Mahāassārohajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 303. Ekarājajātakaṃ (4-1-3)

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Anuttare {pb:T:1.0130}{pb:V:1.0082} kāmaguṇe samiddhe, bhutvāna pubbe vasī ekarāja;
::

::gathalast
So dāni dugge narakamhi khitto, nappajjahe vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbeva khantī ca tapo ca mayhaṃ, sampatthitā dubbhisena {note:dabbasenā (sī. pī.)} ahosi;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ dāni laddhāna kathaṃ nu rāja, jahe ahaṃ vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbā kirevaṃ pariniṭṭhitāni, yasassinaṃ paññavantaṃ visayha;
::

::gathalast
Yaso ca laddhā purimaṃ uḷāraṃ, nappajjahe vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Panujja dukkhena sukhaṃ janinda, sukhena vā dukkhamasayhasāhi;
::

::gathalast
Ubhayattha santo abhinibbutattā, sukhe ca dukkhe ca bhavanti tulyāti.
::

::centre
Ekarājajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 304. Daddarajātakaṃ (4-1-4)

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Imāni {pb:T:1.0131}{pb:M:1.0095} maṃ daddara tāpayanti, vācāduruttāni manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Maṇḍūkabhakkhā udakantasevī, āsīvisaṃ maṃ avisā sapanti.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Sakā raṭṭhā pabbājito, aññaṃ janapadaṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Mahantaṃ koṭṭhaṃ kayirātha, duruttānaṃ {note:duruttāni (ka.)} nidhetave.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Yattha posaṃ na jānanti, jātiyā vinayena vā;
::

::gathalast
Na tattha mānaṃ kayirātha, vasamaññātake jane.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Videsavāsaṃ vasato, jātavedasamenapi {note:jātavedabhayenapi (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Khamitabbaṃ sapaññena, api dāsassa tajjitanti.
::

::centre
Daddarajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 305. Sīlavīmaṃsanajātakaṃ (4-1-5)

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Natthi loke raho nāma, pāpakammaṃ pakubbato;
::

::gathalast
Passanti vanabhūtāni, taṃ bālo maññatī raho.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ raho na passāmi, suññaṃ vāpi na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Yattha aññaṃ {note:suññaṃ (syā. ka.)} na passāmi, asuññaṃ hoti taṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Dujjacco ca sujacco {note:ajacco (pī.)} ca, nando ca sukhavaḍḍhito {note:sukhavacchako (sī.), sukhavacchano (syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Vejjo {pb:T:1.0132} ca addhuvasīlo {note:atha sīlo (ka.)} ca, te dhammaṃ jahu matthikā.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Brāhmaṇo {pb:V:1.0083} ca kathaṃ jahe, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
::

::gathalast
Yo dhammamanupāleti, dhitimā saccanikkamoti.
::

::centre
Sīlavīmaṃsanajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 306. Sujātajātakaṃ (4-1-6)

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Kimaṇḍakā {pb:M:1.0096} ime deva, nikkhittā kaṃsamallake;
::

::gathalast
Upalohitakā vaggū, taṃ {note:te (pī.)} me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Yāni pure tuvaṃ devi, bhaṇḍu nantakavāsinī;
::

::gathalast
Ucchaṅgahatthā pacināsi, tassā te koliyaṃ phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Uḍḍayhate na ramati, bhogā vippajahanti taṃ {note:vippajahanti’maṃ (?)};
::

::gathalast
Tatthevimaṃ paṭinetha, yattha kolaṃ pacissati.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Honti hete mahārāja, iddhippattāya {note:iddhimattāya (ka.)} nāriyā;
::

::gathalast
Khama deva sujātāya, māssā {note:māsu (ka.)} kujjha rathesabhāti.
::

::centre
Sujātajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 307. Palāsajātakaṃ (4-1-7)

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Acetanaṃ brāhmaṇa assuṇantaṃ, jāno ajānantamimaṃ palāsaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āraddhaviriyo dhuvaṃ appamatto, sukhaseyyaṃ {pb:T:1.0133} pucchasi kissa hetu.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Dūre suto ceva brahā ca rukkho, dese ṭhito bhūtanivāsarūpo;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā namassāmi imaṃ palāsaṃ, ye cettha bhūtā te {note:te ca (sī. pī.)} dhanassa hetu.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
So te karissāmi yathānubhāvaṃ, kataññutaṃ brāhmaṇa pekkhamāno;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi āgamma sataṃ sakāse, moghāni te assu pariphanditāni.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0097} tindukarukkhassa paro {note:puro (ka.)} pilakkho {note:pilakkhu (sī. pī.), milakkhu (ka.)}, parivārito pubbayañño uḷāro;
::

::gathalast
Tassesa mūlasmiṃ nidhi nikhāto, adāyādo gaccha taṃ uddharāhīti.
::

::centre
Palāsajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 308. Sakuṇajātakaṃ (4-1-8)

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Akaramhasa te kiccaṃ, yaṃ balaṃ ahuvamhase;
::

::gathalast
Migarāja namo tyatthu, api kiñci labhāmase.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Mama {pb:V:1.0084} lohitabhakkhassa, niccaṃ luddāni kubbato;
::

::gathalast
Dantantaragato santo, taṃ bahuṃ yampi jīvasi.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Akataññumakattāraṃ{pb:T:1.0134}, katassa appaṭikārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiṃ kataññutā natthi, niratthā tassa sevanā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa sammukhaciṇṇena, mittadhammo na labbhati;
::

::gathalast
Anusūya {note:anusuyya (sī. pī.)} manakkosaṃ, saṇikaṃ tamhā apakkameti.
::

::centre
Sakuṇajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 309. Chavakajātakaṃ (4-1-9)

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbamidaṃ carimaṃ kataṃ {note:carimavataṃ (sī. pī.)}, ubho dhammaṃ na passare;
::

::gatha2
Ubho pakatiyā cutā, yo cāyaṃ mantejjhāpeti {note:mantajjhāyati (sī.), sajjhāpayati (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yo ca mantaṃ adhīyati.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Sālīnaṃ odanaṃ bhuñje, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā etaṃ na sevāmi, dhammaṃ isīhi sevitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Paribbaja mahā loko {note:mahābrahme (ka.)}, pacantaññepi pāṇino;
::

::gathalast
Mā taṃ adhammo ācarito, asmā kumbhamivābhidā.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu {pb:M:1.0098} taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vāti.
::

::centre
Chavakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 310. Seyyajātakaṃ (4-1-10)

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ{pb:T:1.0135}, mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na icche saha nindāya, evaṃ seyya {note:sayha (sī. syā. pī.)} vijānahi.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vā.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
::

::gathalast
Sāyeva jīvikā seyyo, yā cādhammena esanā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:V:1.0085} ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ ahiṃsayaṃ loke, api rajjena taṃ varanti.
::

::centre
Seyyajātakaṃ {note:sayhajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kāliṅgavaggo {note:vivaravaggo (sī. pī.)} paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Vivarañca adeyya samiddhavaraṃ, atha daddara pāpamahātiraho;
::

::gathalast
Atha koli palāsavarañca kara, carimaṃ sasamuddavarena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Pucimandavaggo

#### 311. Pucimandajātakaṃ (4-2-1)

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhehi cora kiṃ sesi, ko attho supanena {note:supitena (sī.), supinena (pī. ka.)} te;
::

::gathalast
Mā {pb:T:1.0136} taṃ gahesuṃ {note:gaṇheyyuṃ (ka.)} rājāno, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0099} nu {note:nūna (syā.)} coraṃ gahessanti, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ tattha pucimandassa, vane jātassa tiṭṭhato.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Na tvaṃ assattha jānāsi, mama corassa cantaraṃ;
::

::gatha2
Coraṃ gahetvā rājāno, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appenti {note:accenti (syā.)} nimbasūlasmiṃ, tasmiṃ me saṅkate mano.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkeyya saṅkitabbāni, rakkheyyānāgataṃ bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatabhayā dhīro, ubho loke avekkhatīti.
::

::centre
Pucimandajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 312. Kassapamandiyajātakaṃ (4-2-2)

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Api kassapa mandiyā, yuvā sapati hanti {note:sampaṭihanti (ka.)} vā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ taṃ khamate dhīro, paṇḍito taṃ titikkhati.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Sacepi santo vivadanti, khippaṃ sandhīyare puna;
::

::gathalast
Bālā pattāva bhijjanti, na te samathamajjhagū.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Ete {pb:V:1.0086} bhiyyo samāyanti, sandhi tesaṃ na jīrati;
::

::gathalast
Yo cādhipannaṃ jānāti, yo ca jānāti desanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Eso hi uttaritaro, bhāravaho dhuraddharo;
::

::gathalast
Yo paresādhipannānaṃ{pb:T:1.0137}, sayaṃ sandhātumarahatīti.
::

::centre
Kassapamandiyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 313. Khantīvādījātakaṃ (4-2-3)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Yo te hatthe ca pāde ca, kaṇṇanāsañca chedayi;
::

::gathalast
Tassa kujjha mahāvīra, mā raṭṭhaṃ vinasā {note:vinassa (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} idaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Yo me hatthe ca pāde ca, kaṇṇanāsañca chedayi;
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ jīvatu so rājā, na hi kujjhanti mādisā.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Ahū atītamaddhānaṃ {note:ahu atītamaddhāne (syā. pī. ka.)}, samaṇo khantidīpano;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ khantiyāyeva ṭhitaṃ, kāsirājā achedayi.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {pb:M:1.0100} kamma {note:kammassa (sī. pī.)} pharusassa, vipāko kaṭuko ahu;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ kāsirājā vedesi, nirayamhi samappitoti.
::

::centre
Khantīvādījātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 314. Lohakumbhijātakaṃ (4-2-4)

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Dujjīvitamajīvimha, ye sante {note:yesaṃ no (syā. ka.)} na dadamhase;
::

::gathalast
Vijjamānesu bhogesu, dīpaṃ nākamha attano.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Saṭṭhi {note:saṭṭhiṃ (syā.)} vassasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Niraye paccamānānaṃ, kadā anto bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Natthi anto kuto anto, na anto paṭidissati;
::

::gathalast
Tadā {pb:T:1.0138} hi pakataṃ pāpaṃ, mama tuyhañca mārisā {note:mārisa (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ nūna ito gantvā, yoniṃ laddhāna mānusiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vadaññū sīlasampanno, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahunti.
::

::centre
Lohakumbhijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 315. Sabbamaṃsalābhajātakaṃ (4-2-5)

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Pharusā {pb:V:1.0087} vata te vācā, maṃsaṃ {note:samma (pī. ka.)} yācanako asi {note:casi (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kilomasadisī {note:kilomassa sadisā (pī.)} vācā, kilomaṃ samma dammi te.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Aṅgametaṃ manussānaṃ, bhātā loke pavuccati;
::

::gathalast
Aṅgassa sadisī vācā {note:aṅgassadisī te vācā (ka.)}, aṅgaṃ samma dadāmi te.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Tātāti putto vadamāno, kampeti {note:sammeti (ka.)} hadayaṃ pitu;
::

::gathalast
Hadayassa sadisī {note:hadayassadisī (ka.)} vācā, hadayaṃ samma dammi te.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa gāme sakhā natthi, yathāraññaṃ tatheva taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbassa sadisī vācā, sabbaṃ samma dadāmi teti.
::

::centre
Sabbamaṃsalābhajātakaṃ {note:maṃsajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 316. Sasapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (4-2-6)

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Satta {pb:M:1.0101} me rohitā macchā, udakā thalamubbhatā;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Dussa me khettapālassa, rattibhattaṃ apābhataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Maṃsasūlā {pb:T:1.0139} ca dve godhā, ekañca dadhivārakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Ambapakkaṃ dakaṃ {note:ambapakkodakaṃ (sī. pī.)} sītaṃ, sītacchāyā manoramā {note:sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Na sasassa tilā atthi, na muggā napi taṇḍulā;
::

::gathalast
Iminā agginā pakkaṃ, mamaṃ {note:maṃsaṃ (ka.)} bhutvā vane vasāti.
::

::centre
Sasapaṇḍitajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 317. Matarodanajātakaṃ (4-2-7)

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Mataṃ mataṃ eva {note:matamatameva (sī. syā. pī.)} rodatha, na hi taṃ rodatha yo marissati;
::

::gathalast
Sabbepi {note:sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)} sarīradhārino, anupubbena jahanti jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Devamanussā catuppadā, pakkhigaṇā uragā ca bhogino;
::

::gathalast
Samhi {note:yamhi (syā.), asmiṃ (pī. ka.)} sarīre anissarā, ramamānāva jahanti jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0088} calitaṃ asaṇṭhitaṃ, sukhadukkhaṃ manujesvapekkhiya;
::

::gathalast
Kanditaruditaṃ niratthakaṃ, kiṃ vo sokagaṇābhikīrare.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Dhuttā ca soṇḍā {note:dhuttā soṇḍā (sī.), dhuttā soṇḍā ca (syā.)} akatā, bālā sūrā ayogino {note:bālā sūrā vīrā ayogino (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Dhīraṃ maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidāti.
::

::centre
Matarodanajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 318. Kaṇaverajātakaṃ (4-2-8)

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:T:1.0140}{pb:M:1.0102} taṃ vasantasamaye, kaṇaveresu bhāṇusu;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaṃ bāhāya pīḷesi, sā taṃ ārogyamabravi.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Ambho na kira saddheyyaṃ, yaṃ vāto pabbataṃ vahe;
::

::gatha2
Pabbatañce vahe vāto, sabbampi pathaviṃ vahe;
::

::gathalast
Yattha sāmā kālakatā {note:kālaṅkatā (ka.)}, sā maṃ ārogyamabravi.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Na ceva sā kālakatā, na ca sā aññamicchati;
::

::gathalast
Ekabhattikinī {note:ekabhattā kira (sī. syā.), ekabhattakinī (pī.)} sāmā, tameva abhikaṅkhati.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Asanthutaṃ maṃ cirasanthutena {note:asandhataṃ maṃ cirasandhatena (ka.)}, nimīni sāmā adhuvaṃ dhuvena;
::

::gathalast
Mayāpi sāmā nimineyya aññaṃ, ito ahaṃ dūrataraṃ gamissanti.
::

::centre
Kaṇaverajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 319. Tittirajātakaṃ (4-2-9)

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Susukhaṃ vata jīvāmi, labhāmi ceva bhuñjituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paripantheva tiṭṭhāmi, kā nu bhante gatī mama.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Mano ce te nappaṇamati, pakkhi pāpassa kammuno;
::

::gathalast
Abyāvaṭassa bhadrassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Ñātako no nisinnoti, bahu āgacchate jano;
::

::gathalast
Paṭicca {pb:T:1.0141} kammaṃ phusati, tasmiṃ me saṅkate mano.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Na paṭicca kammaṃ phusati, mano ce nappadussati;
::

::gathalast
Appossukkassa bhadrassa, na pāpamupalimpatīti.
::

::centre
Tittirajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 320. Succajajātakaṃ (4-2-10)

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Succajaṃ {pb:V:1.0089}{pb:M:1.0103} vata naccaji, vācāya adadaṃ giriṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ hitassa cajantassa, vācāya adada pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
::

::gathalast
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Rājaputta namo tyatthu, sacce dhamme ṭhito casi;
::

::gathalast
Yassa te byasanaṃ patto, saccasmiṃ ramate mano.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Yā daliddī daliddassa, aḍḍhā aḍḍhassa kittima {note:kittimā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sā hissa paramā bhariyā, sahiraññassa itthiyoti.
::

::centre
Succajajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Pucimandavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha cora sakassapa khantīvaro, dujjīvitatā ca varā pharusā;
::

::gathalast
Atha {pb:T:1.0142} sasa matañca vasanta sukhaṃ, succajaṃvatanaccajinā ca dasāti.
::

#### 3. Kuṭidūsakavaggo

#### 321. Kuṭidūsakajātakaṃ (4-3-1)

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Manussasseva te sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca vānara;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, agāraṃ te na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Manussasseva me sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca siṅgila {note:siṅgāla (ka.), piṅgala (ṭīkā)};
::

::gathalast
Yāhu seṭṭhā manussesu, sā me paññā na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Anavaṭṭhitacittassa{pb:M:1.0104}, lahucittassa dubbhino {note:dūbhino (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Niccaṃ addhuvasīlassa, sukhabhāvo {note:sucibhāvo (sī.), sukhabhāgo (?)} na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:V:1.0090} karassu ānubhāvaṃ, vītivattassu sīliyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sītavātaparittāṇaṃ, karassu kuṭavaṃ {note:kuṭikaṃ (sī. syā.)} kapīti.
::

::centre
Kuṭidūsaka {note:siṅgālasakuṇa (ka.)} jātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 322. Duddubhajātakaṃ (4-3-2)

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Duddubhāyati {note:daddabhāyati (sī. pī.)} bhaddante, yasmiṃ dese vasāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahampetaṃ na jānāmi, kimetaṃ duddubhāyati.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Beluvaṃ {pb:T:1.0143} patitaṃ sutvā, duddubhanti {note:daddabhanti (sī.)} saso javi;
::

::gathalast
Sasassa vacanaṃ sutvā, santattā migavāhinī.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Appatvā padaviññāṇaṃ, paraghosānusārino;
::

::gathalast
Panādaparamā bālā, te honti parapattiyā.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Ye ca sīlena sampannā, paññāyūpasame ratā;
::

::gathalast
Ārakā viratā dhīrā, na honti parapattiyāti.
::

::centre
Duddubhajātakaṃ {note:daddabhajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)} dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 323. Brahmadattajātakaṃ (4-3-3)

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Dvayaṃ yācanako rāja, brahmadatta nigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Alābhaṃ dhanalābhaṃ vā, evaṃ dhammā hi yācanā.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Yācanaṃ rodanaṃ āhu, pañcālānaṃ rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Yo yācanaṃ paccakkhāti, tamāhu paṭirodanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Mā maddasaṃsu rodantaṃ, pañcālā susamāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Tuvaṃ vā paṭirodantaṃ, tasmā icchāmahaṃ raho.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi {pb:M:1.0105} te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
::

::gathalast
Ariyo hi ariyassa kathaṃ na dajjā {note:dajje (sī.), dajjaṃ (?)}, sutvāna gāthā tava dhammayuttāti.
::

::centre
Brahmadattajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 324. Cammasāṭakajātakaṃ (4-3-4)

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Kalyāṇarūpo {pb:T:1.0144} vatayaṃ catuppado, subhaddako ceva supesalo ca;
::

::gathalast
Yo brāhmaṇaṃ jātimantūpapannaṃ, apacāyati meṇḍavaro yasassī.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:V:1.0091} brāhmaṇa ittaradassanena, vissāsamāpajji catuppadassa;
::

::gathalast
Daḷhappahāraṃ abhikaṅkhamāno {note:abhikattukāmo (syā.)}, avasakkatī dassati suppahāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Ūruṭṭhi {note:ūraṭṭhi (sī.)} bhaggaṃ pavaṭṭito {note:patito (sī. syā.)} khāribhāro, sabbañca bhaṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇassa {note:brāhmaṇassīdha (ka. sī. pī.), brāhmaṇasseva (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} bhinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ubhopi bāhā paggayha {note:paggayyeva (syā.), paggahīya (?)} kandati {note:bāhā paggayya kandati (pī. ka.)}, abhidhāvatha haññate brahmacārī.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ so nihato seti, yo apūjaṃ pasaṃsati {note:namassati (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja pahato, hato meṇḍena dummatīti.
::

::centre
Cammasāṭakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 325. Godharājajātakaṃ (4-3-5)

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Samaṇaṃ {pb:T:1.0145} taṃ maññamāno, upagacchimasaññataṃ;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ daṇḍena pāhāsi, yathā assamaṇo tathā.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ {pb:M:1.0106} te jaṭāhi dummedha, kiṃ te ajinasāṭiyā;
::

::gathalast
Abbhantaraṃ te gahanaṃ, bāhiraṃ parimajjasi.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi godha nivattassu, bhuñja sālīnamodanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Telaṃ loṇañca me atthi, pahūtaṃ mayha pipphali.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Esa bhiyyo pavekkhāmi, vammikaṃ sataporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Telaṃ loṇañca kittesi {note:kintesi (syā. pī.)}, ahitaṃ mayha pipphalīti.
::

::centre
Godharājajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 326. Kakkārujātakaṃ (4-3-6)

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Kāyena yo nāvahare, vācāya na musā bhaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yaso laddhā na majjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena vittameseyya, na nikatyā dhanaṃ hare;
::

::gathalast
Bhoge laddhā na majjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa cittaṃ ahāliddaṃ, saddhā ca avirāginī;
::

::gathalast
Eko sāduṃ na bhuñjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Sammukhā vā tirokkhā vā {note:parokkhā vā (pī.), parammukhā (ka.)}, yo sante na paribhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Yathāvādī {pb:T:1.0146} tathākārī, sa ve kakkārumarahatīti.
::

::centre
Kakkārujātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 327. Kākavatījātakaṃ (4-3-7)

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Vāti {pb:V:1.0092} cāyaṃ {note:vāyaṃ (ka.)} tato gandho, yattha me vasatī piyā;
::

::gathalast
Dūre ito hi kākavatī {note:kākātī (sī.), kākāti (syā. pī.)}, yattha me nirato mano.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ samuddamatarī, kathaṃ atari kepukaṃ {note:kebukaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ satta samuddāni, kathaṃ simbalimāruhi.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Tayā samuddamatariṃ, tayā atari kepukaṃ {note:kebukaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tayā satta samuddāni, tayā simbalimāruhiṃ.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthumaṃ {pb:M:1.0107} mahākāyaṃ, dhiratthumaṃ acetanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yattha jāyāyahaṃ jāraṃ, āvahāmi vahāmi cāti.
::

::centre
Kākavatījātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 328. Ananusociyajātakaṃ (4-3-8)

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Bahūnaṃ vijjatī bhotī, tehi me kiṃ bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, piyaṃ sammillahāsiniṃ.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ ce anusoceyya, yaṃ yaṃ tassa na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Attānamanusoceyya, sadā maccuvasaṃ pataṃ.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0147} heva ṭhitaṃ nāsīnaṃ, na sayānaṃ na paddhaguṃ {note:patthaguṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Yāva byāti nimisati, tatrāpi rasatī {note:saratī (sī. syā. pī.)} vayo.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Tatthattani vatappaddhe {note:vata panthe (syā.), vata bandhe (ka.) vata + pa-addhe = vatappaddhe}, vinābhāve asaṃsaye;
::

::gathalast
Bhūtaṃ sesaṃ dayitabbaṃ, vītaṃ ananusociyanti {note:cavitaṃ nānusociyanti (syā.), matantaṃ nānusociyaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::centre
Ananusociyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 329. Kāḷabāhujātakaṃ (4-3-9)

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ annapānassa pure labhāma, taṃ dāni sākhamigameva gacchati;
::

::gathalast
Gacchāma dāni vanameva rādha, asakkatā casma dhanañjayāya {note:dhanañcayāya (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Lābho alābho yaso ayaso ca, nindā pasaṃsā ca sukhañca dukkhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ete aniccā manujesu dhammā, mā soci kiṃ socasi poṭṭhapāda.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā {pb:M:1.0108} tuvaṃ paṇḍitakosi rādha, jānāsi atthāni anāgatāni;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ {pb:T:1.0148} nu sākhāmigaṃ dakkhisāma {note:dakkhiyāma (ka.), dakkhāma (syā.)}, niddhāvitaṃ {note:niddhāpitaṃ (sī. syā.), nibbāpitaṃ (pī.), nicchadaṃ (ka.)} rājakulatova jammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Cāleti {pb:V:1.0093} kaṇṇaṃ bhakuṭiṃ karoti, muhuṃ muhuṃ bhāyayate {note:bhāyate (syā.), bhāyāpate (ka.)} kumāre;
::

::gathalast
Sayameva taṃ kāhati kāḷabāhu, yenārakā ṭhassati annapānāti.
::

::centre
Kāḷabāhujātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 330. Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ (4-3-10)

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Sīlaṃ kireva kalyāṇaṃ, sīlaṃ loke anuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Passa ghoraviso nāgo, sīlavāti na haññati.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Yāvadevassahū kiñci, tāvadeva akhādisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgamma kulalā loke, na hiṃsanti akiñcanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhaṃ nirāsā supati, āsā phalavatī sukhā;
::

::gathalast
Āsaṃ nirāsaṃ katvāna, sukhaṃ supati piṅgalā.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Na samādhiparo atthi, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca;
::

::gathalast
Na paraṃ nāpi attānaṃ, vihiṃsati samāhitoti.
::

::centre
Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kuṭidūsakavaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Samanussa {pb:T:1.0149} -saduddubha-yācanako, atha meṇḍavaruttama-godhavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha kāyasakepuka bhotīvaro, atha rādhasusīlavarena dasāti.
::

#### 4. Kokilavaggo

#### 331. Kokilajātakaṃ (4-4-1)

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0109} ve kāle asampatte, ativelaṃ pabhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ so nihato seti, kokilāyiva atrajo.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi satthaṃ sunisitaṃ, visaṃ halāhalāmiva {note:halāhalaṃ iva (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ nikaṭṭhe {note:nikkaḍḍhe (syā.), nikaḍḍhe (ka.)} pāteti, vācā dubbhāsitā yathā.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā kāle akāle vā {note:akāle ca (sī. syā.)}, vācaṃ rakkheyya paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Nātivelaṃ pabhāseyya, api attasamamhi vā.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0094} ca kāle mitaṃ bhāse, matipubbo vicakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe amitte ādeti, supaṇṇo uragāmivāti.
::

::centre
Kokilajātakaṃ {note:kokālikajātakaṃ (sabbattha)} paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 332. Rathalaṭṭhijātakaṃ (4-4-2)

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Api hantvā hato brūti, jetvā jitoti bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Pubbavakkhāyino {pb:T:1.0150} {note:pubbamakkhāyino (sī. syā.)} rāja, aññadatthu {note:ekadatthu (sī. pī.)} na saddahe.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā paṇḍitajātiyo, suṇeyya itarassapi;
::

::gathalast
Ubhinnaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, yathā dhammo tathā kare.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
::

::gathalast
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
::

::gathalast
Nisammakārino rāja {note:rañño (sī. syā.)}, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
::

::centre
Rathalaṭṭhijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 333. Pakkagodhajātakaṃ (4-4-3)

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Tadeva {pb:M:1.0110} me tvaṃ vidito, vanamajjhe rathesabha;
::

::gatha2
Yassa te khaggabaddhassa, sannaddhassa tirīṭino;
::

::gathalast
Assatthadumasākhāya, pakkā godhā palāyatha.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Name namantassa bhaje bhajantaṃ, kiccānukubbassa kareyya kiccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nānatthakāmassa kareyya atthaṃ, asambhajantampi na sambhajeyya.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Caje {pb:T:1.0151} cajantaṃ vanathaṃ na kayirā, apetacittena na sambhajeyya;
::

::gathalast
Dijo dumaṃ khīṇaphalanti {note:phalaṃva (ka. sī. syā. ka.), dukanipāte puṭabhattajātakena saṃsandetabbaṃ} ñatvā, aññaṃ samekkheyya mahā hi loko.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
So te karissāmi yathānubhāvaṃ, kataññutaṃ khattiye {note:khattiyo (syā. ka.)} pekkhamāno;
::

::gathalast
Sabbañca te issariyaṃ dadāmi, yassicchasī tassa tuvaṃ dadāmīti.
::

::centre
Pakkagodhajātakaṃ {note:godhajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 334. Rājovādajātakaṃ (4-4-4)

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
135\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

#### 335. Jambukajātakaṃ (4-4-5)

::hangnum
138\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

139\.

#### 336. Brahāchattajātakaṃ (4-4-6)

::hangnum

::gathalast

#### 340. Visayhajātakaṃ (4-4-10)

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
Anariyamariyena sahassanetta, suduggatenāpi akiccamāhu;
::

::gathalast
Mā vo dhanaṃ taṃ ahu devarāja {note:ahuvā janinda (ka. sī. syā. pī.)}, yaṃ bhogahetu vijahemu saddhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
Yena eko ratho yāti, yāti tenāparo ratho;
::

::gathalast
Porāṇaṃ nihitaṃ vattaṃ, vattataññeva {note:vaddhaṃ, vaddhataññeva (ka. sī. pī.)} vāsava.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
Yadi {pb:T:1.0156} hessati dassāma, asante kiṃ dadāmase;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃbhūtāpi dassāma, mā dānaṃ pamadamhaseti.
::

::centre
Visayhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kokilavaggo {note:kokālikavaggo (ka.)} catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Ativelapabhāsati {pb:M:1.0114} jītavaro, vanamajjha rathesabha jimhagamo;
::

::gathalast
Atha jambu tiṇāsanapīṭhavaraṃ, atha taṇḍula mora visayha dasāti.

#### 5. Cūḷakuṇālavaggo

#### 341. Kaṇḍarījātakaṃ (4-5-1)

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
Narānamārāmakarāsu nārisu, anekacittāsu aniggahāsu ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha nāpītikarāpi {note:sabba’ttanā’pītikarāpi (sī. syā.)} ce siyā {note:siyuṃ (syā.)}, na vissase titthasamā hi nāriyo.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0098} ve {note:yañca (syā. ka.)} disvā kaṇḍarīkinnarānaṃ {note:kinnarakinnarīnaṃ (syā.), kinnarīkinnarānaṃ (ka.)}, sabbitthiyo na ramanti agāre;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0157} tādisaṃ maccaṃ cajitvā bhariyā, aññaṃ disvā purisaṃ pīṭhasappiṃ.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
Bakassa ca bāvarikassa {note:pāvārikassa (sī.)} rañño, accantakāmānugatassa bhariyā;
::

::gathalast
Avācarī {note:accācari (syā.), anācari (ka.)} paṭṭhavasānugassa {note:baddhavasānugassa (sī. syā.), pattavasānugatassa (ka.)}, kaṃ vāpi itthī nāticare tadaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
Piṅgiyānī sabbalokissarassa, rañño piyā brahmadattassa bhariyā;
::

::gathalast
Avācarī paṭṭhavasānugassa, taṃ vāpi sā nājjhagā kāmakāminīti.
::

::centre
Kaṇḍarījātakaṃ {note:kinnarījātakaṃ (ka. sī. ka.), kuṇḍalikajātakaṃ (syā.)} paṭhamaṃ.

#### 347. Ayakūṭajātakaṃ (4-5-7)

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
188\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::centre
Ayakūṭajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

::hangnum
191\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
192\.

::gatha1

::centre

#### 349. Sandhibhedajātakaṃ (4-5-9)

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
Neva itthīsu sāmaññaṃ, nāpi bhakkhesu sārathi;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
Asi {pb:V:1.0101} tikkhova maṃsamhi, pesuññaṃ parivattati;
::

::gathalast
Yatthūsabhañca sīhañca, bhakkhayanti migādhamā.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ so sayanaṃ seti, yamimaṃ {note:yayimaṃ (sī. pī.), yimaṃ (ka.)} passasi sārathi;
::

::gathalast
Yo vācaṃ sandhibhedassa, pisuṇassa nibodhati.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
Te janā sukhamedhanti, narā saggagatāriva;
::

::gathalast
Ye vācaṃ sandhibhedassa, nāvabodhanti sārathīti.
::

::centre
Sandhibhedajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 350. Devatāpañhajātakaṃ (4-5-10)

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
Hanti hatthehi pādehi, mukhañca parisumbhati;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi {note:mabhipassasi (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
Akkosati yathākāmaṃ, āgamañcassa icchati;
::

::gathalast
Sa {pb:T:1.0163} ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi.
::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1
Abbhakkhāti abhūtena, alikenābhisāraye;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi.
::

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
Haraṃ annañca pānañca, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
::

::gatha2
Aññadatthuharā santā, te ve rāja piyā honti;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ tena tvābhipassasīti.
::

::centre
Devatāpañhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Cūḷakuṇālavaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Narānaṃ {pb:M:1.0119} asakkhivasimhavaro, nīliyamaggivarañca puna;
::

::gathalast
Puna rasāyasakūṭavaro, tathārañña sārathi hanti dasāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kāliṅgaṃ {note:vivaraṃ (bahūsu)} pucimandañca, kuṭidūsaka kokilā {note:kuṭidūsaṃ bahubhāṇakaṃ (bahūsu)};
::

::gathalast
Cūḷakuṇālavaggo so, pañcamo suppakāsitoti.
::

::centre
Catukkanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 5. Pañcakanipāto

#### 1. Maṇikuṇḍalavaggo

#### 351. Maṇikuṇḍalajātakaṃ (5-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Jīno {pb:T:1.0164}{pb:V:1.0102}{pb:M:1.0120} rathassaṃ maṇikuṇḍale ca, putte ca dāre ca tatheva jīno;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesu bhogesu asesakesu {note:asesitesu (sī. pī.), asesikesu (ka.)}, kasmā na santappasi sokakāle.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbeva maccaṃ vijahanti bhogā, macco vā te {note:ca ne (pī.), dhane (ka.)} pubbataraṃ jahāti;
::

::gathalast
Asassatā bhogino kāmakāmi, tasmā na socāmahaṃ sokakāle.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Udeti āpūrati veti {note:pūreti khīyati (syā.)} cando, atthaṃ tapetvāna {note:andhaṃ tapetvāna (ka.), atthaṅgametvāna (syā.), ettha ‘‘tapetvāna atthaṃ paletī’’ti sambandho} paleti sūriyo;
::

::gathalast
Viditā {note:vijitā (syā.)} mayā sattuka lokadhammā, tasmā na socāmahaṃ sokakāle.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato {pb:T:1.0165} pabbajito na sādhu;
::

::gathalast
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
::

::gathalast
Nisammakārino rāja {note:rañño (sī. syā.)}, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
::

::centre
Maṇikuṇḍalajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 352. Sujātajātakaṃ (5-1-2)

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ {pb:M:1.0121} nu santaramānova, lāyitvā haritaṃ tiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khāda khādāti lapasi, gatasattaṃ jaraggavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi annena pānena, mato goṇo samuṭṭhahe;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca tucchaṃ vilapasi, yathā taṃ dummatī tathā.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Tatheva tiṭṭhati sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca vāladhi;
::

::gathalast
Sotā tatheva tiṭṭhanti {note:so tāta tatheva tiṭṭhati (ka.)}, maññe goṇo samuṭṭhahe.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Nevayyakassa sīsañca {note:sīsaṃ vā (sī. syā. pī.)}, hatthapādā ca dissare;
::

::gathalast
Rudaṃ mattikathūpasmiṃ, nanu tvaññeva dummati.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ {pb:V:1.0103} vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ {note:osiñci (ka.)}, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Abbahī {note:abbūḷhaṃ (sī. syā.), abbhūḷhaṃ (ka.)} vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ {note:sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Yo {pb:T:1.0166} me sokaparetassa, pitu sokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇava.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ karonti sappaññā, ye honti anukampakā;
::

::gathalast
Vinivattenti sokamhā, sujāto pitaraṃ yathāti.
::

::centre
Sujātajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 353. Venasākhajātakaṃ (5-1-3)

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Nayidaṃ niccaṃ bhavitabbaṃ brahmadatta, khemaṃ subhikkhaṃ sukhatā ca kāye;
::

::gathalast
Atthaccaye mā ahu sampamūḷho, bhinnaplavo sāgarasseva majjhe.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Yāni {pb:M:1.0122} karoti puriso, tāni attani passati;
::

::gatha2
Kalyāṇakārī kalyāṇaṃ, pāpakārī ca pāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yādisaṃ vapate bījaṃ, tādisaṃ harate phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ tadācariyavaco, pārāsariyo yadabravi;
::

::gathalast
Mā su {note:mā ssu (sī. syā. pī.)} tvaṃ akari pāpaṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ pacchā kataṃ tape.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Ayameva so piṅgiya {note:so piṅgiyo (syā.), sopi bhiyyo (ka.)} venasākho, {note:dhonasākho (ka. sī. pī.)} yamhi {pb:T:1.0167} ghātayiṃ khattiyānaṃ sahassaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṅkate candanasārānulitte, tameva dukkhaṃ paccāgataṃ mamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Sāmā ca {note:sāmāpi (sī. syā.)} kho candanalittagattā {note:gattī (ka. sī. syā. pī.)}, laṭṭhīva sobhañjanakassa uggatā;
::

::gathalast
Adisvā {note:adisvāva (sī.)} kālaṃ karissāmi ubbariṃ, taṃ me ito dukkhataraṃ bhavissatīti.
::

::centre
Venasākhajātakaṃ {note:dhonasākhajātakaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)} tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 354. Uragajātakaṃ (5-1-4)

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
::

::

::hangnum

::

::gathalast
Yathāgato tathā gato, tattha kā paridevanā.

::hangnum
22\.

::gatha1
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Ñātimittasuhajjānaṃ{pb:T:1.0168}, bhiyyo no aratī siyā.
::

Ḍayhamāno {pb:M:1.0123} na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;

#### 355. Ghaṭajātakaṃ (5-1-5)

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Aññe socanti rodanti, aññe assumukhā janā;
::

::gathalast
Pasannamukhavaṇṇosi, kasmā ghaṭa {note:ghata (sī. pī.)} na socasi.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Nābbhatītaharo soko, nānāgatasukhāvaho;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā dhaṅka {note:vaṃka (pī.)} na socāmi, natthi soke dutīyatā {note:soko dutīyakā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Socaṃ paṇḍu kiso hoti, bhattañcassa na ruccati;
::

::gathalast
Amittā sumanā honti, sallaviddhassa ruppato.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Gāme {pb:T:1.0169} vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
::

::gathalast
Ṭhitaṃ maṃ nāgamissati, evaṃ diṭṭhapado ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Yassattā nālamekova, sabbakāmarasāharo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbāpi pathavī tassa, na sukhaṃ āvahissatīti.
::

::centre
Ghaṭajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 356. Koraṇḍiyajātakaṃ (5-1-6)

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Eko {pb:V:1.0105}{pb:M:1.0124} araññe girikandarāyaṃ, paggayha paggayha silaṃ pavecchasi {note:pavejjhasi (syā. sī. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Punappunaṃ santaramānarūpo, koraṇḍiya {note:kāraṇḍiya (sī. syā. pī.)} ko nu tava yidhattho.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Ahañhimaṃ sāgara sevitantaṃ, samaṃ karissāmi yathāpi pāṇi;
::

::gathalast
Vikiriya sānūni ca pabbatāni ca, tasmā silaṃ dariyā pakkhipāmi.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Nayimaṃ mahiṃ arahati pāṇikappaṃ, samaṃ manusso karaṇāya meko;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmimaññeva dariṃ jigīsaṃ {note:jigiṃsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, koraṇḍiya {pb:T:1.0170} hāhasi {note:hāyasi (syā. ka.)} jīvalokaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Sace ahaṃ {note:ayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} bhūtadharaṃ na sakkā {note:sakko (syā. ka.)}, samaṃ manusso karaṇāya meko;
::

::gathalast
Evameva tvaṃ brahme ime manusse, nānādiṭṭhike nānayissasi te {note:ne (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkhittarūpena bhavaṃ mamatthaṃ, akkhāsi koraṇḍiya evametaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathā na sakkā pathavī samāyaṃ, kattuṃ manussena tathā manussāti.
::

::centre
Koraṇḍiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 357. Laṭukikajātakaṃ (5-1-7)

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Vandāmi taṃ kuñjara saṭṭhihāyanaṃ, āraññakaṃ yūthapatiṃ yasassiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pakkhehi taṃ pañjalikaṃ karomi, mā me vadhī puttake dubbalāya.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Vandāmi {pb:M:1.0125} taṃ kuñjara ekacāriṃ, āraññakaṃ pabbatasānugocaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pakkhehi taṃ pañjalikaṃ karomi, mā {pb:T:1.0171} me vadhī puttake dubbalāya;
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Vamissāmi te laṭukike puttakāni, kiṃ me tuvaṃ kāhasi dubbalāsi;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ sahassānipi tādisīnaṃ, vāmena pādena papothayeyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva sabbattha balena kiccaṃ, balañhi bālassa vadhāya hoti;
::

::gathalast
Karissāmi te nāgarājā anatthaṃ, yo me vadhī puttake dubbalāya.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Kākañca passa laṭukikaṃ, maṇḍūkaṃ nīlamakkhikaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ete nāgaṃ aghātesuṃ, passa verassa verinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi veraṃ na kayirātha, appiyenapi kenacīti.
::

::centre
Laṭukikajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 358. Cūḷadhammapālajātakaṃ (5-1-8)

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Ahameva {pb:V:1.0106} dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, hatthe me deva chedehi.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Ahameva dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, pāde me deva chedehi.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Ahameva dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ {pb:T:1.0172} muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, sīsaṃ me deva chedehi.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi {note:naha (sī. syā. pī.) ettha ha-kāro khede} nūnimassa rañño, mittāmaccā ca vijjare suhadā;
::

::gathalast
Ye na vadanti rājānaṃ, mā ghātayi orasaṃ puttaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi {note:naha (sī. syā. pī.) ettha ha-kāro khede} nūnimassa rañño, ñātī mittā ca vijjare suhadā;
::

::gathalast
Ye na vadanti rājānaṃ, mā ghātayi atrajaṃ puttaṃ.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Candanasārānulittā{pb:M:1.0126}, bāhā chijjanti dhammapālassa;
::

::gathalast
Dāyādassa pathabyā, pāṇā me deva rujjhantīti.
::

::centre
Cūḷadhammapālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 359. Suvaṇṇamigajātakaṃ (5-1-9)

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Vikkama re haripāda {note:mahāmiga (sī. syā. pī.)}, vikkama re mahāmiga {note:harīpada (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Chinda vārattikaṃ pāsaṃ, nāhaṃ ekā vane rame.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Vikkamāmi na pāremi, bhūmiṃ sumbhāmi vegasā;
::

::gathalast
Daḷho vārattiko pāso, pādaṃ me parikantati.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Attharassu palāsāni, asiṃ nibbāha luddaka;
::

::gathalast
Paṭhamaṃ maṃ vadhitvāna, hana pacchā mahāmigaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Na me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā, bhāsantiṃ mānusiṃ migiṃ {note:na me sutā vā diṭṭhā vā, bhāsantī mānusiṃ migī (ṭīkā)};
::

::gathalast
Tvañca bhadde sukhī hohi, eso cāpi mahāmigo.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja {pb:T:1.0173} nandāmi, muttaṃ disvā mahāmiganti.
::

::centre
Suvaṇṇamigajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 360. Suyonandījātakaṃ (5-1-10)

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Vāti {pb:V:1.0107} gandho timirānaṃ, kusamuddo ca {note:va (syā. pī.)} ghosavā;
::

::gathalast
Dūre ito suyonandī {note:ito hi susandī (sī. syā.), itopi sussondī (pī.)}, tambakāmā tudanti maṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ samuddamatari, kathaṃ addakkhi sedumaṃ {note:serumaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ tassā ca tuyhañca, ahu sagga {note:agga (sī. syā.)} samāgamo.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā {note:bharukacchā (sī. syā. pī.)} payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Makarehi abhidā {note:makarehibbhidā (sī.), makarehi’bhidā (syā.), makarehi bhinnā (pī.)} nāvā, phalakenāhamaplaviṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Sā {pb:M:1.0127} maṃ saṇhena mudunā, niccaṃ candanagandhinī;
::

::gathalast
Aṅgena {note:aṅkena (pī. ka.)} uddharī bhaddā, mātā puttaṃva orasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Sā maṃ annena pānena, vatthena sayanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Attanāpi ca mandakkhī, evaṃ tamba vijānāhīti.
::

::centre
Suyonandījātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Maṇikuṇḍalavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha jinavaro haritaṃ tiṇako, atha {pb:T:1.0174} bhinnaplavo uragova ghaṭo;
::

::gathalast
Dariyā puna kuñjara bhūnahatā, migamuttamasaggavarena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Vaṇṇārohavaggo

#### 361. Vaṇṇārohajātakaṃ (5-2-1)

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Vaṇṇārohena jātiyā, balanikkamanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Subāhu na mayā seyyo, sudāṭha iti bhāsasi.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Vaṇṇārohena jātiyā, balanikkamanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Sudāṭho na mayā seyyo, subāhu iti bhāsasi.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ ce maṃ viharantaṃ, subāhu samma dubbhasi;
::

::gathalast
Na dānāhaṃ tayā saddhiṃ, saṃvāsamabhirocaye.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0108} paresaṃ vacanāni, saddaheyya {note:saddahetha (sī. syā. pī.)} yathātathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khippaṃ bhijjetha mittasmiṃ, verañca pasave bahuṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0128} so mitto yo sadā appamatto, bhedāsaṅkī randhamevānupassī;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiñca setī urasīva putto, sa ve mitto yo abhejjo parehīti.
::

::centre
Vaṇṇārohajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 362. Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ (5-2-2)

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Sīlaṃ {pb:T:1.0175} seyyo sutaṃ seyyo, iti me saṃsayo ahu;
::

::gathalast
Sīlameva sutā seyyo, iti me natthi saṃsayo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Moghā jāti ca vaṇṇo ca, sīlameva kiruttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīlena anupetassa, sutenattho na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyo ca adhammaṭṭho, vesso cādhammanissito;
::

::gathalast
Te pariccajjubho loke, upapajjanti duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gathalast
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, bhavanti tidive samā.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Na vedā samparāyāya, na jāti nāpi {note:nopi (pī.)} bandhavā;
::

::gathalast
Sakañca sīlaṃ saṃsuddhaṃ, samparāyāya sukhāya cāti {note:sukhāvahanti (sī. syā.)}.
::

::centre
Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 363. Hirijātakaṃ (5-2-3)

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Hiriṃ tarantaṃ vijigucchamānaṃ, tavāhamasmī iti bhāsamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Seyyāni kammāni anādiyantaṃ, neso mamanti iti naṃ vijaññā.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
::

::gathalast
Akarontaṃ {pb:T:1.0176} bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0129} so mitto yo sadā appamatto, bhedāsaṅkī randhamevānupassī;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiñca setī urasīva putto, sa ve mitto yo abhejjo parehi.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Pāmojjakaraṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ, pasaṃsāvahanaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Phalānisaṃso bhāveti, vahanto porisaṃ dhuraṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Pavivekarasaṃ {pb:V:1.0109} pitvā, rasaṃ upasamassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Niddaro hoti nippāpo, dhammappītirasaṃ pivanti.
::

::centre
Hirijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 364. Khajjopanakajātakaṃ (5-2-4)

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Ko nu santamhi pajjote, aggipariyesanaṃ caraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addakkhi ratti {note:rattiṃ (syā.)} khajjotaṃ, jātavedaṃ amaññatha.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Svassa gomayacuṇṇāni, abhimatthaṃ tiṇāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Viparītāya saññāya, nāsakkhi pajjaletave.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi anupāyena, atthaṃ na labhate migo {note:mūgo (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Visāṇato gavaṃ dohaṃ, yattha khīraṃ na vindati.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Vividhehi upāyehi, atthaṃ papponti māṇavā;
::

::gathalast
Niggahena amittānaṃ, mittānaṃ paggahena ca.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Senāmokkhapalābhena {pb:T:1.0177} {note:senī mokkhūpalābhena (syā.)}, vallabhānaṃ nayena ca;
::

::gathalast
Jagatiṃ jagatipālā, āvasanti vasundharanti.
::

::centre
Khajjopanakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 365. Ahituṇḍikajātakaṃ (5-2-5)

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Dhuttomhi samma sumukha, jūte akkhaparājito;
::

::gathalast
Harehi {note:sevehi (pī.)} ambapakkāni, vīriyaṃ te bhakkhayāmase.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Alikaṃ vata maṃ samma, abhūtena pasaṃsasi;
::

::gathalast
Ko te suto vā diṭṭho vā, sumukho nāma makkaṭo.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjāpi {pb:M:1.0130} me taṃ manasi {note:te maṃ sarasi (ka.)}, yaṃ maṃ tvaṃ ahituṇḍika;
::

::gathalast
Dhaññāpaṇaṃ pavisitvā, matto {note:mutto (ka.)} chātaṃ hanāsi maṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Tāhaṃ saraṃ dukkhaseyyaṃ, api rajjampi kāraye;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Yañca jaññā kule jātaṃ, gabbhe tittaṃ amacchariṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena sakhiñca mittañca, dhīro sandhātumarahatīti.
::

::centre
Ahituṇḍikajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 366. Gumbiyajātakaṃ (5-2-6)

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Madhuvaṇṇaṃ {pb:V:1.0110} madhurasaṃ, madhugandhaṃ visaṃ ahu;
::

::gathalast
Gumbiyo {pb:T:1.0178} ghāsamesāno, araññe odahī visaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Madhu iti maññamānā {note:madhūti maññamānāya (ka.)}, ye taṃ visamakhādisuṃ {note:visamasāyisuṃ (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Ye ca kho paṭisaṅkhāya, visaṃ taṃ parivajjayuṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva manussesu, visaṃ kāmā samohitā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva ime kāme, āturā paricārike {note:paricārake (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ye sadā parivajjenti, saṅgaṃ loke upaccagunti.
::

::centre
Gumbiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 367. Sāḷiyajātakaṃ (5-2-7)

::hangnum
90\.

::gathalast
Tena sappenayaṃ daṭṭho, hato pāpānusāsako.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::centre

#### 368. Tacasārajātakaṃ (5-2-8)

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Amittahatthatthagatā {note:hatthattagatā (katthaci, sī. niyya)}, tacasārasamappitā;
::

::gathalast
Pasannamukhavaṇṇāttha, kasmā tumhe na socatha.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0111} socanāya paridevanāya, atthova labbho {note:attho ca labbhā (sī. syā.), atthodha labbhā (a. ni. 5.48)} api appakopi;
::

::gathalast
Socantamenaṃ dukhitaṃ viditvā, paccatthikā attamanā bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Yato ca kho paṇḍito āpadāsu, na vedhatī atthavinicchayaññū;
::

::gathalast
Paccatthikāssa {note:paccatthikā te (ka.)} dukhitā bhavanti, disvā mukhaṃ avikāraṃ purāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Jappena mantena subhāsitena, anuppadānena paveṇiyā vā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā {pb:T:1.0180} yathā yattha labhetha atthaṃ, tathā tathā tattha parakkameyya.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Yato {pb:M:1.0132} ca jāneyya alabbhaneyyo, mayā va {note:mayā vā (syā. ka.)} aññena vā esa attho;
::

::gathalast
Asocamāno adhivāsayeyya, kammaṃ daḷhaṃ kinti karomi dānīti.
::

::centre
Tacasārajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 369. Mittavindakajātakaṃ (5-2-9)

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Kyāhaṃ devānamakaraṃ, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me sirasmiṃ ohacca {note:uhacca (ka.), uhacca (pī.)}, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Atikkamma ramaṇakaṃ, sadāmattañca dūbhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Brahmattarañca pāsādaṃ, kenatthena idhāgato.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Ito bahutarā bhogā, atra maññe bhavissare;
::

::gathalast
Iti etāya saññāya, passa maṃ byasanaṃ gataṃ.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Catubbhi aṭṭhajjhagamā, aṭṭhāhipi ca {note:aṭṭhāhi cāpi (sī. syā.), aṭṭhābhi cāpi (ka.)} soḷasa;
::

::gathalast
Soḷasāhi ca bāttiṃsa, atricchaṃ cakkamāsado;
::

Icchāhatassa posassa, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Uparivisālā duppūrā, icchā visaṭagāminī {note:upari visālaṃ duppūraṃ, icchāvisadagāminī (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ye {pb:T:1.0181} ca taṃ anugijjhanti, te honti cakkadhārinoti.
::

::centre
Mittavindakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 370. Palāsajātakaṃ (5-2-10)

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Haṃso palāsamavaca, nigrodho samma jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Aṅkasmiṃ {note:aṅgasmiṃ (ka.)} te nisinnova, so te mammāni checchati {note:chijjati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Vaḍḍhatāmeva {note:vaddhitameva (ka.)} nigrodho, patiṭṭhassa bhavāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yathā pitā ca mātā ca {note:pitā vā mātā vā (pī.), mātā vā pitā vā (ka.)}, evaṃ me so bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0112} tvaṃ aṅkasmiṃ vaḍḍhesi, khīrarukkhaṃ bhayānakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma, vuḍḍhi massa na ruccati.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Idāni {pb:M:1.0133} kho maṃ bhāyeti, mahānerunidassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Haṃsassa anabhiññāya, mahā me bhayamāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Na tassa vuḍḍhi kusalappasatthā, yo vaḍḍhamāno ghasate patiṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassūparodhaṃ parisaṅkamāno, patārayī mūlavadhāya dhīroti.
::

::centre
Palāsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Vaṇṇārohavaggo dutiyo {note:imassuddānaṃ tatiyavaggapariyosāne bhavissati}.

#### 3. Aḍḍhavaggo

#### 371. Dīghītikosalajātakaṃ (5-3-1)

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃbhūtassa te rāja, āgatassa vase {note:vaso (pī. ka.)} mama;
::

::gathalast
Atthi nu koci pariyāyo, yo taṃ dukkhā pamocaye.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃbhūtassa {pb:T:1.0182} me tāta, āgatassa vase tava;
::

::gathalast
Natthi no koci pariyāyo, yo maṃ dukkhā pamocaye.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Nāññaṃ sucaritaṃ rāja, nāññaṃ rāja subhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tāyate maraṇakāle, evamevitaraṃ dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca taṃ upanayhanti, veraṃ tesaṃ na sammati.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca taṃ nupanayhanti, veraṃ tesūpasammati.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi verena verāni, sammantīdha kudācanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Averena ca sammanti, esa dhammo sanantanoti.
::

::centre
Dīghītikosalajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 372. Migapotakajātakaṃ (5-3-2)

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Agārā {pb:V:1.0113} paccupetassa, anagārassa te sato;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃvāsena {pb:M:1.0134} have sakka, manussassa migassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Hadaye {pb:T:1.0183} jāyate pemaṃ, na taṃ sakkā asocituṃ.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Mataṃ marissaṃ rodanti, ye rudanti lapanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā tvaṃ isi mā rodi, roditaṃ moghamāhu santo.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Roditena have brahme, mato peto samuṭṭhahe;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe saṅgamma rodāma, aññamaññassa ñātake.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Abbahi vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna vāsavāti.
::

::centre
Migapotakajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 373. Mūsikajātakaṃ (5-3-3)

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Kuhiṃ gatā kattha gatā, iti lālappatī jano;
::

::gathalast
Ahameveko jānāmi, udapāne mūsikā hatā.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Yañcetaṃ {note:yathetaṃ (pī.), yavetaṃ (ka.), yametaṃ (katthaci)} iti cīti ca, gadrabhova nivattasi;
::

::gathalast
Udapāne mūsikaṃ hantvā, yavaṃ bhakkhetumicchasi.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Daharo cāsi dummedha, paṭhamuppattiko {note:paṭhamuppattito (sī. pī.)} susu;
::

::gathalast
Dīghañcetaṃ {pb:T:1.0184} {note:dīghametaṃ (pī.)} samāsajja {note:samāpajja (syā. ka.)}, na te dassāmi jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Nāntalikkhabhavanena, nāṅgaputtapinena {note:nāṅgaputtasirena (sī. syā. pī.)} vā;
::

::gathalast
Puttena hi patthayito, silokehi pamocito.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaṃ {pb:V:1.0114} sutamadhīyetha, hīnamukkaṭṭhamajjhimaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sabbassa atthaṃ jāneyya, na ca sabbaṃ payojaye;
::

::gathalast
Hoti tādisako kālo, yattha atthāvahaṃ sutanti.
::

::centre
Mūsikajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 374. Cūḷadhanuggahajātakaṃ (5-3-4)

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaṃ {pb:M:1.0135} bhaṇḍaṃ samādāya, pāraṃ tiṇṇosi brāhmaṇa;
::

Paccāgaccha lahuṃ khippaṃ, mampi tārehi dānito {note:dānibho (syā.)}.

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Asanthutaṃ maṃ cirasanthutena, nimīni bhotī addhuvaṃ dhuvena;
::

::gathalast
Mayāpi bhotī nimineyya aññaṃ, ito ahaṃ dūrataraṃ gamissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Kāyaṃ eḷagalāgumbe {note:eḷagaṇagumbe (ka.)}, karoti ahuhāsiyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nayīdha naccagītaṃ vā {note:nayidha naccaṃ vā gītaṃ vā (sī. syā. pī.)}, tāḷaṃ vā susamāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anamhikāle {note:anamhakāle (pī.)} susoṇi {note:sussoṇi (sī. syā. pī.)}, kiṃ nu jagghasi sobhane {note:sobhaṇe (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅgāla bāla dummedha, appapaññosi jambuka;
::

::gathalast
Jīno {pb:T:1.0185} macchañca pesiñca, kapaṇo viya jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Sudassaṃ vajjamaññesaṃ, attano pana duddasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jīnā patiñca jārañca, maññe tvaññeva {note:mampi tvaññeva (sī. syā.), tvampi maññeva (pī.)} jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Evametaṃ migarāja, yathā bhāsasi jambuka;
::

::gathalast
Sā nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, bhattu hessaṃ vasānugā.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Yo hare mattikaṃ thālaṃ, kaṃsathālampi so hare;
::

::gathalast
Katañceva {note:kataṃyeva (sī. syā. pī.)} tayā pāpaṃ, punapevaṃ karissasīti.
::

::centre
Cūḷadhanuggahajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 375. Kapotajātakaṃ (5-3-5)

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Idāni khomhi sukhito arogo, nikkaṇṭako nippatito kapoto;
::

::gathalast
Kāhāmi dānī hadayassa tuṭṭhiṃ, tathāhimaṃ maṃsasākaṃ baleti.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Kāyaṃ {pb:M:1.0136} balākā sikhino, corī laṅghipitāmahā;
::

::gathalast
Oraṃ balāke āgaccha, caṇḍo me vāyaso sakhā.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Alañhi te jagghitāye, mamaṃ disvāna edisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vilūnaṃ sūdaputtena, piṭṭhamaṇḍena {note:piṭṭhamaddena (sī. syā. pī.)} makkhitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Sunhāto {pb:V:1.0115} suvilittosi, annapānena tappito;
::

::gathalast
Kaṇṭhe {pb:T:1.0186} ca te veḷuriyo, agamā nu kajaṅgalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Mā te mitto amitto vā, agamāsi kajaṅgalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piñchāni tattha lāyitvā, kaṇṭhe bandhanti vaṭṭanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Punapāpajjasī samma, sīlañhi tava tādisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na hi mānusakā bhogā, subhuñjā honti pakkhināti.
::

::centre
Kapotajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

::centre
Aḍḍhavaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha vaṇṇa sasīla hiri labhate, sumukhā visa sāḷiyamittavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha cakka palāsa sarāja sato, yava bāla kapotaka pannarasāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Jīnañca vaṇṇaṃ asamaṃvaguppari, sudesitā jātakanti santi vīsati {note:jātaka pañcavīsati (?)};
::

::gathalast
Mahesino brahmacarittamutta-mavoca gāthā atthavatī subyañjanāti.
::

::centre
Pañcakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 6. Chakkanipāto

#### 1. Avāriyavaggo

#### 376. Avāriyajātakaṃ (6-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Māsu {pb:T:1.0187}{pb:V:1.0116}{pb:M:1.0137} kujjha bhūmipati, māsu kujjha rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, rājā raṭṭhassa pūjito.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha anusāsāmi, māsu kujjha {note:māssu kujjhi (sī. pī.)} rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Avāriyapitā nāma, ahu gaṅgāya nāviko;
::

::gatha2
Pubbe janaṃ tāretvāna, pacchā yācati vetanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tenassa bhaṇḍanaṃ hoti, na ca bhogehi vaḍḍhati.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Atiṇṇaṃyeva yācassu, apāraṃ tāta nāvika;
::

::gathalast
Añño hi tiṇṇassa mano, añño hoti pāresino {note:taresino (sī. pī.), tiresino (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
::

::gathalast
Sabbattha anusāsāmi, māsu kujjhittha nāvika.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Yāyevānusāsaniyā, rājā gāmavaraṃ adā;
::

::gathalast
Tāyevānusāsaniyā, nāviko paharī mukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Bhattaṃ bhinnaṃ hatā bhariyā, gabbho ca patito chamā;
::

::gathalast
Migova jātarūpena, na tenatthaṃ abandhi sūti {note:avaḍḍhitunti (sī. syā.), avaḍḍhi sūti (?)}.
::

::centre
Avāriyajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 377. Setaketujātakaṃ (6-1-2)

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0188} tāta kujjhi na hi sādhu kodho, bahumpi te adiṭṭhamassutañca;
::

::gathalast
Mātā pitā disatā {note:disā tāta (syā.), disā tā (pī.)} setaketu, ācariyamāhu disataṃ pasatthā.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Agārino {pb:V:1.0117}{pb:M:1.0138} annadapānavatthadā {note:annapānavatthadā (syā. ka.)}, avhāyikā tampi disaṃ vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Esā disā paramā setaketu, yaṃ patvā dukkhī sukhino bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Kharājinā jaṭilā paṅkadantā, dummakkharūpā {note:dumukkharūpā (sī. syā.), dummukkharūpā (pī. ka.)} yeme jappanti mante;
::

::gathalast
Kacci nu te mānusake payoge, idaṃ vidū parimuttā apāyā.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Pāpāni kammāni katvāna rāja, bahussuto ce na {note:bahussuto neva (sī. syā.)} careyya dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamuñce caraṇaṃ apatvā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamuñce caraṇaṃ apatvā;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi {pb:T:1.0189} vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇameva {note:caraṇaññeva (sī. syā. pī.)} saccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇameva saccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kittiñhi pappoti adhicca vede, santiṃ puṇeti {note:santaṃ pune’ti (sī. pī.)} caraṇena dantoti.
::

::centre
Setaketujātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 378. Darīmukhajātakaṃ (6-1-3)

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Paṅko ca kāmā palipo ca kāmā, bhayañca metaṃ timūlaṃ pavuttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rajo ca dhūmo ca mayā pakāsitā, hitvā tuvaṃ pabbaja brahmadatta.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Gadhito {pb:M:1.0139} {note:gathito (sī.)} ca ratto ca adhimucchito ca, kāmesvahaṃ brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ nussahe jīvikattho pahātuṃ, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Yo atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idameva seyyo iti maññamāno, punappunaṃ {pb:T:1.0190} gabbhamupeti mando.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
So ghorarūpaṃ nirayaṃ upeti, subhāsubhaṃ muttakarīsapūraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sattā sakāye na jahanti giddhā, ye honti kāmesu avītarāgā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Mīḷhena littā ruhirena makkhitā, semhena littā upanikkhamanti;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ yañhi kāyena phusanti tāvade, sabbaṃ asātaṃ dukhameva kevalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā vadāmi na hi aññato savaṃ, pubbenivāsaṃ bahukaṃ sarāmi;
::

::gathalast
Citrāhi gāthāhi subhāsitāhi, darīmukho nijjhāpayi sumedhanti.
::

::centre
Darīmukhajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 379. Nerujātakaṃ (6-1-4)

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Kākolā kākasaṅghā ca, mayañca patataṃ varā {note:vara (ka.) mayantipadassa hi visesanaṃ};
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva sadisā homa, imaṃ āgamma pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Idha {pb:V:1.0118} sīhā ca byagghā ca, siṅgālā ca migādhamā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva {pb:T:1.0191} sadisā honti, ayaṃ ko nāma pabbato.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ {pb:M:1.0140} nerūti {note:nerunti (sī. syā.)} jānanti, manussā pabbatuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idha vaṇṇena sampannā, vasanti sabbapāṇino.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Amānanā yattha siyā, santānaṃ vā vimānanā;
::

::gathalast
Hīnasammānanā vāpi, na tattha vasatiṃ vase {note:vasatī vase (syā.), vasa divase (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Yatthālaso ca dakkho ca, sūro bhīru ca pūjiyā;
::

::gathalast
Na tattha santo vasanti, avisesakare nare {note:nage (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ neru vibhajati, hīnaukkaṭṭhamajjhime;
::

::gathalast
Avisesakaro neru, handa neruṃ jahāmaseti.
::

::centre
Nerujātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 380. Āsaṅkajātakaṃ (6-1-5)

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Āsāvatī nāma latā, jātā cittalatāvane;
::

::gathalast
Tassā vassasahassena, ekaṃ nibbattate phalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ devā payirupāsanti, tāva dūraphalaṃ satiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsīseva {note:āsiṃseva (sī. syā. pī.)} tuvaṃ rāja, āsā phalavatī sukhā.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Āsīsateva {note:āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)} so pakkhī, āsīsateva {note:āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)} so dijo;
::

::gatha2
Tassa cāsā {note:tassevāsā (syā.)} samijjhati, tāva dūragatā satī;
::

::gathalast
Āsīseva tuvaṃ rāja, āsā phalavatī sukhā.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Sampesi kho maṃ vācāya, na ca sampesi {note:saṃsesi (ka.)} kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Mālā {pb:T:1.0192} sereyyakasseva, vaṇṇavantā agandhikā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Aphalaṃ madhuraṃ vācaṃ, yo mittesu pakubbati;
::

::gathalast
Adadaṃ avissajaṃ bhogaṃ, sandhi tenassa jīrati.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
::

::gathalast
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Balañca vata me khīṇaṃ, pātheyyañca na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Saṅke pāṇūparodhāya, handa dāni vajāmahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Etadeva {pb:V:1.0119}{pb:M:1.0141} hi me nāmaṃ, yaṃ nāmasmi rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Āgamehi mahārāja, pitaraṃ āmantayāmahanti.
::

::centre
Āsaṅkajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 381. Migālopajātakaṃ (6-1-6)

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Na me rucci migālopa, yassa te tādisī gatī;
::

::gathalast
Atuccaṃ tāta patasi, abhūmiṃ tāta sevasi.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Catukkaṇṇaṃva kedāraṃ, yadā te pathavī siyā;
::

::gathalast
Tato tāta nivattassu, māssu etto paraṃ gami.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Santi aññepi sakuṇā, pattayānā vihaṅgamā;
::

::gathalast
Akkhittā vātavegena, naṭṭhā te sassatīsamā.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Akatvā apanandassa {note:aparaṇṇassa (sī. syā. pī.)}, pitu vuddhassa sāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kālavāte {pb:T:1.0193} atikkamma, verambhānaṃ vasaṃ agā {note:gato (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa puttā ca dārā ca, ye caññe anujīvino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe byasanamāpāduṃ, anovādakare dije.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi idha vuddhānaṃ, yo vākyaṃ nāvabujjhati;
::

::gatha2
Atisīmacaro {note:atisīmaṃ caro (sī. syā. ka.)} ditto, gijjhovātītasāsano;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe byasanaṃ papponti, akatvā buddhasāsananti.
::

::centre
Migālopajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 382. Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ (6-1-7)

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Kā nu kāḷena vaṇṇena, na cāpi {note:na cāsi (sī.)} piyadassanā;
::

::gathalast
Kā vā tvaṃ kassa vā dhītā, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Mahārājassahaṃ dhītā, virūpakkhassa caṇḍiyā;
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ kāḷī alakkhikā, kāḷakaṇṇīti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ yācito dehi, vasemu tava santike.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃsīle {pb:M:1.0142} kiṃsamācāre, purise nivisase tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭhā me kāḷi akkhāhi, kathaṃ {note:yathā (sī. pī.)} jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Makkhī paḷāsī sārambhī, issukī maccharī saṭho;
::

::gathalast
So mayhaṃ puriso kanto, laddhaṃ yassa vinassati.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Kodhano {pb:V:1.0120} upanāhī ca, pisuṇo ca vibhedako;
::

::gathalast
Kaṇḍakavāco {note:aṇḍakavāco (ka. sī. pī.)} pharuso, so me kantataro tato.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Ajja {pb:T:1.0194} suveti puriso, sadatthaṃ nāvabujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Ovajjamāno kuppati, seyyaṃ so atimaññati.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Davappaluddho {note:devappaluddho (ka.), davappaladdho (pī.)} puriso, sabbamittehi dhaṃsati;
::

::gathalast
So mayhaṃ puriso kanto, tasmiṃ homi anāmayā.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Apehi etto tvaṃ kāḷi, netaṃ amhesu vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ janapadaṃ gaccha, nigame rājadhāniyo.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Ahampi kho taṃ {note:cetaṃ (sī.)} jānāmi, netaṃ tumhesu vijjati;
::

::gatha2
Santi loke alakkhikā, saṅgharanti bahuṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ devo ca me bhātā, ubho naṃ vidhamāmase.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Kā nu dibbena vaṇṇena, pathabyā supatiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Kā vā tvaṃ kassa vā dhītā, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Mahārājassahaṃ dhītā, dhataraṭṭhassa sirīmato {note:dhataraṭṭhasirīmato (syā. ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ sirī ca lakkhī ca, bhūripaññāti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Okāsaṃ yācito dehi, vasemu tava santike.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃsīle kiṃsamācāre, purise nivisase tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭhā me lakkhi akkhāhi, kathaṃ {note:yathā (sī. pī.)} jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0143} cāpi sīte athavāpi uṇhe, vātātape ḍaṃsasarīsape ca;
::

::gatha2
Khudhaṃ {note:khuddaṃ (syā. ka.), khudaṃ (pī.)} pipāsaṃ abhibhuyya sabbaṃ, rattintivaṃ yo satataṃ niyutto;
::

::gathalast
Kālāgatañca {pb:T:1.0195} na hāpeti atthaṃ, so me manāpo nivise ca tamhi.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Akkodhano mittavā cāgavā ca, sīlūpapanno asaṭhojubhūto {note:asaṭho ujjubhūto (pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Saṅgāhako sakhilo saṇhavāco, mahattapattopi nivātavutti;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃhaṃ {note:tasmāhaṃ (sī. pī.)} pose vipulā bhavāmi, ūmi samuddassa yathāpi vaṇṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Yo cāpi mitte athavā amitte, seṭṭhe sarikkhe atha vāpi hīne;
::

::gatha2
Atthaṃ carantaṃ athavā anatthaṃ, āvī raho saṅgahameva vatte {note:vatto (syā. ka.)}.
::

::gathalast
Vācaṃ na vajjā pharusaṃ kadāci, matassa jīvassa ca tassa homi.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Etesaṃ yo aññataraṃ labhitvā, kantā sirī {note:kantasiriṃ (katthaci), kantaṃ siriṃ (syā.) aṭṭhakathāyaṃ dutiyatatiyapāṭhantarāni} majjati appapañño;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ dittarūpaṃ visamaṃ carantaṃ, karīsaṭhānaṃva {note:karīsajātaṃ va (sī. syā.)} vivajjayāmi.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Attanā {pb:V:1.0121} kurute lakkhiṃ, alakkhiṃ kurutattanā;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:1.0196} hi lakkhiṃ alakkhiṃ vā, añño aññassa kārakoti.
::

::centre
Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 383. Kukkuṭajātakaṃ (6-1-8)

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Sucittapattachadana{pb:M:1.0144}, tambacūḷa vihaṅgama;
::

::gathalast
Oroha dumasākhāya, mudhā bhariyā bhavāmi te.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Catuppadī tvaṃ kalyāṇi, dvipadāhaṃ manorame;
::

::gathalast
Migī pakkhī asaññuttā, aññaṃ pariyesa sāmikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Komārikā te hessāmi, mañjukā piyabhāṇinī;
::

::gathalast
Vinda maṃ ariyena vedena, sāvaya maṃ yadicchasi.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Kuṇapādini lohitape, cori kukkuṭapothini;
::

::gathalast
Na tvaṃ ariyena vedena, mamaṃ bhattāramicchasi.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi caturā {note:cāturā (syā. ka.)} nārī, disvāna sadhanaṃ {note:pavaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} naraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nenti saṇhāhi vācāhi, biḷārī viya kukkuṭaṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Amittavasamanveti, pacchā ca anutappati.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
::

::gathalast
Muccate {pb:T:1.0197} sattusambādhā, kukkuṭova biḷāriyāti.
::

::centre
Kukkuṭajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 384. Dhammadhajajātakaṃ (6-1-9)

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammaṃ caratha ñātayo, dhammaṃ caratha bhaddaṃ vo {note:bhadda vo (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaddako vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo paramadhammiko;
::

::gathalast
Ekapādena tiṭṭhanto, dhammamevānusāsati.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvā aṇḍañca potañca {note:chāpe ca (sī. pī.)}, dhammo dhammoti bhāsati.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Aññaṃ bhaṇati vācāya, aññaṃ kāyena kubbati;
::

::gathalast
Vācāya no ca kāyena, na taṃ dhammaṃ adhiṭṭhito.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Vācāya {pb:V:1.0122}{pb:M:1.0145} sakhilo manoviduggo, channo kūpasayova kaṇhasappo;
::

::gathalast
Dhammadhajo gāmanigamāsusādhu {note:gāmanigamāsu sādhusammato (sī.), gāmanigamasādhu (pī.)}, dujjāno purisena bālisena.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ {pb:T:1.0198} tuṇḍehi pakkhehi, pādā cimaṃ viheṭhatha {note:vipothatha (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Chavañhimaṃ vināsetha, nāyaṃ saṃvāsanārahoti.
::

::centre
Dhammadhajajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 385. Nandiyamigarājajātakaṃ (6-1-10)

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Sace brāhmaṇa gacchesi, sākete {note:sāketaṃ (sī. syā.)} ajjunaṃ {note:añjhanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Vajjāsi nandiyaṃ nāma, puttaṃ asmākamorasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mātā pitā ca te vuddhā, te taṃ icchanti passituṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Bhuttā mayā nivāpāni, rājino pānabhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ rājapiṇḍaṃ avabhottuṃ {note:avabhottaṃ (ka.)}, nāhaṃ brāhmaṇa mussahe.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Odahissāmahaṃ passaṃ, khurappānissa {note:khurappāṇissa (sī.), khurapāṇissa (pī.), khurappapāṇissa (?)} rājino;
::

::gathalast
Tadāhaṃ sukhito mutto, api passeyya mātaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Migarājā pure āsiṃ, kosalassa niketane {note:niketave (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nandiyo nāma nāmena, abhirūpo catuppado.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ maṃ vadhitumāgacchi, dāyasmiṃ ajjune vane;
::

::gathalast
Dhanuṃ ārajjaṃ {note:ārajjuṃ (niyya), adejjhaṃ (sī. pī.) advedhābhāvaṃ ekībhāvanti attho} katvāna, usuṃ sannayha {note:sandhāya (sī. pī.)} kosalo.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Tassāhaṃ {pb:M:1.0146} odahiṃ passaṃ, khurappānissa rājino;
::

::gathalast
Tadāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0199} sukhito mutto, mātaraṃ daṭṭhumāgatoti.
::

::centre
Nandiyamigarājajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Avāriyavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha kujjharathesabha ketuvaro, sadarīmukha neru latā ca puna;
::

::gathalast
Apananda sirī ca sucittavaro, atha dhammika nandimigena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Kharaputtavaggo

#### 386. Kharaputtajātakaṃ (6-2-1)

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Saccaṃ {pb:V:1.0123} kirevamāhaṃsu, vastaṃ {note:bhastaṃ (sī. pī.), kalakaṃ (syā.), garaṃ (ka.)} bāloti paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Passa bālo rahokammaṃ, āvikubbaṃ na bujjhati.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Tvaṃ khopi {note:tvaṃ nu kho (sī. syā.), tvañca kho (pī.)} samma bālosi, kharaputta vijānahi;
::

::gathalast
Rajjuyā hi {note:rajjuyāsi (pī.)} parikkhitto, vaṅkoṭṭho ohitomukho.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Aparampi samma te bālyaṃ {note:ayampi samma te bālo (ka.)}, yo mutto na palāyasi;
::

::gathalast
So ca bālataro samma, yaṃ tvaṃ vahasi senakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nu samma ahaṃ bālo, ajarāja vijānahi;
::

::gathalast
Atha {pb:T:1.0200} kena senako bālo, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Uttamatthaṃ labhitvāna, bhariyāya yo padassati {note:bhayiyā yo padassati (pī.), bhayiyā na bhavissati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tena jahissatattānaṃ, sā cevassa na hessati.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0147} ve piyammeti {note:na piyameti (ka.), na piyamedanti (katthaci)} janinda tādiso, attaṃ niraṃkatvā piyāni sevati {note:sevaye (?)};
::

::gathalast
Attāva seyyo paramā ca seyyo, labbhā piyā ocitatthena pacchāti.
::

::centre
Kharaputtajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 387. Sūcijātakaṃ (6-2-2)

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Akakkasaṃ apharusaṃ, kharadhotaṃ supāsiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhumaṃ tikhiṇaggañca, ko sūciṃ ketumicchati.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Sumajjañca supāsañca, anupubbaṃ {note:anupubba (sī. syā.)} suvaṭṭitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ghanaghātimaṃ paṭithaddhaṃ, ko sūciṃ ketumicchati.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Ito dāni patāyanti, sūciyo baḷisāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Koyaṃ kammāragāmasmiṃ, sūciṃ vikketumicchati.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Ito satthāni gacchanti, kammantā vividhā puthū;
::

::gathalast
Koyaṃ kammāragāmasmiṃ, sūciṃ vikketumicchati {note:marahati (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Sūciṃ {pb:T:1.0201} kammāragāmasmiṃ, vikketabbā pajānatā;
::

::gathalast
Ācariyāva jānanti {note:ācariyā sañjānanti (ka.), ācariyā pajānanti (syā.), ācariyāva sañjānanti (pī.)}, kammaṃ sukatadukkaṭaṃ {note:dukkataṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ {pb:V:1.0124} ce {note:imañca (sī. syā. pī.)} te pitā bhadde, sūciṃ jaññā mayā kataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayā ca maṃ nimanteyya, yañcatthaññaṃ ghare dhananti.
::

::centre
Sūcijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 388. Tuṇḍilajātakaṃ (6-2-3)

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Navachannake {note:navachandake (sī. pī.), navacchaddake (syā.)} dāni {note:doṇi (ka.), dānaṃ, dāne (katthaci)} diyyati, puṇṇāyaṃ doṇi suvāminī ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Bahuke jane pāsapāṇike, no ca kho me paṭibhāti bhuñjituṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Tasasi {pb:M:1.0148} bhamasi leṇamicchasi, attāṇosi kuhiṃ gamissasi;
::

::gathalast
Appossukko bhuñja tuṇḍila, maṃsatthāya hi positāmhase {note:posiyāmase (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Ogaha rahadaṃ akaddamaṃ, sabbaṃ sedamalaṃ pavāhaya;
::

::gathalast
Gaṇhāhi navaṃ vilepanaṃ, yassa {pb:T:1.0202} gandho na kadāci chijjati.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Katamo rahado akaddamo, kiṃsu sedamalanti vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Katamañca navaṃ vilepanaṃ, yassa gandho na kadāci chijjati.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo rahado akaddamo, pāpaṃ sedamalanti vuccati;
::

::gathalast
Sīlañca navaṃ vilepanaṃ, tassa gandho na kadāci chijjati.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Nandanti sarīraghātino, na ca nandanti sarīradhārino;
::

::gathalast
Puṇṇāya ca puṇṇamāsiyā, ramamānāva jahanti jīvitanti.
::

::centre
Tuṇḍilajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 389. Suvaṇṇakakkaṭajātakaṃ (6-2-4)

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Siṅgīmigo āyatacakkhunetto, aṭṭhittaco vārisayo alomo;
::

::gathalast
Tenābhibhūto kapaṇaṃ rudāmi, hare sakhā kissa nu maṃ jahāsi.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:T:1.0203}{pb:M:1.0149} passasanto mahatā phaṇena, bhujaṅgamo kakkaṭamajjhapatto;
::

::gathalast
Sakhā sakhāraṃ paritāyamāno, bhujaṅgamaṃ kakkaṭako gahesi.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāyasaṃ no pana kaṇhasappaṃ, ghāsatthiko kakkaṭako adeyya;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ āyatacakkhunetta, atha kissa hetumha ubho gahītā.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Ayaṃ puriso mama atthakāmo, yo maṃ gahetvāna dakāya neti;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ mate dukkhamanappakaṃ me, ahañca eso ca ubho na homa.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Mamañca disvāna pavaddhakāyaṃ, sabbo jano hiṃsitumeva micche;
::

::gathalast
Sāduñca thūlañca muduñca maṃsaṃ, kākāpi maṃ disvāna {note:disva (sī. pī.)} viheṭhayeyyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Sacetassa {pb:V:1.0125} hetumha ubho gahītā, uṭṭhātu poso visamāvamāmi {note:visamācamāmi (sī. pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Mamañca kākañca pamuñca khippaṃ, pure {pb:T:1.0204} visaṃ gāḷhamupeti maccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Sappaṃ pamokkhāmi na tāva kākaṃ, paṭibandhako {note:paṭibaddhako (sī. pī.)} hohiti {note:hoti hi (syā.)} tāva kāko;
::

::gathalast
Purisañca disvāna sukhiṃ arogaṃ, kākaṃ pamokkhāmi yatheva sappaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Kāko {pb:M:1.0150} tadā devadatto ahosi, māro pana kaṇhasappo ahosi;
::

::gathalast
Ānandabhaddo kakkaṭako ahosi, ahaṃ tadā brāhmaṇo homi satthāti {note:tatthāti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::centre
Suvaṇṇakakkaṭajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 390. Mayhakajātakaṃ (6-2-5)

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Sakuṇo mayhako nāma, girisānudarīcaro;
::

::gathalast
Pakkaṃ pipphalimāruyha, mayhaṃ mayhanti kandati.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Tassevaṃ vilapantassa, dijasaṅghā samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvāna pipphaliṃ yanti, vilapatveva so dijo.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva idhekacco, saṅgharitvā bahuṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nevattano na ñātīnaṃ, yathodhiṃ paṭipajjati.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Na so acchādanaṃ bhattaṃ, na mālaṃ na vilepanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhoti {pb:T:1.0205} {note:nānubhoti (syā. ka.)} sakiṃ kiñci, na saṅgaṇhāti ñātake.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Tassevaṃ vilapantassa, mayhaṃ mayhanti rakkhato;
::

::gatha2
Rājāno atha vā corā, dāyadā ye va {note:ye ca (syā. ka.)} appiyā;
::

::gathalast
Dhanamādāya gacchanti, vilapatveva so naro.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Dhīro {note:dhīro ca (sī.)} bhoge adhigamma, saṅgaṇhāti ca ñātake;
::

::gathalast
Tena so kittiṃ pappoti, pecca sagge pamodatīti {note:sagge ca modatīti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::centre
Mayhakajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 391. Vijjādharajātakaṃ (6-2-6)

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Dubbaṇṇarūpaṃ tuvamariyavaṇṇī, purakkhatvā {note:purakkhitvā (syā. ka.)} pañjaliko namassasi;
::

::gathalast
Seyyo nu te so udavā {note:udāhu (syā. ka.)} sarikkho, nāmaṃ parassattano cāpi brūhi.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0151} nāmagottaṃ gaṇhanti rāja, sammaggatānujjugatāna {note:samaggatānujjugatāna (syā.), samuggatānujjugatāna (ka.)} devā;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca te nāmadheyyaṃ vadāmi, sakkohamasmī tidasānamindo.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0126} disvā bhikkhuṃ caraṇūpapannaṃ, purakkhatvā pañjaliko namassati;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ devarājetamatthaṃ, ito {pb:T:1.0206} cuto kiṃ labhate sukhaṃ so.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Yo disvā bhikkhuṃ caraṇūpapannaṃ, purakkhatvā pañjaliko namassati;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭheva dhamme labhate pasaṃsaṃ, saggañca so yāti sarīrabhedā.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Lakkhī vata me udapādi ajja, yaṃ vāsavaṃ bhūtapatiddasāma;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhuñca disvāna tuvañca sakka, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhuñca disvāna mamañca rāja, karohi puññāni anappakāni.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Akkodhano niccapasannacitto, sabbātithīyācayogo bhavitvā;
::

::gathalast
Nihacca mānaṃ abhivādayissaṃ, sutvāna devinda subhāsitānīti.
::

::centre
Vijjādhara {note:dhajaviheṭhaka (sī. pī.), pabbajitaviheṭhaka (syā.)} jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 392. Siṅghapupphajātakaṃ (6-2-7)

::hangnum
