115\.
::

::gatha1
Yametaṃ {pb:T:1.0207}{pb:M:1.0152} {note:yamekaṃ (pī.)} vārijaṃ pupphaṃ, adinnaṃ upasiṅghasi;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṅgametaṃ theyyānaṃ, gandhathenosi mārisa.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Na harāmi na bhañjāmi, ārā siṅghāmi vārijaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, gandhathenoti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Yoyaṃ bhisāni khaṇati, puṇḍarīkāni bhañjati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ ākiṇṇakammanto, kasmā eso na vuccati.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Ākiṇṇaluddo puriso, dhāticelaṃva makkhito;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ me vacanaṃ natthi, tañcārahāmi vattave.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Anaṅgaṇassa posassa, niccaṃ sucigavesino;
::

::gathalast
Vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa, abbhāmattaṃva khāyati.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā maṃ yakkha jānāsi, atho maṃ anukampasi;
::

::gathalast
Punapi yakkha vajjāsi, yadā passasi edisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Neva taṃ upajīvāmi, napi te bhatakāmhase {note:bhatakamhase (sī. pī.), bhatikamhase (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Tvameva bhikkhu jāneyya, yena gaccheyya suggatinti.
::

::centre
Siṅghapuppha {note:bhisapuppha (sī. pī.), upasiṅghapuppha (syā.)} jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 393. Vighāsādajātakaṃ (6-2-8)

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Susukhaṃ {pb:V:1.0127} vata jīvanti, ye janā vighāsādino;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭheva {pb:T:1.0208} dhamme pāsaṃsā, samparāye ca suggatī.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Sukassa {note:suvassa (sī. syā. pī.)} bhāsamānassa, na nisāmetha paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Idaṃ suṇātha sodariyā, amhevāyaṃ pasaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Nāhaṃ tumhe pasaṃsāmi, kuṇapādā suṇātha me;
::

::gathalast
Ucchiṭṭhabhojino {note:bhojanā (ka.)} tumhe, na tumhe vighāsādino.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Sattavassā {pb:M:1.0153} pabbajitā, mejjhāraññe {note:majjheraññe (ka.)} sikhaṇḍino;
::

::gatha2
Vighāseneva yāpentā, mayaṃ ce bhoto gārayhā;
::

::gathalast
Ke nu bhoto pasaṃsiyā.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Tumhe sīhānaṃ byagghānaṃ, vāḷānañcāvasiṭṭhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ucchiṭṭheneva yāpentā, maññivho vighāsādino.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Ye brāhmaṇassa samaṇassa, aññassa vā {note:aññassa ca (sī. syā.), aññasseva (pī.)} vanibbino {note:vaṇibbino (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Datvāva {note:datvāna (pī. ka.)} sesaṃ bhuñjanti, te janā vighāsādinoti.
::

::centre
Vighāsādajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 394. Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ (6-2-9)

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Paṇītaṃ bhuñjase bhattaṃ, sappitelañca mātula;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, kiso tvamasi vāyasa.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Amittamajjhe vasato, tesu āmisamesato;
::

::gathalast
Niccaṃ ubbiggahadayassa, kuto kākassa daḷhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Niccaṃ ubbegino {note:ubbiggino (syā. ka.), ubbedhino (sī.)} kākā, dhaṅkā pāpena kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Laddho {pb:T:1.0209} piṇḍo na pīṇeti, kiso tenasmi vaṭṭaka.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Lūkhāni tiṇabījāni, appasnehāni bhuñjasi;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, thūlo tvamasi vaṭṭaka.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Appicchā appacintāya, adūragamanena ca;
::

::gathalast
Laddhāladdhena yāpento, thūlo tenasmi vāyasa.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Appicchassa {pb:V:1.0128} hi posassa, appacintasukhassa {note:appacintisukhassa (sī. syā. pī.)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Susaṅgahitamānassa {note:susaṅgahitapamāṇassa (sī. syā. pī.)}, vuttī susamudānayāti.
::

::centre
Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 395. Pārāvatajātakaṃ (6-2-10)

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Cirassaṃ vata passāmi, sahāyaṃ maṇidhārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukatā {note:sukatāya (sī. pī.)} massukuttiyā, sobhate vata me sakhā.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Parūḷhakacchanakhalomo{pb:M:1.0154}, ahaṃ kammesu byāvaṭo;
::

::gathalast
Cirassaṃ nhāpitaṃ laddhā, lomaṃ taṃ ajjaṃ hārayiṃ {note:apahārayiṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nu lomaṃ ahāresi, dullabhaṃ laddha kappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha kiñcarahi te samma, kaṇṭhe kiṇikiṇāyati {note:idaṃ kaṇṭhe kiṇāyati (ka.), kaṇṭhe kiṃnikilāyati (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Manussasukhumālānaṃ, maṇi kaṇṭhesu lambati;
::

::gathalast
Tesāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0210} anusikkhāmi, mā tvaṃ maññi davā kataṃ.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Sacepimaṃ pihayasi, massukuttiṃ sukāritaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kārayissāmi te samma, maṇiñcāpi dadāmi te.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Tvaññeva maṇinā channo, sukatāya ca massuyā;
::

::gathalast
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāmi, piyaṃ me tava dassananti.
::

::centre
Pārāvatajātakaṃ {note:kākajātakaṃ (sī. pī.), maṇijātakaṃ (syā.)} dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kharaputtavaggo {note:senakavaggo (sī. pī.), khuraputtavaggo (syā.), sūcivaggo (ka.)} dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha passa sasūci ca tuṇḍilako, miga mayhakapañcamapakkhivaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha pañjali vārija mejjha puna, atha vaṭṭa kapotavarena dasāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha vaggaṃ pakittissaṃ, chanipātaṃ varuttame;
::

::gathalast
Avāriyā ca kharo ca {note:senaka (sī.), sūci ca (syā. ka.)}, dve ca vuttā subyañjanāti.
::

::centre
Chakkanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 7. Sattakanipāto

#### 1. Kukkuvaggo

#### 396. Kukkujātakaṃ (7-1-1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Diyaḍḍhakukkū {pb:T:1.0211}{pb:V:1.0129}{pb:M:1.0155} udayena kaṇṇikā, vidatthiyo aṭṭha parikkhipanti naṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā siṃsapā {note:sasiṃsapā (sī. pī.), sā sīsapā (syā.), yā siṃsapā (ka. sī. niyya)} sāramayā apheggukā, kuhiṃ ṭhitā upparito {note:uparito (sī. syā. pī.)} na dhaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Yā tiṃsati sāramayā anujjukā, parikiriya {note:pakiriyā (ka.)} gopāṇasiyo samaṃ ṭhitā {note:samaṭṭhitā (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Tāhi susaṅgahitā balasā pīḷitā {note:tā saṅgahitā balasā ca pīḷitā (sī.), tāhi susaṅgahitā balasā ca pīḷitā (syā.), tāhi saṅgahītā balasā ca pīḷitā (pī.)}, samaṃ ṭhitā upparito na dhaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi mittehi daḷhehi paṇḍito, abhejjarūpehi sucīhi mantibhi;
::

::gathalast
Susaṅgahīto siriyā na dhaṃsati, gopāṇasī bhāravahāva kaṇṇikā.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Kharattacaṃ bellaṃ yathāpi satthavā, anāmasantopi karoti tittakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samāharaṃ sāduṃ karoti patthiva, asāduṃ kayirā tanubandhamuddharaṃ {note:tanuvaṭṭamuddharaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi {pb:T:1.0212} gāmanigamesu paṇḍito, asāhasaṃ rājadhanāni saṅgharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammānuvattī paṭipajjamāno, sa phāti kayirā aviheṭhayaṃ paraṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Odātamūlaṃ {pb:M:1.0156} sucivārisambhavaṃ, jātaṃ yathā pokkharaṇīsu ambujaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Padumaṃ yathā agginikāsiphālimaṃ, na kaddamo na rajo na vāri limpati.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi vohārasuciṃ asāhasaṃ, visuddhakammantamapetapāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na limpati kammakilesa tādiso, jātaṃ yathā pokkharaṇīsu ambujanti.
::

::centre
Kukkujātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 397. Manojajātakaṃ (7-1-2)

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā cāpo ninnamati, jiyā cāpi nikūjati;
::

::gathalast
Haññate nūna manojo, migarājā sakhā mama.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Handa dāni vanantāni, pakkamāmi yathāsukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Netādisā sakhā honti, labbhā me jīvato sakhā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0130} pāpajanasaṃsevī, accantaṃ sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Manojaṃ {pb:T:1.0213} passa semānaṃ, giriyassānusāsanī {note:ariyassānusāsanī (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Na pāpasampavaṅkena, mātā puttena nandati;
::

::gathalast
Manojaṃ passa semānaṃ, acchannaṃ {note:sacchannaṃ (ka.)} samhi lohite.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Evamāpajjate poso, pāpiyo ca nigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Yo ve hitānaṃ vacanaṃ, na karoti atthadassinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Evañca so hoti tato ca pāpiyo, yo uttamo adhamajanūpasevī;
::

::gathalast
Passuttamaṃ adhamajanūpasevitaṃ {note:seviṃ (syā.)}, migādhipaṃ saravaraveganiddhutaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Nihīyati {pb:M:1.0157} puriso nihīnasevī, na ca hāyetha kadāci tulyasevī;
::

::gathalast
Seṭṭhamupagamaṃ {note:mupanamaṃ (sī. pī. a. ni. 3.26)} udeti khippaṃ, tasmāttanā uttaritaraṃ {note:tasmā attano uttariṃ (sī. pī.), tasmā attano uttaraṃ (syā.)} bhajethāti.
::

::centre
Manojajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 398. Sutanujātakaṃ (7-1-3)

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Rājā te bhattaṃ pāhesi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maghadevasmiṃ {note:makhādevasmiṃ (sī. pī.), māghadevasmiṃ (ka.)} adhivatthe, ehi nikkhamma bhuñjassu.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi māṇava orena, bhikkhamādāya sūpitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tvañca {pb:T:1.0214} māṇava bhikkhā ca {note:bhakkhosi (syā.), bhakkhāva (ka.)}, ubho bhakkhā bhavissatha.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Appakena tuvaṃ yakkha, thullamatthaṃ jahissasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhaṃ te nāharissanti, janā maraṇasaññino.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Laddhāya yakkhā {note:laddhāyaṃ yakkha (sī. syā. pī.)} tava niccabhikkhaṃ, suciṃ paṇītaṃ rasasā upetaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhañca te āhariyo naro idha, sudullabho hehiti bhakkhite {note:khādite (sī. syā. pī.)} mayi.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Mameva {note:mamesa (sī. pī.)} sutano attho, yathā bhāsasi māṇava;
::

::gathalast
Mayā tvaṃ samanuññāto, sotthiṃ passāhi mātaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Khaggaṃ chattañca pātiñca, gacchamādāya {note:gacchevādāya (sī. syā. pī.)} māṇava;
::

::gathalast
Sotthiṃ passatu te mātā, tvañca passāhi mātaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ yakkha sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Dhanañca me adhigataṃ, rañño ca vacanaṃ katanti.
::

::centre
Sutanujātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 399. Mātuposakagijjhajātakaṃ (7-1-4)

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:V:1.0131}{pb:M:1.0158} kathaṃ nu karissanti, vuddhā giridarīsayā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ baddhosmi pāsena, nilīyassa vasaṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ gijjha paridevasi, kā nu te paridevanā;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:1.0215} me suto vā diṭṭho vā, bhāsanto mānusiṃ dijo.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Bharāmi mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsaye;
::

::gathalast
Te kathaṃ nu karissanti, ahaṃ vasaṃ gato tava.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nu gijjho yojanasataṃ, kuṇapāni avekkhati;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhasi.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
::

::gathalast
Atha jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhati.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Bharassu mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsaye;
::

::gathalast
Mayā tvaṃ samanuññāto, sotthiṃ passāhi ñātake.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Bharissaṃ mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsayeti.
::

::centre
Mātuposakagijjhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 400. Dabbhapupphajātakaṃ (7-1-5)

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Anutīracārī bhaddante, sahāyamanudhāva maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahā me gahito {note:rohito (ka.)} maccho, so maṃ harati vegasā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Gambhīracārī bhaddante, daḷhaṃ gaṇhāhi thāmasā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ taṃ uddharissāmi, supaṇṇo uragāmiva {note:uragammiva (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Vivādo no samuppanno, dabbhapuppha suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Samehi {pb:T:1.0216} medhagaṃ {note:medhakaṃ (pī.)} samma, vivādo vūpasammataṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammaṭṭhohaṃ pure āsiṃ, bahū aḍḍā me tīritā {note:bahuaṭṭaṃ me tīritaṃ (sī.), bahuaṭṭaṃva tīritaṃ (syā.), bahu atthaṃ me tīritaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Samemi medhagaṃ samma, vivādo vūpasammataṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Anutīracāri {pb:M:1.0159} naṅguṭṭhaṃ, sīsaṃ gambhīracārino;
::

::gathalast
Accāyaṃ {note:athāyaṃ (sī. pī.)} majjhimo khaṇḍo, dhammaṭṭhassa bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Cirampi {pb:V:1.0132} bhakkho abhavissa, sace na vivademase;
::

::gathalast
Asīsakaṃ anaṅguṭṭhaṃ, siṅgālo harati rohitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi rājā nandeyya, rajjaṃ laddhāna khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Evāhamajja nandāmi, disvā puṇṇamukhaṃ patiṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ nu thalajo santo, udake macchaṃ parāmasi;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kathaṃ adhigataṃ tayā.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Vivādena kisā honti, vivādena dhanakkhayā;
::

::gathalast
Jīnā uddā vivādena, bhuñja māyāvi rohitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva manussesu, vivādo yattha jāyati;
::

::gatha2
Dhammaṭṭhaṃ paṭidhāvanti, so hi nesaṃ vināyako;
::

::gathalast
Dhanāpi tattha jīyanti, rājakoso pavaḍḍhatīti {note:ca vaḍḍhati (pī.)}.
::

::centre
Dabbhapupphajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 401. Paṇṇakajātakaṃ (7-1-6)

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Paṇṇakaṃ {note:dasaṇṇakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} tikhiṇadhāraṃ, asiṃ sampannapāyinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Parisāyaṃ {pb:T:1.0217} puriso gilati, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Gileyya puriso lobhā, asiṃ sampannapāyinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yo ca vajjā dadāmīti, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava {note:māgadha (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Byākāsi āyuro pañhaṃ, atthaṃ {note:attha (pī. sī. niyya)} dhammassa kovido;
::

::gatha2
Pukkusaṃ dāni pucchāmi, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0160} vācamupajīvanti, aphalaṃ giramudīritaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yo ca datvā avākayirā, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Byākāsi pukkuso pañhaṃ, atthaṃ dhammassa kovido;
::

::gatha2
Senakaṃ dāni pucchāmi, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Dadeyya {pb:V:1.0133} puriso dānaṃ, appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yo ca datvā nānutappe {note:tape (sī. pī.)}, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Byākāsi āyuro pañhaṃ, atho pukkusaporiso;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe {pb:T:1.0218} pañhe atibhoti, yathā bhāsati senakoti.
::

::centre
Paṇṇaka {note:dasaṇṇaka (sī. syā. pī.)} jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 402. Sattubhastajātakaṃ (7-1-7)

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Vibbhantacitto kupitindriyosi, nettehi te vārigaṇā savanti;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ te naṭṭhaṃ kiṃ pana patthayāno, idhāgamā brahme tadiṅgha {note:brāhmaṇa iṅgha (sī. syā.)} brūhi.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Miyyetha bhariyā vajato mamajja, agacchato maraṇamāha yakkho;
::

::gathalast
Etena dukkhena pavedhitosmi, akkhāhi me senaka etamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Bahūni ṭhānāni vicintayitvā, yamettha vakkhāmi tadeva saccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi te brāhmaṇa sattubhastaṃ, ajānato kaṇhasappo paviṭṭho.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Ādāya {pb:M:1.0161} daṇḍaṃ parisumbha bhastaṃ, passeḷamūgaṃ uragaṃ dujivhaṃ {note:dijivhaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, bhujaṅgamaṃ passa pamuñca bhastaṃ.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃviggarūpo {pb:T:1.0219} parisāya majjhe, so brāhmaṇo sattubhastaṃ pamuñci;
::

::gathalast
Atha nikkhami urago uggatejo, āsīviso sappo phaṇaṃ karitvā.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Suladdhalābhā janakassa rañño, yo passatī senakaṃ sādhupaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭṭachaddo {note:vivattacchaddo (sī.), vivaṭṭacchado (syā.), vivaṭṭacchaddā (pī.)} nusi sabbadassī, ñāṇaṃ nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Imāni me sattasatāni atthi, gaṇhāhi sabbāni dadāmi tuyhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayā hi me jīvitamajja laddhaṃ, athopi bhariyāya makāsi sotthiṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Na paṇḍitā vetanamādiyanti, citrāhi gāthāhi subhāsitāhi;
::

::gathalast
Itopi te brahme dadantu vittaṃ, ādāya tvaṃ gaccha sakaṃ niketanti.
::

::centre
Sattubhastajātakaṃ {note:senakajātakaṃ (syā.)} sattamaṃ.
::

#### 403. Aṭṭhisenakajātakaṃ (7-1-8)

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Yeme {pb:T:1.0220} ahaṃ na jānāmi, aṭṭhisena vanibbake;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ saṅgamma yācanti, kasmā maṃ tvaṃ na yācasi.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Yācako {pb:V:1.0134} appiyo hoti, yācaṃ adadamappiyo;
::

::gathalast
Tasmāhaṃ taṃ na yācāmi, mā me videssanā {note:viddesanā (sī. pī.)} ahu.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0162} ve yācanajīvāno, kāle yācaṃ na yācati;
::

::gathalast
Parañca puññā {note:puññaṃ (syā. ka.)} dhaṃseti, attanāpi na jīvati.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca {note:yo ve (ka.)} yācanajīvāno, kāle yācañhi yācati {note:yācaṃpi yācati (syā.), yācāni yācati (pī.), yācati yācanaṃ (sī. niyya), yācanaṃ yācati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Parañca puññaṃ labbheti, attanāpi ca jīvati.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Na ve dessanti {note:na ve dussanti (syā.), na ve dissanti (pī.), na videssanti (ka. aṭṭha.)} sappaññā, disvā yācakamāgate;
::

::gathalast
Brahmacāri piyo mesi, vada tvaṃ {note:vara taṃ (sī.), vara tvaṃ (pī.)} bhaññamicchasi {note:yaññamicchasi (?)}.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Na ve yācanti sappaññā, dhīro ca veditumarahati;
::

::gathalast
Uddissa ariyā tiṭṭhanti, esā ariyāna yācanā.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
::

::gathalast
Ariyo hi ariyassa kathaṃ na dajjā, sutvāna gāthā tava dhammayuttāti.
::

::centre
Aṭṭhisenakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 404. Kapijātakaṃ (7-1-9)

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Yattha {pb:T:1.0221} verī nivasati, na vase tattha paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Ekarattaṃ dirattaṃ vā, dukkhaṃ vasati verisu.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Diso ve lahucittassa, posassānuvidhīyato;
::

::gathalast
Ekassa kapino hetu, yūthassa anayo kato.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Bālova {note:ca (sī. syā. pī.)} paṇḍitamānī, yūthassa parihārako;
::

::gathalast
Sacittassa vasaṃ gantvā, sayethāyaṃ {note:passethāyaṃ (ka.)} yathā kapi.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Na sādhu balavā bālo, yūthassa parihārako;
::

::gathalast
Ahito bhavati ñātīnaṃ, sakuṇānaṃva cetako {note:ceṭako (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Dhīrova {pb:M:1.0163} balavā sādhu, yūthassa parihārako;
::

::gathalast
Hito bhavati ñātīnaṃ, tidasānaṃva vāsavo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca sīlañca paññañca, sutañcattani passati;
::

::gathalast
Ubhinnamatthaṃ carati, attano ca parassa ca.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā tuleyya mattānaṃ, sīlapaññāsutāmiva {note:sīlaṃ paññaṃ sutaṃpiva (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Gaṇaṃ vā parihare dhīro, eko vāpi paribbajeti.
::

::centre
Kapijātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 405. Bakajātakaṃ (7-1-10)

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Dvāsattati {pb:V:1.0135} gotama {note:bho gotama (ka.)} puññakammā, vasavattino {pb:T:1.0222} jātijaraṃ atītā;
::

::gathalast
Ayamantimā vedagū brahmapatti {note:brahmupapatti (syā. ka.)}, asmābhijappanti janā {note:pajā (ka.)} anekā.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Appañhi etaṃ {note:appañca hetaṃ (syā.), appaṃsi etaṃ (ka.)} na hi dīghamāyu, yaṃ tvaṃ baka maññasi dīghamāyuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ sahassāni {note:sahassānaṃ (sī. pī. saṃ. ni. 1.175), sahassāna (syā. kaṃ.)} nirabbudānaṃ, āyuṃ pajānāmi tavāha brahme.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Anantadassī bhagavāhamasmi, jātijjaraṃ sokamupātivatto;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ me purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ {note:sīlavantaṃ (pī. ka.)}, ācikkha me taṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ tvaṃ apāyesi bahū manusse, pipāsite ghammani samparete;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0164} eṇikūlasmi janaṃ gahītaṃ, amocayī gayhaka niyyamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Gaṅgāya sotasmiṃ gahītanāvaṃ, luddena {pb:T:1.0223} nāgena manussakappā;
::

::gatha2
Amocayi tvaṃ balasā pasayha, taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Kappo ca te baddhacaro {note:patthacaro (syā.), paṭṭhacaro (ka.)} ahosi, sambuddhimantaṃ {note:sambuddhivantaṃ (syā. pī.), sambuddhavantaṃ (ka.)} vatinaṃ {note:vatitaṃ (syā.), vatidaṃ (ka.)} amaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā pajānāsi mametamāyuṃ, aññampi jānāsi tathā hi buddho;
::

::gathalast
Tathā hi tāyaṃ {note:tyāyaṃ (saṃ. ni. 1.175)} jalitānubhāvo, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati brahmalokanti.
::

::centre
Bakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Kukkuvaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varakaṇṇika cāpavaro sutano, atha gijjha sarohitamacchavaro;
::

::gathalast
Puna paṇṇaka {note:dasaṇṇaka (sī. syā. pī.)} senaka yācanako, atha veri sabrahmabakena dasāti.
::

#### 2. Gandhāravaggo

#### 406. Gandhārajātakaṃ (7-2-1)

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Hitvā {pb:T:1.0224}{pb:V:1.0136}{pb:M:1.0165} gāmasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni soḷasa;
::

::gathalast
Koṭṭhāgārāni phītāni, sannidhiṃ dāni kubbasi.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Hitvā gandhāravisayaṃ, pahūtadhanadhāriyaṃ {note:dhāniyaṃ (sī. pī.), dhaññanti attho};
::

::gathalast
Pasāsanato {note:pasāsanito (sī. syā.), pasāsanāto (pī.)} nikkhanto, idha dāni pasāsasi.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammaṃ bhaṇāmi vedeha, adhammo me na ruccati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ me bhaṇamānassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, paro labhati ruppanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahatthiyampi ce vācaṃ, na taṃ bhāseyya paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ ruppatu vā mā vā, bhusaṃva vikirīyatu;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ me bhaṇamānassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
No ce assa sakā buddhi, vinayo vā susikkhito;
::

::gathalast
Vane andhamahiṃsova {note:andhamahisova (sī. pī.)} careyya bahuko jano.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmā ca panidhekacce, āceramhi {note:ācāramhi (sī. pī.)} susikkhitā;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā vinītavinayā, caranti susamāhitāti.
::

::centre
Gandhārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 407. Mahākapijātakaṃ (7-2-2)

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Attānaṃ {pb:T:1.0225} saṅkamaṃ katvā, yo sotthiṃ samatārayi;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ tvaṃ tesaṃ kime {note:kimo (sī. pī.), kiṃ me (syā.)} tuyhaṃ, honti ete {note:hete (syā.), so te (ka.)} mahākapi.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Rājāhaṃ issaro tesaṃ, yūthassa parihārako;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ sokaparetānaṃ, bhītānaṃ te arindama.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Ullaṅghayitvā {note:sa laṅghayitvā (pī.), sulaṅghayitvā (ka.)} attānaṃ, vissaṭṭhadhanuno sataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato aparapādesu, daḷhaṃ bandhaṃ latāguṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Chinnabbhamiva {pb:M:1.0166} vātena, nuṇṇo {note:nunno (sī.)} rukkhaṃ upāgamiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ appabhavaṃ tattha, sākhaṃ hatthehi aggahiṃ.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:V:1.0137} maṃ viyāyataṃ santaṃ, sākhāya ca latāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Samanukkamantā pādehi, sotthiṃ sākhāmigā gatā.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ maṃ na tapate bandho, mato {note:vadho (sī. syā. pī.)} me na tapessati;
::

::gathalast
Sukhamāharitaṃ tesaṃ, yesaṃ rajjamakārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Esā te upamā rāja, taṃ suṇohi arindama {note:atthasandassanī katā (pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Raññā raṭṭhassa yoggassa, balassa nigamassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ sukhameṭṭhabbaṃ, khattiyena pajānatāti.
::

::centre
Mahākapijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 408. Kumbhakārajātakaṃ (7-2-3)

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Ambāhamaddaṃ {pb:T:1.0226} vanamantarasmiṃ, nīlobhāsaṃ phalitaṃ {note:phalinaṃ (pī.)} saṃvirūḷhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamaddasaṃ phalahetu vibhaggaṃ, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Selaṃ sumaṭṭhaṃ naravīraniṭṭhitaṃ {note:naravidduniṭṭhitaṃ (ka.)}, nārī yugaṃ dhārayi appasaddaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dutiyañca āgamma ahosi saddo, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Dijā dijaṃ kuṇapamāharantaṃ, ekaṃ samānaṃ bahukā samecca;
::

::gathalast
Āhārahetū paripātayiṃsu, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Usabhāhamaddaṃ yūthassa majjhe, calakkakuṃ vaṇṇabalūpapannaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamaddasaṃ kāmahetu vitunnaṃ, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Karaṇḍako {pb:M:1.0167} {note:karaṇḍunāma (sī. pī.)} kaliṅgānaṃ, gandhārānañca naggaji;
::

::gathalast
Nimirājā videhānaṃ, pañcālānañca dummukho;
::

::gathalast
Ete raṭṭhāni hitvāna, pabbajiṃsu akiñcanā.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbepime {pb:T:1.0227} devasamā samāgatā, aggī yathā pajjalito tathevime;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi eko carissāmi bhaggavi, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Ayameva kālo na hi añño atthi, anusāsitā me na bhaveyya pacchā;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi ekā carissāmi bhaggava, sakuṇīva muttā purisassa hatthā.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Āmaṃ pakkañca jānanti, atho loṇaṃ aloṇakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ disvāna pabbajiṃ, careva tvaṃ carāmahanti.
::

::centre
Kumbhakārajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 409. Daḷhadhammajātakaṃ (7-2-4)

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ {pb:V:1.0138} ce daḷhadhammassa {note:daḷhadhammāya (pī.)}, vahanti nābhirādhayiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dharantī urasi sallaṃ, yuddhe vikkantacārinī.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Nūna rājā na jānāti {note:na ha nūna rājā jānāti (sī. pī.)}, mama vikkamaporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgāme sukatantāni, dūtavippahitāni ca.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Sā nūnāhaṃ marissāmi, abandhu aparāyinī {note:aparāyiṇī (sī.), aparāyaṇī (?)};
::

::gathalast
Tadā {pb:T:1.0228} hi {note:tathā hi (pī.)} kumbhakārassa, dinnā chakaṇahārikā.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Yāvatāsīsatī poso, tāvadeva pavīṇati;
::

::gathalast
Atthāpāye jahanti naṃ, oṭṭhibyādhiṃva khattiyo.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Yo pubbe katakalyāṇo, katattho nāvabujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Atthā tassa palujjanti, ye honti abhipatthitā.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0168} pubbe katakalyāṇo, katattho manubujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Atthā tassa pavaḍḍhanti, ye honti abhipatthitā.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante {note:bhaddaṃ vo (sī. syā. pī.)}, yāvantettha samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe kataññuno hotha, ciraṃ saggamhi ṭhassathāti.
::

::centre
Daḷhadhammajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 410. Somadattajātakaṃ (7-2-5)

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Yo maṃ pure paccuḍḍeti {note:paccudeti (sī. syā. pī.), paccuṭṭheti (ka.)}, araññe dūramāyato;
::

::gathalast
So na dissati mātaṅgo, somadatto kuhiṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Ayaṃ vā so mato seti, allasiṅgaṃva vacchito {note:allapiṅkava chijjito (sī. pī.), allapītaṃva vicchito (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhumyā nipatito seti, amarā vata kuñjaro.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Anagāriyupetassa, vippamuttassa te sato;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇassa na taṃ sādhu, yaṃ petamanusocasi.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃvāsena have sakka, manussassa migassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Hadaye {pb:T:1.0229} jāyate pemaṃ, taṃ na sakkā asocituṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Mataṃ marissaṃ rodanti, ye rudanti lapanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā tvaṃ isi mā rodi, roditaṃ moghamāhu santo.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Kanditena {pb:V:1.0139} have brahme, mato peto samuṭṭhahe;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe saṅgamma rodāma, aññamaññassa ñātake.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Abbahī vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna vāsavāti.
::

::centre
Somadattajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 411. Susīmajātakaṃ (7-2-6)

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Kāḷāni {pb:M:1.0169} kesāni pure ahesuṃ, jātāni sīsamhi yathāpadese;
::

::gathalast
Tānajja setāni susīma {note:susima (ka.)} disvā, dhammaṃ cara brahmacariyassa kālo.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Mameva deva palitaṃ na tuyhaṃ, mameva sīsaṃ mama uttamaṅgaṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Atthaṃ {pb:T:1.0230} karissa’’nti musā abhāṇiṃ {note:abhāsiṃ (ka.)}, ekāparādhaṃ khama rājaseṭṭha.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Daharo tuvaṃ dassaniyosi rāja, paṭhamuggato hosi {note:hohi (sī.), hoti (ka.)} yathā kaḷīro;
::

::gathalast
Rajjañca kārehi mamañca passa, mā kālikaṃ anudhāvī janinda.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Passāmi vohaṃ dahariṃ kumāriṃ, sāmaṭṭhapassaṃ sutanuṃ sumajjhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāḷappavāḷāva pavellamānā, palobhayantīva {note:sā lobhayantīva (pī.)} naresu gacchati.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Tamena passāmiparena nāriṃ, āsītikaṃ nāvutikaṃ va jaccā;
::

::gathalast
Daṇḍaṃ gahetvāna pavedhamānaṃ, gopānasībhoggasamaṃ carantiṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ tamevānuvicintayanto, eko sayāmi {note:passāmi (ka.)} sayanassa majjhe;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Ahampi evaṃ’’ iti pekkhamāno, na gahe rame {note:na gehe rame (sī.), gehe na rame (syā. ka.)} brahmacariyassa kālo.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Rajjuvālambanī {pb:M:1.0170} cesā, yā gehe vasato rati;
::

::gathalast
Evampi {pb:T:1.0231} chetvāna vajanti dhīrā, anapekkhino kāmasukhaṃ pahāyāti.
::

::centre
Susīmajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 412. Koṭasimbalijātakaṃ (7-2-7)

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ dasasataṃbyāmaṃ, uragamādāya āgato;
::

::gathalast
Tañca mañca mahākāyaṃ, dhārayaṃ nappavedhasi {note:na pavedhayi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Athimaṃ {pb:V:1.0140} khuddakaṃ pakkhiṃ, appamaṃsataraṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Dhārayaṃ byathasi {note:byādhase (sī.), byadhase (pī.), byādhasi (ka.)} bhītā {note:bhīto (sī. syā. pī.)}, kamatthaṃ koṭasimbali {note:koṭisimbali (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Maṃsabhakkho tuvaṃ rāja, phalabhakkho ayaṃ dijo;
::

::gatha2
Ayaṃ nigrodhabījāni, pilakkhudumbarāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Assatthāni ca bhakkhitvā, khandhe me ohadissati.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Te rukkhā saṃvirūhanti, mama passe nivātajā;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ pariyonandhissanti, arukkhaṃ maṃ karissare.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Santi aññepi rukkhā se, mūlino khandhino dumā;
::

::gathalast
Iminā sakuṇajātena, bījamāharitā hatā.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjhārūhābhivaḍḍhanti {note:ajjhārūḷhābhivaḍḍhanti (sī. pī.)}, brahantampi vanappatiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā rāja pavedhāmi, sampassaṃnāgataṃ bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkeyya saṅkitabbāni, rakkheyyānāgataṃ bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatabhayā {pb:T:1.0232} dhīro, ubho loke avekkhatīti.
::

::centre
Koṭasimbalijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 413. Dhūmakārijātakaṃ (7-2-8)

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Rājā apucchi vidhuraṃ, dhammakāmo yudhiṭṭhilo;
::

::gathalast
Api brāhmaṇa jānāsi, ko eko bahu socati.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Brāhmaṇo {pb:M:1.0171} ajayūthena, pahūtedho {note:bahūtejo (pī. ka.), bahutendo (syā.)} vane vasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhūmaṃ akāsi vāseṭṭho, rattindivamatandito.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa taṃ dhūmagandhena, sarabhā makasaḍḍitā {note:makasadditā (sī. syā.), makasaṭṭitā (pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Vassāvāsaṃ upāgacchuṃ, dhūmakārissa santike.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Sarabhesu manaṃ katvā, ajā so nāvabujjhatha;
::

::gathalast
Āgacchantī vajantī vā {note:āgacchanti vajanti vā (syā. pī.), āgacchantiṃ vajantiṃ vā (ka.)}, tassa tā vinasuṃ {note:vinassuṃ (sī.)} ajā.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Sarabhā sarade kāle, pahīnamakase vane;
::

::gathalast
Pāvisuṃ giriduggāni, nadīnaṃ pabhavāni ca.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Sarabhe ca gate disvā, ajā ca vibhavaṃ gatā {note:aje ca vibhavaṃ gate (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Kiso ca vivaṇṇo cāsi, paṇḍurogī ca brāhmaṇo.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0141} yo saṃ niraṃkatvā, āgantuṃ kurute piyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So eko bahu socati, dhūmakārīva brāhmaṇoti.
::

::centre
Dhūmakārijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 414. Jāgarajātakaṃ (7-2-9)

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Kodha {pb:T:1.0233} jāgarataṃ sutto, kodha suttesu jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Ko mametaṃ vijānāti, ko taṃ paṭibhaṇāti me.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ jāgarataṃ sutto, ahaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Ahametaṃ vijānāmi, ahaṃ paṭibhaṇāmi te.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ jāgarataṃ sutto, kathaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ etaṃ vijānāsi, kathaṃ paṭibhaṇāsi me.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Ye dhammaṃ nappajānanti, saṃyamoti damoti ca;
::

::gathalast
Tesu suppamānesu, ahaṃ jaggāmi devate.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
::

::gathalast
Tesu jāgaramānesu, ahaṃ suttosmi devate.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0172} jāgarataṃ sutto, evaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Evametaṃ vijānāmi, evaṃ paṭibhaṇāmi te.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu jāgarataṃ sutto, sādhu suttesu jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Sādhumetaṃ vijānāsi, sādhu paṭibhaṇāsi meti.
::

::centre
Jāgarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 415. Kummāsapiṇḍijātakaṃ (7-2-10)

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
Na kiratthi anomadassisu, pāricariyā buddhesu appikā {note:appakā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sukkhāya {pb:T:1.0234} aloṇikāya ca, passaphalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
Hatthigavassā cime bahū {note:hatthigavāssā ca me bahū (sī.), hatthī gavāssā cime bahū (syā.), hatthī gavāssā ca me bahū (pī.)}, dhanadhaññaṃ pathavī ca kevalā;
::

::gathalast
Nāriyo cimā accharūpamā, passaphalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
Abhikkhaṇaṃ rājakuñjara, gāthā bhāsasi kosalādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana, bāḷhaṃ pītimano pabhāsasi.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
Imasmiññeva nagare, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Parakammakaro āsiṃ, bhatako sīlasaṃvuto.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Kammāya {pb:V:1.0142} nikkhamantohaṃ, caturo samaṇeddasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ācārasīlasampanne, sītibhūte anāsave.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Tesu cittaṃ pasādetvā, nisīdetvā {note:nisādetvā (?)} paṇṇasanthate;
::

::gathalast
Adaṃ buddhāna kummāsaṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {pb:M:1.0173} kammassa kusalassa, idaṃ me edisaṃ phalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anubhomi idaṃ rajjaṃ, phītaṃ dharaṇimuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Dadaṃ bhuñja mā ca pamādo {note:dada bhuñja ca mā ca pamādo (sī. pī.)}, cakkaṃ vattaya kosalādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Mā {pb:T:1.0235} rāja adhammiko ahu, dhammaṃ pālaya kosalādhipa.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ tadeva punappunaṃ, vaṭumaṃ ācarissāmi sobhane;
::

::gathalast
Ariyācaritaṃ sukosale, arahanto me manāpāva passituṃ.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
Devī viya accharūpamā, majjhe nārigaṇassa sobhasi;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ kammamakāsi bhaddakaṃ, kenāsi vaṇṇavatī sukosale.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
Ambaṭṭhakulassa khattiya, dāsyāhaṃ parapesiyā ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saññatā ca {note:saññatā (sī. pī.)} dhammajīvinī, sīlavatī ca apāpadassanā.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
Uddhaṭabhattaṃ ahaṃ tadā, caramānassa adāsi bhikkhuno;
::

::gathalast
Vittā sumanā sayaṃ ahaṃ, tassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedisanti.
::

::centre
Kummāsapiṇḍijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

#### 416. Parantapajātakaṃ (7-2-11)

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
Āgamissati {pb:T:1.0236} me pāpaṃ, āgamissati me bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadā hi calitā sākhā, manussena migena vā.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
Bhīruyā nūna me kāmo, avidūre vasantiyā;
::

::gathalast
Karissati kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
Socayissati {pb:M:1.0174} maṃ kantā, gāme vasamaninditā;
::

::gathalast
Karissati kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1
Tayā maṃ asitāpaṅgi {note:hasitāpaṅgi (sī. syā. pī.)}, sitāni {note:mihitāni (sī. syā. pī.)} bhaṇitāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ karissanti, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
Agamā nūna so saddo, asaṃsi nūna so tava;
::

::gathalast
Akkhātaṃ nūna taṃ tena, yo taṃ sākhamakampayi.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ {pb:V:1.0143} kho taṃ samāgamma, mama bālassa cintitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadā hi calitā sākhā, manussena migena vā.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
Tatheva tvaṃ avedesi, avañci {note:avajjhi (ka.)} pitaraṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Hantvā sākhāhi chādento, āgamissati me {note:te (syā. ka.)} bhayanti.
::

::centre
Parantapajātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Gandhāravaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varagāma {pb:T:1.0237} mahākapi bhaggava ca, daḷhadhamma sakuñjara kesavaro;
::

::gathalast
Urago vidhuro puna jāgarataṃ, atha kosalādhipa parantapa cāti.
::

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Atha sattanipātamhi, vaggaṃ me bhaṇato suṇa;
::

::gathalast
Kukku ca puna gandhāro, dveva guttā mahesināti.
::

::centre
Sattakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

### 8. Aṭṭhakanipāto

#### 417. Kaccānijātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Odātavatthā {pb:T:1.0238}{pb:V:1.0144}{pb:M:1.0175} suci allakesā, kaccāni kiṃ kumbhimadhissayitvā {note:kumbhimapassayitvā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Piṭṭhā tilā dhovasi taṇḍulāni, tilodano hehiti kissa hetu.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Na kho ayaṃ brāhmaṇa bhojanatthā {note:bhojanatthaṃ (syā.)}, tilodano hehiti sādhupakko;
::

::gathalast
Dhammo mato tassa pahuttamajja {note:pahūnamajja (syā.), pahūtamajja (sī.), bahūtamajjā (pī.)}, ahaṃ karissāmi susānamajjhe.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Anuvicca kaccāni karohi kiccaṃ, dhammo mato ko nu taveva {note:taveta (sī. syā. pī.)} saṃsi;
::

::gathalast
Sahassanetto atulānubhāvo, na miyyatī dhammavaro kadāci.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Daḷhappamāṇaṃ mama ettha brahme, dhammo mato natthi mamettha kaṅkhā;
::

::gathalast
Ye yeva dāni pāpā bhavanti, te {pb:T:1.0239} teva dāni sukhitā bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇisā hi mayhaṃ vañjhā ahosi, sā maṃ vadhitvāna vijāyi puttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dāni sabbassa kulassa issarā, ahaṃ panamhi {note:vasāmi (syā.)} apaviddhā ekikā.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Jīvāmi {pb:M:1.0176} vohaṃ na matohamasmi {note:nāhaṃ matosmi (sī. pī.)}, taveva atthāya idhāgatosmi;
::

::gathalast
Yā taṃ vadhitvāna vijāyi puttaṃ, sahāva puttena karomi bhasmaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Evañca {note:etañca (sī. pī.)} te ruccati devarāja, mameva atthāya idhāgatosi;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca putto suṇisā ca nattā, sammodamānā gharamāvasema.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Evañca te ruccati kātiyāni, hatāpi santā na jahāsi dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tuvañca {note:tvañca (pī. ka.)} putto suṇisā ca nattā, sammodamānā gharamāvasetha.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Sā kātiyānī suṇisāya saddhiṃ, sammodamānā gharamāvasittha;
::

::gathalast
Putto {pb:T:1.0240} ca nattā ca upaṭṭhahiṃsu, devānamindena adhiggahītāti.
::

::centre
Kaccānijātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 418. Aṭṭhasaddajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ {pb:V:1.0145} pure ninnamāhu, bahumacchaṃ mahodakaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Āvāso bakarājassa, pettikaṃ bhavanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Tyajja bhekena {note:bhiṅgena (ka.)} yāpema, okaṃ na vajahāmase {note:okantaṃ na jahāmase (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Ko dutiyaṃ asīlissa, bandharassakkhi bhecchati {note:bhejjati (sī. syā. pī.), bhindati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ko me putte kulāvakaṃ, mañca sotthiṃ karissati.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbā parikkhayā pheggu, yāva tassā gatī ahu;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇabhakkho mahārāja, sāre na ramatī ghuṇo.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Sā {pb:M:1.0177} nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, rañño muttā nivesanā;
::

::gathalast
Attānaṃ ramayissāmi, dumasākhaniketinī.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
So nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, rañño mutto nivesanā;
::

::gathalast
Aggodakāni pissāmi, yūthassa purato vajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ maṃ kāmehi sammattaṃ, rattaṃ kāmesu mucchitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ānayī bharato {note:vanato (ka.)} luddo, bāhiko bhaddamatthu te.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Andhakāratimisāyaṃ, tuṅge uparipabbate;
::

::gathalast
Sā {pb:T:1.0241} maṃ saṇhena mudunā, mā pādaṃ khali {note:khaṇi (sī. syā. pī.)} yasmani.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Asaṃsayaṃ jātikhayantadassī, na gabbhaseyyaṃ punarāvajissaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ayamantimā pacchimā gabbhaseyyā {note:ayaṃ hi me antimā gabbhaseyyā (sī. pī.)}, khīṇo me saṃsāro punabbhavāyāti.
::

::centre
Aṭṭhasaddajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 419. Sulasājātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ suvaṇṇakāyūraṃ, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ harassu bhaddante, mañca dāsīti sāvaya.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Oropayassu kalyāṇi, mā bāḷhaṃ {note:bahuṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} paridevasi;
::

::gathalast
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, ahantvā dhanamābhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattāsmi viññutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi taṃ upagūhissaṃ {note:upaguyhissaṃ (ka.)}, karissañca padakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na hi dāni puna atthi, mama tuyhañca saṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0146} hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, tattha tattha vicakkhaṇā.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0178} hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Itthīpi {pb:T:1.0242} paṇḍitā hoti, lahuṃ atthaṃ vicintikā {note:lahumatthavicintikā (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Lahuñca vata khippañca, nikaṭṭhe samacetayi;
::

::gathalast
Migaṃ puṇṇāyateneva {note:puṇṇāyataneva (syā.)}, sulasā sattukaṃ vadhi.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Yodha uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
::

::gathalast
So haññati mandamati, corova girigabbhare.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
::

::gathalast
Muccate sattusambādhā, sulasā sattukāmivāti.
::

::centre
Sulasājātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 420. Sumaṅgalajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Bhusamhi {note:bhusampi (ka.), bhusaṃ hi (sī. niyya)} kuddhoti avekkhiyāna, na tāva daṇḍaṃ paṇayeyya issaro;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭhānaso appatirūpamattano, parassa dukkhāni bhusaṃ udīraye.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Yato ca jāneyya pasādamattano, atthaṃ niyuñjeyya parassa dukkaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tadāyamatthoti sayaṃ avekkhiya, athassa daṇḍaṃ sadisaṃ nivesaye.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Na cāpi jhāpeti paraṃ na attanaṃ, amucchito yo nayate nayānayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo {pb:T:1.0243} daṇḍadhāro bhavatīdha issaro, sa vaṇṇagutto siriyā na dhaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Ye khattiyā se anisammakārino, paṇenti daṇḍaṃ sahasā pamucchitā;
::

::gathalast
Avaṇṇasaṃyutā {note:yuttāva (ka.)} jahanti jīvitaṃ, ito vimuttāpi ca yanti duggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Dhamme {pb:M:1.0179} ca ye ariyappavedite ratā, anuttarā te vacasā manasā kammunā ca;
::

::gathalast
Te santisoraccasamādhisaṇṭhitā, vajanti lokaṃ dubhayaṃ tathāvidhā.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Rājāhamasmi narapamadānamissaro, sacepi kujjhāmi ṭhapemi attanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisedhayanto janataṃ tathāvidhaṃ, paṇemi daṇḍaṃ anukampa yoniso.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Sirī ca lakkhī ca taveva khattiya, janādhipa mā vijahi kudācanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akkodhano niccapasannacitto, anīgho tuvaṃ vassasatāni pālaya.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Guṇehi etehi upeta khattiya, ṭhitamariyavattī {note:vatti (sī.), vutti (ka.)} suvaco akodhano;
::

::gathalast
Sukhī {pb:T:1.0244} anuppīḷa pasāsamediniṃ {note:anuppīḷaṃ sahasamedaniṃ (ka.)}, ito vimuttopi ca yāhi suggatiṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0147} sunītena {note:suvinītena (pī.)} subhāsitena, dhammena ñāyena upāyaso nayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbāpaye saṅkhubhitaṃ mahājanaṃ, mahāva megho salilena medininti {note:medaninti (syā. ka.)}.
::

::centre
Sumaṅgalajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 421. Gaṅgamālajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Aṅgārajātā pathavī, kukkuḷānugatā mahī;
::

::gathalast
Atha gāyasi vattāni {note:vatthāni (ka.)}, na taṃ tapati ātapo.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Uddhaṃ tapati ādicco, adho tapati vālukā;
::

::gathalast
Atha gāyasi vattāni {note:vatthāni (ka.)}, na taṃ tapati ātapo.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0180} maṃ tapati ātapo, ātapā {note:ātappā (sī. syā. pī.)} tapayanti maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atthā hi vividhā rāja, te tapanti na ātapo.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Addasaṃ kāma te mūlaṃ, saṅkappā kāma jāyasi;
::

::gathalast
Na taṃ saṅkappayissāmi, evaṃ kāma na hehisi.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Appāpi kāmā na alaṃ, bahūhipi na tappati;
::

::gathalast
Ahahā bālalapanā, parivajjetha {note:paṭivijjhetha (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)} jaggato.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Appassa {pb:T:1.0245} kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ, udayo ajjhāgamā mahattapattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suladdhalābho vata māṇavassa, yo pabbajī kāmarāgaṃ pahāya.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Tapasā pajahanti pāpakammaṃ, tapasā nhāpitakumbhakārabhāvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tapasā abhibhuyya gaṅgamāla, nāmenālapasajja brahmadattaṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Sandiṭṭhikameva ‘‘amma’’ passatha, khantīsoraccassa ayaṃ {note:yo (syā. pī. ka.)} vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Yo {note:so (syā. ka.)} sabbajanassa vanditohu, taṃ vandāma sarājikā samaccā.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Mā kiñci avacuttha gaṅgamālaṃ, muninaṃ monapathesu sikkhamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Eso hi atari aṇṇavaṃ, yaṃ taritvā caranti vītasokāti.
::

::centre
Gaṅgamālajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 422. Cetiyajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo {pb:T:1.0246} have hato hanti, nāhato hanti kiñcanaṃ {note:kañcinaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi dhammaṃ na hane, mā tvaṃ {note:taṃ (syā. pī.)} dhammo hato hani.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Alikaṃ {pb:V:1.0148}{pb:M:1.0181} bhāsamānassa, apakkamanti devatā;
::

::gatha2
Pūtikañca mukhaṃ vāti, sakaṭṭhānā ca dhaṃsati;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhūmiyaṃ tiṭṭha cetiya.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Akāle vassatī tassa, kāle tassa na vassati;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhūmiṃ pavisa cetiya.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Jivhā tassa dvidhā hoti, uragasseva disampati;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Jivhā tassa na bhavati, macchasseva disampati;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Thiyova {pb:T:1.0247} tassa jāyanti {note:thiyo tassa pajāyanti (ka.)}, na pumā jāyare kule;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Puttā tassa na bhavanti, pakkamanti disodisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
::

::gathalast
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Sa {pb:M:1.0182} rājā isinā satto, antalikkhacaro pure;
::

::gathalast
Pāvekkhi pathaviṃ cecco, hīnatto patva pariyāyaṃ {note:attapariyāyaṃ (sī. syā.), pattapariyāyaṃ (ka. sī. niyya)}.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā {pb:V:1.0149} hi chandāgamanaṃ, nappasaṃsanti paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Aduṭṭhacitto bhāseyya, giraṃ saccūpasaṃhitanti.
::

::centre
Cetiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 423. Indriyajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Yo indriyānaṃ kāmena, vasaṃ nārada gacchati;
::

::gathalast
So pariccajjubho loke, jīvantova visussati {note:jīvantopivisussati (syā.), jīvanto vāpi sussati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhassānantaraṃ dukkhaṃ, dukkhassānantaraṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sosi {note:sopi (syā. pī. ka.)} patto sukhā {note:sukha (syā.), sukhaṃ (ka.)} dukkhaṃ, pāṭikaṅkha varaṃ sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Kicchakāle {pb:T:1.0248} kicchasaho, yo kicchaṃ nātivattati;
::

::gathalast
Sa kicchantaṃ sukhaṃ dhīro, yogaṃ samadhigacchati.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva kāmāna kāmā, nānatthā nātthakāraṇā;
::

::gathalast
Na katañca niraṅkatvā, dhammā cavitumarahasi.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Dakkhaṃ gahapatī {note:gahapataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), gahavataṃ (?)} sādhu, saṃvibhajjañca bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahāso atthalābhesu, atthabyāpatti abyatho.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Ettāvatetaṃ paṇḍiccaṃ, api so {note:asito (sī. syā. pī.)} davilo {note:devalo (sī. pī.)} bravi;
::

::gathalast
Na yito kiñci pāpiyo, yo indriyānaṃ vasaṃ vaje.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Amittānaṃva hatthatthaṃ, sivi pappoti māmiva;
::

::gatha2
Kammaṃ vijjañca dakkheyyaṃ, vivāhaṃ sīlamaddavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ete ca yase hāpetvā, nibbatto sehi kammehi.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ sahassajīnova abandhu aparāyaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Ariyadhammā apakkanto, yathā peto tathevahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhakāme {pb:M:1.0183} dukkhāpetvā, āpannosmi padaṃ imaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So sukhaṃ nādhigacchāmi, ṭhito {note:cito (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)} bhāṇumatāmivāti.
::

::centre
Indriyajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 424. Ādittajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittasmiṃ agārasmiṃ, yaṃ nīharati bhājanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0249} tassa hoti atthāya, no ca yaṃ tattha ḍayhati.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Evāmādīpito {pb:V:1.0150} loko, jarāya maraṇena ca;
::

::gathalast
Nīharetheva dānena, dinnaṃ hoti sunīhataṃ {note:sunībhataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), sunibbhataṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Yo dhammaladdhassa dadāti dānaṃ, uṭṭhānavīriyādhigatassa jantu;
::

::gathalast
Atikkamma so vetaraṇiṃ {note:vettaraṇiṃ (ka.)} yamassa, dibbāni ṭhānāni upeti macco.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Dānañca yuddhañca samānamāhu, appāpi santā bahuke jinanti;
::

::gathalast
Appampi ce saddahāno dadāti, teneva so hoti sukhī parattha.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Viceyya dānaṃ sugatappasatthaṃ, ye dakkhiṇeyyā idha jīvaloke;
::

::gathalast
Etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni, bījāni vuttāni yathā sukhette.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Yo pāṇabhūtāni aheṭhayaṃ caraṃ, parūpavādā na karoti pāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhīruṃ pasaṃsanti na tattha sūraṃ, bhayā hi santo na karonti pāpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Hīnena brahmacariyena, khattiye upapajjati;
::

::gathalast
Majjhimena {pb:T:1.0250} ca devattaṃ, uttamena visujjhati.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā {pb:M:1.0184} hi dānaṃ bahudhā pasatthaṃ, dānā ca kho dhammapadaṃva seyyo;
::

::gathalast
Pubbeva hi pubbatareva santo {note:pubbe ca hi pubbatare ca santo (saṃ. ni. 1.33)}, nibbānamevajjhagamuṃ sapaññāti.
::

::centre
Ādittajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 425. Aṭṭhānajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Gaṅgā kumudinī santā, saṅkhavaṇṇā ca kokilā;
::

::gathalast
Jambu tālaphalaṃ dajjā, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā kacchapalomānaṃ, pāvāro tividho siyā;
::

::gathalast
Hemantikaṃ pāvuraṇaṃ {note:pāpuraṇaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā makasapādānaṃ {note:dāṭhānaṃ (sī. pī.)}, aṭṭālo sukato siyā;
::

::gathalast
Daḷho ca avikampī ca {note:appakampī ca (sī. pī.)}, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā sasavisāṇānaṃ, nisseṇī sukatā siyā;
::

::gathalast
Saggassārohaṇatthāya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā nisseṇimāruyha, candaṃ khādeyyu mūsikā;
::

::gathalast
Rāhuñca paripāteyyuṃ {note:paribāheyyuṃ (syā.)}, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā surāghaṭaṃ pitvā, makkhikā gaṇacāriṇī;
::

::gathalast
Aṅgāre {pb:T:1.0251} vāsaṃ kappeyyuṃ, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā {pb:V:1.0151} bimboṭṭhasampanno, gadrabho sumukho siyā;
::

::gathalast
Kusalo naccagītassa, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā kākā ulūkā ca, mantayeyyuṃ rahogatā;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññaṃ pihayeyyuṃ, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā muḷāla {note:pulasa (sī. pī.), pulāsa (syā.)} pattānaṃ, chattaṃ thirataraṃ siyā;
::

::gathalast
Vassassa paṭighātāya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā {pb:M:1.0185} kulako {note:kuluṅko (sī. pī.), kuluko (syā.)} sakuṇo, pabbataṃ gandhamādanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tuṇḍenādāya gaccheyya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā sāmuddikaṃ nāvaṃ, sa-yantaṃ sa-vaṭākaraṃ {note:sapaṭākāraṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ceṭo ādāya gaccheyya, atha nūna tadā siyāti.
::

::centre
Aṭṭhānajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 426. Dīpijātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Khamanīyaṃ yāpanīyaṃ, kacci mātula te sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sukhaṃ te ammā avaca, sukhakāmāva {note:sukhakāmā hi (sī. syā. pī.)} te mayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Naṅguṭṭhaṃ me avakkamma {note:apakkamma (ka.)}, heṭhayitvāna {note:pothayitvāna (ka.)} eḷike {note:eḷaki (syā.), eḷiki (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sājja mātulavādena, muñcitabbā nu maññasi.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Puratthāmukho nisinnosi, ahaṃ te mukhamāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Pacchato tuyhaṃ naṅguṭṭhaṃ, kathaṃ khvāhaṃ avakkamiṃ {note:apakkamiṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Yāvatā {pb:T:1.0252} caturo dīpā, sasamuddā sapabbatā;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatā mayhaṃ naṅguṭṭhaṃ, kathaṃ kho tvaṃ vivajjayi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbeva metamakkhiṃsu {note:metaṃ akkhaṃsu (sī. pī.)}, mātā pitā ca bhātaro;
::

::gathalast
Dīghaṃ duṭṭhassa naṅguṭṭhaṃ, sāmhi vehāyasāgatā.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ, antalikkhasmi eḷike;
::

::gathalast
Migasaṅgho palāyittha, bhakkho me nāsito tayā.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Iccevaṃ vilapantiyā, eḷakiyā ruhagghaso;
::

::gathalast
Galakaṃ anvāvamaddi, natthi duṭṭhe subhāsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Neva {pb:V:1.0152}{pb:M:1.0186} duṭṭhe nayo atthi, na dhammo na subhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nikkamaṃ duṭṭhe yuñjetha, so ca sabbhiṃ na rañjatīti.
::

::centre
Dīpijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Aṭṭhakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Parisuddhā manāvilā vatthadharā, bakarājassa kāyuraṃ daṇḍavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha aṅgāra cetiya devilinā, atha āditta gaṅgā daseḷakināti.
::

### 9. Navakanipāto

#### 427. Gijjhajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Parisaṅkupatho {pb:T:1.0253}{pb:V:1.0153}{pb:M:1.0187} nāma, gijjhapantho sanantano;
::

::gatha2
Tatrāsi mātāpitaro, gijjho posesi jiṇṇake;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ ajagaramedaṃ, accahāsi bahuttaso {note:pahuttato (ka. sī.), pahūtaso (syā. pī.), bahudhaso (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Pitā ca puttaṃ avaca, jānaṃ uccaṃ papātinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Supattaṃ thāmasampannaṃ {note:pakkhasampannaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, tejassiṃ dūragāminaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Pariplavantaṃ pathaviṃ, yadā tāta vijānahi;
::

::gatha2
Sāgarena parikkhittaṃ, cakkaṃva parimaṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato tāta nivattassu, māssu etto paraṃ gami.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Udapattosi {note:uddhaṃ pattosi (ka. sī.)} vegena, balī pakkhī dijuttamo;
::

::gathalast
Olokayanto vakkaṅgo, pabbatāni vanāni ca.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Addassa pathaviṃ gijjho, yathāsāsi {note:yathāssāsi (syā. aṭṭha. pāṭhantaraṃ)} pitussutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāgarena parikkhittaṃ, cakkaṃva parimaṇḍalaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Tañca so samatikkamma, paramevaccavattatha {note:parameva pavattatha (sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Tañca vātasikhā tikkhā, accahāsi baliṃ dijaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Nāsakkhātigato poso, punadeva nivattituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dijo byasanamāpādi, verambhānaṃ {note:verambānaṃ (sī. pī.)} vasaṃ gato.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {pb:T:1.0254} puttā ca dārā ca, ye caññe anujīvino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe byasanamāpāduṃ, anovādakare dije.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi idha vuḍḍhānaṃ, yo vākyaṃ nāvabujjhati;
::

::gatha2
Atisīmacaro ditto, gijjhovātītasāsano;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve byasanaṃ pappoti, akatvā vuḍḍhasāsananti.
::

::centre
Gijjhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 428. Kosambiyajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Puthusaddo {pb:V:1.0154}{pb:M:1.0188} samajano, na bālo koci maññatha;
::

::gathalast
Saṅghasmiṃ bhijjamānasmiṃ, nāññaṃ bhiyyo amaññaruṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Parimuṭṭhā paṇḍitābhāsā, vācāgocarabhāṇino;
::

::gathalast
Yāvicchanti mukhāyāmaṃ, yena nītā na taṃ vidū.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca taṃ upanayhanti, veraṃ tesaṃ na sammati.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca taṃ nupanayhanti, veraṃ tesūpasammati.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi verena verāni, sammantīdha kudācanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Averena ca sammanti, esa dhammo sanantano.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Pare ca na vijānanti, mayamettha yamāmase;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca tattha vijānanti, tato sammanti medhagā.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhicchinnā {pb:T:1.0255} pāṇaharā, gavassa {note:gavāssa (sī. syā. pī.)} dhanahārino;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhaṃ vilumpamānānaṃ, tesampi hoti saṅgati;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā tumhāka no siyā.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhibhuyya sabbāni parissayāni, careyya tenattamano satīmā.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
No ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya, eko care mātaṅgaraññeva nāgo.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Ekassa {pb:M:1.0189} caritaṃ seyyo, natthi bāle sahāyatā;
::

::gathalast
Eko care na pāpāni kayirā, appossukko mātaṅgaraññeva nāgoti.
::

::centre
Kosambiyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 429. Mahāsuvajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Dumo yadā hoti phalūpapanno, bhuñjanti naṃ vihaṅgamā {note:vihagā (sī. pī.)} sampatantā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇanti ñatvāna dumaṃ phalaccaye {note:ñatvā dumapphalaccayena (ka.)}, disodisaṃ {pb:T:1.0256} yanti tato vihaṅgamā.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Cara cārikaṃ lohitatuṇḍa māmari, kiṃ tvaṃ suva sukkhadumamhi jhāyasi;
::

::gathalast
Tadiṅgha maṃ brūhi vasantasannibha, kasmā suva sukkhadumaṃ na riñcasi.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:V:1.0155} ve sakhīnaṃ sakhāro bhavanti, pāṇaccaye {note:pāṇaṃ caje (ka.), pāṇaccaye maraṇakāle ca sukhadukkhesu ca na jahantīti sambandho} dukkhasukhesu haṃsa;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇaṃ akhīṇanti na taṃ jahanti, santo sataṃ dhammamanussarantā.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ sataṃ aññatarosmi haṃsa, ñātī ca me hoti sakhā ca rukkho;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ nussahe jīvikattho pahātuṃ, khīṇanti ñatvāna na hesa dhammo {note:na sosa (ka.), na esa (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu sakkhi kataṃ hoti, metti saṃsati santhavo {note:mittaṃ saṅgati sandhavo (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sacetaṃ dhammaṃ rocesi, pāsaṃsosi vijānataṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
So te suva varaṃ dammi, pattayāna vihaṅgama;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ varassu vakkaṅga, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Varañca {pb:M:1.0190} me haṃsa bhavaṃ dadeyya, ayañca rukkho punarāyuṃ labhetha;
::

::gathalast
So {pb:T:1.0257} sākhavā phalimā saṃvirūḷho, madhutthiko tiṭṭhatu sobhamāno.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ passa samma phalimaṃ uḷāraṃ, sahāva te hotu udumbarena;
::

::gathalast
So sākhavā phalimā saṃvirūḷho, madhutthiko tiṭṭhatu sobhamāno.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ sakka sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja sukhito, disvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Suvassa ca varaṃ datvā, katvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pakkāmi saha bhariyāya, devānaṃ nandanaṃ vananti.
::

::centre
Mahāsuvajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 430. Cūḷasuvajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Santi rukkhā haripattā {note:haritapattā (sī. syā. pī.)}, dumā nekaphalā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā nu sukkhe {note:sukkha (ka.)} koḷāpe, suvassa nirato mano.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Phalassa upabhuñjimhā, nekavassagaṇe bahū;
::

::gathalast
Aphalampi viditvāna, sāva metti yathā pure.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhañca rukkhaṃ koḷāpaṃ, opattamaphalaṃ dumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ohāya sakuṇā yanti, kiṃ dosaṃ passase dija.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:T:1.0258} phalatthā sambhajanti, aphaloti jahanti naṃ;
::

::gathalast
Attatthapaññā dummedhā, te honti pakkhapātino.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu sakkhi kataṃ hoti, metti saṃsati santhavo;
::

::gathalast
Sacetaṃ dhammaṃ rocesi, pāsaṃsosi vijānataṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:V:1.0156} te suva varaṃ dammi, pattayāna vihaṅgama;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ varassu vakkaṅga, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Api {pb:M:1.0191} nāma naṃ passeyyaṃ {note:api nāma naṃ puna passe (sī. syā.)}, sapattaṃ saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Daliddova nidhi laddhā, nandeyyāhaṃ punappunaṃ.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Tato amatamādāya, abhisiñci mahīruhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa sākhā virūhiṃsu {note:virūḷhassa (ka.)}, sītacchāyā manoramā.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ sakka sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja sukhito, disvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Suvassa ca varaṃ datvā, katvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pakkāmi saha bhariyāya, devānaṃ nandanaṃ vananti.
::

::centre
Cūḷasuvajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 431. Haritacajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Sutaṃ metaṃ mahābrahme, kāme bhuñjati hārito;
::

Kaccetaṃ vacanaṃ tucchaṃ, kacci suddho iriyyasi.

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Evametaṃ mahārāja, yathā te vacanaṃ sutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kummaggaṃ {pb:T:1.0259} paṭipannosmi, mohaneyyesu mucchito.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Adu {note:ādu (sī. pī.)} paññā kimatthiyā, nipuṇā sādhucintinī {note:cintanī (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yāya uppatitaṃ rāgaṃ, kiṃ mano na vinodaye.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Cattārome mahārāja, loke atibalā bhusā;
::

::gathalast
Rāgo doso mado moho, yattha paññā na gādhati.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Arahā sīlasampanno, suddho carati hārito;
::

::gathalast
Medhāvī paṇḍito ceva, iti no sammato bhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Medhāvīnampi hiṃsanti, isiṃ dhammaguṇe rataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vitakkā pāpakā rāja, subhā rāgūpasaṃhitā.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Uppannāyaṃ {pb:M:1.0192} sarīrajo, rāgo vaṇṇavidūsano tava;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ pajaha bhaddamatthu te, bahunnāsi medhāvisammato.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Te andhakārake {note:karaṇe (sī. syā. pī.)} kāme, bahudukkhe mahāvise;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ mūlaṃ gavesissaṃ, checchaṃ rāgaṃ sabandhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ {pb:V:1.0157} vatvāna hārito, isi saccaparakkamo;
::

::gathalast
Kāmarāgaṃ virājetvā, brahmalokūpago ahūti.
::

::centre
Haritacajātakaṃ {note:hāritajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)} pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 432. Padakusalamāṇavajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Bahussutaṃ cittakathiṃ {note:cittakathaṃ (syā. ka.)}, gaṅgā vahati pāṭaliṃ {note:pāṭalaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Vuyhamānaka {pb:T:1.0260} bhaddante, ekaṃ me dehi gāthakaṃ {note:gītakaṃ (ka. aṭṭha.)}.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Yena siñcanti dukkhitaṃ, yena siñcanti āturaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa majjhe marissāmi, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Yattha bījāni rūhanti, sattā yattha patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Sā me sīsaṃ nipīḷeti, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Yena bhattāni paccanti, sītaṃ yena vihaññati;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ ḍahati {note:dayhati (ka.)} gattāni, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Yena bhuttena {note:bhattena (syā. ka.)} yāpenti, puthū brāhmaṇakhattiyā;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ bhutto byāpādeti, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Gimhānaṃ pacchime māse, vātamicchanti paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ {note:so me (sī. pī.)} bhañjati gattāni, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nissitā jagatiruhaṃ, svāyaṃ aggiṃ pamuñcati;
::

::gathalast
Disā bhajatha vakkaṅgā, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yamānayiṃ {pb:M:1.0193} somanassaṃ, māliniṃ candanussadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā maṃ gharā nicchubhati {note:nīharati (sī. syā.)}, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Yena jātena nandissaṃ, yassa ca bhavamicchisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ gharā nicchubhati {note:nīharati (sī. syā.)}, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇantu me jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Yatodakaṃ tadādittaṃ, yato khemaṃ tato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Rājā {pb:T:1.0261} vilumpate raṭṭhaṃ, brāhmaṇo ca purohito;
::

::gathalast
Attaguttā viharatha, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayanti.
::

::centre
Padakusalamāṇavajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 433. Lomasakassapajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Assa {pb:V:1.0158} indasamo rāja, accantaṃ ajarāmaro;
::

::gathalast
Sace tvaṃ yaññaṃ yājeyya, isiṃ lomasakassapaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ, mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na icche saha nindāya, evaṃ seyya {note:sayha (sī. syā. pī.)} vijānahi.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vā.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
::

::gathalast
Sāyeva jīvikā seyyo, yā cādhammena esanā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ ahiṃsayaṃ loke, api rajjena taṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Balaṃ cando balaṃ suriyo, balaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Balaṃ velā samuddassa, balātibalamitthiyo.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā uggatapaṃ santaṃ, isiṃ lomasakassapaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pitu atthā candavatī, vājapeyyaṃ {note:vācapeyyaṃ (pī. ka.)} ayājayi.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ lobhapakataṃ kammaṃ, kaṭukaṃ kāmahetukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa {pb:T:1.0262} mūlaṃ gavesissaṃ, checchaṃ rāgaṃ sabandhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu {pb:M:1.0194} kāme subahūpi loke, tapova seyyo kāmaguṇehi rāja;
::

::gathalast
Tapo karissāmi pahāya kāme, taveva raṭṭhaṃ candavatī ca hotūti.
::

::centre
Lomasakassapajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 434. Cakkavākajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Kāsāyavatthe sakuṇe vadāmi, duve duve nandamane {note:nandimane (sī. pī.)} carante;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ aṇḍajaṃ aṇḍajā mānusesu, jātiṃ pasaṃsanti tadiṅgha brūtha.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Amhe manussesu manussahiṃsa, anubbate {note:anupubbake (ka.)} cakkavāke vadanti;
::

::gathalast
Kalyāṇabhāvamhe {note:bhāva’mha (sī. pī.)} dijesu sammatā, abhirūpā {note:abhītarūpā (sī. syā. pī.)} vicarāma aṇṇave. ( ) {note:(na ghāsahetūpi karoma pāpaṃ) (ka.)}
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ aṇṇave kāni phalāni bhuñje, maṃsaṃ kuto khādatha cakkavākā;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ bhojanaṃ bhuñjatha vo anomā {note:abhiṇhaṃ (ka.)}, balañca {pb:T:1.0263} vaṇṇo ca anapparūpā {note:anapparūpo (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0159} aṇṇave santi phalāni dhaṅka, maṃsaṃ kuto khādituṃ cakkavāke;
::

::gathalast
Sevālabhakkhamha {note:bhakkhimha (ka.)} apāṇabhojanā {note:avākabhojanā (sī. pī.)}, na ghāsahetūpi karoma pāpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Na me idaṃ ruccati cakkavāka, asmiṃ bhave bhojanasannikāso;
::

::gathalast
Ahosi pubbe tato me aññathā, icceva me vimati ettha jātā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Ahampi {pb:M:1.0195} maṃsāni phalāni bhuñje, annāni ca loṇiyateliyāni;
::

::gatha2
Rasaṃ manussesu labhāmi bhottuṃ, sūrova saṅgāmamukhaṃ vijetvā;
::

::gathalast
Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo, cakkavāka yathā tava.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Asuddhabhakkhosi khaṇānupātī, kicchena te labbhati annapānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tussasī rukkhaphalehi dhaṅka, maṃsāni vā yāni susānamajjhe.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Yo sāhasena adhigamma bhoge, paribhuñjati {pb:T:1.0264} dhaṅka khaṇānupātī;
::

::gathalast
Tato upakkosati naṃ sabhāvo, upakkuṭṭho vaṇṇabalaṃ jahāti.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Appampi ce nibbutiṃ bhuñjatī yadi, asāhasena aparūpaghātī {note:asāhasenānupaghātino (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Balañca vaṇṇo ca tadassa hoti, na hi sabbo āhāramayena vaṇṇoti.
::

::centre
Cakkavākajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 435. Haliddirāgajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Sutitikkhaṃ araññamhi, pantamhi sayanāsane;
::

::gathalast
Ye ca gāme titikkhanti, te uḷāratarā tayā.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Araññā gāmamāgamma, kiṃsīlaṃ kiṃvataṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Purisaṃ tāta seveyyaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Yo te {note:yo taṃ (syā. jā. 1.4.190 araññajātakepi)} vissāsaye tāta, vissāsañca khameyya te;
::

::gathalast
Sussūsī ca titikkhī ca, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa {pb:M:1.0196} kāyena vācāya, manasā natthi dukkaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Urasīva patiṭṭhāya, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca dhammena carati, carantopi na maññati;
::

::gathalast
Visuddhakāriṃ sappaññaṃ, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Haliddirāgaṃ {pb:T:1.0265} kapicittaṃ, purisaṃ rāgavirāginaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tādisaṃ tāta mā sevi, nimmanussampi ce siyā.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Āsīvisaṃva kupitaṃ, mīḷhalittaṃ mahāpathaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārakā parivajjehi, yānīva visamaṃ pathaṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Anatthā {pb:V:1.0160} tāta vaḍḍhanti, bālaṃ accupasevato;
::

::gathalast
Māssu bālena saṃgacchi, amitteneva sabbadā.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tāhaṃ tāta yācāmi, karassu vacanaṃ mama;
::

::gathalast
Māssu bālena saṃgacchi {note:saṃgañchi (sī. pī.)}, dukkho bālehi saṅgamoti.
::

::centre
Haliddirāgajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 436. Samuggajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Kuto nu āgacchatha bho tayo janā, svāgatā etha {note:svāgataṃ ettha (sī. pī.)} nisīdathāsane;
::

::gathalast
Kaccittha bhonto kusalaṃ anāmayaṃ, cirassamabbhāgamanaṃ hi vo idha.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Ahameva eko idha majja patto, na cāpi me dutiyo koci vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva sandhāya te bhāsitaṃ ise, ‘‘kuto nu āgacchatha bho tayo janā’’.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Tuvañca eko bhariyā ca te piyā, samuggapakkhittanikiṇṇamantare{pb:T:1.0266};
::

::gathalast
Sā rakkhitā kucchigatāva {note:kucchigatā ca (ka.)} te sadā, vāyussa {note:harissa (ka.)} puttena sahā tahiṃ ratā.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃviggarūpo {pb:M:1.0197} isinā viyākato {note:pabyākato (ka.), byākato (syā. pī.)}, so dānavo tattha samuggamuggili;
::

::gathalast
Addakkhi bhariyaṃ suci māladhāriniṃ, vāyussa puttena sahā tahiṃ rataṃ.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Sudiṭṭharūpamuggatapānuvattinā {note:sudiṭṭharūpuggatapānuvattinā (sī. syā. pī.)}, hīnā narā ye pamadāvasaṃ gatā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā have pāṇarivettha rakkhitā, duṭṭhā mayī aññamabhippamodayi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Divā ca ratto ca mayā upaṭṭhitā, tapassinā jotirivā vane vasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dhammamukkamma adhammamācari, akiriyarūpo pamadāhi santhavo.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Sarīramajjhamhi ṭhitātimaññahaṃ, mayhaṃ ayanti asatiṃ asaññataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dhammamukkamma adhammamācari, akiriyarūpo pamadāhi santhavo.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Surakkhitaṃ {pb:T:1.0267} meti kathaṃ nu vissase, anekacittāsu na hatthi {note:anekacittā puna hettha (ka.)} rakkhaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Etā hi pātālapapātasannibhā, etthappamatto byasanaṃ nigacchati.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā hi te sukhino vītasokā, ye mātugāmehi caranti nissaṭā;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ sivaṃ uttamamābhipatthayaṃ, na mātugāmehi kareyya santhavanti.
::

::centre
Samuggajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

#### 437. Pūtimaṃsajātakaṃ (11)

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0198} kho me ruccati āḷi, pūtimaṃsassa pekkhanā;
::

::gathalast
Etādisā sakhārasmā, ārakā parivajjaye.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Ummattikā {pb:V:1.0161} ayaṃ veṇī, vaṇṇeti patino sakhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pajjhāyi {note:pajjhāti (sī. pī.), pajjhāyati (sī. niyya)} paṭigacchantiṃ, āgataṃ meṇḍa {note:meḷa (sī. pī.)} mātaraṃ.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Tvaṃ khosi samma ummatto, dummedho avicakkhaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Yo tvaṃ {note:so tvaṃ (syā.)} matālayaṃ katvā, akālena vipekkhasi.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Na akāle vipekkheyya, kāle pekkheyya paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Pūtimaṃsova pajjhāyi {note:pajjhāti (sī. pī.), pajjhāyati (sī. niyya)}, yo akāle vipekkhati.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Piyaṃ kho āḷi me hotu, puṇṇapattaṃ dadāhi me;
::

::gathalast
Pati {pb:T:1.0268} sañjīvito mayhaṃ, eyyāsi piyapucchikā {note:pucchitā (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Piyaṃ kho āḷi te hotu, puṇṇapattaṃ dadāmi te;
::

::gathalast
Mahatā parivārena {note:parihārena (syā.)}, essaṃ {note:esaṃ (sī. pī.)} kayirāhi {note:kayirāsi (pī.)} bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Kīdiso tuyhaṃ parivāro, yesaṃ kāhāmi bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃnāmakā ca te sabbe, taṃ {note:te (sī. syā. pī.)} me akkhāhi pucchitā.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Māliyo caturakkho ca, piṅgiyo atha jambuko;
::

::gathalast
Ediso mayhaṃ parivāro, tesaṃ kayirāhi {note:kayirāsi (pī.)} bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Nikkhantāya agārasmā, bhaṇḍakampi vinassati;
::

::gathalast
Ārogyaṃ āḷino vajjaṃ {note:vacchaṃ (?)}, idheva vasa māgamāti.
::

::centre
Pūtimaṃsajātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.
::

#### 438. Daddarajātakaṃ (12)

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Yo te puttake akhādi, dinnabhatto adūsake;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ dāṭhaṃ nipātehi, mā te muccittha jīvato.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Ākiṇṇaluddo {pb:M:1.0199} puriso, dhāticelaṃva makkhito;
::

::gathalast
Padesaṃ taṃ na passāmi, yattha dāṭhaṃ nipātaye.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Akataññussa posassa, niccaṃ vivaradassino;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ ce pathaviṃ dajjā, neva naṃ abhirādhaye.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Kinnu subāhu taramānarūpo, paccāgatosi saha māṇavena;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ {pb:T:1.0269} kiccamatthaṃ idhamatthi tuyhaṃ, akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Yo te sakhā daddaro sādhurūpo, tassa vadhaṃ parisaṅkāmi ajja;
::

::gathalast
Purisassa kammāyatanāni sutvā, nāhaṃ sukhiṃ daddaraṃ ajja maññe.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Kānissa {pb:V:1.0162} kammāyatanāni assu, purisassa vuttisamodhānatāya;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ vā paṭiññaṃ purisassa sutvā, parisaṅkasi daddaraṃ māṇavena.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Ciṇṇā kaliṅgā caritā vaṇijjā, vettācaro saṅkupathopi ciṇṇo;
::

::gathalast
Naṭehi ciṇṇaṃ saha vākurehi {note:vākarehi (pī. sī. niyya), vāgurehi (?)}, daṇḍena yuddhampi samajjamajjhe.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Baddhā kulīkā {note:kuliṅkā (sī. pī.)} mitamāḷhakena, akkhā jitā {note:akkhācitā (sī. aṭṭha.)} saṃyamo abbhatīto;
::

::gathalast
Abbāhitaṃ {note:appahitaṃ (sī. syā.), abbūhitaṃ (pī. sī. niyya)} pubbakaṃ {note:pupphakaṃ (sī. syā.)} aḍḍharattaṃ, hatthā daḍḍhā piṇḍapaṭiggahena.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Tānissa {pb:M:1.0200} kammāyatanāni assu, purisassa {pb:T:1.0270} vuttisamodhānatāya;
::

::gathalast
Yathā ayaṃ dissati lomapiṇḍo, gāvo hatā kiṃ pana daddarassāti.
::

::centre
Daddarajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Navakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Varagijjha samajjana haṃsavaro, nidhisavhaya hārita pāṭaliko;
::

::gathalast
Ajarāmara dhaṅka titikkha kuto, atha dvādasa pekkhana daddaribhīti.
::

### 10. Dasakanipāto

#### 439. Catudvārajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Catudvāramidaṃ {pb:T:1.0271}{pb:V:1.0163}{pb:M:1.0201} nagaraṃ, āyasaṃ daḷhapākāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Oruddhapaṭiruddhosmi, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbe apihitā dvārā, oruddhosmi yathā dijo;
::

::gathalast
Kimādhikaraṇaṃ yakkha, cakkābhinihato ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Laddhā satasahassāni, atirekāni vīsati;
::

::gathalast
Anukampakānaṃ ñātīnaṃ, vacanaṃ samma nākari.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Laṅghiṃ samuddaṃ pakkhandi, sāgaraṃ appasiddhikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Catubbhi aṭṭhajjhagamā, aṭṭhāhipi ca soḷasa.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Soḷasāhi ca bāttiṃsa, atricchaṃ cakkamāsado;
::

Icchāhatassa posassa, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Uparivisālā duppūrā, icchā visaṭagāminī {note:visaṭagāminiṃ (pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ye ca taṃ anugijjhanti, te honti cakkadhārino.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Bahubhaṇḍaṃ {note:bahuṃ bhaṇḍaṃ (sī. pī.)} avahāya, maggaṃ appaṭivekkhiya;
::

::gathalast
Yesañcetaṃ asaṅkhātaṃ, te honti cakkadhārino.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Kammaṃ samekkhe vipulañca bhogaṃ, icchaṃ {pb:T:1.0272} na seveyya anatthasaṃhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kareyya vākyaṃ anukampakānaṃ, taṃ tādisaṃ nātivatteyya cakkaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Kīvaciraṃ nu me yakkha, cakkaṃ sirasi ṭhassati;
::

::gathalast
Kati vassasahassāni, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Atisaro paccasaro {note:accasaro (sī. syā. pī.)}, mittavinda suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Cakkaṃ te sirasi {note:sirasmi (syā.)} māviddhaṃ, na taṃ jīvaṃ pamokkhasīti.
::

::centre
Catudvārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 440. Kaṇhajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Kaṇho {pb:V:1.0164}{pb:M:1.0202} vatāyaṃ puriso, kaṇhaṃ bhuñjati bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaṇhe bhūmipadesasmiṃ, na mayhaṃ manaso piyo.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Na kaṇho tacasā hoti, antosāro hi brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Yasmiṃ pāpāni kammāni, sa ve kaṇho sujampati.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Varañce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Sunikkodhaṃ suniddosaṃ, nillobhaṃ vuttimattano;
::

::gathalast
Nisnehamabhikaṅkhāmi, ete me caturo vare.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu kodhe vā {note:kodheva (sī. pī.)} dose vā, lobhe snehe ca brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ {pb:T:1.0273} tvaṃ passasi {note:sampassasi (sī. pī.)}, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Appo hutvā bahu hoti, vaḍḍhate so akhantijo;
::

::gathalast
Āsaṅgī bahupāyāso, tasmā kodhaṃ na rocaye.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Duṭṭhassa pharusā {note:paṭhamā (pī. sī. niyya)} vācā, parāmāso anantarā;
::

::gatha2
Tato pāṇi tato daṇḍo, satthassa paramā gati {note:parāmasati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Doso kodhasamuṭṭhāno, tasmā dosaṃ na rocaye.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Ālopasāhasākārā {note:sahasākārā (sī. syā. pī.)}, nikatī vañcanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Dissanti lobhadhammesu, tasmā lobhaṃ na rocaye.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Snehasaṅgathitā {note:saṅgadhitā (ka.), saṅgantitā (syā.)} ganthā, senti manomayā puthū;
::

::gathalast
Te bhusaṃ upatāpenti, tasmā snehaṃ na rocaye.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Varañce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Araññe me viharato, niccaṃ ekavihārino;
::

::gathalast
Ābādhā mā {note:na (syā. pī.)} uppajjeyyuṃ, antarāyakarā bhusā.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ {pb:M:1.0203} te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Varañce {pb:V:1.0165} me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Na mano vā sarīraṃ vā, maṃ-kate sakka kassaci;
::

::gathalast
Kadāci {pb:T:1.0274} upahaññetha, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vareti.
::

::centre
Kaṇhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 441. Catuposathiyajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Yo kopaneyye na karoti kopaṃ, na kujjhati sappuriso kadāci;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhopi so nāvikaroti kopaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu {note:samaṇaṃ āhu (sī.)} loke.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Ūnūdaro yo sahate jighacchaṃ, danto tapassī mitapānabhojano;
::

::gathalast
Āhārahetu na karoti pāpaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ vippajahitvāna sabbaṃ, na cālikaṃ bhāsasi kiñci loke;
::

::gathalast
Vibhūsaṭṭhānā virato methunasmā, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Pariggahaṃ lobhadhammañca sabbaṃ, yo ve pariññāya pariccajeti;
::

::gathalast
Dantaṃ ṭhitattaṃ amamaṃ nirāsaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Pucchāma {pb:T:1.0275} kattāramanomapaññaṃ {note:manomapañña (syā. ka.)}, kathāsu no viggaho atthi jāto;
::

::gathalast
Chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, tadajja {note:tayājja (sī.)} kaṅkhaṃ vitaremu sabbe.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:M:1.0204} paṇḍitā atthadasā bhavanti, bhāsanti te yoniso tattha kāle;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ nu kathānaṃ abhāsitānaṃ, atthaṃ nayeyyuṃ kusalā janindā.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ have bhāsati nāgarājā, garuḷo pana venateyyo kimāha;
::

::gathalast
Gandhabbarājā pana kiṃ vadesi, kathaṃ pana kurūnaṃ rājaseṭṭho.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Khantiṃ have bhāsati nāgarājā, appāhāraṃ garuḷo venateyyo;
::

::gathalast
