Gandhabbarājā rativippahānaṃ, akiñcanaṃ kurūnaṃ rājaseṭṭho.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbāni etāni subhāsitāni, na hettha dubbhāsitamatthi kiñci;
::

::gatha2
Yasmiñca etāni patiṭṭhitāni, arāva {pb:T:1.0276} nābhyā susamohitāni;
::

::gathalast
Catubbhi dhammehi samaṅgibhūtaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Tuvañhi {note:tuvaṃ nu (sī. pī.)} seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi, tvaṃ dhammagū dhammavidū sumedho;
::

::gatha2
Paññāya pañhaṃ samadhiggahetvā, acchecchi dhīro vicikicchitāni;
::

::gathalast
Acchecchi kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, cundo yathā nāgadantaṃ kharena.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Nīluppalābhaṃ vimalaṃ anagghaṃ, vatthaṃ idaṃ dhūmasamānavaṇṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa {pb:T:1.0277} veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Suvaṇṇamālaṃ {pb:V:1.0166}{pb:M:1.0205} satapattaphullitaṃ, sakesaraṃ ratnasahassamaṇḍitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Maṇiṃ anagghaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, kaṇṭhāvasattaṃ {note:vasitaṃ (ka.)} maṇibhūsitaṃ me;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ, ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te gāmavarāni soḷasa.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Sāriputto tadā nāgo, supaṇṇo pana kolito;
::

::gatha2
Gandhabbarājā anuruddho, rājā ānanda paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Vidhuro bodhisatto ca, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
::

::centre
Catuposathiyajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 442. Saṅkhajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Bahussuto sutadhammosi saṅkha, diṭṭhā tayā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca;
::

::gathalast
Athakkhaṇe dassayase vilāpaṃ, añño nu ko te paṭimantako mayā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Subbhū {note:subbhā (syā.), sumbhā, subhmā (ka.)} subhā suppaṭimukkakambu, paggayha sovaṇṇamayāya pātiyā;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Bhuñjassu bhattaṃ’’ iti maṃ vadeti, saddhāvittā {note:saddhācittā (sī. pī. ka.)}, tamahaṃ noti brūmi.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Etādisaṃ {pb:T:1.0278}{pb:M:1.0206} brāhmaṇa disvāna {note:disva (sī. pī.)} yakkhaṃ, puccheyya poso sukhamāsisāno {note:sukhamāsasāno (syā.), sukhamāsisamāno (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Uṭṭhehi naṃ pañjalikābhipuccha, devī nusi tvaṃ uda mānusī nu.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ tvaṃ sukhenābhisamekkhase maṃ, bhuñjassu bhattaṃ iti maṃ vadesi;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ nāri mahānubhāve, devī nusi tvaṃ uda mānusī nu.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Devī ahaṃ saṅkha mahānubhāvā, idhāgatā sāgaravārimajjhe;
::

::gathalast
Anukampikā no ca paduṭṭhacittā, taveva atthāya idhāgatāsmi.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Idhannapānaṃ sayanāsanañca, yānāni nānāvividhāni saṅkha;
::

::gathalast
Sabbassa tyāhaṃ paṭipādayāmi, yaṃ kiñci tuyhaṃ manasābhipatthitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ kiñci yiṭṭhañca hutañca {note:yiṭṭhaṃva hutaṃva (sī. pī.)} mayhaṃ, sabbassa no issarā tvaṃ sugatte;
::

::gathalast
Susoṇi subbhamu {note:subbhu (sī.), subbhā (syā.)} suvilaggamajjhe {note:suvilākamajjhe (syā. pī. sī. aṭṭha.), suvilātamajjhe (ka.)}, kissa me kammassa ayaṃ vipāko.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Ghamme {pb:T:1.0279} pathe brāhmaṇa ekabhikkhuṃ, ugghaṭṭapādaṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṭipādayī saṅkha upāhanāni {note:upāhanāhi (sī. pī.)}, sā dakkhiṇā kāmaduhā tavajja.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Sā {pb:M:1.0207} hotu nāvā phalakūpapannā, anavassutā erakavātayuttā;
::

::gathalast
Aññassa yānassa na hettha {note:na hatthi (pī.)} bhūmi, ajjeva maṃ moḷiniṃ pāpayassu.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Sā {pb:V:1.0167} tattha vittā sumanā patītā, nāvaṃ sucittaṃ abhinimminitvā;
::

::gathalast
Ādāya saṅkhaṃ purisena saddhiṃ, upānayī nagaraṃ sādhurammanti.
::

::centre
Saṅkhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 443. Cūḷabodhijātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Yo te imaṃ visālakkhiṃ, piyaṃ samhitabhāsiniṃ {note:sammillabhāsiniṃ (sī. pī.), sammillahāsiniṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Ādāya balā gaccheyya, kiṃ nu kayirāsi brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Uppajje {note:uppajja (sī. pī.)} me na mucceyya, na me mucceyya jīvato;
::

::gathalast
Rajaṃva {pb:T:1.0280} vipulā vuṭṭhi, khippameva nivāraye {note:nivārayiṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ nu pubbe vikatthittho {note:vikatthito (ka. sī. syā. ka.)}, balamhiva apassito;
::

::gathalast
Svajja tuṇhikato {note:tuṇhikato (sī.), tuṇhikkhako (pī.)} dāni, saṅghāṭiṃ sibbamacchasi.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Uppajji me na muccittha, na me muccittha jīvato;
::

::gathalast
Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi, khippameva nivārayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ te uppajji no mucci, kiṃ te na mucci jīvato;
::

::gathalast
Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi, katamaṃ tvaṃ nivārayi.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Yamhi jāte na passati, ajāte sādhu passati;
::

::gathalast
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Yena jātena nandanti, amittā dukkhamesino;
::

::gathalast
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmiñca {pb:M:1.0208} jāyamānamhi, sadatthaṃ nāvabujjhati;
::

::gathalast
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Yenābhibhūto kusalaṃ jahāti, parakkare vipulañcāpi atthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sa bhīmaseno balavā pamaddī, kodho mahārāja na me amuccatha.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Kaṭṭhasmiṃ matthamānasmiṃ {note:manthamānasmiṃ (pī.), maddamānasmiṃ (ka.)}, pāvako nāma jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Tameva kaṭṭhaṃ ḍahati, yasmā so jāyate gini.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ mandassa posassa, bālassa avijānato;
::

::gathalast
Sārambhā {pb:T:1.0281} {note:sārabbhā (ka.)} jāyate kodho, sopi teneva ḍayhati.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Aggīva tiṇakaṭṭhasmiṃ, kodho yassa pavaḍḍhati;
::

::gathalast
Nihīyati tassa yaso, kāḷapakkheva candimā.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Anedho {pb:V:1.0168} {note:anindho (sī. ka.), anindo (syā.)} dhūmaketūva, kodho yassūpasammati;
::

::gathalast
Āpūrati tassa yaso, sukkapakkheva candimāti.
::

::centre
Cūḷabodhijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 444. Kaṇhadīpāyanajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Sattāhamevāhaṃ pasannacitto, puññatthiko ācariṃ {note:acariṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} brahmacariyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Athāparaṃ yaṃ caritaṃ mamedaṃ {note:mama yidaṃ (syā.), mamāyidaṃ (pī.)}, vassāni paññāsa samādhikāni;
::

::gatha2
Akāmako vāpi {note:vāhi (pī. ka.)} ahaṃ carāmi, etena {pb:T:1.0282} saccena suvatthi hotu;
::

::gathalast
Hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmā {pb:M:1.0209} dānaṃ nābhinandiṃ kadāci, disvānahaṃ atithiṃ vāsakāle;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi me appiyataṃ aveduṃ, bahussutā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca.
::

::gatha1
Akāmako vāpi ahaṃ dadāmi, etena saccena suvatthi hotu;
::

::gathalast
Hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Āsīviso tāta pahūtatejo, yo taṃ adaṃsī {note:aḍaṃsī (syā.)} sacarā {note:bilarā (sī.), piḷārā (syā.), patarā (pī.)} udicca;
::

::gatha2
Tasmiñca me appiyatāya ajja, pitari ca te natthi koci viseso;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu, hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Santā dantāyeva {note:dantā santā ye ca (syā. ka.)} paribbajanti, aññatra kaṇhā natthākāmarūpā {note:anakāmarūpā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Dīpāyana kissa jigucchamāno, akāmako carasi brahmacariyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Saddhāya nikkhamma punaṃ nivatto, so eḷamūgova bālo {note:eḷamūgo capalo (syā. ka.)} vatāyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Etassa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako carāmi brahmacariyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Viññuppasatthañca satañca ṭhānaṃ {note:viññūpasatthaṃ vasitaṃ ca ṭhānaṃ (ka.)}, evampahaṃ puññakaro bhavāmi.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Samaṇe {pb:M:1.0210} tuvaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca, santappayāsi {pb:T:1.0283} annapānena bhikkhaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Opānabhūtaṃva gharaṃ tava yidaṃ, annena pānena upetarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha kissa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāsi.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Pitaro ca me āsuṃ pitāmahā ca, saddhā ahuṃ dānapatī vadaññū;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamāno, māhaṃ kule antimagandhano {note:gandhino (syā. pī. ka.), gandhinī (sī.)} ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etassa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāmi.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Dahariṃ kumāriṃ asamatthapaññaṃ, yaṃ tānayiṃ ñātikulā sugatte;
::

::gatha2
Na cāpi me appiyataṃ avedi, aññatra kāmā paricārayantā {note:paricārayantī (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Atha kena vaṇṇena mayā te bhoti, saṃvāsadhammo ahu evarūpo.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Ārā {pb:V:1.0169} dūre nayidha kadāci atthi, paramparā nāma kule imasmiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamānā, māhaṃ {pb:T:1.0284} kule antimagandhinī ahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etassa vādassa jigucchamānā, akāmikā paddhacarāmhi {note:paṭṭhacarāmhi (syā. ka.)} tuyhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Maṇḍabya {pb:M:1.0211} bhāsiṃ yamabhāsaneyyaṃ {note:bhāsissaṃ abhāsaneyyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), bhāsissa’mabhāsaneyyaṃ (?)}, taṃ khamyataṃ puttakahetu majja;
::

::gathalast
Puttapemā na idha paratthi kiñci, so no ayaṃ jīvati yaññadattoti.
::

::centre
Kaṇhadīpāyanajātakaṃ {note:maṇḍabyajātakaṃ (syā. ka.)} chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 445. Nigrodhajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhametaṃ {note:na cāhametaṃ (sī.)} jānāmi, ko vāyaṃ kassa vāti vā {note:cāti vā (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yathā sākho cari {note:vadī (sī. syā. pī.)} evaṃ, nigrodha kinti maññasi.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Tato galavinītena, purisā nīhariṃsu maṃ;
::

::gathalast
Datvā mukhapahārāni, sākhassa vacanaṃkarā.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Etādisaṃ dummatinā, akataññuna dubbhinā;
::

::gathalast
Kataṃ anariyaṃ sākhena, sakhinā te janādhipa.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhametaṃ jānāmi, napi me koci saṃsati;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ me tvaṃ samma akkhāsi, sākhena kāraṇaṃ {note:kaḍḍhanaṃ (sī. syā.)} kataṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Sakhīnaṃ {pb:T:1.0285} sājīvakaro, mama sākhassa cūbhayaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tvaṃ nosissariyaṃ dātā, manussesu mahantataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tayāmā labbhitā iddhī, ettha me natthi saṃsayo.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi bījamaggimhi, ḍayhati na virūhati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ kataṃ asappurise, nassati na virūhati.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Kataññumhi ca posamhi, sīlavante ariyavuttine;
::

::gathalast
Sukhette viya bījāni, kataṃ tamhi na nassati.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ jammaṃ nekatikaṃ, asappurisacintakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hanantu sākhaṃ sattīhi, nāssa icchāmi jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Khamatassa {pb:M:1.0212} mahārāja, pāṇā na paṭiānayā {note:duppaṭiānayā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Khama deva asappurisassa, nāssa icchāmahaṃ vadhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Nigrodhameva seveyya, na sākhamupasaṃvase;
::

::gathalast
Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo, yañce sākhasmi jīvitanti.
::

::centre
Nigrodhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 446. Takkalajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0170} takkalā santi na āluvāni {note:ālupāni (sī. syā. pī.)}, na biḷāliyo na kaḷambāni tāta;
::

::gathalast
Eko araññamhi susānamajjhe, kimatthiko tāta khaṇāsi kāsuṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Pitāmaho {pb:T:1.0286} tāta sudubbalo te, anekabyādhīhi dukhena phuṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Tamajjahaṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe, na hissa taṃ jīvitaṃ rocayāmi.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Saṅkappametaṃ paṭiladdha pāpakaṃ, accāhitaṃ kamma karosi luddaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Mayāpi tāta paṭilacchase tuvaṃ, etādisaṃ kamma jarūpanīto;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamāno, ahampi taṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Pharusāhi vācāhi pakubbamāno, āsajja maṃ tvaṃ vadase kumāra;
::

::gathalast
Putto mamaṃ orasako samāno, ahitānukampī mama tvaṃsi putta.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0213} tāhaṃ {note:tyāhaṃ (syā.)} tāta ahitānukampī, hitānukampī te ahampi {note:ahañhi (syā.)} tāta;
::

::gathalast
Pāpañca taṃ kamma pakubbamānaṃ, arahāmi no vārayituṃ tato.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ saviṭṭha {note:mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā vasiṭṭha (sī. pī.)}, adūsake hiṃsati pāpadhammo;
::

::gathalast
Kāyassa {pb:T:1.0287} bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, asaṃsayaṃ so nirayaṃ upeti {note:pareti (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ saviṭṭha, annena pānena upaṭṭhahāti;
::

::gathalast
Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, asaṃsayaṃ so sugatiṃ upeti.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Na me tvaṃ putta ahitānukampī, hitānukampī me {note:mama (?)} tvaṃsi putta;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca taṃ mātarā vuccamāno, etādisaṃ kamma karomi luddaṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā, mātā mamesā sakiyā janetti;
::

::gathalast
Niddhāpaye {note:niddhāmase (pī.)} tañca sakā agārā, aññampi te sā dukhamāvaheyya.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā, mātā mamesā sakiyā janetti;
::

::gathalast
Dantā kareṇūva vasūpanītā, sā pāpadhammā punarāvajātūti.
::

::centre
Takkalajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 447. Mahādhammapālajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ {pb:T:1.0288}{pb:M:1.0214} te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ, kasmā nu tumhaṃ daharā na miyyare {note:mīyare (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammaṃ carāma na musā bhaṇāma, pāpāni kammāni parivajjayāma {note:vivajjayāma (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Anariyaṃ parivajjemu sabbaṃ, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇoma {pb:V:1.0171} dhammaṃ asataṃ satañca, na cāpi dhammaṃ asataṃ rocayāma;
::

::gathalast
Hitvā asante na jahāma sante, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Pubbeva dānā sumanā bhavāma, dadampi ve attamanā bhavāma;
::

::gathalast
Datvāpi ve nānutappāma pacchā, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Samaṇe mayaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca, vanibbake yācanake dalidde;
::

::gathalast
Annena pānena abhitappayāma, tasmā {pb:T:1.0289} hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Mayañca bhariyaṃ nātikkamāma, amhe ca bhariyā nātikkamanti;
::

::gathalast
Aññatra tāhi brahmacariyaṃ carāma, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātā {pb:M:1.0215} viramāma sabbe, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayāma;
::

::gathalast
Amajjapā nopi musā bhaṇāma, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Etāsu ve jāyare suttamāsu, medhāvino honti pahūtapaññā;
::

::gathalast
Bahussutā vedaguno {note:vedaguṇā (syā. ka.)} ca honti, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā pitā ca {note:mātā ca pitā (ka.), mātāpitarā (syā.)} bhaginī bhātaro ca, puttā ca dārā ca mayañca sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ carāma paralokahetu, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Dāsā ca dāsyo {note:dāsso (sī. pī.), dāsī (syā.)} anujīvino ca, paricārakā kammakarā ca sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ caranti paralokahetu, tasmā {pb:T:1.0290} hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast
Esānisaṃso dhamme suciṇṇe, na duggatiṃ gacchati dhammacārī.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, chattaṃ mahantaṃ viya vassakāle;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena gutto mama dhammapālo, aññassa aṭṭhīni sukhī kumāroti.
::

::centre
Mahādhammapālajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 448. Kukkuṭajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Nāsmase {pb:M:1.0216} katapāpamhi, nāsmase alikavādine;
::

::gathalast
Nāsmase attatthapaññamhi, atisantepi nāsmase.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Bhavanti heke purisā, gopipāsikajātikā {note:gopipāsakajātikā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ghasanti maññe mittāni, vācāya na ca kammunā.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Sukkhañjalipaggahitā, vācāya paliguṇṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Manussapheggū nāsīde, yasmiṃ natthi kataññutā.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0172} hi aññaññacittānaṃ, itthīnaṃ purisāna vā;
::

::gathalast
Nānāvikatvā {note:nānāva katvā (sī. pī.)} saṃsaggaṃ, tādisampi ca nāsmase {note:tādisampi na vissase (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Anariyakammamokkantaṃ{pb:T:1.0291}, athetaṃ {note:atthetaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} sabbaghātinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisitaṃva paṭicchannaṃ, tādisampi ca nāsmase.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Mittarūpenidhekacce, sākhalyena acetasā;
::

::gathalast
Vividhehi upāyanti, tādisampi ca nāsmase.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Āmisaṃ vā dhanaṃ vāpi, yattha passati tādiso;
::

::gathalast
Dubbhiṃ karoti dummedho, tañca hantvāna {note:jhātvāna (sī. pī.), hitvāna (syā.)} gacchati.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Mittarūpena bahavo, channā sevanti sattavo;
::

::gathalast
Jahe kāpurise hete, kukkuṭo viya senakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca {note:yodha (jā. 1.8.25 sulasājātake)} uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Amittavasamanveti, pacchā ca anutappati.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
::

::gathalast
Muccate sattusambādhā, kukkuṭo viya senakā;
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tādisaṃ kūṭamivoḍḍitaṃ vane, adhammikaṃ niccavidhaṃsakārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārā vivajjeyya naro vicakkhaṇo, senaṃ yathā kukkuṭo vaṃsakānaneti.
::

::centre
Kukkuṭajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

#### 449. Maṭṭhakuṇḍalījātakaṃ (11)

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Alaṅkato {pb:T:1.0292}{pb:M:1.0217} maṭṭhakuṇḍalī {note:maṭṭakuṇḍalī (sī. pī.)}, māladhārī {note:mālabhārī (sī. pī.)} haricandanussado;
::

::gathalast
Bāhā paggayha kandasi, vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Sovaṇṇamayo pabhassaro, uppanno rathapañjaro mama;
::

::gathalast
Tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi, tena dukkhena jahāmi jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇīmayaṃ, lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
{note:ācikkha me bhaddamāṇava (vi. va. 1209)} Pāvada rathaṃ karissāmi {note:kārayāmi (sī. pī.)} te {note:ācikkha me bhaddamāṇava (vi. va. 1209)}, cakkayugaṃ paṭipādayāmi taṃ.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
So {note:atha (syā.)} māṇavo tassa pāvadi, candimasūriyā {note:candimasūriyā (syā.)} ubhayettha bhātaro {note:dissare (vi. va. 1210)};
::

::gathalast
Sovaṇṇamayo ratho mama, tena cakkayugena sobhati.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Bālo kho tvaṃsi māṇava, yo tvaṃ patthayase apatthiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi tuvaṃ marissasi, na {pb:T:1.0293} hi tvaṃ lacchasi candasūriye.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Gamanāgamanampi {pb:V:1.0173} dissati, vaṇṇadhātu ubhayettha vīthiyo;
::

::gathalast
Peto pana neva dissati, ko nu kho {note:ko nidha (vi. va. 1212)} kandataṃ bālyataro.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Saccaṃ {pb:M:1.0218} kho vadesi māṇava, ahameva kandataṃ bālyataro;
::

::gathalast
Candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ, petaṃ kālakatābhipatthaye.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Abbahī {note:abbuhi (syā.), abbhuḷhaṃ (ka.)} vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ {note:sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ (vi. va. 1215)};
::

::gathalast
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇavāti.
::

::centre
Maṭṭhakuṇḍalījātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.
::

#### 450. Bilārakosiyajātakaṃ (12)

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Apacantāpi dicchanti, santo laddhāna bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kimeva tvaṃ pacamāno, yaṃ na dajjā na taṃ samaṃ.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Maccherā {pb:T:1.0294} ca pamādā ca, evaṃ dānaṃ na diyyati;
::

::gathalast
Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānena, deyyaṃ hoti vijānatā.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Yasseva bhīto na dadāti maccharī, tadevādadato bhayaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Jighacchā ca pipāsā ca, yassa bhāyati maccharī;
::

::gathalast
Tameva bālaṃ phusati, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā vineyya maccheraṃ, dajjā dānaṃ malābhibhū;
::

::gathalast
Puññāni paralokasmiṃ, patiṭṭhā honti pāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo durannayo.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā satañca asataṃ {note:asatañca (sī. syā. pī.)}, nānā hoti ito gati;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyanā.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Appasmeke {pb:M:1.0219} {note:appampeke (syā.)} pavecchanti, bahuneke na dicchare;
::

::gathalast
Appasmā dakkhiṇā dinnā, sahassena samaṃ mitā.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammaṃ care yopi samuñchakaṃ care, dārañca posaṃ dadamappakasmiṃ {note:dadaṃ appakasmipi (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi {pb:T:1.0295} nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Kenesa {pb:V:1.0174} yañño vipulo mahagghato {note:mahaggato (saṃ. ni. 1.32)}, samena dinnassa na agghameti;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ sataṃ sahassānaṃ {note:kathaṃ sahassānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Dadanti heke visame niviṭṭhā, chetvā {note:jhatvā (sī. pī.), ghatvā (syā.)} vadhitvā atha socayitvā;
::

::gatha2
Sā dakkhiṇā assumukhā sadaṇḍā, samena dinnassa na agghameti;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ sataṃ sahassānaṃ {note:evaṃ sahassānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa teti.
::

::centre
Bilārakosiyajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.
::

#### 451. Cakkavākajātakaṃ (13)

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Vaṇṇavā abhirūposi, ghano sañjātarohito;
::

::gathalast
Cakkavāka surūposi, vippasannamukhindriyo.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṭhīnaṃ pāvusaṃ macchaṃ, balajaṃ {note:vālajaṃ (sī. pī.), balajjaṃ (syā.)} muñjarohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gaṅgāya tīre nisinno {note:gaṅgātīre nisinnosi (syā. ka.)}, evaṃ bhuñjasi bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhametaṃ {note:sabbatthapi samānaṃ} bhuñjāmi, jaṅgalānodakāni vā;
::

::gathalast
Aññatra sevālapaṇakā, etaṃ {note:aññaṃ (syā.)} me samma bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0220} vāhametaṃ saddahāmi, cakkavākassa bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi samma bhuñjāmi, gāme loṇiyateliyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Manussesu kataṃ bhattaṃ, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:1.0296} ca me tādiso vaṇṇo, cakkavāka yathā tuvaṃ.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Sampassaṃ attani veraṃ, hiṃsayaṃ {note:hiṃsāya (syā. pī. ka.)} mānusiṃ pajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Utrasto ghasasī bhīto, tena vaṇṇo tavediso.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbalokaviruddhosi, dhaṅka pāpena kammunā;
::

::gathalast
Laddho piṇḍo na pīṇeti, tena vaṇṇo tavediso.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
Ahampi {note:ahañca (?)} samma bhuñjāmi, ahiṃsaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appossukko nirāsaṅkī, asoko akutobhayo.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
So karassu ānubhāvaṃ, vītivattassu sīliyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahiṃsāya cara loke, piyo hohisi maṃmiva.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
Yo na hanti na ghāteti, na jināti na jāpaye;
::

::gathalast
Mettaṃso sabbabhūtesu, veraṃ tassa na kenacīti.
::

::centre
Cakkavākajātakaṃ terasamaṃ.
::

#### 452. Bhūripaññajātakaṃ (14)

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
Saccaṃ {pb:V:1.0175} kira tvaṃ api {note:tvampi (sī.), tuvampi (syā.), tvaṃ asi (ka.)} bhūripañña, yā tādisī sīri dhitī matī ca;
::

::gathalast
Na tāyatebhāvavasūpanitaṃ, yo yavakaṃ bhuñjasi appasūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhaṃ dukkhena paripācayanto, kālā kālaṃ vicinaṃ chandachanno;
::

::gathalast
Atthassa {pb:T:1.0297} dvārāni avāpuranto, tenāhaṃ tussāmi yavodanena.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Kālañca {pb:M:1.0221} ñatvā abhijīhanāya, mantehi atthaṃ paripācayitvā;
::

::gathalast
Vijambhissaṃ sīhavijambhitāni, tāyiddhiyā dakkhasi maṃ punāpi.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhīpi heke {note:sukhī hi eke (sī.), sukhīti heke (?)} na karonti pāpaṃ, avaṇṇasaṃsaggabhayā puneke;
::

::gathalast
Pahū samāno vipulatthacintī, kiṃkāraṇā me na karosi dukkhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Na paṇḍitā attasukhassa hetu, pāpāni kammāni samācaranti;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhena phuṭṭhā khalitāpi santā, chandā ca dosā na jahanti dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, mudunā dāruṇena vā;
::

::gathalast
Uddhare dīnamattānaṃ, pacchā dhammaṃ samācare.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
Yassāpi {note:yassa hi (sī. ka.)} dhammaṃ puriso {note:manujo (sī.)} vijaññā, ye cassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santo;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0298} hissa dīpañca parāyanañca, na tena mettiṃ jarayetha pañño.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
::

::gathalast
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
::

::gathalast
Nisammakārino rāja, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
::

::centre
Bhūripaññajātakaṃ cuddasamaṃ.
::

#### 453. Mahāmaṅgalajātakaṃ (15)

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃsu {pb:M:1.0222} naro jappamadhiccakāle, kaṃ vā vijjaṃ katamaṃ vā sutānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So macco asmiñca {note:asmiṃva (pī.)} paramhi loke, kathaṃ karo sotthānena gutto.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa devā pitaro ca sabbe, sarīsapā {note:siriṃsapā (sī. syā. pī.)} sabbabhūtāni cāpi;
::

::gathalast
Mettāya niccaṃ apacitāni honti, bhūtesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0176} sabbalokassa nivātavutti, itthīpumānaṃ {pb:T:1.0299} sahadārakānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khantā duruttānamappaṭikūlavādī, adhivāsanaṃ sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
Yo nāvajānāti sahāyamitte {note:sahāyamatte (sī. pī.)}, sippena kulyāhi dhanena jaccā;
::

::gathalast
Rucipañño atthakāle matīmā {note:mutīmā (sī. pī.)}, sahāyesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
Mittāni ve yassa bhavanti santo, saṃvissatthā avisaṃvādakassa;
::

::gathalast
Na mittadubbhī saṃvibhāgī dhanena, mittesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa bhariyā tulyavayā samaggā, anubbatā dhammakāmā pajātā {note:sajātā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Koliniyā sīlavatī patibbatā, dāresu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa {pb:M:1.0223} rājā bhūtapati {note:bhūtapatī (sī. syā. pī.)} yasassī, jānāti soceyyaṃ parakkamañca;
::

::gathalast
Advejjhatā suhadayaṃ mamanti, rājūsu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
Annañca {pb:T:1.0300} pānañca dadāti saddho, mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca;
::

::gathalast
Pasannacitto anumodamāno, saggesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
Yamariyadhammena punanti vuddhā, ārādhitā samacariyāya santo;
::

::gathalast
Bahussutā isayo sīlavanto, arahantamajjhe sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
Etāni kho sotthānāni loke, viññuppasatthāni sukhudrayāni {note:sukhindriyāni (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tānīdha sevetha naro sapañño, na hi maṅgale kiñcanamatthi saccanti.
::

::centre
Mahāmaṅgalajātakaṃ pannarasamaṃ.
::

#### 454. Ghaṭapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (16)

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhehi kaṇha kiṃ sesi, ko attho supanena te;
::

::gatha2
Yopi tuyhaṃ {note:tāyaṃ (pī.)} sako bhātā, hadayaṃ cakkhu ca {note:cakkhuṃva (pī.)} dakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa vātā balīyanti, ghaṭo jappati {note:sasaṃ jappati (?)} kesava.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, rohiṇeyyassa kesavo;
::

::gathalast
Taramānarūpo vuṭṭhāsi, bhātusokena aṭṭito.
::

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu {pb:T:1.0301} ummattarūpova, kevalaṃ dvārakaṃ imaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saso sasoti lapasi, ko nu te sasamāhari.
::

::hangnum
168\.
::

::gatha1
Sovaṇṇamayaṃ {pb:M:1.0224} maṇīmayaṃ, lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhasilāpavāḷamayaṃ, kārayissāmi te sasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
169\.
::

::gatha1
Santi aññepi sasakā, araññe vanagocarā;
::

::gathalast
Tepi te ānayissāmi, kīdisaṃ sasamicchasi.
::

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0177} cāhamete {note:na cāhametaṃ (sī.), na vāhamete (syā.), na vāhametaṃ (pī.)} icchāmi, ye sasā pathavissitā {note:paṭhaviṃsitā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Candato sasamicchāmi, taṃ me ohara kesava.
::

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
So nūna madhuraṃ ñāti, jīvitaṃ vijahissasi;
::

::gathalast
Apatthiyaṃ yo patthayasi, candato sasamicchasi.
::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ ce kaṇha jānāsi, yadaññamanusāsasi;
::

::gathalast
Kasmā pure mataṃ puttaṃ, ajjāpi manusocasi.
::

::hangnum
173\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ na labbhā manussena, amanussena vā puna {note:pana (pe. va. 215)};
::

::gathalast
Jāto me mā marī putto, kuto labbhā alabbhiyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
174\.
::

::gatha1
Na mantā mūlabhesajjā, osadhehi dhanena vā;
::

::gathalast
Sakkā ānayituṃ kaṇha, yaṃ petamanusocasi.
::

::hangnum
175\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa etādisā assu, amaccā purisapaṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Yathā nijjhāpaye ajja, ghaṭo purisapaṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
176\.
::

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
::

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1
Abbahī {pb:T:1.0302} vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
::

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇava {note:bhātika (pe. va. 224)}.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ karonti sappaññā, ye honti anukampakā;
::

::gathalast
Nivattayanti sokamhā, ghaṭo jeṭṭhaṃva bhātaranti.
::

::centre
Ghaṭapaṇḍitajātakaṃ soḷasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Dasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Daḷha {pb:M:1.0225} kaṇha dhanañjaya saṅkhavaro, raja sattaha kassa ca {note:sattāhasasākha (syā.)} takkalinā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ kukkuṭa kuṇḍali bhojanadā, cakkavāka subhūrisa sotthi ghaṭoti.
::

### 11. Ekādasakanipāto

#### 455. Mātuposakajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {pb:T:1.0303}{pb:V:1.0178}{pb:M:1.0226} nāgassa vippavāsena, virūḷhā sallakī ca kuṭajā ca;
::

::gathalast
Kuruvindakaravīrā {note:karavarā (sī. syā.)} tisasāmā ca, nivāte pupphitā ca kaṇikārā.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Kocideva suvaṇṇakāyurā, nāgarājaṃ bharanti piṇḍena;
::

::gathalast
Yattha rājā rājakumāro vā, kavacamabhihessati achambhito {note:asambhīto (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Gaṇhāhi nāga kabaḷaṃ, mā nāga kisako bhava;
::

::gathalast
Bahūni rājakiccāni, tāni {note:yāni (sī. pī.)} nāga karissasi.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Sā nūnasā kapaṇikā, andhā apariṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Kā nu te sā mahānāga, andhā apariṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā me sā mahārāja, andhā apariṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Muñcathetaṃ mahānāgaṃ, yoyaṃ bharati mātaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sametu {pb:T:1.0304} mātarā nāgo, saha sabbehi ñātibhi.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Mutto ca bandhanā nāgo, muttamādāya kuñjaro {note:kāsirājena pesito (sī. syā.), mutto dāmāto kuñjaro (pī. sī. niyya)};
::

::gathalast
Muhuttaṃ assāsayitvā {note:vissamitvāna (sī.)}, agamā yena pabbato.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Tato so naḷiniṃ {note:nilinaṃ (syā.)} gantvā, sītaṃ kuñjarasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Soṇḍāyūdakamāhatvā {note:māhitvā (syā. ka.)}, mātaraṃ abhisiñcatha.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Koya {pb:M:1.0227} anariyo devo, akālenapi vassati {note:akālena pavassati (sī. syā.), akālena’tivassati (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Gato me atrajo putto, yo mayhaṃ paricārako.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhehi amma kiṃ sesi, āgato tyāhamatrajo;
::

::gathalast
Muttomhi kāsirājena, vedehena yasassinā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Ciraṃ {pb:V:1.0179} jīvatu so rājā, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Yo me puttaṃ pamocesi, sadā vuddhāpacāyikanti.
::

::centre
Mātuposakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 456. Juṇhajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇohi mayhaṃ vacanaṃ janinda, atthena juṇhamhi idhānupatto;
::

::gathalast
Na brāhmaṇe addhike tiṭṭhamāne, gantabba {note:gantabya (ka.)} māhu dvipadinda {note:dipadāna (sī. pī.), dvipadāna (syā.)} seṭṭha.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇomi {pb:T:1.0305} tiṭṭhāmi vadehi brahme, yenāsi {note:yenāpi (syā. ka.)} atthena idhānupatto;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ vā tvamatthaṃ mayi patthayāno, idhāgamā brahme tadiṅgha brūhi.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāhi me gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃsatāni;
::

::gathalast
Parosahassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe, bhariyā ca me sādisī dve dadāhi.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Tapo nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpo, mantā nu te brāhmaṇa cittarūpā;
::

::gathalast
Yakkhā nu {note:yakkhā va (sī. pī.)} te assavā santi keci, atthaṃ vā me abhijānāsi kattaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0228} me tapo atthi na cāpi mantā, yakkhāpi me assavā natthi keci;
::

::gathalast
Atthampi te nābhijānāmi kattaṃ, pubbe ca kho {note:pubbeva kho (syā. ka.)} saṅgatimattamāsi.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Paṭhamaṃ idaṃ dassanaṃ jānato me, na tābhijānāmi ito puratthā;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, kadā kuhiṃ vā ahu saṅgamo no.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Gandhārarājassa {pb:T:1.0306} puramhi ramme, avasimhase takkasīlāyaṃ deva;
::

::gathalast
Tatthandhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ {note:timissikāyaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.), timissakāyaṃ (syā.)}, aṃsena aṃsaṃ samaghaṭṭayimha.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Te tattha ṭhatvāna ubho janinda, sārāṇiyaṃ {note:sāraṇīyaṃ (ka.)} vītisārayimha {note:vītisārimha (sī. syā. pī.)} tattha;
::

::gathalast
Sāyeva no saṅgatimattamāsi, tato na pacchā na pure ahosi.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā kadāci manujesu brahme, samāgamo sappurisena hoti;
::

::gathalast
Na paṇḍitā saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi vināsayanti.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Bālāva {note:bālā ca (sī. syā. pī.)} kho saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi vināsayanti;
::

::gathalast
Bahumpi bālesu kataṃ vinassati, tathā hi bālā akataññurūpā.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Dhīrā ca kho saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi na nāsayanti;
::

::gathalast
Appampi dhīresu kataṃ na nassati, tathā hi dhīrā sukataññurūpā.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi {pb:T:1.0307}{pb:M:1.0229} te gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃsatāni;
::

::gathalast
Parosahassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe, bhariyā ca te sādisī dve dadāmi.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0180} sataṃ hoti samecca rāja, nakkhattarājāriva tārakānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āpūratī kāsipatī tathāhaṃ, tayāpi me saṅgamo ajja laddhoti.
::

::centre
Juṇhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 457. Dhammadevaputtajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Yasokaro puññakarohamasmi, sadātthuto samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Maggāraho devamanussapūjito, dhammo ahaṃ dehi adhamma maggaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Adhammayānaṃ daḷhamāruhitvā, asantasanto balavāhamasmi;
::

::gathalast
Sa kissa hetumhi tavajja dajjaṃ, maggaṃ ahaṃ dhamma adinnapubbaṃ.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo have pāturahosi pubbe, pacchā {pb:T:1.0308} adhammo udapādi loke;
::

::gathalast
Jeṭṭho ca seṭṭho ca sanantano ca, uyyāhi jeṭṭhassa kaniṭṭha maggā.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Na yācanāya napi pātirūpā, na arahatā {note:na arahati (sī. pī.), arahati (ka.)} tehaṃ dadeyyaṃ maggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yuddhañca no hotu ubhinnamajja, yuddhamhi yo jessati tassa maggo.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbā {pb:M:1.0230} disā anuvisaṭohamasmi, mahabbalo amitayaso atulyo;
::

::gathalast
Guṇehi sabbehi upetarūpo, dhammo adhamma tvaṃ kathaṃ vijessasi.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Lohena ve haññati jātarūpaṃ, na jātarūpena hananti lohaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace adhammo hañchati {note:haññati (sī. syā.), haññiti (katthaci)} dhammamajja, ayo suvaṇṇaṃ viya dassaneyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Sace tuvaṃ yuddhabalo adhamma {note:yuddhabalo’si’dhamma (ka. sī.), yuddhabalo’sa’dhamma (pī.)}, na tuyha vuḍḍhā {note:vaddhā (sī. pī.)} ca garū ca atthi;
::

::gathalast
Maggañca te dammi piyāppiyena, vācāduruttānipi te khamāmi.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Idañca sutvā vacanaṃ adhammo, avaṃsiro {pb:T:1.0309} patito uddhapādo;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Yuddhatthiko ce na labhāmi yuddhaṃ’’, ettāvatā hoti hato adhammo.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Khantībalo yuddhabalaṃ vijetvā, hantvā adhammaṃ nihanitva {note:vihanitvā (ka.)} bhūmyā;
::

::gathalast
Pāyāsi vitto {note:citto (syā.)} abhiruyha sandanaṃ, maggeneva atibalo saccanikkamo.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā pitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca, asammānitā yassa sake agāre;
::

::gatha2
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti te {note:vajanti (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yathā adhammo patito avaṃsiro.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā {pb:M:1.0231} pitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca, susammānitā yassa sake agāre;
::

::gatha2
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti te;
::

::gathalast
Yathāpi dhammo abhiruyha sandananti.
::

::centre
Dhammadevaputtajātakaṃ {note:dhammajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)} tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 458. Udayajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Ekā {pb:T:1.0310}{pb:V:1.0181} nisinnā suci saññatūrū, pāsādamāruyha aninditaṅgī;
::

::gathalast
Yācāmi taṃ kinnaranettacakkhu, imekarattiṃ ubhayo vasema.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Okiṇṇantaraparikhaṃ, daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhitaṃ khaggahatthehi, duppavesamidaṃ puraṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Daharassa yuvino cāpi, āgamo ca na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, saṅgamaṃ icchase mayā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Yakkhohamasmi kalyāṇi, āgatosmi tavantike {note:tavantikaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tvaṃ maṃ nandaya {note:nandassu (syā. ka.)} bhaddante, puṇṇakaṃsaṃ dadāmi te.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Devaṃ va yakkhaṃ atha vā manussaṃ, na patthaye udayamaticca aññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gaccheva tvaṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, mā cassu gantvā punarāvajittha.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yā sā rati uttamā kāmabhoginaṃ, yaṃ hetu sattā visamaṃ caranti;
::

::gathalast
Mā taṃ ratiṃ jīyi tuvaṃ sucimhi te, dadāmi te rūpiyaṃ kaṃsapūraṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Nāriṃ {pb:T:1.0311}{pb:M:1.0232} naro nijjhapayaṃ dhanena, ukkaṃsatī yattha karoti chandaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vipaccanīko tava devadhammo, paccakkhato thokatarena esi.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Āyu ca vaṇṇo ca {note:āyuṃ ca vaṇṇaṃ ca (ka. sī. pī.)} manussaloke, nihīyati manujānaṃ suggatte;
::

::gathalast
Teneva vaṇṇena dhanampi tuyhaṃ, nihīyati jiṇṇatarāsi ajja.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ me pekkhamānassa, rājaputti yasassini;
::

::gathalast
Hāyateva tava {note:hāyate vata te (sī. syā. ka.), hāyateva tato (pī.)} vaṇṇo, ahorattānamaccaye.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Imināva tvaṃ vayasā, rājaputti sumedhase;
::

::gathalast
Brahmacariyaṃ careyyāsi, bhiyyo vaṇṇavatī siyā.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Devā na jīranti yathā manussā, gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, kathaṃ nu devāna {note:kathaṃ na devānaṃ (pī.)} sarīradeho.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Devā na jīranti yathā manussā, gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti;
::

::gathalast
Suve suve bhiyyatarova {note:bhiyyataro ca (ka.)} tesaṃ, dibbo {pb:T:1.0312} ca vaṇṇo vipulā ca bhogā.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃsūdha bhītā janatā anekā, maggo ca nekāyatanaṃ pavutto;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, katthaṭṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Vācaṃ {pb:V:1.0182}{pb:M:1.0233} manañca paṇidhāya sammā, kāyena pāpāni akubbamāno;
::

::gatha2
Bahunnapānaṃ gharamāvasanto, saddho mudū saṃvibhāgī vadaññū;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgāhako sakhilo saṇhavāco, etthaṭṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Anusāsasi maṃ yakkha, yathā mātā yathā pitā;
::

::gathalast
Uḷāravaṇṇaṃ pucchāmi, ko nu tvamasi subrahā.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Udayohamasmi kalyāṇi, saṅkarattā idhāgato {note:saṅgaratthā idhāgato (sī. pī.), saṅgaratthāyidhāgato (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāmi, muttosmi tava saṅkarā {note:saṅgarā (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Sace kho tvaṃ udayosi, saṅkarattā idhāgato;
::

::gathalast
Anusāsa maṃ rājaputta, yathāssa puna saṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Atipatati {note:adhipatatī (sī. pī.)} vayo khaṇo tatheva, ṭhānaṃ natthi dhuvaṃ cavanti sattā;
::

::gathalast
Parijiyyati addhuvaṃ sarīraṃ, udaye {pb:T:1.0313} mā pamāda {note:mā pamādaṃ (sī.)} carassu dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Kasiṇā pathavī dhanassa pūrā, ekasseva siyā anaññadheyyā;
::

::gathalast
Tañcāpi jahati {note:jahāti (sī. syā. pī.), jahātī (?)} avītarāgo, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā ca pitā ca bhātaro ca, bhariyā yāpi dhanena hoti kītā {note:bhariyāpi dhanena honti atittā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Te cāpi jahanti aññamaññaṃ, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Kāyo {pb:M:1.0234} parabhojananti ñatvā {note:kāyo ca parabhojanaṃ viditvā (ka.)}, saṃsāre sugatiñca duggatiñca {note:sugatī ca duggatī ca (sī. syā. pī.), suggatiṃ duggatiñca (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ittaravāsoti jāniyāna, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu bhāsatiyaṃ {note:bhāsatayaṃ (sī. pī.)} yakkho, appaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kasirañca parittañca, tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāhaṃ ekā pabbajissāmi, hitvā kāsiṃ surundhananti.
::

::centre
Udayajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 459. Pānīyajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Mitto {pb:T:1.0314} mittassa pānīyaṃ, adinnaṃ paribhuñjisaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Paradārañca disvāna, chando me udapajjatha {note:upapajjatha (syā. ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Pitaraṃ {pb:V:1.0183} me mahārāja, corā agaṇhu {note:agaṇhuṃ (sī. pī.), agaṇhi (ka.)} kānane;
::

::gathalast
Tesāhaṃ pucchito jānaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākariṃ.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
::

::gathalast
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātamakaruṃ, somayāge upaṭṭhite;
::

::gathalast
Tesāhaṃ samanuññāsiṃ, tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā, mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Surāmerayamādhukā {note:madhukā (sī. syā. pī.)}, ye janā paṭhamāsu no;
::

::gathalast
Bahūnaṃ te anatthāya, majjapānamakappayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Tesāhaṃ {pb:M:1.0235} samanuññāsiṃ, tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā, mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu {pb:T:1.0315} subahū kāme, duggandhe bahukaṇṭake;
::

::gathalast
Ye ahaṃ paṭisevanto, nālabhiṃ tādisaṃ sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Mahassādā sukhā kāmā, natthi kāmā paraṃ {note:kāmaparaṃ (sī. pī.)} sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye kāme paṭisevanti, saggaṃ te upapajjare.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Appassādā dukhā kāmā, natthi kāmā paraṃ dukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye kāme paṭisevanti, nirayaṃ te upapajjare.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Asī yathā sunisito, nettiṃsova supāyiko {note:supāsito (ka. sī. niyya), supāyito (ka. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Sattīva urasi khittā, kāmā dukkhatarā tato.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Aṅgārānaṃva jalitaṃ, kāsuṃ sādhikaporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Phālaṃva divasaṃtattaṃ, kāmā dukkhatarā tato.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Visaṃ yathā halāhalaṃ, telaṃ pakkuthitaṃ {note:ukkaṭṭhitaṃ (sī. pī.), pakkuṭṭhitaṃ (syā.)} yathā;
::

::gathalast
Tambaloha {note:tampalohaṃ (syā.)} vilīnaṃva, kāmā dukkhatarā tatoti.
::

::centre
Pānīyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 460. Yudhañcayajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Mittāmaccaparibyūḷhaṃ {note:paribbūḷhaṃ (sī. pī.)}, ahaṃ vande rathesabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pabbajissāmahaṃ rāja {note:pabbajissaṃ mahārāja (sī. pī.)}, taṃ devo anumaññatu.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:V:1.0184} te ūnaṃ kāmehi, ahaṃ paripūrayāmi {note:ahaṃva pūrayāmi (ka.)} te;
::

::gathalast
Yo taṃ hiṃsati vāremi, mā pabbaja {note:pabbaji (pī.)} yudhañcaya {note:yudhañjaya (sī. syā.), yuvañjaya (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0316} matthi ūnaṃ kāmehi, hiṃsitā me na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Dīpañca kātumicchāmi, yaṃ jarā nābhikīrati.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Putto {pb:M:1.0236} vā pitaraṃ yāce, pitā vā puttamorasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Negamo taṃ yāce {note:negamo yācate (sī. syā. pī.)} tāta, mā pabbaja yudhañcaya.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Mā maṃ deva nivārehi, pabbajantaṃ rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Māhaṃ kāmehi sammatto, jarāya vasamanvagū.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ taṃ tāta yācāmi, ahaṃ putta nivāraye;
::

::gathalast
Ciraṃ taṃ daṭṭhumicchāmi, mā pabbaja yudhañcaya.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Ussāvova tiṇaggamhi, sūriyuggamanaṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Evamāyu manussānaṃ, mā maṃ amma nivāraya.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Taramāno imaṃ yānaṃ, āropetu {note:taramānā imaṃ yānaṃ, āropentu (sī. pī.)} rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Mā me mātā tarantassa, antarāyakarā ahu.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Abhidhāvatha bhaddante, suññaṃ hessati rammakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yudhañcayo anuññāto, sabbadattena rājinā.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Yohu seṭṭho sahassassa {note:manussānaṃ (syā.), sahassānaṃ (ka.)}, yuvā kañcanasannibho;
::

::gathalast
Soyaṃ kumāro pabbajito, kāsāyavasano balī.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Ubho kumārā pabbajitā, yudhañcayo yudhiṭṭhilo;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mātāpitaro, saṅgaṃ chetvāna maccunoti.
::

::centre
Yudhañcayajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 461. Dasarathajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Etha {pb:T:1.0317} lakkhaṇa sītā ca, ubho otarathodakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evāyaṃ bharato āha, ‘‘rājā dasaratho mato’’.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Kena rāmappabhāvena, socitabbaṃ na socasi;
::

::gathalast
Pitaraṃ kālakataṃ {note:kālaṅkataṃ (ka.)} sutvā, na taṃ pasahate dukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ na sakkā nipāletuṃ, posena lapataṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sa kissa viññū medhāvī, attānamupatāpaye.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Daharā {pb:V:1.0185}{pb:M:1.0237} ca hi vuddhā ca {note:ye vuddhā (sī. aṭṭha.), ye vuḍḍhā (syā.)}, ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Aḍḍhā ceva daliddā ca, sabbe maccuparāyaṇā.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Phalānamiva pakkānaṃ, niccaṃ patanato bhayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ jātāna maccānaṃ, nicca maraṇato bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Sāyameke na dissanti, pāto diṭṭhā bahujjanā;
::

::gathalast
Pāto eke na dissanti, sāyaṃ diṭṭhā bahujjanā.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Paridevayamāno ce, kiñcidatthaṃ udabbahe;
::

::gathalast
Sammūḷho hiṃsamattānaṃ, kayirā taṃ vicakkhaṇo.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Kiso vivaṇṇo bhavati, hiṃsamattānamattano {note:mattanā (sī. aṭṭha. su. ni. 590)};
::

::gathalast
Na tena petā pālenti, niratthā paridevanā.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā saraṇamādittaṃ, vārinā parinibbaye {note:vārināvanibbāpaye (syā. ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Evampi dhīro sutavā, medhāvī paṇḍito naro;
::

::gathalast
Khippamuppatitaṃ sokaṃ, vāto tūlaṃva dhaṃsaye.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Macco ekova {pb:T:1.0318} {note:ekova macco (sī. syā. pī.)} acceti, ekova jāyate kule;
::

::gathalast
Saṃyogaparamātveva, sambhogā sabbapāṇinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā hi dhīrassa bahussutassa, sampassato lokamimaṃ parañca;
::

::gathalast
Aññāya dhammaṃ hadayaṃ manañca, sokā mahantāpi na tāpayanti.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ dassañca bhokkhañca, bharissāmi ca {note:sohaṃ yasañca bhogañca, bhariyāpi ca (syā. ka.)} ñātake;
::

::gathalast
Sesañca pālayissāmi, kiccametaṃ {note:kiccamevaṃ (pī.)} vijānato.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Dasa vassasahassāni, saṭṭhi vassasatāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Kambugīvo mahābāhu, rāmo rajjamakārayīti.
::

::centre
Dasarathajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 462. Saṃvarajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Jānanto {pb:M:1.0238} no mahārāja, tava sīlaṃ janādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Ime kumāre pūjento, na taṃ kenaci maññatha.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Tiṭṭhante no mahārāje, adu {note:ādu (sī. pī.), ādū (syā.)} deve divaṅgate;
::

::gathalast
Ñātī taṃ samanuññiṃsu, sampassaṃ atthamattano.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Kena saṃvaravattena, sañjāte abhitiṭṭhasi;
::

::gathalast
Kena taṃ nātivattanti, ñātisaṅghā samāgatā.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:V:1.0186} rājaputta usūyāmi {note:rājaputta nussuyyāmi (ka.)}, samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkaccaṃ {pb:T:1.0319} te namassāmi, pāde vandāmi tādinaṃ.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Te maṃ dhammaguṇe yuttaṃ, sussūsamanusūyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇā manusāsanti {note:samanusāsanti (sī. syā. pī.)}, isī dhammaguṇe ratā.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na kiñci atimaññāmi, dhamme me nirato mano.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ {note:tesu (pī.)} nappaṭibandhāmi, niviṭṭhaṃ {note:nibaddhaṃ (sī. pī.)} bhattavetanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Mahāmattā ca me atthi, mantino paricārakā;
::

::gathalast
Bārāṇasiṃ voharanti, bahumaṃsasurodakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Athopi vāṇijā phītā, nānāraṭṭhehi āgatā;
::

::gathalast
Tesu me vihitā rakkhā, evaṃ jānāhuposatha.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena kira ñātīnaṃ, rajjaṃ kārehi saṃvara;
::

::gathalast
Medhāvī paṇḍito cāsi {note:cāpi (sī. pī.)}, athopi ñātinaṃ hito.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ ñātiparibyūḷhaṃ, nānāratanamocitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Amittā nappasahanti, indaṃva asurādhipoti.
::

::centre
Saṃvarajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 463. Suppārakajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Ummujjanti {pb:M:1.0239} nimujjanti, manussā khuranāsikā;
::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ {pb:T:1.0320} taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā {note:bharukacchā (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.)} payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, khuramālīti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā aggīva suriyova {note:aggi suriyo ca (syā.), aggīva sūriyo (ka.)}, samuddo paṭidissati;
::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, aggimālīti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
112\.

::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā {pb:V:1.0187} payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, dadhimālīti {note:khīramālīti (ka.)} vuccati.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā kusova sassova, samuddo paṭidissati;
::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, kusamālīti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā naḷova veḷūva, samuddo paṭidissati;
::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
