::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Mahabbhayo bhiṃsanako, saddo suyyatimānuso {note:samuddo suyyata’mānuso (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gatha2
Yathā {pb:T:1.0321} sobbho papātova, samuddo paṭidissati;
::

::gathalast
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Kurukacchā {pb:M:1.0240} payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, baḷavāmukhīti {note:vaḷabhāmukhīti (sī. syā.), balavāmukhīti (syā. ka.)} vuccati.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nābhijānāmi sañcicca, ekapāṇampi hiṃsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccavajjena, sotthiṃ nāvā nivattatūti.
::

::centre
Suppārakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

::centre
Ekādasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sirimātusuposakanāgavaro, puna juṇhaka dhammamudayavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha pāni yudhañcayako ca, dasaratha saṃvara pāragatena navāti.
::

### 12. Dvādasakanipāto

#### 464. Cūḷakuṇālajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Luddhānaṃ {pb:T:1.0322}{pb:V:1.0188}{pb:M:1.0241} {note:khuddānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} lahucittānaṃ, akataññūna dubbhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nādevasatto puriso, thīnaṃ saddhātumarahati.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Na tā pajānanti kataṃ na kiccaṃ, na mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhātaraṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Anariyā samatikkantadhammā, sasseva cittassa vasaṃ vajanti.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Cirānuvuṭṭhampi {note:cirānuvutthampi (sī. pī.)} piyaṃ manāpaṃ, anukampakaṃ pāṇasamampi bhattuṃ {note:santaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Āvāsu kiccesu ca naṃ jahanti, tasmāhamitthīnaṃ na vissasāmi.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Thīnañhi cittaṃ yathā vānarassa, kannappakannaṃ yathā rukkhachāyā;
::

::gathalast
Calācalaṃ hadayamitthiyānaṃ, cakkassa nemi viya parivattati.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā tā passanti samekkhamānā, ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṇhāhi vācāhi nayanti menaṃ, kambojakā {pb:T:1.0323} jalajeneva assaṃ.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā na passanti samekkhamānā, ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samantato naṃ parivajjayanti, tiṇṇo nadīpāragatova kullaṃ.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Silesūpamā {pb:M:1.0242} sikhiriva sabbabhakkhā, tikkhamāyā nadīriva sīghasotā;
::

::gathalast
Sevanti hetā piyamappiyañca, nāvā yathā orakūlaṃ parañca.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Na tā ekassa na dvinnaṃ, āpaṇova pasārito;
::

::gathalast
Yo tā mayhanti maññeyya, vātaṃ jālena bādhaye {note:bandhaye (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā nadī ca pantho ca, pānāgāraṃ sabhā papā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ lokitthiyo nāma, velā tāsaṃ na vijjati {note:imissā gāthāya pubbaddhāparaddhaṃ vipariyāyena dissati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Ghatāsanasamā etā, kaṇhasappasirūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Gāvo bahitiṇasseva, omasanti varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Ghatāsanaṃ kuñjaraṃ kaṇhasappaṃ, muddhābhisittaṃ pamadā ca sabbā;
::

::gathalast
Ete naro niccayato {note:niccayatto (sī. pī.)} bhajetha, tesaṃ have dubbidu sabbabhāvo {note:saccabhāvo (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Naccantavaṇṇā {pb:T:1.0324}{pb:V:1.0189} na bahūnaṃ kantā, na dakkhiṇā pamadā sevitabbā;
::

::gathalast
Na parassa bhariyā na dhanassa hetu, etitthiyo pañca na sevitabbāti.
::

::centre
Cūḷakuṇālajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 465. Bhaddasālajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Kā tvaṃ suddhehi vatthehi, aghe vehāyasaṃ {note:vehāsayaṃ (sī. pī.)} ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Kena tyāssūni vattanti, kuto taṃ bhayamāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Taveva deva vijite, bhaddasāloti maṃ vidū;
::

::gathalast
Saṭṭhi {note:saṭṭhiṃ (sī. pī.)} vassasahassāni, tiṭṭhato pūjitassa me.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Kārayantā {pb:M:1.0243} nagarāni, agāre ca disampati;
::

::gatha2
Vividhe cāpi pāsāde, na maṃ te accamaññisuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yatheva maṃ te pūjesuṃ, tatheva tvampi pūjaya.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ ivāhaṃ {note:tañca ahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} na passāmi, thūlaṃ kāyena te dumaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ārohapariṇāhena, abhirūposi jātiyā.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Pāsādaṃ kārayissāmi, ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tattha taṃ upanessāmi, ciraṃ te yakkha jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ cittaṃ udapādi, sarīrena vinābhāvo;
::

::gathalast
Puthuso maṃ vikantitvā, khaṇḍaso avakantatha.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Agge {pb:T:1.0325} ca chetvā majjhe ca, pacchā mūlamhi chindatha {note:mūlañca chindatha (sī.), mūlaṃ vichindatha (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ me chijjamānassa, na dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Hatthapādaṃ {note:hatthapāde (ka.)} yathā chinde {note:chinne (ka.)}, kaṇṇanāsañca jīvato;
::

::gathalast
Tato pacchā siro chinde, taṃ dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Sukhaṃ nu khaṇḍaso chinnaṃ, bhaddasālavanappati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ hetu kiṃ upādāya, khaṇḍaso chinnamicchasi.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Yañca hetumupādāya, hetuṃ dhammūpasaṃhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khaṇḍaso chinnamicchāmi, mahārāja suṇohi me.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Ñātī me sukhasaṃvaddhā, mama passe nivātajā;
::

::gathalast
Tepihaṃ upahiṃseyyaṃ, paresaṃ asukhocitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Ceteyyarūpaṃ {pb:V:1.0190} {note:cetabbarūpaṃ (sī. pī.)} cetesi, bhaddasālavanappati;
::

::gathalast
Hitakāmosi ñātīnaṃ, abhayaṃ samma dammi teti.
::

::centre
Bhaddasālajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 466. Samuddavāṇijajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Kasanti {pb:M:1.0244} vapanti te janā, manujā kammaphalūpajīvino;
::

::gathalast
Nayimassa dīpakassa bhāgino, jambudīpā idameva no varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Tipañcarattūpagatamhi cande, vego {pb:T:1.0326} mahā hehiti sāgarassa;
::

::gathalast
Uplavissaṃ dīpamimaṃ uḷāraṃ, mā vo vadhī gacchatha leṇamaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Na jātuyaṃ sāgaravārivego, uplavissaṃ dīpamimaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ me nimittehi bahūhi diṭṭhaṃ, mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathavho {note:modatha vo (ka.) 6.38 moggallānasuttaṃ passitabbaṃ}.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ, pattattha āvāsamimaṃ uḷāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na vo bhayaṃ paṭipassāmi kiñci, āputtaputtehi pamodathavho.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Yo devoyaṃ dakkhiṇāyaṃ {note:dakkhiṇassaṃ (sī.)} disāyaṃ, khemanti pakkosati tassa saccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na uttaro vedi bhayābhayassa, mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathavho.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā ime vippavadanti yakkhā, eko bhayaṃ saṃsati khemameko;
::

::gathalast
Tadiṅgha mayhaṃ vacanaṃ suṇātha, khippaṃ {pb:T:1.0327} lahuṃ mā vinassimha sabbe.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbe {pb:M:1.0245} samāgamma karoma nāvaṃ, doṇiṃ daḷhaṃ sabbayantūpapannaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sace ayaṃ dakkhiṇo saccamāha, moghaṃ paṭikkosati uttaroyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā ceva no hehiti āpadatthā, imañca dīpaṃ na pariccajema.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Sace ca kho uttaro saccamāha, moghaṃ paṭikkosati dakkhiṇoyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tameva nāvaṃ abhiruyha sabbe, evaṃ mayaṃ sotthi taremu pāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Na ve sugaṇhaṃ paṭhamena seṭṭhaṃ, kaniṭṭhamāpāthagataṃ gahetvā;
::

::gathalast
Yo cīdha tacchaṃ {note:majjhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} paviceyya gaṇhati {note:gaṇhi (ka.)}, sa ve naro seṭṭhamupeti ṭhānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi te sāgaravārimajjhe, sakammunā sotthi vahiṃsu vāṇijā;
::

::gathalast
Anāgatatthaṃ paṭivijjhiyāna, appampi nācceti sa bhūripañño.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Bālā {pb:T:1.0328} ca mohena rasānugiddhā, anāgataṃ appaṭivijjhiyatthaṃ;
::

Paccuppanne sīdanti atthajāte, samuddamajjhe yathā te manussā.

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Anāgataṃ {pb:V:1.0191} paṭikayirātha kiccaṃ, ‘‘mā maṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle byadhesi’’;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tādisaṃ paṭikata {note:paṭikataṃ (ka.), paṭigata (sī. aṭṭha.), paṭikacca (?)} kiccakāriṃ, na taṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle byadhetīti.
::

::centre
Samuddavāṇijajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 467. Kāmajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ {pb:M:1.0246} kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Addhā pītimano hoti, laddhā macco yadicchati.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
::

::gathalast
Tato naṃ aparaṃ kāme, dhamme taṇhaṃva vindati.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Gavaṃva siṅgino siṅgaṃ, vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati;
::

::gatha2
Evaṃ mandassa posassa, bālassa avijānato;
::

::gathalast
Bhiyyo taṇhā pipāsā ca, vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Pathabyā sāliyavakaṃ, gavassaṃ {note:gavāsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} dāsaporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Datvā ca {note:datvāpi (sī. syā.), datvā vā (pī.)} nālamekassa, iti vidvā {note:viddhā (syā.)} samaṃ care.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Rājā {pb:T:1.0329} pasayha pathaviṃ vijitvā, sasāgarantaṃ mahimāvasanto;
::

::gathalast
Oraṃ samuddassa atittarūpo {note:atittirūpo (ka.)}, pāraṃ samuddassapi patthayetha.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yāva anussaraṃ kāme, manasā titti nājjhagā;
::

::gathalast
Tato nivattā paṭikamma disvā, te ve sutittā ye {note:tittā (sī. syā. pī.)} paññāya tittā.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Paññāya tittinaṃ {note:tittīnaṃ (sī. syā.)} seṭṭhaṃ, na so kāmehi tappati;
::

::gathalast
Paññāya tittaṃ purisaṃ, taṇhā na kurute vasaṃ.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Apacinetheva kāmānaṃ {note:kāmāni (sī. syā. pī.)}, appicchassa alolupo;
::

::gathalast
Samuddamatto puriso, na so kāmehi tappati.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Rathakārova cammassa, parikantaṃ upāhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yaṃ yaṃ cajati {note:jahati (syā. ka.)} kāmānaṃ, taṃ taṃ sampajjate sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ ce sukhamiccheyya, sabbe kāme pariccaje.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭha {pb:M:1.0247} te bhāsitā gāthā, sabbā honti sahassiyo {note:sahassiyā (?) upari sutasomajātake tathā dissati};
::

::gathalast
Paṭigaṇha mahābrahme, sādhetaṃ tava bhāsitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Na me attho sahassehi, satehi nahutehi vā;
::

::gathalast
Pacchimaṃ bhāsato gāthaṃ, kāme me na rato mano.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Bhadrako {pb:V:1.0192} {note:saddo (sī.)} vatāyaṃ māṇavako, sabbalokavidū muni;
::

::gathalast
Yo {pb:T:1.0330} imaṃ taṇhaṃ {note:yo taṇhaṃ (sī. syā.)} dukkhajananiṃ, parijānāti paṇḍitoti.
::

::centre
Kāmajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 468. Janasandhajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Dasa khalu imāni {note:khalumāni (syā.)} ṭhānāni, yāni pubbe akaritvā;
::

::gathalast
Sa pacchā manutappati, iccevāha {note:iccāha rājā (sī. syā. pī.)} janasandho.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Aladdhā vittaṃ tappati, pubbe asamudānitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na pubbe dhanamesissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Sakyarūpaṃ pure santaṃ, mayā sippaṃ na sikkhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kicchā vutti asippassa, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Kūṭavedī pure āsiṃ, pisuṇo piṭṭhimaṃsiko;
::

::gathalast
Caṇḍo ca pharuso cāpi {note:cāsiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātī pure āsiṃ, luddo cāpi {note:cāsiṃ (sī. pī.)} anāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Bhūtānaṃ nāpacāyissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Bahūsu vata santīsu, anāpādāsu itthisu;
::

::gathalast
Paradāraṃ asevissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Bahumhi vata santamhi, annapāne upaṭṭhite;
::

::gathalast
Na pubbe adadaṃ {note:adadiṃ (sī.)} dānaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ {note:jiṇṇake gatayobbane (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pahu {pb:T:1.0331} santo na posissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Ācariyamanusatthāraṃ{pb:M:1.0248}, sabbakāmarasāharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pitaraṃ atimaññissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi, sīlavante bahussute;
::

::gathalast
Na pubbe payirupāsissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu hoti tapo ciṇṇo, santo ca payirupāsito;
::

::gathalast
Na ca pubbe tapo ciṇṇo, iti pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni, yoniso paṭipajjati;
::

::gathalast
Karaṃ purisakiccāni, sa pacchā nānutappatīti.
::

::centre
Janasandhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 469. Mahākaṇhajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Kaṇho {pb:V:1.0193} kaṇho ca ghoro ca, sukkadāṭho pabhāsavā {note:patāpavā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Baddho pañcahi rajjūhi, kiṃ ravi {note:dhīra (sī. pī.), vīra (syā.)} sunakho tava.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Nāyaṃ migānamatthāya, usīnaka {note:usīnara (sī. pī.), usīnnara (syā.)} bhavissati;
::

::gathalast
Manussānaṃ anayo hutvā, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Pattahatthā samaṇakā, muṇḍā saṅghāṭipārutā;
::

::gathalast
Naṅgalehi kasissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Tapassiniyo {note:tapanīyā (ka.) dutiyantapadāni hetāni} pabbajitā, muṇḍā saṅghāṭipārutā;
::

::gathalast
Yadā loke gamissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Dīghottaroṭṭhā {pb:T:1.0332} jaṭilā, paṅkadantā rajassirā;
::

::gathalast
Iṇaṃ codāya {note:vodāya (sī. pī.), codaya (syā.)} gacchanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Adhicca vede {note:vedaṃ (ka.)} sāvittiṃ, yaññatantañca {note:tantrañca (sī. syā. pī.)} brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Bhatikāya yajissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahū santo {note:santā (sī.)} na bharanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Mātaraṃ {pb:M:1.0249} pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bālā tumheti vakkhanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Ācariyabhariyaṃ sakhiṃ {note:ācariyabhariyaṃ sakhābhariyaṃ (sī. pī.)}, mātulāniṃ pitucchakiṃ {note:pitucchayaṃ (sī.), pitucchasaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yadā loke gamissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Asicammaṃ gahetvāna, khaggaṃ paggayha brāhmaṇā;
::

::gathalast
Panthaghātaṃ karissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Sukkacchavī vedhaverā, thūlabāhū apātubhā;
::

::gathalast
Mittabhedaṃ karissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Māyāvino nekatikā, asappurisacintakā;
::

::gathalast
Yadā loke bhavissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhatīti.
::

::centre
Mahākaṇhajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 470. Kosiyajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Neva {pb:V:1.0194} kiṇāmi napi vikkiṇāmi, na {pb:T:1.0333} cāpi me sannicayo ca atthi {note:idhatthi (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Sukiccharūpaṃ vatidaṃ parittaṃ, patthodano nālamayaṃ duvinnaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Appamhā appakaṃ dajjā, anumajjhato majjhakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bahumhā bahukaṃ dajjā, adānaṃ nupapajjati {note:na upapajjati (sī. pī.), nūpapajjati (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca.
::

::gathalast
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha {note:ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha (sī. pī.)}, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Moghañcassa hutaṃ hoti, moghañcāpi samīhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
::

::gathalast
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Saccañcassa {pb:M:1.0250} hutaṃ hoti, saccañcāpi samīhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
::

::gathalast
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Sarañca juhati poso, bahukāya gayāya ca;
::

::gathalast
Doṇe timbarutitthasmiṃ, sīghasote mahāvahe.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Atra cassa hutaṃ hoti, atra cassa samīhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
::

::gathalast
Ariyamaggaṃ {pb:T:1.0334} samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Baḷisañhi so nigilati {note:niggilati (sī. pī.)}, dīghasuttaṃ sabandhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
::

::gathalast
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Uḷāravaṇṇā vata brāhmaṇā ime, ayañca vo sunakho kissa hetu;
::

::gathalast
Uccāvacaṃ vaṇṇanibhaṃ vikubbati, akkhātha no brāhmaṇā ke nu tumhe.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Cando ca suriyo ca {note:sūriyo ca (ka.)} ubho idhāgatā, ayaṃ pana mātali devasārathi;
::

::gathalast
Sakkohamasmi tidasānamindo, eso ca kho pañcasikhoti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇissarā {pb:V:1.0195} mudiṅgā ca {note:mutiṅgā ca (sī. syā. pī.}, murajālambarāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Suttamenaṃ pabodhenti, paṭibuddho ca nandati.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Ye kecime maccharino kadariyā, paribhāsakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:M:1.0251} kecime suggatimāsamānā {note:suggatimāsasānā (sī. pī.), suggatāsisamānā (ka.)}, dhamme {pb:T:1.0335} ṭhitā saṃyame saṃvibhāge;
::

::gathalast
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Tvaṃ nosi ñāti purimāsu jātisu, so maccharī rosako {note:kosiyo (syā. ka.)} pāpadhammo;
::

::gathalast
Taveva atthāya idhāgatamhā, mā pāpadhammo nirayaṃ gamittha {note:appattha (ka. sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi maṃ vo hitakāmā, yaṃ maṃ samanusāsatha;
::

::gathalast
Sohaṃ tathā karissāmi, sabbaṃ vuttaṃ hitesibhi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Esāhamajjeva upāramāmi, na cāpihaṃ {note:na cāpahaṃ (sī. pī.)} kiñci kareyya pāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi me kiñci adeyyamatthi, na cāpidatvā udakaṃ pivāmi {note:udakampahaṃ pibe (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Evañca me dadato sabbakālaṃ {note:kāle (ka.)}, bhogā ime vāsava khīyissanti;
::

::gathalast
Tato ahaṃ pabbajissāmi sakka, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikānīti.
::

::centre
Kosiyajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 471. Meṇḍakapañhajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Yesaṃ {pb:T:1.0336} na kadāci bhūtapubbaṃ, sakhyaṃ {note:sakkhiṃ (sī. pī.), sakhi (syā.)} sattapadampimasmi loke;
::

::gathalast
Jātā amittā duve sahāyā, paṭisandhāya caranti kissa hetu.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Yadi {pb:M:1.0252} me ajja pātarāsakāle, pañhaṃ na sakkuṇeyyātha vattumetaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhā pabbājayissāmi vo sabbe, na hi mattho duppaññajātikehi.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Mahājanasamāgamamhi ghore, janakolāhalasaṅgamamhi jāte;
::

::gathalast
Vikkhittamanā anekacittā, pañhaṃ na sakkuṇoma vattumetaṃ.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Ekaggacittāva ekamekā, rahasi gatā atthaṃ nicintayitvā {note:atthāni cintayitvā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Paviveke sammasitvāna dhīrā, atha vakkhanti janinda etamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Uggaputta-rājaputtiyānaṃ, urabbhassa maṃsaṃ piyaṃ manāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na sunakhassa te adenti maṃsaṃ, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Cammaṃ vihananti eḷakassa, assapiṭṭhattharassukhassa {note:assapiṭṭhattharaṇasukhassa (sī.)} hetu;
::

::gathalast
Na ca te sunakhassa attharanti, atha {pb:T:1.0337} meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Āvellitasiṅgiko {pb:V:1.0196} hi meṇḍo, na ca sunakhassa visāṇakāni atthi;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇabhakkho maṃsabhojano ca, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Tiṇamāsi palāsamāsi meṇḍo, na ca sunakho tiṇamāsi no palāsaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gaṇheyya suṇo sasaṃ biḷāraṃ, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhaḍḍhapado {pb:M:1.0253} catuppadassa, meṇḍo aṭṭhanakho adissamāno;
::

::gathalast
Chādiyamāharatī ayaṃ imassa, maṃsaṃ āharatī ayaṃ amussa.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Pāsādavaragato videhaseṭṭho, vitihāraṃ aññamaññabhojanānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Addakkhi {note:addasa (syā. ka.)} kira sakkhikaṃ janindo, bubhukkassa {pb:T:1.0338} puṇṇaṃ mukhassa {note:bhobhukkhassa ca puṇṇamukhassa (sī.)} cetaṃ.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Lābhā vata me anapparūpā, yassa medisā paṇḍitā kulamhi;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa gambhīragataṃ nipuṇamatthaṃ, paṭivijjhanti subhāsitena dhīrā.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Assatarirathañca ekamekaṃ, phītaṃ gāmavarañca ekamekaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ vo dammi paṇḍitānaṃ, paramappatītamano subhāsitenāti.
::

::centre
Meṇḍakapañhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 472. Mahāpadumajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Nādaṭṭhā {note:nādiṭṭhā (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} parato dosaṃ, aṇuṃ thūlāni sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Issaro paṇaye daṇḍaṃ, sāmaṃ appaṭivekkhiya.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca appaṭivekkhitvā, daṇḍaṃ kubbati khattiyo;
::

::gathalast
Sakaṇṭakaṃ so gilati, jaccandhova samakkhikaṃ.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Adaṇḍiyaṃ daṇḍayati {note:daṇḍiyati (syā. pī.)}, daṇḍiyañca adaṇḍiyaṃ {note:adaṇḍiya (niyya), na daṇḍaye (?)};
::

::gathalast
Andhova visamaṃ maggaṃ, na jānāti samāsamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni, aṇuṃ thūlāni sabbaso;
::

::gathalast
Sudiṭṭhamanusāseyya, sa ve voharitu {note:vohātu (pī.)} marahati.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Nekantamudunā {pb:T:1.0339}{pb:M:1.0254} sakkā, ekantatikhiṇena vā;
::

::gathalast
Attaṃ mahante {note:mahatte (syā. ka.)} ṭhapetuṃ {note:ṭhāpetuṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, tasmā ubhayamācare.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Paribhūto mudu hoti, atitikkho ca veravā;
::

::gathalast
Etañca ubhayaṃ ñatvā, anumajjhaṃ samācare.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Bahumpi ratto bhāseyya, duṭṭhopi bahu bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Na itthikāraṇā rāja, puttaṃ ghātetumarahasi.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbova {pb:V:1.0197} {note:sabbo ca (ka. sī. pī.)} loko ekato {note:ekanto (sī. pī.)}, itthī ca ayamekikā;
::

::gathalast
Tenāhaṃ paṭipajjissaṃ, gacchatha pakkhipatheva {note:pakkhipetha (syā. aṭṭha.)} taṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Anekatāle narake, gambhīre ca suduttare {note:gambhīre suduruttare (pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Pātito giriduggasmiṃ, kena tvaṃ tattha nāmari.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Nāgo jātaphaṇo tattha, thāmavā girisānujo;
::

::gathalast
Paccaggahi maṃ bhogehi, tenāhaṃ tattha nāmariṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi taṃ paṭinessāmi, rājaputta sakaṃ gharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rajjaṃ kārehi {note:kāresi (sī.)} bhaddante, kiṃ araññe karissasi.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā gilitvā baḷisaṃ, uddhareyya salohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uddharitvā sukhī assa, evaṃ {note:sukhaṃ (pī. ka.)} passāmi attanaṃ {note:attani (pī. ka.), attanā (syā.), evaṃ ahampi puna sotthibhāvappattaṃ gilitabaḷisaṃ purisamiva attānaṃ passāmīti (aṭṭha. saṃvaṇṇanā)}.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu tvaṃ baḷisaṃ brūsi, kiṃ tvaṃ brūsi salohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ nu tvaṃ ubbhataṃ brūsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmāhaṃ baḷisaṃ brūmi, hatthiassaṃ salohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cattāhaṃ ubbhataṃ brūmi, evaṃ jānāhi khattiya.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Ciñcāmāṇavikā {pb:T:1.0340} mātā, devadatto ca me pitā;
::

::gatha2
Ānando paṇḍito nāgo, sāriputto ca devatā;
::

::gathalast
Rājaputto ahaṃ āsiṃ {note:ahaṃ tadā rājaputto (sī. syā. pī.)}, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
::

::centre
Mahāpadumajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 473. Mittāmittajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Kāni {pb:M:1.0255} kammāni kubbānaṃ, kathaṃ viññū parakkame;
::

::gathalast
Amittaṃ jāneyya medhāvī, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Na naṃ umhayate disvā, na ca naṃ paṭinandati;
::

::gathalast
Cakkhūni cassa {note:cakkhūnissa (syā. ka.)} na dadāti, paṭilomañca vattati.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Amitte tassa bhajati, mitte tassa na sevati;
::

::gathalast
Vaṇṇakāme nivāreti, akkosante pasaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Guyhañca tassa nakkhāti, tassa guyhaṃ na gūhati;
::

::gathalast
Kammaṃ tassa na vaṇṇeti, paññassa nappasaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Abhave {pb:V:1.0198} nandati tassa, bhave tassa na nandati;
::

::gatha2
Accheraṃ {note:acchariyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} bhojanaṃ laddhā, tassa nuppajjate sati;
::

::gathalast
Tato naṃ nānukampati, aho sopi {note:ahāsopi (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} labheyyito.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Iccete soḷasākārā, amittasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Yehi amittaṃ jāneyya, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Kāni kammāni kubbānaṃ, kathaṃ viññū parakkame;
::

::gathalast
Mittaṃ {pb:T:1.0341} jāneyya medhāvī, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Pavutthaṃ tassa sarati, āgataṃ abhinandati;
::

::gathalast
Tato kelāyito hoti, vācāya paṭinandati.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Mitte tasseva bhajati, amitte tassa na sevati;
::

::gathalast
Akkosante nivāreti, vaṇṇakāme pasaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Guyhañca tassa akkhāti, tassa guyhañca gūhati;
::

::gathalast
Kammañca tassa vaṇṇeti, paññaṃ tassa {note:paññamassa (syā. ka.)} pasaṃsati.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Bhave ca nandati tassa {note:bhave nandati tassa ca (ka.)}, abhave tassa na nandati;
::

::gatha2
Accheraṃ {note:acchariyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} bhojanaṃ laddhā, tassa uppajjate sati;
::

::gathalast
Tato naṃ anukampati, aho sopi {note:pahāsopi (ka. sī. syā. ka.)} labheyyito.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Iccete {pb:M:1.0256} soḷasākārā, mittasmiṃ suppatiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Yehi mittañca jāneyya {note:mittaṃ sujāneyya (pī. ka.)}, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍitoti.
::

::centre
Mittāmittajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

::centre
Dvādasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Lahucitta sasāla kasanti puna, atha kāma dasakhaluṭṭhānavaro;
::

::gathalast
Atha kaṇha sukosiya meṇḍavaro, padumo puna mittavarena dasāti.
::

### 13. Terasakanipāto

#### 474. Ambajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Ahāsi {pb:T:1.0342}{pb:V:1.0199}{pb:M:1.0257} {note:āhāsi (?)} me ambaphalāni pubbe, aṇūni thūlāni ca brahmacāri;
::

::gathalast
Teheva mantehi na dāni tuyhaṃ, dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Nakkhattayogaṃ paṭimānayāmi, khaṇaṃ muhuttañca mante na passaṃ {note:khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na maṃ tosayanti (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Nakkhattayogañca khaṇañca laddhā, addhāharissambaphalaṃ {note:athāharissambaphalaṃ (sī. pī.)} pahūtaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Nakkhattayogaṃ na pure abhāṇi, khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na pure asaṃsi;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃ harī {note:athāharī (sī. syā. pī.)} ambaphalaṃ pahūtaṃ, vaṇṇena gandhena rasenupetaṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Mantābhijappena pure hi {note:pura’ssa (sī. pī.), purepi (syā.)} tuyhaṃ, dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme;
::

::gathalast
Svājja na pāresi jappampi mantaṃ {note:japampi mante (sī. pī.)}, ayaṃ so ko nāma tavajja dhammo.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Caṇḍālaputto {pb:T:1.0343} mama sampadāsi, dhammena mante pakatiñca saṃsi;
::

::gathalast
Mā cassu me pucchito nāmagottaṃ, guyhittho atthaṃ {note:mā taṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vijaheyya manto {note:vijaheyyumantā (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ {pb:M:1.0258} janindena janamhi puṭṭho, makkhābhibhūto alikaṃ abhāṇiṃ;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Mantā ime brāhmaṇassā’’ti micchā, pahīnamanto kapaṇo rudāmi.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Eraṇḍā pucimandā vā, atha vā pālibhaddakā;
::

::gathalast
Madhuṃ madhutthiko vinde, so hi tassa dumuttamo.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gathalast
Yamhā dhammaṃ vijāneyya, so hi tassa naruttamo.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Imassa daṇḍañca vadhañca datvā, gale gahetvā khalayātha {note:balayātha (syā.), galayātha (ka.)} jammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yo uttamatthaṃ kasirena laddhaṃ, mānātimānena vināsayittha.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā samaṃ maññamāno pateyya, sobbhaṃ guhaṃ narakaṃ pūtipādaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Rajjūti vā akkame kaṇhasappaṃ, andho {pb:T:1.0344} yathā jotimadhiṭṭhaheyya;
::

::gathalast
Evampi maṃ tvaṃ khalitaṃ sapañña {note:sapaññā (pī.)}, pahīnamantassa punappadāhi {note:puna sampadāhi (syā.), punappasīda (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena mantaṃ {note:mante (sī. syā. pī.)} tava sampadāsiṃ, tuvampi dhammena {note:tvampi dhammeneva (ka.)} pariggahesi;
::

::gathalast
Pakatimpi te attamano asaṃsiṃ, dhamme ṭhitaṃ taṃ {note:patiṭṭhaṃ (ka.)} na jaheyya manto.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:V:1.0200} bāla mantaṃ {note:balamantaṃ (ka.)} kasirena laddhaṃ, yaṃ dullabhaṃ ajja manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Kiñcāpi laddhā jīvituṃ appapañño {note:kicchā laddhaṃ jīvikaṃ appapañño (sī. syā.), kacchāpi laddhā jīvikaṃ appañña (pī.)}, vināsayī alikaṃ bhāsamāno.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Bālassa {pb:M:1.0259} mūḷhassa akataññuno ca, musā bhaṇantassa asaññatassa;
::

::gathalast
Mante mayaṃ tādisake na dema, kuto mantā gaccha na mayha ruccasīti.
::

::centre
Ambajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 475. Phandanajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Kuṭhārihattho {pb:T:1.0345} {note:kudhārihattho (ka.)} puriso, vanamogayha tiṭṭhasi;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ dāruṃ chetumicchasi.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Isso {note:iso (sī.), īso (syā. pī.)} vanāni carasi, samāni visamāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Neva sālo na khadiro, nāssakaṇṇo kuto dhavo;
::

::gathalast
Rukkho ca {note:rukkhova (sī. pī.)} phandano nāma, taṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Kīdisānissa pattāni, khandho vā pana kīdiso;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, yathā jānemu phandanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa sākhā palambanti, namanti na ca bhañjare;
::

::gathalast
So rukkho phandano nāma, yassa mūle ahaṃ ṭhito.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Arānaṃ cakkanābhīnaṃ, īsānemirathassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Sabbassa te kammaniyo, ayaṃ hessati phandano.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Iti phandanarukkhopi, tāvade ajjhabhāsatha;
::

::gathalast
Mayhampi vacanaṃ atthi, bhāradvāja suṇohi me.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Issassa {note:imassa (ka. sī. ka.)} upakkhandhamhā {note:upakhandhamhā (ka. sī. pī. ka.)}, ukkacca caturaṅgulaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena nemiṃ pasāresi {note:pariharesi (sī. pī.)}, evaṃ daḷhataraṃ siyā.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Iti phandanarukkhopi, veraṃ appesi tāvade;
::

::gathalast
Jātānañca ajātānaṃ, issānaṃ dukkhamāvahi.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Iccevaṃ {pb:M:1.0260} {note:icceva (sī. pī.)} phandano issaṃ, isso ca pana phandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññaṃ {pb:T:1.0346} vivādena, aññamaññamaghātayuṃ.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva manussānaṃ, vivādo yattha jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Mayūranaccaṃ naccanti, yathā te issaphandanā.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:V:1.0201} vo vadāmi bhaddaṃ vo {note:bhaddante (ka.)}, yāvantettha samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Sammodatha mā vivadatha {note:māvivadittha (sī. syā. pī.)}, mā hotha issaphandanā.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Sāmaggimeva {note:sāmagyameva (syā. ka.)} sikkhetha, buddhehetaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaggirato dhammaṭṭho, yogakkhemā na dhaṃsatīti.
::

::centre
Phandanajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 476. Javanahaṃsajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Idheva haṃsa nipata, piyaṃ me tava dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Issarosi anuppatto, yamidhatthi pavedaya.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Savanena ekassa piyā bhavanti, disvā panekassa viyeti {note:vineti (syā.), viheti (pī.), vigeti (ka. aṭṭha.)} chando;
::

::gathalast
Disvā ca sutvā ca piyā bhavanti, kaccinnu me pīyasi {note:piyyasi (sī. pī.)} dassanena.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Savanena piyo mesi, bhiyyo cāgamma dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ piyadassano me {note:evaṃ piyadassano samāno (sī. syā. pī.)}, vasa haṃsa mamantike {note:mama santike (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Vaseyyāma tavāgāre, niccaṃ sakkatapūjitā;
::

::gathalast
Matto ca ekadā vajje {note:vajjā (sī. pī.)}, ‘‘haṃsarājaṃ pacantu me’’.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Dhiratthu {pb:T:1.0347} taṃ majjapānaṃ, yaṃ me piyataraṃ tayā;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi majjaṃ pissāmi {note:pivissāmi (syā.), pāyāmi (sī. pī.)}, yāva me vacchasī ghare.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Suvijānaṃ {pb:M:1.0261} siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañca {note:sakuntānañca (sī. syā. pī.)} vassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussavassitaṃ rāja, dubbijānataraṃ tato.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
::

::gathalast
Yo pubbe sumano hutvā, pacchā sampajjate diso.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmiṃ mano nivisati, avidūre sahāpi so;
::

::gathalast
Santikepi hi so dūre, yasmiṃ nāvisate {note:yasmā vivasate (sī. syā. pī.)} mano.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Antopi so hoti pasannacitto, pāraṃ samuddassa pasannacitto;
::

::gathalast
Antopi so hoti paduṭṭhacitto, pāraṃ samuddassa paduṭṭhacitto.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Saṃvasantā vivasanti, ye disā te rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Ārā santo saṃvasanti, manasā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Aticiraṃ nivāsena, piyo bhavati appiyo;
::

::gathalast
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma {note:gacchāmi (syā.)}, purā te homa appiyā {note:homi appiyo (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0202} ce yācamānānaṃ, añjaliṃ nāvabujjhasi;
::

::gatha2
Paricārakānaṃ sataṃ {note:santānaṃ (sī. syā.), sattānaṃ (pī.)}, vacanaṃ na karosi no;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ taṃ abhiyācāma, puna kayirāsi pariyāyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ ce no viharataṃ, antarāyo na hessati;
::

::gatha2
Tuyhañcāpi {pb:T:1.0348} {note:vāpi (syā. pī. ka.)} mahārāja, mayhañca {note:vā (bahūsu)} raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Appeva nāma passemu {note:passema (sī. syā. pī.)}, ahoratānamaccayeti.
::

::centre
Javanahaṃsajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 477. Cūḷanāradajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Na te kaṭṭhāni bhinnāni, na te udakamābhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aggīpi te na hāpito {note:hāsito (sī. syā.)}, kiṃ nu mandova jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0262} ussahe vane vatthuṃ, kassapāmantayāmi taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkho vāso araññasmiṃ, raṭṭhaṃ icchāmi gantave.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā ahaṃ ito gantvā, yasmiṃ janapade vasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ācāraṃ brahme {note:brahmaṃ (ka.)} sikkheyyaṃ, taṃ dhammaṃ anusāsa maṃ.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Sace araññaṃ hitvāna, vanamūlaphalāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhe rocayase vāsaṃ, taṃ dhammaṃ nisāmehi me.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Visaṃ mā paṭisevittho {note:paṭisevittha (syā. ka.)}, papātaṃ parivajjaya;
::

::gathalast
Paṅke ca mā visīdittho {note:paṅko ca mā visiyittho (ka.)}, yatto cāsīvise care.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu visaṃ papāto vā, paṅko vā brahmacārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kaṃ tvaṃ āsīvisaṃ brūsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito;
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Āsavo tāta lokasmiṃ, surā nāma pavuccati;
::

::gatha2
Manuñño {note:manuññā (sī. syā. pī.)} surabhī vaggu, sādu {note:madhu (sī. syā.)} khuddarasūpamo {note:rasūpamā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Visaṃ tadāhu ariyā se, brahmacariyassa nārada.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Itthiyo {pb:T:1.0349} tāta lokasmiṃ, pamattaṃ pamathenti tā;
::

::gatha2
Haranti yuvino cittaṃ, tūlaṃ bhaṭṭhaṃva māluto;
::

::gathalast
Papāto eso akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Lābho siloko sakkāro, pūjā parakulesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Paṅko eso ca {note:esova (sī. syā. pī.)} akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Sasatthā {pb:V:1.0203} {note:mahantā (syā. ka.)} tāta rājāno, āvasanti mahiṃ imaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te tādise manussinde, mahante tāta nārada.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Issarānaṃ adhipatīnaṃ, na tesaṃ pādato care;
::

::gathalast
Āsīvisoti {note:āsīviso so (sī. pī.)} akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Bhattattho bhattakāle ca {note:yaṃ (sī. pī.)}, yaṃ gehamupasaṅkame;
::

::gathalast
Yadettha kusalaṃ jaññā, tattha ghāsesanaṃ care.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Pavisitvā {pb:M:1.0263} parakulaṃ, pānatthaṃ {note:pānattho (syā. pī.)} bhojanāya vā;
::

::gathalast
Mitaṃ khāde mitaṃ bhuñje, na ca rūpe manaṃ kare.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Goṭṭhaṃ majjaṃ kirāṭañca {note:kirāsañca (sī. syā.), kirāsaṃ vā (pī.)}, sabhā nikiraṇāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Ārakā parivajjehi, yānīva visamaṃ pathanti.
::

::centre
Cūḷanāradajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 478. Dūtajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Dūte {pb:T:1.0350} te brahme {note:dūte brāhmaṇa (ka.)} pāhesiṃ, gaṅgātīrasmi jhāyato;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ puṭṭho na byākāsi, dukkhaṃ guyhamataṃ {note:guyhaṃ mataṃ (sī.), tuyhaṃ mataṃ (syā. ka.)} nu te.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Sace te dukkhamuppajje, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Mā kho naṃ tassa akkhāhi, yo taṃ dukkhā na mocaye.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yo tassa {note:yo ca tathā (pī.)} dukkhajātassa, ekaṅgamapi bhāgaso {note:ekantamapi bhāsato (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Vippamoceyya dhammena, kāmaṃ tassa pavedaya {note:pavedaye (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Suvijānaṃ siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañca vassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Manussavassitaṃ rāja, dubbijānataraṃ tato.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
::

::gathalast
Yo pubbe sumano hutvā, pacchā sampajjate diso.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Yo attano dukkhamanānupuṭṭho, pavedaye jantu akālarūpe;
::

::gathalast
Ānandino tassa bhavantimittā {note:bhavanta’mittā (sī. pī.)}, hitesino tassa dukhī bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Kālañca ñatvāna tathāvidhassa, medhāvīnaṃ ekamanaṃ viditvā;
::

::gathalast
Akkheyya tibbāni {note:tippāni (sī. syā. pī.)} parassa dhīro, saṇhaṃ giraṃ atthavatiṃ pamuñce.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:T:1.0351}{pb:M:1.0264} ca jaññā avisayhamattano, na te hi mayhaṃ {note:nāyaṃ nīti mayha (sī. pī.)} sukhāgamāya;
::

::gathalast
Ekova tibbāni saheyya dhīro, saccaṃ hirottappamapekkhamāno.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ {pb:V:1.0204} raṭṭhāni vicaranto, nigame rājadhāniyo;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhamāno mahārāja, ācariyassa dhanatthiko.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Gahapatī rājapurise, mahāsāle ca brāhmaṇe;
::

::gatha2
Alatthaṃ satta nikkhāni, suvaṇṇassa janādhipa;
::

::gathalast
Te me naṭṭhā mahārāja, tasmā socāmahaṃ bhusaṃ.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Purisā te mahārāja, manasānuvicintitā;
::

::gathalast
Nālaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ, tasmā tesaṃ na byāhariṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Tvañca kho me mahārāja, manasānuvicintito;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ, tasmā tuyhaṃ pavedayiṃ.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Tassādāsi pasannatto, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Jātarūpamaye nikkhe, suvaṇṇassa catuddasāti.
::

::centre
Dūtajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 479. Kāliṅgabodhijātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Rājā {pb:T:1.0352} kāliṅgo cakkavatti, dhammena pathavimanusāsaṃ {note:manusāsi (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Agamā {note:agamāsi (syā. ka.)} bodhisamīpaṃ, nāgena mahānubhāvena.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Kāliṅgo bhāradvājo ca, rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ samaṇakolaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cakkaṃ vattayato pariggahetvā {note:pariṇetvā (pī.)}, pañjalī idamavoca.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Paccoroha mahārāja, bhūmibhāgo yathā samaṇuggato {note:samanugīto (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Idha anadhivarā buddhā, abhisambuddhā virocanti.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Padakkhiṇato {pb:M:1.0265} āvaṭṭā, tiṇalatā asmiṃ bhūmibhāgasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pathaviyā nābhiyaṃ {note:puthuviyā ayaṃ (sī.), paṭhaviyā ayaṃ (syā.), puthaviyā’yaṃ (pī.)} maṇḍo, iti no sutaṃ mante mahārāja {note:sutaṃ mahārāja (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Sāgarapariyantāya, mediniyā sabbabhūtadharaṇiyā;
::

::gathalast
Pathaviyā ayaṃ maṇḍo, orohitvā namo karohi.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Ye te bhavanti nāgā ca, abhijātā ca kuñjarā;
::

::gathalast
Ettāvatā padesaṃ te, nāgā neva mupayanti.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Abhijāto nāgo {note:abhijāto te nāgo (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)} kāmaṃ, pesehi kuñjaraṃ dantiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ettāvatā padeso {note:padeso ca (syā. ka.)}, sakkā {note:na sakkā (syā.)} nāgena mupagantuṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ sutvā rājā kāliṅgo, veyyañjanikavaco nisāmetvā;
::

::gathalast
Sampesesi nāgaṃ ñassāma, mayaṃ yathimassidaṃ {note:yathā idaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vacanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Sampesito {pb:V:1.0205} ca raññā, nāgo koñcova abhinaditvāna;
::

::gathalast
Paṭisakkitvā {pb:T:1.0353} {note:paṭiosakkitvā (ka.)} nisīdi, garuṃva bhāraṃ asahamāno.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Kāliṅgabhāradvājo, nāgaṃ khīṇāyukaṃ viditvāna;
::

::gatha2
Rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ, taramāno ajjhabhāsittha;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ saṅkama nāgaṃ, nāgo khīṇāyuko mahārāja.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ sutvā kāliṅgo, taramāno saṅkamī nāgaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saṅkanteva raññe, nāgo tattheva pati {note:patito (ka.)} bhumyā;
::

::gathalast
Veyyañjanikavaco, yathā tathā ahu nāgo.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Kāliṅgo rājā kāliṅgaṃ, brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca;
::

::gathalast
Tvameva asi sambuddho, sabbaññū sabbadassāvī.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ anadhivāsento kāliṅgaṃ {note:kāliṅgo (sī. syā. pī.)}, brāhmaṇo idamavoca;
::

::gathalast
Veyyañjanikā hi mayaṃ, buddhā sabbaññuno mahārāja.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaññū sabbavidū ca, buddhā na lakkhaṇena jānanti;
::

::gathalast
Āgamabalasā {note:āgamapurisā (pī.)} hi mayaṃ, buddhā sabbaṃ pajānanti.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Mahayitvā {pb:M:1.0266} sambodhiṃ {note:mahāyitvāna sambodhiṃ (sī. pī.), pahaṃsitvāna sambodhiṃ (syā.), mamāyitvāna taṃ bodhiṃ (ka.)}, nānāturiyehi vajjamānehi;
::

::gathalast
Mālāvilepanaṃ abhiharitvā {note:mālāgandhavilepanaṃ āharitvā (sī. pī.); pākāraparikkhepaṃ kāresi; atha rājā pāyāsi (sī. syā. pī.)} atha rājā manupāyāsi {note:pākāraparikkhepaṃ kāresi; atha rājā pāyāsi (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Saṭṭhi vāhasahassāni, pupphānaṃ sannipātayi;
::

::gathalast
Pūjesi {pb:T:1.0354} rājā kāliṅgo, bodhimaṇḍamanuttaranti {note:varuttameti (sī.)}.
::

::centre
Kāliṅgabodhijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.
::

#### 480. Akittijātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Akittiṃ {note:akattiṃ (ka.)} disvā sammantaṃ, sakko bhūtapatī bravi;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ patthayaṃ mahābrahme, eko sammasi ghammani.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Dukkho punabbhavo sakka, sarīrassa ca bhedanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sammohamaraṇaṃ dukkhaṃ, tasmā sammāmi vāsava.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Yena putte ca dāre ca, dhanadhaññaṃ piyāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Laddhā narā na {note:laddhā naññāni (ka.)} tappanti, so lobho na mayī vase.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ {pb:V:1.0206} te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ {pb:T:1.0355} kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññañca, gavassaṃ dāsaporisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yena jātena jīyanti, so doso na mayī vase.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ {pb:M:1.0267} ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Bālaṃ na passe na suṇe, na ca bālena saṃvase;
::

::gathalast
Bālenallāpa {note:bālenā’lāpa (?)} sallāpaṃ, na kare na ca rocaye.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu te akaraṃ bālo, vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kena kassapa bālassa, dassanaṃ nābhikaṅkhasi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Anayaṃ nayati dummedho, adhurāyaṃ niyuñjati;
::

::gatha2
Dunnayo seyyaso hoti, sammā vutto pakuppati;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ so na jānāti, sādhu tassa adassanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gatha2
Dhīraṃ passe suṇe dhīraṃ, dhīrena saha saṃvase;
::

::gathalast
Dhīrenallāpasallāpaṃ, taṃ kare tañca rocaye.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ nu te akaraṃ dhīro, vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kena kassapa dhīrassa, dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhasi.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Nayaṃ nayati medhāvī, adhurāyaṃ na yuñjati;
::

::gatha2
Sunayo seyyaso hoti, sammā vutto na kuppati;
::

::gathalast
Vinayaṃ so pajānāti, sādhu tena samāgamo.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast
Varaṃ {pb:T:1.0356} kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gathalast
Tato ratyā vivasāne {note:vivasane (sī. syā. pī.)}, sūriyuggamanaṃ {note:suriyassuggamanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} pati;
::

::gathalast
Dibbā bhakkhā pātubhaveyyuṃ, sīlavanto ca yācakā.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Dadato {pb:V:1.0207} me {note:dadato ca me (pī.)} na khīyetha, datvā nānutapeyyahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dadaṃ cittaṃ pasādeyyaṃ, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ {pb:M:1.0268} te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
::

::gathalast
Na maṃ puna upeyyāsi, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vare.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Bahūhi vatacariyāhi {note:vattacariyāhi (sī. syā. ka.)}, narā ca atha nāriyo;
::

::gathalast
Dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhanti, kiṃ nu me dassane bhayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tādisaṃ devavaṇṇaṃ {note:devavaṇṇiṃ (pī.)}, sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Disvā tapo pamajjeyya {note:disvā tapo pamajjeyyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), disvānahaṃ pamajjeyyaṃ (cariyāpiṭakaṭṭhakathā)}, etaṃ te dassane bhayanti.
::

::centre
Akittijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 481. Takkāriyajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Ahameva dubbhāsitaṃ bhāsi bālo, bhekovaraññe ahimavhāyamāno {note:mavhayāno (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Takkāriye sobbhamimaṃ {note:sobbhamhi ahaṃ (ka.)} patāmi, na {pb:T:1.0357} kireva sādhu ativelabhāṇī {note:sādhūtyativelabhāṇī (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Pappoti macco ativelabhāṇī, bandhaṃ vadhaṃ sokapariddavañca;
::

::gathalast
Attānameva garahāsi ettha, ācera yaṃ taṃ nikhaṇanti sobbhe.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Kimevahaṃ tuṇḍilamanupucchiṃ, kareyya saṃ {note:kareyyāsaṃ (syā.), kareyya sa (ka.), bhareyya saṃ (?)} bhātaraṃ kāḷikāyaṃ {note:kāḷikāya (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Naggovahaṃ {note:naggoca’haṃ (?)} vatthayugañca jīno, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:M:1.0269} yujjhamānānamayujjhamāno {note:yujjhamānena ayujjhamāno (ka.)}, meṇḍantaraṃ accupatī kuliṅgo;
::

::gathalast
So piṃsito meṇḍasirehi tattha, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Caturo janā potthakamaggahesuṃ, ekañca posaṃ anurakkhamānā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva te bhinnasirā sayiṃsu, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Ajā yathā veḷugumbasmiṃ baddhā {note:bandhaṃ (syā. ka.)}, avakkhipantī asimajjhagacchi;
::

::gathalast
Teneva {pb:T:1.0358} tassā galakāvakantaṃ {note:galayā vikantuṃ (ka.), galakaṃ vikantā (syā.)}, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Ime na devā na gandhabbaputtā, migā ime atthavasaṃ gatā me {note:atthavasābhatā ime (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ekañca naṃ sāyamāse pacantu, ekaṃ punappātarāse {note:ekañca naṃ pātarāse (ka. sī. pī.)} pacantu.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Sataṃ sahassāni dubhāsitāni, kalampi nāgghanti subhāsitassa;
::

::gathalast
Dubbhāsitaṃ saṅkamāno kileso {note:kilissati (?)}, tasmā tuṇhī kimpurisā {note:kiṃpuriso (sī. syā.)} na bālyā.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Yā {pb:V:1.0208} mesā byāhāsi {note:byākāsi (sī. syā. pī.)} pamuñcathetaṃ, giriñca naṃ {note:giriṃ varaṃ (ka.)} himavantaṃ nayantu;
::

::gathalast
Imañca kho dentu mahānasāya, pātova naṃ pātarāse pacantu.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Pajjunnanāthā {pb:M:1.0270} pasavo, pasunāthā ayaṃ pajā;
::

::gathalast
Tvaṃ nāthosi {note:tvaṃ-nātho’smi (sī. syā. pī.)} mahārāja, nāthohaṃ bhariyāya me {note:amha-nāthā mama bhariyā (ka. sī. syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Dvinnamaññataraṃ ñatvā, mutto gaccheyya pabbataṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Na ve nindā suparivajjayetha {note:suparivajjayātha (syā.)}, nānā {pb:T:1.0359} janā sevitabbā janinda;
::

::gathalast
Yeneva eko labhate pasaṃsaṃ, teneva añño labhate ninditāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbo loko paricitto aticitto {note:paracittena aticitto (sī. syā.), paracittena acitto (sī. aṭṭha.)}, sabbo loko cittavā samhi citte;
::

::gathalast
Paccekacittā puthu sabbasattā, kassīdha cittassa vase na vatte.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Tuṇhī ahū kimpuriso sabhariyo {note:abhāṇī (ka.)}, yo dāni byāhāsi bhayassa bhīto;
::

::gathalast
So dāni mutto sukhito arogo, vācākirevattavatī narānanti.
::

::centre
Takkāriyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 482. Rurumigarājajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa {note:kassa (sī. pī.)} gāmavaraṃ dammi, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Yo {note:ko (sī. syā. pī.)} metaṃ migamakkhāti {note:makkhāsi (syā. ka.)}, migānaṃ migamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Mayhaṃ gāmavaraṃ dehi, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ te migamakkhissaṃ, migānaṃ migamuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Etasmiṃ vanasaṇḍasmiṃ, ambā sālā ca pupphitā;
::

::gathalast
Indagopakasañchannā{pb:T:1.0360}, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Dhanuṃ advejjhaṃ {note:adejjhaṃ (sī. pī.), sarajjaṃ (ka.)} katvāna, usuṃ sannayhupāgami {note:sandhāyupāgami (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Migo ca disvā rājānaṃ, dūrato ajjhabhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Āgamehi {pb:M:1.0271} mahārāja, mā maṃ vijjhi rathesabha;
::

::gathalast
Ko nu te idamakkhāsi, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Esa pāpacaro poso, samma tiṭṭhati ārakā;
::

::gathalast
Soyaṃ {note:so hi (sī. syā. pī.)} me idamakkhāsi, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Saccaṃ kireva māhaṃsu, narā ekacciyā idha;
::

::gathalast
Kaṭṭhaṃ niplavitaṃ seyyo, na tvevekacci yo naro.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ {pb:V:1.0209} nu ruru garahasi migānaṃ, kiṃ pakkhīnaṃ kiṃ pana mānusānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhayañhi maṃ vindatinapparūpaṃ, sutvāna taṃ mānusiṃ bhāsamānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Yamuddhariṃ vāhane vuyhamānaṃ, mahodake salile sīghasote;
::

::gathalast
Tatonidānaṃ bhayamāgataṃ mama, dukkho have rāja asabbhi saṅgamo.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ catuppattamimaṃ vihaṅgamaṃ, tanucchidaṃ hadaye ossajāmi;
::

::gathalast
Hanāmi {pb:T:1.0361} taṃ mittadubbhiṃ akiccakāriṃ {note:hanāmi mittaddu’makiccakāriṃ (sī. pī.)}, yo tādisaṃ kammakataṃ na jāne.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Dhīrassa bālassa have janinda, santo vadhaṃ nappasaṃsanti jātu;
::

::gatha2
Kāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo, yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dehi;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca te kāmakaro bhavāmi.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā ruru aññataro sataṃ so {note:sataṃ’se (sī.)}, yo dubbhato {note:dubbhino (syā.), dūbhato (pī.)} mānusassa na dubbhi;
::

::gatha2
Kāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo, yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dammi;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Suvijānaṃ {pb:M:1.0272} siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañcavassitaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ janapado māsi, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
::

::gathalast
Na tvevāhaṃ ruruṃ dubbhe, datvā abhayadakkhiṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
133\.

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0362} me janapado āsi {note:mā maṃ janapado ahu (syā.)}, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
::

::gathalast
Na tvevāhaṃ {note:na tveva (ka. sī. ka.)} migarājassa, varaṃ datvā musā bhaṇeti.

::centre

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Sarabhaṃ {pb:T:1.0363} giriduggasmiṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ anusarī pure;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
Yo taṃ viduggā narakā samuddhari, silāya yoggaṃ sarabho karitvā;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhūpanītaṃ maccumukhā pamocayi, alīnacittaṃ taṃ migaṃ {note:tameva (syā. ka.)} vadesi.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ tvaṃ nu {note:tuvannu (sī. pī.)} tattheva tadā ahosi, udāhu te koci naṃ {note:taṃ (ka.)} etadakkhā;
::

::gathalast
Vivaṭṭacchaddo nusi sabbadassī, ñāṇaṃ nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
Na cevahaṃ tattha tadā ahosiṃ, na cāpi me koci naṃ {note:taṃ (ka.)} etadakkhā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
Ādāya pattiṃ {note:pattaṃ (syā.), paṭṭiṃ (ka.)} paraviriyaghātiṃ, cāpe saraṃ kiṃ vicikicchase tuvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nunno {note:nuṇṇo (ka. sī. syā.), tuṇṇo (ka.)} saro sarabhaṃ hantu khippaṃ, annañhi etaṃ varapañña rañño.
::

::hangnum
145\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Pubbe {pb:T:1.0364} katañca {note:pubbe ca kataṃ (ka.)} apacāyamāno, tasmā migaṃ sarabhaṃ no hanāmi.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Neso migo mahārāja, asureso disampati;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ hantvā manussinda, bhavassu amarādhipo.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:M:1.0274} ca rājā {note:rāja (sī. syā. pī.)} vicikicchase tuvaṃ, hantuṃ migaṃ sarabhaṃ sahāyakaṃ {note:sahāyakaṃ me (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Saputtadāro naravīraseṭṭha {note:naraviriyaseṭṭha (sī. pī.)}, gantvā {note:gantā (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)} tuvaṃ vetaraṇiṃ yamassa.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmaṃ ahaṃ jānapadā ca sabbe, puttā ca dārā ca sahāyasaṅghā;
::

::gathalast
Gacchemu taṃ vetaraṇiṃ yamassa, na tveva hañño mama pāṇado yo {note:pāṇada’ssa (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Ayaṃ migo kicchagatassa mayhaṃ, ekassa kattā vivanasmi ghore;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Mittābhirādhī {pb:V:1.0211} cirameva jīva, rajjaṃ imaṃ dhammaguṇe {note:rajjampimaṃ cassa gaṇe (ka.)} pasāsa;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
151\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::centre

::centre

::gatha1

### 14. Pakiṇṇakanipāto

#### 484. Sālikedārajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Sampannaṃ {pb:T:1.0366}{pb:V:1.0212}{pb:M:1.0276} sālikedāraṃ, suvā bhuñjanti kosiya;
::

::gathalast
Paṭivedemi te brahme, na ne {note:te (sī. syā.), naṃ (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.), taṃ (ka. aṭṭha.)} vāretumussahe.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Eko ca tattha sakuṇo, yo nesaṃ {note:tesaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.)} sabbasundaro;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, tuṇḍenādāya gacchati.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Oḍḍentu {note:ujjhuntu (syā. ka.) aṅguttaranikāye passitabbaṃ} vāḷapāsāni, yathā vajjhetha so dijo;
::

::gathalast
Jīvañca naṃ gahetvāna, ānayehi {note:ānayetha (sī. pī.)} mamantike.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Ete bhutvā pivitvā ca {note:bhutvā ca pitvā ca (pī.)}, pakkamanti vihaṅgamā;
::

::gathalast
Eko baddhosmi pāsena, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Udaraṃ nūna aññesaṃ, suva accodaraṃ tava;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, tuṇḍenādāya gacchasi.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Koṭṭhaṃ nu tattha pūresi, suva veraṃ nu te mayā;
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kuhiṃ sāliṃ nidāhasi {note:nidhīyasi (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Na me veraṃ tayā saddhiṃ, koṭṭho mayhaṃ na vijjati;
::

::gatha2
Iṇaṃ muñcāmiṇaṃ dammi, sampatto koṭasimbaliṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nidhimpi tattha nidahāmi, evaṃ jānāhi kosiya.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Kīdisaṃ te iṇadānaṃ, iṇamokkho ca kīdiso;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Ajātapakkhā taruṇā, puttakā mayha kosiya;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ bhatā bharissanti, tasmā tesaṃ iṇaṃ dade.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Mātā pitā ca me vuddhā, jiṇṇakā gatayobbanā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ tuṇḍena hātūna, muñce pubbakataṃ {note:pubbe kataṃ (sī.)} iṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Aññepi {pb:M:1.0277} tattha sakuṇā, khīṇapakkhā sudubbalā;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ puññatthiko dammi, taṃ nidhiṃ āhu paṇḍitā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Īdisaṃ {pb:V:1.0213} {note:edisaṃ (sī. pī.)} me iṇadānaṃ, iṇamokkho ca īdiso;
::

::gathalast
Nidhinidhānamakkhāmi {note:nidhiṃ nidhānaṃ akkhātaṃ (sī. pī.)}, evaṃ jānāhi kosiya.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaddako vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo paramadhammiko;
::

::gathalast
Ekaccesu manussesu, ayaṃ dhammo na vijjati.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Bhuñja sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Punāpi suva passemu, piyaṃ me tava dassanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Bhuttañca pītañca tavassamamhi {note:tavassabyamhi (ka.)}, rattiñca {note:ratī ca (sī. pī.)} no kosiya te sakāse;
::

::gathalast
Nikkhittadaṇḍesu dadāhi dānaṃ, jiṇṇe ca mātāpitaro bharassu.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Lakkhī vata me udapādi ajja, yo addasāsiṃ pavaraṃ {note:yohaṃ adassaṃ paramaṃ (syā. ka.)} dijānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suvassa sutvāna subhāsitāni, kāhāmi {pb:T:1.0368} puññāni anappakāni.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Annena pānena pasannacitto, santappayi samaṇabrāhmaṇe cāti.

::centre

#### 485. Candakinnarījātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Upanīyatidaṃ maññe, cande {note:lohitamadena majjāmi; vijahāmi jīvitaṃ pāṇā, (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)} lohitamaddane;
::

::gathalast
Ajja jahāmi jīvitaṃ, pāṇā {note:lohitamadena majjāmi; vijahāmi jīvitaṃ pāṇā, (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)} me cande nirujjhanti.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Osīdi {pb:M:1.0278} {note:osadhi (sī. syā. pī.), osaṭṭhi (ka.), osati (abhinavaṭīkā), osīdati (?)} me dukkhaṃ {note:dukkhaṃ me (sī. pī.)} hadayaṃ, me ḍayhate nitammāmi;
::

::gathalast
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Tiṇamiva vanamiva milāyāmi {note:milayāmi (sī.), miyyāmi (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)}, nadī aparipuṇṇāva {note:aparipuṇṇiyāva (sī. pī.)} sussāmi;
::

::gathalast
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Pāpo khosi {note:pāposi kho (sī.), pāpo kho (syā. pī.)} rājaputta, yo me icchitaṃ {note:icchita (sī. syā. pī.)} patiṃ varākiyā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Imaṃ mayhaṃ hadayasokaṃ, paṭimuñcatu rājaputta tava mātā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
24\.

::gatha1

::gathalast
Yo {pb:T:1.0369} mayhaṃ hadayasoko, kimpurisaṃ avekkhamānāya.
::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi, adūsakaṃ mayha kāmā hi {note:mayhaṃ kāmā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
27\.

::gatha1

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:M:1.0279} pabbatā tā ca kandarā, {note:tā ca giriguhāyo (sī. syā. pī.)} tā ca giriguhāyo tatheva tiṭṭhanti {note:tā ca giriguhāyo (sī. syā. pī.)};

::gathalast

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Acchā savanti girivana {note:girivara (sī. pī.)} nadiyo, kusumābhikiṇṇasotāyo;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
::

::hangnum

::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::centre

#### 486. Mahāukkusajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Ukkā cilācā {note:milācā (sī. syā. pī.)} bandhanti dīpe {note:bandhanti luddā, dīpe (ka.)}, pajā mamaṃ khādituṃ patthayanti;
::

::gathalast
Mittaṃ sahāyañca vadehi senaka, ācikkha ñātibyasanaṃ dijānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Dijo dijānaṃ pavarosi pakkhima {note:pakkhi (sī. pī.), pakkhi ca (syā.)}, ukkusarāja saraṇaṃ taṃ upema {note:upemi (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pajā mamaṃ khādituṃ patthayanti, luddā cilācā {note:milācā (sī. syā. pī.)} bhava me sukhāya.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā, kāle akāle sukhamesamānā {note:māsayānā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ, ariyo {pb:T:1.0372} hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ hoti kiccaṃ anukampakena, ariyassa ariyena kataṃ tayīdaṃ {note:tava yidaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Attānurakkhī bhava mā adayhi {note:aḍayha (sī. pī.)}, lacchāma putte tayi jīvamāne.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Taveva {pb:M:1.0281} {note:tameva (syā. ka.)} rakkhāvaraṇaṃ karonto, sarīrabhedāpi na santasāmi;
::

::gathalast
Karonti heke {note:hete (ka. sī. syā. pī.)} sakhīnaṃ sakhāro, pāṇaṃ cajantā {note:cajanti (sī. pī.)} satamesa {note:satānesa (pī.)} dhammo.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Sudukkaraṃ kammamakāsi {note:makā (sī. pī.)}, aṇḍajāyaṃ vihaṅgamo;
::

::gathalast
Atthāya kuraro putte, aḍḍharatte anāgate.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Cutāpi heke {note:eke (sī. pī.)} khalitā sakammunā, mittānukampāya patiṭṭhahanti;
::

::gathalast
Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi, atthaṃ caretho {note:caretha (sī. syā. pī.)} mama vāricara {note:vārichanna (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Dhanena dhaññena ca attanā ca, mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ, ariyo hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Appossukko tāta tuvaṃ nisīda, putto {pb:T:1.0373} pitu carati atthacariyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ carissāmi tavetamatthaṃ, senassa putte paritāyamāno.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā {pb:V:1.0216} hi tāta satamesa dhammo, putto pitu yaṃ care {note:pitunaṃ care (ka.), pitu yañcaretha (sī. pī.)} atthacariyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appeva maṃ disvāna pavaḍḍhakāyaṃ, senassa puttā na viheṭhayeyyuṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Pasū manussā migavīraseṭṭha {note:migaviriyaseṭṭha (sī. pī.)}, bhayaṭṭitā {note:bhayadditā (sī. pī.)} seṭṭhamupabbajanti;
::

::gathalast
Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi, tvaṃ nosi rājā bhava me sukhāya.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Karomi {pb:M:1.0282} te senaka etamatthaṃ, āyāmi te taṃ disataṃ vadhāya;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi viññū pahu sampajāno, na vāyame attajanassa guttiyā.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Mittañca kayirātha suhadayañca {note:suhaddayañca (sī.), sakhāgharañca (pī.)}, ayirañca kayirātha sukhāgamāya;
::

::gathalast
Nivatthakocova {note:kojova (sī. pī.)} sarebhihantvā, modāma puttehi samaṅgibhūtā.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Sakamittassa kammena, sahāyassāpalāyino;
::

::gathalast
Kūjantamupakūjanti{pb:T:1.0374}, lomasā hadayaṅgamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Mittaṃ sahāyaṃ adhigamma paṇḍito, so bhuñjatī putta pasuṃ dhanaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca puttā ca patī ca mayhaṃ, mittānukampāya samaṅgibhūtā.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Rājavatā sūravatā ca attho, sampannasakhissa bhavanti hete;
::

::gathalast
So mittavā yasavā uggatatto, asmiṃdhaloke {note:asmiñca loke (sī. syā. pī.)} modati kāmakāmī.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Karaṇīyāni mittāni, daliddenāpi senaka;
::

::gathalast
Passa mittānukampāya, samaggamhā sañātake {note:sañātakā (?)}.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Sūrena balavantena, yo mitte {note:mette (sī.), mittaṃ (syā.)} kurute dijo;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ so sukhito hoti, yathāhaṃ tvañca senakāti.
::

::centre
Mahāukkusajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 487. Uddālakajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Kharājinā {pb:M:1.0283} jaṭilā paṅkadantā, dummakkharūpā {note:dummudharūpā (sī. pī. ka.)} ye mantaṃ jappanti {note:yeme japanti (sī. pī.), ye’me jappanti mante (jā. 1.6.10)};
::

::gathalast
Kaccinnu te mānusake payoge, idaṃ vidū parimuttā apāyā.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Pāpāni {pb:T:1.0375} kammāni karetha {note:kareyya (syā.), katvāna (jā. 1.6.11)} rāja, bahussuto ce na careyya dhammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamucce {note:pamuñce (syā.)} caraṇaṃ apatvā.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamucce caraṇaṃ apatvā;
::

::gathalast
Maññāmi vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaññeva saccaṃ.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaññeva saccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kittiñhi {note:kittiñca (syā.)} pappoti adhicca vede, santiṃ puṇāti {note:punoti (sī. aṭṭha.), puṇeti (syā. jā. 1.6.13), puneti (pī.)} caraṇena danto.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaccā {pb:V:1.0217} mātā pitā bandhū, yena jāto sayeva so;
::

::gathalast
Uddālako ahaṃ bhoto {note:bhoti (ka.)}, sottiyākulavaṃsako {note:vaṃsato (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ bho brāhmaṇo hoti, kathaṃ bhavati kevalī;
::

::gathalast
Kathañca parinibbānaṃ, dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Niraṃkatvā {pb:M:1.0284} aggimādāya brāhmaṇo, āpo siñcaṃ yajaṃ usseti yūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃkaro brāhmaṇo hoti khemī, dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0376} suddhi secanenatthi, nāpi kevalī brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Na khantī nāpi soraccaṃ, nāpi so parinibbuto.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ so {note:bho (syā. ka.)} brāhmaṇo hoti, kathaṃ bhavati kevalī;
::

::gathalast
Kathañca parinibbānaṃ, dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Akhettabandhū amamo nirāso, nillobhapāpo bhavalobhakhīṇo;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃkaro brāhmaṇo hoti khemī, dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gatha2
Sabbeva soratā dantā, sabbeva parinibbutā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, atthi seyyotha {note:seyyova (sī. pī.)} pāpiyo.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gatha2
Sabbeva soratā dantā, sabbeva parinibbutā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, natthi seyyotha pāpiyo.

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, natthi seyyotha pāpiyo;
::

::gathalast
Panatthaṃ {note:pasatthaṃ (syā.), pasaṭṭhaṃ (ka.)} carasi brahmaññaṃ, sottiyākulavaṃsataṃ.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Nānārattehi vatthehi, vimānaṃ bhavati chāditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na tesaṃ chāyā vatthānaṃ, so rāgo anupajjatha.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Evameva {pb:T:1.0377}{pb:M:1.0285} {note:evamevaṃ (pī.)} manussesu, yadā sujjhanti māṇavā;
::

::gathalast
Te sajātiṃ pamuñcanti {note:na tesaṃ jātiṃ pucchanti (sī. syā. pī.), na tesaṃ jāti sujjhati (ka.)}, dhammamaññāya subbatāti.
::

::centre
Uddālakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 488. Bhisajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Assaṃ {pb:V:1.0218} gavaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ, bhariyañca so idha labhataṃ manāpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Puttehi dārehi samaṅgi hotu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Mālañca so kāsikacandanañca, dhāretu puttassa bahū bhavantu;
::

::gathalast
Kāmesu tibbaṃ kurutaṃ apekkhaṃ, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Pahūtadhañño kasimā yasassī, putte gihī dhanimā sabbakāme;
::

::gathalast
Vayaṃ apassaṃ gharamāvasātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
So khattiyo hotu pasayhakārī, rājābhirājā {note:rājādhirājā (syā. ka.)} balavā yasassī;
::

::gathalast
Sa {pb:T:1.0378} cāturantaṃ mahimāvasātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
So brāhmaṇo hotu avītarāgo, muhuttanakkhattapathesu yutto;
::

::gathalast
Pūjetu naṃ raṭṭhapatī yasassī, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjhāyakaṃ {pb:M:1.0286} sabbasamantavedaṃ {note:sabbasamattavedaṃ (sī.), sabbasamattavedanaṃ (pī.)}, tapassīnaṃ maññatu sabbaloko;
::

::gathalast
Pūjentu naṃ jānapadā samecca, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Catussadaṃ gāmavaraṃ samiddhaṃ, dinnañhi so bhuñjatu vāsavena;
::

::gathalast
Avītarāgo maraṇaṃ upetu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
So gāmaṇī hotu sahāyamajjhe, naccehi gītehi pamodamāno;
::

::gathalast
So rājato byasana mālattha {note:mā rājato vyasana’malattha (sī. syā. pī.)} kiñci, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ekarājā pathaviṃ vijetvā, itthīsahassāna {note:itthīsahassassa (sī. pī.)} ṭhapetu aggaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sīmantinīnaṃ {pb:T:1.0379} pavarā bhavātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yā ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Isīnañhi sā sabbasamāgatānaṃ, bhuñjeyya sāduṃ avikampamānā;
::

::gathalast
Carātu lābhena vikatthamānā, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yā ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Āvāsiko hotu mahāvihāre, navakammiko hotu gajaṅgalāyaṃ {note:kajaṅgalāyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Ālokasandhiṃ divasaṃ {note:divasā (sī. syā. pī.)} karotu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:M:1.0287} bajjhatū pāsasatehi chabbhi {note:chamhi (sī. pī.), chassu (?)}, rammā vanā niyyatu rājadhāniṃ {note:rājaṭhāniṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tuttehi so haññatu pācanehi, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Alakkamālī tipukaṇṇaviddho, laṭṭhīhato sappamukhaṃ upetu;
::

::gathalast
Sakacchabandho {note:sakkaccabaddho (sī. pī.), saṃkaccabandho (niyya)} visikhaṃ carātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve anaṭṭhaṃva {note:anaṭṭhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} naṭṭhanti cāha, kāmeva {pb:T:1.0380} so labhataṃ bhuñjatañca {note:labhatu bhuñjatu ca (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Agāramajjhe maraṇaṃ upetu, yo vā bhonto saṅkati kañcideva {note:kiñcideva (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Yadesamānā {pb:V:1.0219} vicaranti loke, iṭṭhañca kantañca bahūnametaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Piyaṃ manuññaṃ cidha jīvaloke, kasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmesu ve haññare bajjhare ca, kāmesu dukkhañca bhayañca jātaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmesu bhūtādhipatī pamattā, pāpāni kammāni karonti mohā.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Te pāpadhammā pasavetva pāpaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti;
::

::gathalast
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, tasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Vīmaṃsamāno isino bhisāni, tīre gahetvāna thale nidhesiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suddhā apāpā isayo vasanti, etāni te brahmacārī bhisāni.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0288} te naṭā no pana kīḷaneyyā, na {pb:T:1.0381} bandhavā no pana te sahāyā;
::

::gathalast
Kismiṃ vupatthambha sahassanetta, isīhi tvaṃ kīḷasi devarāja.
::

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Ācariyo mesi pitā ca mayhaṃ, esā patiṭṭhā khalitassa brahme;
::

::gathalast
Ekāparādhaṃ khama bhūripañña, na paṇḍitā kodhabalā bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Suvāsitaṃ isinaṃ ekarattaṃ, yaṃ vāsavaṃ bhūtapatiddasāma;
::

::gathalast
Sabbeva bhonto sumanā bhavantu, yaṃ brāhmaṇo paccupādī bhisāni.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Ahañca sāriputto ca, moggallāno ca kassapo;
::

::gathalast
Anuruddho puṇṇo ānando, tadāsuṃ satta bhātaro.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Bhaginī uppalavaṇṇā ca, dāsī khujjuttarā tadā;
::

::gathalast
Citto gahapati dāso, yakkho sātāgiro tadā.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Pālileyyo {note:pārileyyo (sī. pī.)} tadā nāgo, madhudo {note:madhuvā (sī. pī.)} seṭṭhavānaro;
::

::gathalast
Kāḷudāyī tadā sakko, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
::

::centre
Bhisajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.
::

#### 489. Surucijātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Mahesī {pb:T:1.0382} surucino {note:rucino (sī. syā. pī.)} bhariyā, ānītā paṭhamaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dasa vassasahassāni, yaṃ maṃ surucimānayi.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Sāhaṃ brāhmaṇa rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
::

::gatha2

::gathalast
Suruciṃ atimaññittha {note:atimaññittho (sī. pī.), atimaññitā (?)}, āvi {note:āviṃ (sī. pī.)} vā yadi vā raho.

#### 490. Pañcuposathikajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Appossukko {pb:M:1.0291} dāni tuvaṃ kapota, vihaṅgama na tava bhojanattho;
::

::gathalast
Khudaṃ {note:khuddaṃ (syā. ka.), khudhaṃ (sakkata-pākatānurūpaṃ)} pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā bhavaṃposathiko kapota {note:kapoto (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ pure giddhigato kapotiyā, asmiṃ padesasmimubho ramāma;
::

::gathalast
Athaggahī sākuṇiko kapotiṃ, akāmako tāya vinā ahosiṃ.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Nānābhavā vippayogena tassā, manomayaṃ vedana vedayāmi {note:vedanaṃ vediyāmi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, rāgo mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Anujjugāmī uragā dujivha {note:uraga dvijivha (sī.)}, dāṭhāvudho ghoravisosi sappa;
::

::gathalast
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā {pb:T:1.0385} bhavaṃposathiko nu dīgha {note:dīgho (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Usabho ahū balavā gāmikassa, calakkakū vaṇṇabalūpapanno;
::

::gathalast
So maṃ akkami taṃ kupito aḍaṃsi, dukkhābhituṇṇo maraṇaṃ upāgā {note:upāgami (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:V:1.0222} janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā, kanditvā roditvā {note:kanditva roditva (sī.)} apakkamiṃsu;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, kodho {pb:T:1.0386} mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Matāna {pb:M:1.0292} maṃsāni bahū susāne, manuññarūpaṃ tava bhojane taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā bhavaṃposathiko siṅgāla {note:sigālo (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Pavisi {note:pavissaṃ (sī. pī.), pavissa (syā.)} kucchiṃ mahato gajassa, kuṇape rato hatthimaṃsesu giddho {note:hatthimaṃse pagiddho (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Uṇho ca vāto tikhiṇā ca rasmiyo, te sosayuṃ tassa karīsamaggaṃ.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Kiso ca paṇḍū ca ahaṃ bhadante, na me ahū nikkhamanāya maggo;
::

::gathalast
Mahā ca megho sahasā pavassi, so temayī tassa karīsamaggaṃ.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Tato ahaṃ nikkhamisaṃ bhadante, cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutto;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, lobho mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Vammīkathūpasmiṃ kipillikāni, nippothayanto tuvaṃ pure carāsi;
::

::gathalast
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā {pb:T:1.0387} bhavaṃposathiko nu accha {note:accho (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Sakaṃ niketaṃ atihīḷayāno {note:atiheḷayāno (syā. ka.)}, atricchatā {note:atricchatāya (sī. syā. pī.)} mallagāmaṃ {note:malataṃ (sī. pī.), mallayataṃ (ka.)} agacchiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā, kodaṇḍakena paripothayiṃsu maṃ.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
So {pb:M:1.0293} bhinnasīso ruhiramakkhitaṅgo, paccāgamāsiṃ sakaṃ {note:sa sakaṃ (syā. ka.),’tha sakaṃ (?)} niketaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, atricchatā mā punarāgamāsi.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
141\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
142\.

::gathalast

#### 491. Mahāmorajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
Sace hi tyāhaṃ dhanahetu gāhito, mā maṃ vadhī jīvagāhaṃ gahetvā;
::

::gathalast
Rañño ca {note:raññova (sī. pī.)} maṃ samma upantikaṃ {note:upanti (sī. syā. pī.)} nehi, maññe dhanaṃ lacchasinapparūpaṃ.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
Na me ayaṃ tuyha vadhāya ajja, samāhito cāpadhure {note:cāpavare (sī. pī.), cāpavaro (syā.)} khurappo;
::

::gathalast
Pāsañca tyāhaṃ adhipātayissaṃ, yathāsukhaṃ gacchatu morarājā.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0223}{pb:M:1.0294} satta vassāni mamānubandhi, rattindivaṃ khuppipāsaṃ sahanto;
::

::gathalast
Atha kissa maṃ pāsavasūpanītaṃ, pamuttave {pb:T:1.0389} icchasi bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
146\ .
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātā virato nusajja, abhayaṃ nu te sabbabhūtesu dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ maṃ tuvaṃ pāsavasūpanītaṃ, pamuttave icchasi bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūhi, abhayañca yo sabbabhūtesu deti;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ morarājetamatthaṃ, ito cuto kiṃ labhate sukhaṃ so.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūmi, abhayañca yo sabbabhūtesu deti;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭheva dhamme labhate pasaṃsaṃ, saggañca so yāti sarīrabhedā.
::

::hangnum
149\.
::

::gatha1
Na santi devā iti āhu {note:iccāhu (sī. pī.)} eke, idheva jīvo vibhavaṃ upeti;
::

::gatha2
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattañca vadanti dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tesaṃ vaco arahataṃ saddahāno, tasmā ahaṃ sakuṇe bādhayāmi.
::

::hangnum
150\.
::

::gatha1
Cando ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā, gacchanti obhāsayamantalikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Imassa lokassa parassa vā te, kathaṃ nu te āhu manussaloke.
::

::hangnum
151\.
::

::gatha1
Cando {pb:M:1.0295} ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā, gacchanti {pb:T:1.0390} obhāsayamantalikkhe;
::

::gathalast
Parassa lokassa na te imassa, devāti te āhu manussaloke.
::

::hangnum
152\.
::

::gatha1
Ettheva te nīhatā hīnavādā, ahetukā ye na vadanti kammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattaṃ ye ca vadanti dānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
153\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavedaṃ {note:tavetaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, kathañhi dānaṃ aphalaṃ bhaveyya {note:vadeyya (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattañca kathaṃ bhaveyya.
::

::hangnum
154\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃkaro kintikaro kimācaraṃ, kiṃ sevamāno kena tapoguṇena;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi {note:akkhāhi taṃ dāni (ka.)} me morarājetamatthaṃ, yathā ahaṃ no nirayaṃ pateyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
155\.
::

::gatha1
Ye keci atthi samaṇā pathabyā, kāsāyavatthā anagāriyā te;
::

::gathalast
Pātova piṇḍāya caranti kāle, vikālacariyā viratā hi santo.
::

::hangnum
156\.
::

::gatha1
Te tattha kālenupasaṅkamitvā, pucchāhi {pb:T:1.0391} yaṃ te manaso piyaṃ siyā;
::

::gathalast
Te te pavakkhanti yathāpajānaṃ, imassa lokassa parassa catthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
157\.
::

::gatha1
Tacaṃva jiṇṇaṃ urago purāṇaṃ, paṇḍūpalāsaṃ harito dumova;
::

::gathalast
Esappahīno mama luddabhāvo, jahāmahaṃ luddakabhāvamajja.
::

::hangnum
158\.
::

::gatha1
Ye {pb:M:1.0296} cāpi me sakuṇā atthi baddhā, satāninekāni nivesanasmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tesampahaṃ {note:tesaṃ ahaṃ (syā. ka.)} jīvitamajja dammi, mokkhañca te pattā {note:patto (sī.), accha (syā.)} sakaṃ niketaṃ.
::

::hangnum
159\.
::

::gatha1
Luddo {pb:V:1.0224} carī pāsahattho araññe, bādhetu morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bandhitvā {note:bandhitva (sī. pī.)} morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ, dukkhā sa pamucci {note:dukkhā pamucci (sī.), dukkhā pamuñci (syā. pī.)} yathāhaṃ pamuttoti.
::

::centre
Mahāmorajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.
