#### 492. Tacchasūkarajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
160\.
::

::gatha1
Yadesamānā vicarimha, pabbatāni vanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Anvesaṃ {pb:T:1.0392} vicariṃ {note:vipule (syā. ka.)} ñātī, teme adhigatā mayā.
::

::hangnum
161\.
::

::gatha1
Bahuñcidaṃ mūlaphalaṃ, bhakkho cāyaṃ anappako;
::

::gathalast
Rammā cimā girīnajjo {note:girinadiyo (sī. pī.)}, phāsuvāso bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
162\.
::

::gatha1
Idhevāhaṃ vasissāmi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
::

::gathalast
Appossukko nirāsaṅkī, asoko akutobhayo.
::

::hangnum
163\.
::

::gatha1
Aññampi {note:aññaṃ hi (sī. pī.)} leṇaṃ pariyesa, sattu no idha vijjati;
::

::gathalast
So taccha sūkare hanti, idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
164\.
::

::gatha1
Ko numhākaṃ {note:ko namhākaṃ (sī. pī.)} idha sattu, ko ñātī susamāgate;
::

::gathalast
Duppadhaṃse {note:appadhaṃse (sī. pī.)} padhaṃseti, taṃ me akkhātha pucchitā.
::

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1
Uddhaggarājī migarājā, balī dāṭhāvudho migo;
::

::gathalast
So taccha sūkare hanti, idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1
Na no dāṭhā na vijjanti {note:nu vijjanti (ka.)}, balaṃ kāye samohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe samaggā hutvāna, vasaṃ kāhāma ekakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1
Hadayaṅgamaṃ {pb:M:1.0297} kaṇṇasukhaṃ, vācaṃ bhāsasi tacchaka;
::

::gathalast
Yopi yuddhe palāyeyya, tampi pacchā hanāmase.
::

::hangnum
168\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇātipātā virato nu ajja, abhayaṃ nu te sabbabhūtesu dinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dāṭhā nu te migavadhāya {note:miga viriyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} na santi, yo saṅghapatto kapaṇova jhāyasi.
::

::hangnum
169\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0393} me dāṭhā na vijjanti, balaṃ kāye samohitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ñātī ca disvāna sāmaggī ekato, tasmā ca jhāyāmi vanamhi ekako.
::

::hangnum
170\.
::

::gatha1
Imassudaṃ yanti disodisaṃ pure, bhayaṭṭitā leṇagavesino puthu;
::

::gathalast
Te dāni saṅgamma vasanti ekato, yatthaṭṭhitā duppasahajja te mayā.
::

::hangnum
171\.
::

::gatha1
Pariṇāyakasampannā, sahitā ekavādino;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ samaggā hiṃseyyuṃ, tasmā nesaṃ na patthaye {note:apatthave (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
172\.
::

::gatha1
Ekova {pb:V:1.0225} indo asure jināti, ekova seno hanti dije pasayha;
::

::gathalast
Ekova byaggho migasaṅghapatto, varaṃ varaṃ hanti balañhi tādisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
173\.
::

::gatha1
Na heva indo na seno, napi byaggho migādhipo;
::

::gathalast
Samagge sahite ñātī, na byagghe {note:byagghe ca (sī. pī.), byaggho na (syā.)} kurute vase.
::

::hangnum
174\.
::

::gatha1
Kumbhīlakā sakuṇakā, saṅghino gaṇacārino;
::

::gathalast
Sammodamānā ekajjhaṃ, uppatanti ḍayanti ca.
::

::hangnum
175\.
::

::gatha1
Tesañca ḍayamānānaṃ, ekettha apasakkati {note:apavattati (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Tañca seno nitāḷeti, veyyagghiyeva sā gati.
::

::hangnum
176\.
::

::gatha1
Ussāhito {pb:T:1.0394}{pb:M:1.0298} jaṭilena, luddenāmisacakkhunā;
::

::gathalast
Dāṭhī dāṭhīsu pakkhandi, maññamāno yathā pure.
::

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu sambahulā ñātī, api rukkhā araññajā;
::

::gathalast
Sūkarehi samaggehi, byaggho ekāyane hato.
::

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
Brāhmaṇañceva byagghañca, ubho hantvāna sūkarā.
::

::gathalast
Ānandino pamuditā, mahānādaṃ panādisuṃ.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
Te su udumbaramūlasmiṃ, sūkarā susamāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Tacchakaṃ abhisiñciṃsu, ‘‘tvaṃ no rājāsi issaro’’ti.
::

::centre
Tacchasūkarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 493. Mahāvāṇijajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
Vāṇijā samitiṃ katvā, nānāraṭṭhato āgatā;
::

::gathalast
Dhanāharā pakkamiṃsu, ekaṃ katvāna gāmaṇiṃ.
::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
Te taṃ kantāramāgamma, appabhakkhaṃ anodakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahānigrodhamaddakkhuṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ.
::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
Te ca tattha nisīditvā, tassa rukkhassa chāyayā {note:chādiyā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Vāṇijā samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
Allāyate {note:addāyate (sī. pī.)} ayaṃ rukkho, api vārīva {note:vāri ca (sī. pī.)} sandati;
::

::gathalast
Iṅghassa purimaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, acchaṃ vāriṃ anāvilaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te {pb:T:1.0395} tattha nhatvā pivitvā, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
Dutiyaṃ {pb:V:1.0226} samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
::

::gathalast
Iṅghassa dakkhiṇaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, sālimaṃsodanaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appodavaṇṇe kummāse, siṅgiṃ vidalasūpiyo {note:siṅgiṃ bidalasūpiyo (sī. pī.), siṅgīveraṃ lasūpiyo (ka.) siṅgīnti siṅgīverādikaṃ uttaribhaṅgaṃ; vidalasūpiyoti muggasūpādayo (aṭṭha.) vidalaṃ kalāyādimhi vattatīti sakkatābhidhāne}.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:M:1.0299} tattha bhutvā khāditvā {note:bhutvā ca pivitvā ca (pī.)}, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā;
::

::gatha2
Tatiyaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
::

::gathalast
Iṅghassa pacchimaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Vicitravatthābharaṇā, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
Api su vāṇijā ekā, nāriyo paṇṇavīsati;
::

::gathalast
Samantā parivāriṃsu {note:parikariṃsu (sī. syā. pī.)}, tassa rukkhassa chāyayā {note:chādiyā (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
Te tāhi paricāretvā {note:parivāretvā (sī. syā. pī.)}, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā;
::

::gatha2
Catutthaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
::

::gathalast
Iṅghassa uttaraṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Rajataṃ jātarūpañca, kuttiyo paṭiyāni ca.
::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
Kāsikāni ca vatthāni, uddiyāni ca kambalā {note:uddiyāne ca kambale (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Te tattha bhāre bandhitvā, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā.
::

::hangnum
193\.
::

::gatha1
Pañcamaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
::

::gathalast
Iṅghassa {pb:T:1.0396} mūle {note:mūlaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)} chindāma, api bhiyyo labhāmase.
::

::hangnum
194\.
::

::gatha1
Athuṭṭhahi satthavāho, yācamāno katañjalī;
::

::gathalast
Nigrodho kiṃ parajjhati {note:aparajjhatha (sī.), aparajjhati (syā. pī.)}, vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te.
::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
Vāridā purimā sākhā, annapānañca dakkhiṇā;
::

::gatha2
Nāridā pacchimā sākhā, sabbakāme ca uttarā;
::

::gathalast
Nigrodho kiṃ parajjhati, vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te.
::

::hangnum
196\.
::

::gatha1
Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
::

::gathalast
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
::

::hangnum
197\.
::

::gatha1
Te ca tassānādiyitvā {note:tassa anāditvā (sī. syā.)}, ekassa vacanaṃ bahū;
::

::gathalast
Nisitāhi kuṭhārīhi {note:kudhārīhi (ka.)}, mūlato naṃ upakkamuṃ.
::

::hangnum
198\.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:V:1.0227}{pb:M:1.0300} nāgā nikkhamiṃsu, sannaddhā paṇṇavīsati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
199\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Ṭhapetvā satthavāhaṃva, sabbe bhasmaṃ {note:bhasmī (sī.)} karotha ne.
::

::hangnum
200\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Lobhassa na vasaṃ gacche, haneyyārisakaṃ {note:haneyya disataṃ (sī.), haneyya disakaṃ (syā.)} manaṃ.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
Eva {note:eta (sī. pī.)} mādīnavaṃ ñatvā, taṇhā dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vītataṇho anādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbajeti.
::

::centre
Mahāvāṇijajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 494. Sādhinajātakaṃ (11)

::hangnum
202\.
::

::gatha1
Abbhuto {pb:T:1.0397} vata lokasmiṃ, uppajji lomahaṃsano;
::

::gathalast
Dibbo ratho pāturahu, vedehassa yasassino.
::

::hangnum
203\.
::

::gatha1
Devaputto mahiddhiko, mātali {note:mātalī (sī.)} devasārathi;
::

::gathalast
Nimantayittha rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
204\.
::

::gatha1
Ehimaṃ rathamāruyha, rājaseṭṭha disampati;
::

::gatha2
Devā dassanakāmā te, tāvatiṃsā saindakā;
::

::gathalast
Saramānā hi te devā, sudhammāyaṃ samacchare.
::

::hangnum
205\.
::

::gatha1
Tato ca rājā sādhino {note:sādhīno (sī. pī.)}, vedeho mithilaggaho {note:pamukho rathamāruhi (sī. pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Sahassayuttamāruyha {note:yuttaṃ abhiruyha (sī.)}, agā devāna santike;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ devā paṭinandiṃsu, disvā rājānamāgataṃ.
::

::hangnum
206\.
::

::gatha1
Svāgataṃ te mahārāja, atho te adurāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nisīda dāni rājīsi {note:rājisi (sī. syā. pī.)}, devarājassa santike.
::

::hangnum
207\.
::

::gatha1
Sakkopi paṭinandittha, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nimantayittha {note:nimantayī ca (sī. pī.)} kāmehi, āsanena ca vāsavo.
::

::hangnum
208\.
::

::gatha1
Sādhu {pb:M:1.0301} khosi anuppatto, āvāsaṃ vasavattinaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Vasa {pb:T:1.0398} devesu rājīsi, sabbakāmasamiddhisu;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, bhuñja kāme amānuse.
::

::hangnum
209\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ {pb:V:1.0228} pure saggagato ramāmi, naccehi gītehi ca vāditehi;
::

::gatha2
So dāni ajja na ramāmi sagge, āyuṃ nu khīṇo {note:khīṇaṃ (syā.)} maraṇaṃ nu santike;
::

::gathalast
Udāhu mūḷhosmi janindaseṭṭha.
::

::hangnum
210\.
::

::gatha1
Na tāyu {note:na cāyu (sī. pī. ka.)} khīṇaṃ maraṇañca {note:maraṇaṃ te (sī. pī.)} dūre, na cāpi mūḷho naravīraseṭṭha;
::

::gathalast
Tuyhañca {note:tavañca (sī. pī.), tava ca (ka.)} puññāni parittakāni, yesaṃ vipākaṃ idha vedayittho {note:vedayato (pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
211\.
::

::gatha1
Vasa devānubhāvena, rājaseṭṭha disampati;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, bhuñja kāme amānuse.
::

::hangnum
212\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā yācitakaṃ yānaṃ, yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ sampadamevetaṃ, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā.
::

::hangnum
213\.
::

::gatha1
Na cāhametamicchāmi, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃkatāni puññāni, taṃ me āveṇikaṃ {note:āveṇiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), āvenikaṃ (ka.)} dhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
214\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ gantvā manussesu, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
::

::gatha2
Dānena samacariyāya, saṃyamena damena ca;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ katvā sukhito hoti, na ca pacchānutappati.
::

::hangnum
215\.
::

::gatha1
Imāni {pb:T:1.0399} tāni khettāni, imaṃ nikkhaṃ sukuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Imā tā haritānūpā, imā najjo savantiyo.
::

::hangnum
216\.
::

::gatha1
Imā tā pokkharaṇī rammā, cakkavākapakūjitā {note:cakkavākūpakūjitā (sī. pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca;
::

::gathalast
Yassimāni mamāyiṃsu, kiṃ nu te disataṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
217\.
::

::gatha1
Tānīdha {pb:M:1.0302} khettāni so bhūmibhāgo, teyeva ārāmavanupacārā {note:te ārāmā te vana’me pacārā (sī. pī.), te yeva ārāmavanāni sañcarā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tameva mayhaṃ janataṃ apassato, suññaṃva me nārada khāyate disā.
::

::hangnum
218\.
::

::gatha1
Diṭṭhā mayā vimānāni, obhāsentā catuddisā;
::

::gathalast
Sammukhā devarājassa, tidasānañca sammukhā.
::

::hangnum
219\.
::

::gatha1
Vutthaṃ me bhavanaṃ dibyaṃ {note:dibbaṃ (sī. pī.)}, bhuttā kāmā amānusā;
::

::gathalast
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, sabbakāmasamiddhisu.
::

::hangnum
220\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ etādisaṃ hitvā, puññāyamhi idhāgato;
::

::gathalast
Dhammameva carissāmi, nāhaṃ rajjena atthiko.
::

::hangnum
221\.
::

::gatha1
Adaṇḍāvacaraṃ maggaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ maggaṃ paṭipajjissaṃ, yena gacchanti subbatāti.
::

::centre
Sādhinajātakaṃ {note:sādhinarājajātakaṃ (syā.)} ekādasamaṃ.
::

Bahū te {note:ne (syā. ka.)} paripucchanti, aṇḍacchedā nilañchakā {note:tilañchakā (pī.)}.

::hangnum

#### 496. Bhikkhāparamparajātakaṃ (13)

::hangnum
270\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, mahāsayanamupāsitaṃ {note:mupocitaṃ (bahūsu)}.
::

::hangnum
271\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sālīnaṃ vicitaṃ bhattaṃ, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
272\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha, brāhmaṇassa adāsayi {note:adāpayi (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Attānaṃ {pb:T:1.0406} {note:attanā (pī. aṭṭha. pāṭhantaraṃ)} anasitvāna, koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te.
::

::hangnum
273\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Garu ca āmantanīyo {note:āmantaṇīyo (sī. pī.)} ca, dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
274\.
::

::gatha1
Brāhmaṇaṃ dāni pucchāmi, gotamaṃ rājapūjitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rājā te bhattaṃ pādāsi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
275\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha, isissa bhojanaṃ adā;
::

::gathalast
Akhettaññūsi dānassa, koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te.
::

::hangnum
276\.
::

::gatha1
Bharāmi putta {note:putte (sī. pī.)} dāre ca, gharesu gadhito {note:gathito (sī. pī.)} ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhuñje mānusake kāme, anusāsāmi rājino.
::

::hangnum
277\.
::

::gatha1
Āraññikassa {note:āraññakassa (sī. pī.)} isino, cirarattaṃ tapassino;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
278\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
279\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
280\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Dhunaṃ sāmākanīvāraṃ, saṅghāriyaṃ pasāriyaṃ {note:saṃhāriyaṃ pahāriyaṃ (syā.), saṃsāriyaṃ pasāriyaṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
281\.
::

::gatha1
Sākaṃ {pb:V:1.0234} bhisaṃ madhuṃ maṃsaṃ, badarāmalakāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Tāni āharitvā {note:āhatva (sī. syā.)} bhuñjāmi, atthi me so pariggaho.
::

::hangnum
282\.
::

::

::hangnum
283\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
284\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
285\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

286\.

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
287\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
288\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

289\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::centre

::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Suva {pb:T:1.0408} kinnara mukka kharājinaso, bhisajāta mahesi kapotavaro;

::gathalast

::centre

### 15. Vīsatinipāto

#### 497. Mātaṅgajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Kuto {pb:T:1.0409}{pb:V:1.0235}{pb:M:1.0309} nu āgacchasi dummavāsī {note:rummavāsī (sī. pī.)}, otallako paṃsupisācakova;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkāracoḷaṃ paṭimuñca {note:paṭimucca (sī. pī.)} kaṇṭhe, ko re tuvaṃ hosi {note:hohisi (sī. pī.)} adakkhiṇeyyo.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Annaṃ tavedaṃ {note:tava idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), tavayidaṃ (syā.)} pakataṃ yasassi, taṃ khajjare bhuñjare piyyare ca;
::

::gathalast
Jānāsi maṃ tvaṃ paradattūpajīviṃ, uttiṭṭhapiṇḍaṃ labhataṃ sapāko.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Annaṃ mamedaṃ {note:mama idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), mamayidaṃ (syā.)} pakataṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ, attatthāya saddahato mamedaṃ {note:mama idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), mamayidaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Apehi etto kimidhaṭṭhitosi, na mādisā tuyhaṃ dadanti jamma.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Thale ca ninne ca vapanti bījaṃ, anūpakhette phalamāsamānā {note:māsasānā (sī. pī.), māsiṃ samānā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Etāya saddhāya dadāhi dānaṃ, appeva ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyye.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Khettāni mayhaṃ viditāni loke, yesāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0410} bījāni patiṭṭhapemi;
::

::gathalast
Ye brāhmaṇā jātimantūpapannā, tānīdha khettāni supesalāni.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Jātimado ca atimānitā ca, lobho ca doso ca mado ca moho;
::

::gathalast
Ete aguṇā yesu ca santi {note:yesu vasanti (sī. pī.)} sabbe, tānīdha khettāni apesalāni.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Jātimado {pb:M:1.0310} ca atimānitā ca, lobho ca doso ca mado ca moho;
::

::gathalast
Ete aguṇā yesu na santi sabbe, tānīdha khettāni supesalāni.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Kvettha gatā {note:kvattha gatā (syā.), kattheva bhaṭṭhā (pī.)} upajotiyo ca, upajjhāyo ca athavā gaṇḍakucchi {note:aṇḍakucchi (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Imassa daṇḍañca vadhañca datvā, gale gahetvā khalayātha {note:galayātha (ka.)} jammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Giriṃ nakhena khaṇasi, ayo dantehi {note:dantena (sī. pī.)} khādasi;
::

::gathalast
Jātavedaṃ padahasi, yo isiṃ paribhāsasi.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ vatvāna mātaṅgo, isi saccaparakkamo;
::

::gathalast
Antalikkhasmiṃ {pb:T:1.0411} pakkāmi {note:pakkami (ka.)}, brāhmaṇānaṃ udikkhataṃ.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Āvellitaṃ {note:aveṭhitaṃ (sī. pī.)} piṭṭhito uttamaṅgaṃ, bāhuṃ {note:bāhaṃ (sī. pī.)} pasāreti akammaneyyaṃ {note:akampaneyyaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Setāni akkhīni yathā matassa, ko me imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Idhāgamā {pb:V:1.0236} samaṇo dummavāsī, otallako paṃsupisācakova;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkāracoḷaṃ paṭimuñca kaṇṭhe, so te imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Katamaṃ disaṃ agamā bhūripañño, akkhātha me māṇavā etamatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gantvāna taṃ paṭikaremu accayaṃ, appeva naṃ putta labhemu jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Vehāyasaṃ {pb:M:1.0311} agamā bhūripañño, pathaddhuno pannaraseva cando;
::

::gathalast
Api cāpi so purimadisaṃ agacchi, saccappaṭiñño isi sādhurūpo.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Āvellitaṃ piṭṭhito uttamaṅgaṃ, bāhuṃ pasāreti akammaneyyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Setāni akkhīni yathā matassa, ko {pb:T:1.0412} me imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Yakkhā have santi mahānubhāvā, anvāgatā isayo sādhurūpā;
::

::gathalast
Te duṭṭhacittaṃ kupitaṃ viditvā, yakkhā hi te puttamakaṃsu evaṃ.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Yakkhā ca me puttamakaṃsu evaṃ, tvaññeva me mā kuddho {note:kuddha (ka.)} brahmacāri;
::

::gathalast
Tumheva {note:tuyheva (ka.)} pāde saraṇaṃ gatāsmi, anvāgatā puttasokena bhikkhu.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Tadeva hi etarahi ca mayhaṃ, manopadoso na mamatthi {note:mama natthi (pī.)} koci;
::

::gathalast
Putto ca te vedamadena matto, atthaṃ na jānāti adhicca vede.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā have bhikkhu muhuttakena, sammuyhateva purisassa saññā;
::

::gathalast
Ekāparādhaṃ {note:etāparādhaṃ (ka.)} khama bhūripañña, na paṇḍitā kodhabalā bhavanti.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Idañca mayhaṃ uttiṭṭhapiṇḍaṃ, tava {note:natthi sī. pī. potthakesu} maṇḍabyo bhuñjatu appapañño;
::

::gathalast
Yakkhā ca te naṃ {note:te puttaṃ (syā.)} na viheṭhayeyyuṃ, putto {pb:T:1.0413} ca te hessati {note:hohiti (sī. pī.)} so arogo.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Maṇḍabya {pb:M:1.0312} bālosi parittapañño, yo puññakhettānamakovidosi;
::

::gathalast
Mahakkasāvesu dadāsi dānaṃ, kiliṭṭhakammesu asaññatesu.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Jaṭā ca kesā ajinā nivatthā, jarūdapānaṃva mukhaṃ parūḷhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pajaṃ imaṃ passatha dummarūpaṃ {note:rummarūpiṃ (sī. pī.)}, na jaṭājinaṃ tāyati appapaññaṃ.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, tesu dinnaṃ mahapphalanti.
::

::centre
Mātaṅgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 498. Cittasambhūtajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaṃ narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
::

::gathalast
Passāmi sambhūtaṃ mahānubhāvaṃ, sakammunā {pb:T:1.0414} puññaphalūpapannaṃ.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaṃ {pb:V:1.0237} narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
::

::gathalast
Kaccinnu cittassapi evamevaṃ, iddho mano tassa yathāpi mayhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbaṃ narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
::

::gathalast
Cittampi jānāhi {note:cittaṃ vijānāhi (sī. pī.)} tatheva deva, iddho mano tassa yathāpi tuyhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Bhavaṃ nu citto sutamaññato te, udāhu te koci naṃ etadakkhā;
::

::gathalast
Gāthā sugītā na mamatthi kaṅkhā, dadāmi te gāmavaraṃ satañca.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0313} cāhaṃ citto sutamaññato me, isī ca me etamatthaṃ asaṃsi;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Gantvāna rañño paṭigāhi {note:paṭigāyi (syā. ka.), paṭigāya (?)} gāthaṃ, api te varaṃ attamano dadeyya’’ {note:api nu te varaṃ attamano dadeyya (syā.), api nu te attamano varaṃ dade (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Yojentu ve rājarathe, sukate cittasibbane;
::

::gathalast
Kacchaṃ nāgānaṃ bandhatha, gīveyyaṃ paṭimuñcatha.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Āhaññantu {pb:T:1.0415} {note:āhaññare (syā.)} bherimudiṅgasaṅkhe {note:saṅkhā (syā.)}, sīghāni yānāni ca yojayantu;
::

::gathalast
Ajjevahaṃ assamaṃ taṃ gamissaṃ, yattheva dakkhissamisiṃ nisinnaṃ.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Suladdhalābho vata me ahosi, gāthā sugītā parisāya majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ isiṃ sīlavatūpapannaṃ, disvā patīto sumanohamasmi.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Āsanaṃ udakaṃ pajjaṃ, paṭiggaṇhātu no bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Agghe bhavantaṃ pucchāma, agghaṃ kurutu no bhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Rammañca te āvasathaṃ karontu, nārīgaṇehi paricārayassu;
::

::gathalast
Karohi okāsamanuggahāya, ubhopi maṃ issariyaṃ karoma.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
Disvā phalaṃ duccaritassa rāja, atho suciṇṇassa mahāvipākaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Attānameva paṭisaṃyamissaṃ, na patthaye putta {note:puttaṃ (sī. pī.)} pasuṃ dhanaṃ vā.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Dasevimā vassadasā, maccānaṃ idha jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apattaññeva {pb:T:1.0416} taṃ odhiṃ, naḷo chinnova sussati.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Tattha {pb:M:1.0314} kā nandi kā khiḍḍā, kā ratī kā dhanesanā;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ me puttehi dārehi, rāja muttosmi bandhanā.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ evaṃ pajānāmi {note:so ahaṃ suppajānāmi (sī. pī.)}, maccu me nappamajjati;
::

::gathalast
Antakenādhipannassa, kā ratī kā dhanesanā.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Jāti narānaṃ adhamā janinda, caṇḍālayoni dvipadākaniṭṭhā {note:dipadākaniṭṭhā (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sakehi kammehi supāpakehi, caṇḍālagabbhe {note:caṇḍāligabbhe (syā.)} avasimha pubbe.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Caṇḍālāhumha avantīsu, migā nerañjaraṃ pati;
::

::gathalast
Ukkusā nammadātīre {note:rammadātīre (syā. ka.)}, tyajja brāhmaṇakhattiyā.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Karohi pañcāla mameta {note:mameva (syā. ka.)} vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammāni dukkhudrayāni.

::gatha1
Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu, jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;

::gathalast

::gatha1
Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu, jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
::

43\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Karohi pañcāla mameta vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammaṃ nirayūpapattiyā.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā {pb:M:1.0315} hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavetaṃ, yathā isī bhāsasi evametaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmā ca me santi anapparūpā, te duccajā mādisakena bhikkhu.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Nāgo yathā paṅkamajjhe byasanno, passaṃ thalaṃ nābhisambhoti gantuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evampahaṃ {note:evamahaṃ (syā.)} kāmapaṅke byasanno, na bhikkhuno maggamanubbajāmi.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi mātā ca pitā ca puttaṃ, anusāsare kinti sukhī bhaveyya;
::

::gathalast
Evampi maṃ tvaṃ anusāsa bhante, yathā ciraṃ {note:yamācaraṃ (sī. pī. ka. aṭṭha.)} pecca sukhī bhaveyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
No {pb:T:1.0418} ce tuvaṃ ussahase janinda, kāme ime mānusake pahātuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammiṃ {note:dhammaṃ (sī. pī.)} baliṃ paṭṭhapayassu rāja, adhammakāro tava {note:adhammakāro ca te (sī. syā. pī.)} māhu raṭṭhe.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Dūtā vidhāvantu disā catasso, nimantakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Sace ca taṃ rāja mado saheyya, nārīgaṇehi paricārayantaṃ;
::

::gathalast

51\.

::

::gathalast

::centre

#### 499. Sivijātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Dūre {pb:T:1.0419} apassaṃ therova, cakkhuṃ yācitumāgato;
::

::gathalast
Ekanettā bhavissāma, cakkhuṃ me dehi yācito.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Kenānusiṭṭho {pb:V:1.0239} idha māgatosi, vanibbaka {note:vaṇibbaka (sī.)} cakkhupathāni yācituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Suduccajaṃ yācasi uttamaṅgaṃ, yamāhu nettaṃ purisena duccajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Yamāhu devesu sujampatīti, maghavāti naṃ āhu manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Tenānusiṭṭho idha māgatosmi, vanibbako cakkhupathāni yācituṃ.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Vanibbato {note:vanibbako (syā. pī.)} mayha vaniṃ {note:vanaṃ (ka.), vaṇiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} anuttaraṃ, dadāhi te cakkhupathāni yācito;
::

::gathalast
Dadāhi me cakkhupathaṃ anuttaraṃ, yamāhu nettaṃ purisena duccajaṃ.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yena atthena āgacchi {note:āgañchi (sī. pī.)}, yamatthamabhipatthayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te te ijjhantu saṅkappā, labha cakkhūni brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Ekaṃ te yācamānassa, ubhayāni dadāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sa cakkhumā gaccha janassa pekkhato, yadicchase tvaṃ tadate samijjhatu.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Mā {pb:T:1.0420}{pb:M:1.0317} no deva adā cakkhuṃ, mā no sabbe parākari {note:parakkari (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), parikkari (ka.) pari + ā + kari = parākari};
::

::gathalast
Dhanaṃ dehi mahārāja, muttā veḷuriyā bahū.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Yutte deva rathe dehi, ājānīye calaṅkate;
::

::gathalast
Nāge dehi mahārāja, hemakappanavāsase.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā taṃ sivayo {note:sīviyo (syā.)} sabbe, sayoggā sarathā sadā;
::

::gathalast
Samantā parikireyyuṃ {note:parikareyyuṃ (syā. pī.)}, evaṃ dehi rathesabha.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve dassanti vatvāna, adāne kurute mano;
::

::gathalast
Bhūmyaṃ {note:bhūmyā (sī. pī.)} so patitaṃ pāsaṃ, gīvāyaṃ paṭimuñcati.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve dassanti vatvāna, adāne kurute mano;
::

::gathalast
Pāpā pāpataro hoti, sampatto yamasādhanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Yañhi yāce tañhi dade, yaṃ na yāce na taṃ dade;
::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ tameva dassāmi, yaṃ maṃ yācati brāhmaṇo.
::

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Āyuṃ nu vaṇṇaṃ nu sukhaṃ balaṃ nu, kiṃ patthayāno nu janinda desi;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi rājā sivinaṃ anuttaro, cakkhūni dajjā paralokahetu.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhametaṃ yasasā dadāmi, na puttamicche na dhanaṃ na raṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satañca dhammo carito purāṇo, icceva dāne ramate mano mama {note:mamaṃ (sī. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Sakhā {pb:T:1.0421} ca mitto ca mamāsi sīvika {note:sīvaka (sī. pī.)}, susikkhito sādhu karohi me vaco;
::

::gathalast
Uddharitvā {note:uddhatva (sī.), laddha tvaṃ (pī.)} cakkhūni mamaṃ jigīsato, hatthesu ṭhapehi {note:āvesi (sī.)} vanibbakassa.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Codito {pb:V:1.0240}{pb:M:1.0318} sivirājena, siviko vacanaṅkaro;
::

::gatha2
Rañño cakkhūnuddharitvā {note:cakkhūni uddhatvā (sī. pī.)}, brāhmaṇassūpanāmayi;
::

::gathalast
Sacakkhu brāhmaṇo āsi, andho rājā upāvisi.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Tato so katipāhassa, uparūḷhesu cakkhusu;
::

::gathalast
Sūtaṃ āmantayī rājā, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Yojehi sārathi yānaṃ, yuttañca paṭivedaya;
::

::gathalast
Uyyānabhūmiṃ gacchāma, pokkharañño vanāni ca.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
So ca pokkharaṇītīre {note:pokkharaṇiyā tīre (sī. pī.)}, pallaṅkena upāvisi;
::

::gathalast
Tassa sakko pāturahu, devarājā sujampati.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Sakkohamasmi devindo, āgatosmi tavantike;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Pahūtaṃ me dhanaṃ sakka, balaṃ koso canappako;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
73\.

::gatha1
Yāni {pb:T:1.0422} saccāni dvipadinda, tāni bhāsassu khattiya;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ te bhaṇamānassa, puna cakkhu bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Ye maṃ yācitumāyanti, nānāgottā vanibbakā;
::

::gatha2
Yopi maṃ yācate tattha, sopi me manaso piyo;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccavajjena, cakkhu me upapajjatha.

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ maṃ so yācituṃ āgā, dehi cakkhunti brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Bhiyyo maṃ āvisī pīti, somanassañcanappakaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
77\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
79\.

::gathalast
Datvāna {pb:T:1.0423} mānusaṃ {note:datvā mānusakaṃ (sī.)} cakkhuṃ, laddhaṃ me {note:me iti padaṃ natthi sī. potthake} cakkhuṃ amānusaṃ.

#### 500. Sirīmantajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Paññāyupetaṃ siriyā vihīnaṃ, yasassinaṃ vāpi apetapaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi taṃ senaka etamatthaṃ, kamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Dhīrā ca bālā ca have janinda, sippūpapannā ca asippino ca;
::

::gathalast
Sujātimantopi ajātimassa, yasassino pesakarā {note:pessakarā (sī. pī.)} bhavanti;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva {note:sirimāva (sī. syā. pī.)} seyyo.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Tuvampi pucchāmi anomapañña, mahosadha kevaladhammadassi;
::

::gathalast
Bālaṃ yasassiṃ paṇḍitaṃ appabhogaṃ, kamettha {pb:T:1.0424} seyyo kusalā vadanti.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Pāpāni {pb:M:1.0320} kammāni karoti bālo {note:karonti bālā (syā. ka.)}, idhameva {note:idameva (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), imameva (ka.)} seyyo iti maññamāno {note:maññamānā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gatha2
Idhalokadassī paralokamadassī, ubhayattha bālo kalimaggahesi;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Na sippametaṃ vidadhāti bhogaṃ, na bandhuvā {note:na bandhavā (sī. syā. ka.)} na sarīravaṇṇo yo {note:na sarīrāvakāso (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Passeḷamūgaṃ sukhamedhamānaṃ, sirī hi naṃ bhajate goravindaṃ {note:gorimandaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Laddhā sukhaṃ majjati appapañño, dukkhena phuṭṭhopi pamohameti;
::

::gatha2
Āgantunā dukkhasukhena phuṭṭho, pavedhati vāricarova ghamme;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Dumaṃ yathā sāduphalaṃ araññe, samantato {pb:T:1.0425} samabhisaranti {note:samabhicaranti (sī. pī.)} pakkhī;
::

::gatha2
Evampi aḍḍhaṃ sadhanaṃ sabhogaṃ, bahujjano bhajati atthahetu;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Na sādhu balavā bālo, sāhasā vindate dhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kandantametaṃ dummedhaṃ, kaḍḍhanti nirayaṃ bhusaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Yā {pb:V:1.0242}{pb:M:1.0321} kāci najjo gaṅgamabhissavanti, sabbāva tā nāmagottaṃ jahanti;
::

::gatha2
Gaṅgā samuddaṃ paṭipajjamānā, na khāyate iddhiṃ paññopi loke {note:iddhiparo hi loke (ka. sī. syā.), iddhiparo hi loko (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Yametamakkhā udadhiṃ mahantaṃ, savanti najjo sabbakālamasaṅkhyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So sāgaro niccamuḷāravego, velaṃ na acceti mahāsamuddo.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Evampi {pb:T:1.0426} bālassa pajappitāni, paññaṃ na acceti sirī kadāci;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Asaññato cepi paresamatthaṃ, bhaṇāti sandhānagato {note:saṇṭhānagato (syā. pī.), santhānagato (sī.)} yasassī;
::

::gatha2
Tasseva taṃ rūhati ñātimajjhe, sirī hi naṃ {note:sirihīnaṃ (sī. ka.), sirīhīnaṃ (syā. pī.)} kārayate na paññā {note:na pañño (sī.), na paññaṃ (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Parassa vā attano vāpi hetu, bālo musā bhāsati appapañño;
::

::gatha2
So nindito hoti sabhāya majjhe, pacchāpi {note:peccampi (sī. pī.), peccāpi (?)} so duggatigāmī hoti;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Atthampi {pb:M:1.0322} ce bhāsati bhūripañño, anāḷhiyo {note:anālayo (pī.)} appadhano daliddo;
::

::gatha2
Na tassa taṃ rūhati ñātimajjhe, sirī {pb:T:1.0427} ca paññāṇavato na hoti;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.

::hangnum
97\.

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::gathalast

::hangnum
98\.

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Pañca paṇḍitā mayaṃ bhaddante, sabbe {pb:T:1.0428} pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā;
::

::gatha2
Tvaṃ no abhibhuyya issarosi, sakkova bhūtapati devarājā;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Dāsova {pb:V:1.0243}{pb:M:1.0323} paññassa yasassi bālo, atthesu jātesu tathāvidhesu;
::

::gatha2
Yaṃ paṇḍito nipuṇaṃ saṃvidheti, sammohamāpajjati tattha bālo;
::

::gathalast
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi paññāva sataṃ pasatthā, kantā sirī bhogaratā manussā;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇañca buddhānamatulyarūpaṃ, paññaṃ na acceti sirī kadāci.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ taṃ apucchimha akittayī no, mahosadha kevaladhammadassī;
::

::gatha2
Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ, ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime;
::

::gathalast
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi {pb:T:1.0429} te gāmavarāni soḷasāti.
::

::centre
Sirīmantajātakaṃ {note:sirimandajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} catutthaṃ.
::

#### 501. Rohaṇamigajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum

::gathalast

::gathalast

#### 502. Cūḷahaṃsajātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Ete {pb:M:1.0326} haṃsā pakkamanti, vakkaṅgā bhayameritā;
::

::gathalast
Harittaca hemavaṇṇa, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Ohāya maṃ ñātigaṇā, ekaṃ pāsavasaṃ gataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anapekkhamānā {note:nāpekkhamānā (ka.)} gacchanti, kiṃ eso avahiyyasi.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Pateva patataṃ seṭṭha, natthi baddhe sahāyatā {note:sahāyakā (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Mā anīghāya hāpesi, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Nāhaṃ ‘‘dukkhapareto’’ti {note:dukkhaparetopi (ka.)}, dhataraṭṭha tuvaṃ {note:tavaṃ (sī. pī.)} jahe;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
::

::gathalast
Atha {pb:T:1.0433} jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhati.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Ete haṃsā pakkamanti, vakkaṅgā bhayameritā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
142\.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1

145\.

158\.

#### 503. Sattigumbajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
159\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

160\.

161\.

::gathalast

163\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
164\.

::hangnum
165\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
166\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
167\.
::

::gatha1

::

::hangnum
168\.

169\.

170\.
::

::gatha1

171\.

::gatha1

172\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
173\.

::gatha1

174\.

175\.

::gatha1

176\.

::hangnum
177\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ yañhi rāja bhajati, santaṃ vā yadi vā asaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Sopi tādisako hoti, sahavāso hi {note:sahavāsopi (syā. ka.)} tādiso.
::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
Sevamāno {pb:M:1.0330} sevamānaṃ, samphuṭṭho samphusaṃ paraṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saro diddho kalāpaṃva, alittamupalimpati;
::

::gathalast
Upalepabhayā {note:upalimpabhayā (syā. ka.)} dhīro, neva pāpasakhā siyā.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
Pūtimacchaṃ {pb:V:1.0249} kusaggena, yo naro upanayhati;
::

::gathalast
Kusāpi pūti {note:pūtī (sī. pī.)} vāyanti, evaṃ bālūpasevanā.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
Tagarañca palāsena, yo naro upanayhati;
::

::gathalast
Pattāpi surabhi {note:surabhī (sī. syā. pī.)} vāyanti, evaṃ dhīrūpasevanā.
::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā pattapuṭasseva {note:phalapuṭasseva (sī. pī.), palapuṭasseva (ka. aṭṭha.), palāsapuṭasseva (syā. ka.)}, ñatvā sampākamattano;
::

::gatha2
Asante nopaseveyya, sante seveyya paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nirayaṃ nenti, santo pāpenti suggatinti.
::

::centre
Sattigumbajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.
::

#### 504. Bhallātiyajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
186\.
::

::gatha1
Bhallātiyo {pb:T:1.0438} {note:bhallāṭiyo (sī. pī.)} nāma ahosi rājā, raṭṭhaṃ pahāya migavaṃ acāri so;
::

::gathalast
Agamā girivaraṃ gandhamādanaṃ, supupphitaṃ {note:sampupphitaṃ (sī. pī.)} kimpurisānuciṇṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
187\.
::

::gatha1
Sāḷūrasaṅghañca nisedhayitvā, dhanuṃ {note:dhanu (sī. syā. pī.)} kalāpañca so nikkhipitvā;
::

::gathalast
Upāgami vacanaṃ vattukāmo, yatthaṭṭhitā kimpurisā ahesuṃ.
::

::hangnum
188\.
::

::gatha1
Himaccaye hemavatāya tīre, kimidhaṭṭhitā mantayavho abhiṇhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kathaṃ nu {note:kathaṃ vo (sī. syā. pī.)} jānanti manussaloke.
::

::hangnum
189\.
::

::gatha1
Mallaṃ {pb:M:1.0331} giriṃ paṇḍarakaṃ tikūṭaṃ, sītodakā {note:sītodiyā (sī. pī.), sītodikā (?)} anuvicarāma najjo;
::

::gathalast
Migā manussāva nibhāsavaṇṇā, jānanti no kimpurisāti ludda.
::

::hangnum
190\.
::

::gatha1
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho {note:paridevathavho (?) moggallānabyākaraṇe 6.38 suttaṃ}, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
::

::gathalast
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kimidha vane rodatha appatītā.
::

::hangnum
191\.
::

::gatha1
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
192\.
::

::gatha1
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
193\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
194\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
195\.
::

::gatha1
Yamimaṃ {pb:V:1.0250} {note:yayimaṃ (ka. sī.)} nadiṃ passasi sīghasotaṃ, nānādumacchādanaṃ selakūlaṃ {note:dumacchadanaṃ selakūṭaṃ (sī. pī.), dumasañchannaṃ selakūlaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
196\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
197\.

‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti mālabhārī, ahañca naṃ mālinī ajjhupessaṃ’’.

::gatha1

199\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
200\.
::

::gatha1
Ahañca kho agaḷuṃ {note:aggalu (syā. ka.), akaluṃ (pī.)} candanañca, silāya piṃsāmi pamattarūpā;
::

::gathalast
‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti rositaṅgo, ahañca {pb:T:1.0441} naṃ rositā ajjhupessaṃ’’.
::

::hangnum
201\.
::

::gatha1
Athāgamā salilaṃ sīghasotaṃ, nudaṃ sāle salaḷe kaṇṇikāre;
::

::gathalast
Āpūratha {note:apūratha (sī. pī.), āpūrathe (syā.)} tena muhuttakena, sāyaṃ nadī āsi mayā suduttarā.
::

::hangnum
202\.
::

::gatha1
Ubhosu tīresu mayaṃ tadā ṭhitā, sampassantā ubhayo aññamaññaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakimpi rodāma sakiṃ hasāma, kicchena no āgamā {note:agamā (sī. syā. pī.)} saṃvarī sā.
::

::hangnum
203\.
::

::gatha1
Pātova {pb:M:1.0333} {note:pāto ca (sī. syā. pī.)} kho uggate sūriyamhi, catukkaṃ nadiṃ uttariyāna ludda;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
204\.
::

::gatha1
Tīhūnakaṃ sattasatāni ludda, yamidha mayaṃ vippavasimha pubbe;
::

::gathalast
Vassekimaṃ {note:vāsekimaṃ (sī. pī.)} jīvitaṃ bhūmipāla, ko nīdha kantāya vinā vaseyya.
::

::hangnum
205\.
::

::gatha1
Āyuñca vo kīvatako nu samma, sacepi jānātha vadetha āyuṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
206\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
207\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::gathalast

::

::gathalast
Muñcaṃ {note:muñca (sī. pī.)} giraṃ nudaseva me daraṃ, samaṇa {pb:T:1.0443} sukhāvaha jīva me ciranti.

#### 505. Somanassajātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
211\.
::

::gatha1
Ko taṃ hiṃsati heṭheti, kiṃ {note:kinnu (pī. ka.)} dummano socasi appatīto;
::

::gathalast
Kassajja mātāpitaro rudantu, kvajja setu {note:ko nvejja seti (ka.), ko ajja setu (?)} nihato pathabyā.
::

::hangnum
212\.
::

::gatha1
Tuṭṭhosmi deva tava dassanena, cirassaṃ passāmi taṃ bhūmipāla;
::

::gathalast
Ahiṃsako reṇumanuppavissa, puttena te heṭhayitosmi {note:pothayitosmi (ka.)} deva.
::

::hangnum
213\.
::

::gatha1
Āyantu dovārikā khaggabandhā {note:khaggabaddhā (sī. pī.)}, kāsāviyā yantu {note:hantu (ka.)} antepurantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hantvāna taṃ somanassaṃ kumāraṃ, chetvāna sīsaṃ varamāharantu.
::

::hangnum
214\.
::

::gatha1
Pesitā rājino dūtā, kumāraṃ etadabravuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Issarena vitiṇṇosi, vadhaṃ pattosi khattiya.
::

::hangnum
215\.
::

::gatha1
Sa rājaputto paridevayanto, dasaṅguliṃ añjaliṃ paggahetvā;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi {pb:T:1.0444} icchāmi janinda daṭṭhuṃ, jīvaṃ maṃ netvā {note:jīvaṃ panetvā (sī. pī.)} paṭidassayetha.
::

::hangnum
216\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, rañño puttaṃ adassayuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Putto ca pitaraṃ disvā, dūratovajjhabhāsatha.
::

::hangnum
217\.
::

::gatha1
Āgacchuṃ {pb:M:1.0335} {note:āgañchuṃ (sī.), āgañchu (pī.)} dovārikā khaggabandhā, kāsāviyā hantu mamaṃ janinda;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, aparādho ko nidha mamajja atthi.
::

::hangnum
218\.
::

::gatha1
Sāyañca pāto udakaṃ sajāti, aggiṃ sadā pāricaratappamatto;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tādisaṃ saṃyataṃ brahmacāriṃ, kasmā tuvaṃ brūsi gahappatīti.
::

::hangnum
219\.
::

::gatha1
Tālā ca mūlā ca phalā ca deva, pariggahā vividhā santimassa;
::

::gathalast
Te rakkhati gopayatappamatto, {note:brāhmaṇo gahapati tena hoti (sī. syā. pī.)} tasmā ahaṃ brūmi gahappatīti {note:brāhmaṇo gahapati tena hoti (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
220\.
::

::gatha1
Saccaṃ kho etaṃ vadasi kumāra, pariggahā vividhā santimassa;
::

::gathalast
Te rakkhati gopayatappamatto, sa {note:natthi idaṃ sī. syā. pī. potthakesu} brāhmaṇo {pb:T:1.0445} gahapati tena hoti.
::

::hangnum
221\.
::

::gatha1
Suṇantu mayhaṃ parisā samāgatā, sanegamā jānapadā ca sabbe;
::

::gathalast
Bālāyaṃ bālassa vaco nisamma, ahetunā ghātayate maṃ {note:ghātayate (sī. pī.)} janindo.
::

::hangnum
222\.
::

::gatha1
Daḷhasmi {pb:V:1.0252} mūle visaṭe virūḷhe, dunnikkayo veḷu pasākhajāto;
::

::gathalast
Vandāmi pādāni tava {note:tavaṃ (sī. pī.)} janinda, anujāna maṃ pabbajissāmi deva.
::

::hangnum
223\.
::

::gatha1
Bhuñjassu bhoge vipule kumāra, sabbañca te issariyaṃ dadāmi;
::

::gathalast
Ajjeva tvaṃ kurūnaṃ hohi rājā, mā pabbajī pabbajjā hi dukkhā.
::

::hangnum
224\.
::

::gatha1
Kinnūdha {pb:M:1.0336} deva tavamatthi bhogā, pubbevahaṃ {note:pubbe cahaṃ (ka.)} devaloke ramissaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rūpehi saddehi atho rasehi, gandhehi phassehi manoramehi.
::

::hangnum
225\.
::

::gatha1
Bhuttā ca me {note:bhuttā (sī. pī.)} bhogā tidivasmiṃ deva, parivāritā {note:paricāritā (ka.)} accharānaṃ gaṇena {note:accharāsaṃgaṇena (syā. pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tuvañca {note:tavañca (sī. pī.)} bālaṃ paraneyyaṃ viditvā, na {pb:T:1.0446} tādise rājakule vaseyyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
226\.
::

::gatha1
Sacāhaṃ bālo paraneyyo asmi, ekāparādhaṃ {note:etāparādhaṃ (ka.)} khama putta mayhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Punapi ce edisakaṃ bhaveyya, yathāmatiṃ somanassa karohi.
::

::hangnum
227\.
::

::gatha1
Anisamma kataṃ kammaṃ, anavatthāya cintitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhesajjasseva vebhaṅgo, vipāko hoti pāpako.
::

::hangnum
228\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma ca kataṃ kammaṃ, sammāvatthāya cintitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhesajjasseva sampatti, vipāko hoti bhadrako.
::

::hangnum
229\.
::

::gatha1
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
::

::gathalast
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
::

::hangnum
230\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
::

::gathalast
Nisammakārino rāja, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhati.
::

::hangnum
231\.
::

::gatha1
Nisamma daṇḍaṃ paṇayeyya issaro, vegā kataṃ tappati bhūmipāla;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
232\.
::

::gatha1
Anānutappāni {pb:M:1.0337} hi ye karonti, vibhajja {pb:T:1.0447} kammāyatanāni loke;
::

::gathalast
Viññuppasatthāni sukhudrayāni, bhavanti buddhānumatāni {note:vaddhānumatāni (sī. pī.)} tāni.
::

::hangnum
233\.
::

::gatha1
Āgacchuṃ dovārikā khaggabandhā, kāsāviyā hantu mamaṃ janinda;
::

::gathalast
Mātuñca {note:mātucca (pī.)} aṅkasmimahaṃ nisinno, ākaḍḍhito sahasā tehi deva.
::

::hangnum
234\.
::

::gatha1
Kaṭukañhi sambādhaṃ sukicchaṃ {note:sukiccha (sī. pī.)} patto, madhurampi yaṃ jīvitaṃ laddha rāja;
::

::gathalast
Kicchenahaṃ ajja vadhā pamutto, pabbajjamevābhimanohamasmi.
::

::hangnum
235\.
::

::gatha1
Putto tavāyaṃ taruṇo sudhamme, anukampako somanasso kumāro;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ yācamāno na labhāmi svajja {note:sajja (sī. pī.)}, arahasi naṃ yācitave {note:yācituye (ka.)} tuvampi.
::

::hangnum
236\.
::

::gatha1
Ramassu {pb:V:1.0253} bhikkhācariyāya putta, nisamma dhammesu paribbajassu;
::

::gathalast
Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, anindito brahmamupehi ṭhānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
237\.
::

::gatha1
Acchera {note:acchariya (sī. syā. pī.)} rūpaṃ vata yādisañca, dukkhitaṃ {pb:T:1.0448} maṃ dukkhāpayase sudhamme;
::

::gathalast
Yācassu puttaṃ iti vuccamānā, bhiyyova ussāhayase kumāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
238\.
::

::gatha1
Ye vippamuttā anavajjabhogino {note:bhojino (sī. syā. pī.)}, parinibbutā lokamimaṃ caranti;
::

::gathalast
Tamariyamaggaṃ paṭipajjamānaṃ, na ussahe vārayituṃ kumāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
239\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā {pb:M:1.0338} have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
::

::gathalast
Yesāyaṃ sutvāna subhāsitāni, appossukkā vītasokā sudhammāti.
::

::centre
Somanassajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 506. Campeyyajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
240\.
::

::gatha1
Kā nu vijjurivābhāsi, osadhī viya tārakā;
::

::gathalast
Devatā nusi gandhabbī, na taṃ maññāmi mānusiṃ {note:mānusī (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
241\.
::

::gatha1
Namhi devī na gandhabbī, na mahārāja mānusī;
::

::gathalast
Nāgakaññāsmi bhaddante, atthenamhi idhāgatā.
::

::hangnum
242\.
::

::gatha1
Vibbhantacittā kupitindriyāsi, nettehi te vārigaṇā savanti;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ {pb:T:1.0449} te naṭṭhaṃ kiṃ pana patthayānā, idhāgatā nāri tadiṅgha brūhi.
::

::hangnum
243\.
::

::gatha1
Yamuggatejo uragoti cāhu, nāgoti naṃ āhu janā janinda;
::

::gathalast
Tamaggahī puriso jīvikattho, taṃ bandhanā muñca patī mameso.
::

::hangnum
244\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃ nvayaṃ balaviriyūpapanno, hatthatta {note:hatthattha (sī. syā. pī.)} māgacchi vanibbakassa;
::

::gathalast
Akkhāhi me nāgakaññe tamatthaṃ, kathaṃ vijānemu gahītanāgaṃ.
::

::hangnum
245\.
::

::gatha1
Nagarampi nāgo bhasmaṃ kareyya, tathā hi so balaviriyūpapanno;
::

::gathalast
Dhammañca nāgo apacāyamāno, tasmā parakkamma tapo karoti.
::

::hangnum
246\.
::

::gatha1
Cātuddasiṃ {pb:M:1.0339} pañcadasiṃ {note:pannarasiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} ca rāja, catuppathe sammati nāgarājā;
::

::gathalast
Tamaggahī puriso jīvikattho, taṃ bandhanā muñca patī mameso.
::

::hangnum
247\.
::

::gatha1
Soḷasitthisahassāni, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
::

::gathalast
Vārigehasayā nārī {note:nāriyo (pī.)}, tāpi taṃ saraṇaṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
248\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena {pb:T:1.0450} mocehi asāhasena, gāmena nikkhena gavaṃ satena;
::

::gathalast
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
249\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena {pb:V:1.0254} mocemi asāhasena, gāmena nikkhena gavaṃ satena;
::

::gathalast
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
250\.
::

::gatha1
Dammi nikkhasataṃ ludda, thūlañca maṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Catussadañca pallaṅkaṃ, umāpupphasarinnibhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
251\.
::

::gatha1
Dve ca sādisiyo bhariyā, usabhañca gavaṃ sataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
::

::hangnum
252\.
::

::gatha1
Vināpi dānā tava vacanaṃ janinda, muñcemu naṃ uragaṃ bandhanasmā;
::

::gathalast
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.

#### 507. Mahāpalobhanajātakaṃ (11)

::hangnum
284\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Rañño putto udapādi, sabbakāmasamiddhisu.
::

::hangnum
285\.
::

::gatha1
Kāmā {pb:T:1.0457} vā kāmasaññā vā, brahmaloke na vijjati;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
286\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
287\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
288\.
::

::gatha1

291\.

#### 508. Pañcapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (12)

::hangnum
315\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, kassevāvikareyya {note:kassa vāvīkareyya (ka.)} guyhamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
316\.
::

::gatha1
Tvaṃ {pb:V:1.0259} āvikarohi bhūmipāla, bhattā bhārasaho tuvaṃ vade taṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tava chandarucīni {note:chandañca ruciñca (sī. pī.)} sammasitvā, atha vakkhanti janinda pañca dhīrā.
::

::hangnum
317\.
::

::gatha1
Yā sīlavatī anaññatheyyā {note:anaññadheyyā (sī. pī.)}, bhattucchandavasānugā (piyā) {note:( ) natthi sī. pī. potthakesu} manāpā;
::

::gathalast
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, bhariyāyāvikareyya {note:bhariyāya vāvīkareyya (ka.)} guyhamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
318\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
319\.

::gatha1
Jeṭṭho {pb:T:1.0461} {note:yo jeṭṭho (syā.)} atha majjhimo kaniṭṭho, yo {note:so (sī. syā. pī.)} ce sīlasamāhito ṭhitatto;
::

::gathalast
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, bhātu vāvīkareyya guyhamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
320\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve pituhadayassa paddhagū {note:patthagū (syā.), pattagū (ka.)}, anujāto pitaraṃ anomapañño;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
321\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, mātuyāvīkareyya {note:mātuyā vāvīkareyya (ka.)} guyhamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
322\.
::

::gatha1
Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu, na hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anipphannatā {note:anipphādāya (sī. pī.), anipphannatāya (syā.), ā nipphādā (?)} saheyya dhīro, nipphannova {note:nipphannattho (sī. pī.), nipphannatthova (syā.)} yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya.
::

::hangnum
323\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ tvaṃ vimanosi rājaseṭṭha, dvipadajaninda {note:dipadinda (sī. syā. pī.)} vacanaṃ suṇoma metaṃ {note:netaṃ (sī. pī.), tetaṃ (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ cintayamāno dummanosi, nūna deva aparādho atthi mayhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
324\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇhe {pb:T:1.0462} {note:pañño (sī. pī.), pañhe (syā.), panhe (ka.)} vajjho mahosadho’’ti, āṇatto me vadhāya bhūripañño;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ cintayamāno dummanosmi, na hi devī aparādho atthi tuyhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
325\.
::

::gatha1
Abhidosagato dāni ehisi, kiṃ sutvā kiṃ saṅkate mano te;
::

::gathalast
Ko te kimavoca bhūripañña, iṅgha vacanaṃ suṇoma brūhi metaṃ.
::

::hangnum
326\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṇhe vajjho mahosadho’’ti, yadi te mantayitaṃ janinda dosaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhariyāya rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
::

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0349} sālavanasmiṃ senako, pāpakammaṃ akāsi asabbhirūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakhinova rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
::

::hangnum
328\.
::

::gatha1
Pukkusa {note:pakkusa (ka.) jā. 1.7.41 paṇṇajātake passitabbaṃ} purisassa te janinda, uppanno rogo arājayutto;
::

::gathalast
Bhātuñca {note:bhātucca (sī. pī.), bhātuva (syā.)} rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
::

::hangnum
329\.
::

::gatha1
Ābādhoyaṃ {pb:T:1.0463} asabbhirūpo, kāmindo {note:kāvindo (sī. pī.)} naradevena phuṭṭho;
::

::gathalast
Puttassa rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
::

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
Aṭṭhavaṅkaṃ {pb:V:1.0260} maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ, sakko te adadā pitāmahassa;
::

::gatha2
Devindassa gataṃ tadajja hatthaṃ {note:devindassa tadajja hatthagataṃ (ka.)}, mātuñca rahogato asaṃsi;
::

::gathalast
Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
::

::hangnum
331\.
::

::gatha1
Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu, na hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anipphannatā saheyya dhīro, nipphannova yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya.
::

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1
Na guyhamatthaṃ vivareyya, rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na hi pātukato sādhu, guyho attho pajānatā.
::

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya, amittassa ca paṇḍito;
::

::gathalast
Yo cāmisena saṃhīro, hadayattheno ca yo naro.
::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
Guyhamatthaṃ asambuddhaṃ, sambodhayati yo naro;
::

::gathalast
Mantabhedabhayā tassa, dāsabhūto titikkhati.
::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
Yāvanto {pb:M:1.0350} purisassatthaṃ, guyhaṃ jānanti mantinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tāvanto {pb:T:1.0464} tassa ubbegā, tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃ, rattiṃ giraṃ nātivelaṃ pamuñce;
::

::gathalast
Upassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃ, tasmā manto khippamupeti bhedanti.
::

::centre
Pañcapaṇḍitajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 509. Hatthipālajātakaṃ (13)

::hangnum
337\.
::

::gatha1
Cirassaṃ vata passāma, brāhmaṇaṃ devavaṇṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mahājaṭaṃ khāridharaṃ {note:bhāradharaṃ (pī.)}, paṅkadantaṃ rajassiraṃ.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

::gatha1
Cirassaṃ vata passāma, isiṃ dhammaguṇe rataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāsāyavatthavasanaṃ, vākacīraṃ paṭicchadaṃ.
::

::hangnum
339\.
::

::gatha1
Āsanaṃ udakaṃ pajjaṃ, paṭigaṇhātu no bhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Agghe bhavantaṃ pucchāma, agghaṃ kurutu no bhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
340\.
::

::gatha1
Adhicca vede pariyesa vittaṃ, putte gahe {note:gehe (sī. syā. pī.)} tāta patiṭṭhapetvā;
::

::gathalast
Gandhe rase paccanubhuyya {note:paccanubhotva (syā.), paccanubhutva (pī.)} sabbaṃ, araññaṃ sādhu muni so pasattho.
::

::hangnum
341\.
::

::gatha1
Vedā na saccā na ca vittalābho, na puttalābhena jaraṃ vihanti;
::

::gathalast
Gandhe {pb:T:1.0465} rase muccana {note:muñcana (sī. ka.)} māhu santo, sakammunā {note:sakammanā (sī. pī.)} hoti phalūpapatti.
::

::hangnum
342\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavetaṃ, sakammunā hoti phalūpapatti;
::

::gathalast
Jiṇṇā ca mātāpitaro tavīme {note:taveme (sī.), tava yime (syā. pī.)}, passeyyuṃ taṃ vassasataṃ arogaṃ {note:arogyaṃ (syā. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
343\.
::

::gatha1
Yassassa {pb:V:1.0261}{pb:M:1.0351} sakkhī maraṇena rāja, jarāya mettī naravīraseṭṭha;
::

::gathalast
Yo cāpi jaññā na marissaṃ kadāci, passeyyuṃ taṃ vassasataṃ arogaṃ.
::

::hangnum
344\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi nāvaṃ puriso dakamhi, ereti ce naṃ upaneti tīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evampi byādhī satataṃ jarā ca, upaneti maccaṃ {note:maccu (syā. pī.)} vasamantakassa.
::

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
Paṅko ca kāmā palipo ca kāmā, manoharā duttarā maccudheyyā;
::

::gathalast
Etasmiṃ paṅke palipe byasannā {note:visannā (syā. ka.)}, hīnattarūpā na taranti pāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
Ayaṃ pure luddamakāsi kammaṃ, svāyaṃ gahīto na hi mokkhito me;
::

::gathalast
Orundhiyā {pb:T:1.0466} naṃ parirakkhissāmi, māyaṃ puna luddamakāsi kammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
Gavaṃva {note:gāvaṃva (sī.)} naṭṭhaṃ puriso yathā vane, anvesatī {note:pariyesatī (sī. pī.)} rāja apassamāno;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ naṭṭho esukārī mamattho, sohaṃ kathaṃ na gaveseyyaṃ rāja.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
Hiyyoti hiyyati {note:hīyoti hīyati (sī.)} poso, pareti parihāyati;
::

::gathalast
Anāgataṃ netamatthīti ñatvā, uppannachandaṃ ko panudeyya dhīro.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
Passāmi vohaṃ daharaṃ {note:daharī (syā. pī. ka.)} kumāriṃ, mattūpamaṃ ketakapupphanettaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhuttabhoge {note:abhutva bhoge (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), abhutva bhoge (pī.), bhoge atutvā (ka.)} paṭhame vayasmiṃ, ādāya maccu vajate kumāriṃ.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
Yuvā {pb:M:1.0352} sujāto sumukho sudassano, sāmo kusumbhaparikiṇṇamassu;
::

::gathalast
Hitvāna kāme paṭikacca {note:paṭigacca (sī.), paṭigaccha (syā. pī.)} gehaṃ, anujāna maṃ pabbajissāmi deva.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
Sākhāhi rukkho labhate samaññaṃ, pahīnasākhaṃ pana khāṇumāhu;
::

::gathalast
Pahīnaputtassa mamajja bhoti, vāseṭṭhi {pb:T:1.0467} bhikkhācariyāya kālo.
::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
Aghasmi koñcāva yathā himaccaye, katāni {note:tantāni (sī. pī.)} jālāni padāliya {note:padāleyya (sī.)} haṃsā;
::

Gacchanti puttā ca patī ca mayhaṃ, sāhaṃ kathaṃ nānuvaje pajānaṃ.

::hangnum
353\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
Avamī brāhmaṇo kāme, so {note:te (sī. pī.)} tvaṃ paccāvamissasi;

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
355\.

::gatha1

::hangnum
356\.

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
357\.

::gathalast

358\.

::

::gathalast

#### 510. Ayogharajātakaṃ (14)

::hangnum
363\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Abbhuṭṭhitova so yāti {note:sayati (sī. pī.), sa yāti (katthaci)}, sagacchaṃ na nivattati.
::

::hangnum
364\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0354} yujjhamānā na balenavassitā, narā na jīranti na cāpi miyyare;
::

::gathalast

365\.

::gathalast

370\.

::

::gathalast

371\.

374\.

378\.

381\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
382\.

::

::gathalast
Na maccuno daṭṭhavisaṃ {note:daṭṭhassa visaṃ (ka.)} hananti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
383\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammantarī vettaraṇī {note:vetaraṇī (sī. pī.)} ca bhojo, visāni {pb:T:1.0473} hantvāna bhujaṅgamānaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
384\.
::

::gatha1
Vijjādharā {pb:V:1.0264} ghoramadhīyamānā, adassanaṃ osadhehi vajanti;
::

::gathalast
Na maccurājassa vajantadassanaṃ {note:vajanti adassanaṃ (syā. ka.)}, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
::

::hangnum
385\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammo {pb:M:1.0357} have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
386\.
::

::gatha1
Na hi dhammo adhammo ca, ubho samavipākino;
::

::gathalast
Adhammo nirayaṃ neti, dhammo pāpeti suggatinti.
::

::centre
Ayogharajātakaṃ cuddasamaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Mātaṅga sambhūta sivi sirimanto, rohaṇa haṃsa sattigumbo bhallātiya;
::

::gathalast
Somanassa campeyya brahma pañca-paṇḍita cirassaṃvata ayogharāti.
::

::centre
Vīsatinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
