### 16. Tiṃsanipāto

#### 511. Kiṃchandajātakaṃ (1)

::hangnum
1\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃchando {pb:T:1.0474}{pb:V:1.0265}{pb:M:1.0358} kimadhippāyo, eko sammasi ghammani;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ patthayāno kiṃ esaṃ, kena atthena brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
2\.
::

::gatha1
Yathā mahā vāridharo, kumbho supariṇāhavā {note:supariṇāmavā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tathūpamaṃ ambapakkaṃ, vaṇṇagandharasuttamaṃ.
::

::hangnum
3\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ vuyhamānaṃ sotena, disvānāmalamajjhime;
::

::gathalast
Pāṇīhi naṃ gahetvāna, agyāyatanamāhariṃ.
::

::hangnum
4\.
::

::gatha1
Tato kadalipattesu, nikkhipitvā sayaṃ ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Satthena naṃ vikappetvā, khuppipāsaṃ ahāsi me.
::

::hangnum
5\.
::

::gatha1
Sohaṃ apetadaratho, byantībhūto {note:byantibhūto (sī. pī. ka.)} dukhakkhamo;
::

::gathalast
Assādaṃ nādhigacchāmi, phalesvaññesu kesuci {note:kesupi (ka. sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
6\.
::

::gatha1
Sosetvā nūna maraṇaṃ, taṃ mamaṃ āvahissati;
::

::gatha2
Ambaṃ yassa phalaṃ sādu, madhuraggaṃ manoramaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yamuddhariṃ vuyhamānaṃ, udadhismā mahaṇṇave.
::

::hangnum
7\.
::

::gatha1
Akkhātaṃ te mayā sabbaṃ, yasmā upavasāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rammaṃ pati nisinnosmi, puthulomāyutā puthu.
::

::hangnum
8\.
::

::gatha1
Tvañca kho meva {note:me (sī.), mama (?)} akkhāhi, attānamapalāyini;
::

::gathalast
Kā vā tvamasi kalyāṇi, kissa vā tvaṃ sumajjhime.
::

::hangnum
9\.
::

::gatha1
Ruppapaṭṭapalimaṭṭhīva {pb:T:1.0475} {note:ruppapaṭṭaplamaṭṭhīva (syā.), rūpapaṭṭapamaṭṭhīva (ka.)}, byagghīva girisānujā;
::

::gathalast
Yā santi nāriyo devesu, devānaṃ paricārikā.
::

::hangnum
10\.
::

::gatha1
Yā ca manussalokasmiṃ, rūpenānvāgatitthiyo;
::

::gatha2
Rūpena te sadisī natthi, devesu gandhabbamanussaloke {note:devagandhabbamānuse (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭhāsi me cārupubbaṅgi, brūhi nāmañca bandhave.
::

::hangnum
11\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0266}{pb:M:1.0359} tvaṃ pati nisinnosi, rammaṃ brāhmaṇa kosikiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāhaṃ bhusālayā vutthā, varavārivahoghasā.
::

::hangnum
12\.
::

::gatha1
Nānādumagaṇākiṇṇā, bahukā girikandarā;
::

::gathalast
Mameva pamukhā honti, abhisandanti pāvuse.
::

::hangnum
13\.
::

::gatha1
Atho bahū vanatodā, nīlavārivahindharā;
::

::gathalast
Bahukā nāgavittodā, abhisandanti vārinā.
::

::hangnum
14\.
::

::gatha1
Tā ambajambulabujā, nīpā tālā cudumbarā {note:tālamudumbarā (syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Bahūni phalajātāni, āvahanti abhiṇhaso.
::

::hangnum
15\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ kiñci ubhato tīre, phalaṃ patati ambuni;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃsayaṃ taṃ sotassa, phalaṃ hoti vasānugaṃ.
::

::hangnum
16\.
::

::gatha1
Etadaññāya medhāvi, puthupañña suṇohi me;
::

::gathalast
Mā rocaya mabhisaṅgaṃ, paṭisedha janādhipa.
::

::hangnum
17\.
::

::gatha1
Na vāhaṃ vaḍḍhavaṃ {note:vaddhavaṃ (sī. pī.)} maññe, yaṃ tvaṃ raṭṭhābhivaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Āceyyamāno rājisi, maraṇaṃ abhikaṅkhasi.
::

::hangnum
18\.
::

::gatha1
Tassa jānanti pitaro, gandhabbā ca sadevakā;
::

::gathalast
Ye {pb:T:1.0476} cāpi isayo loke, saññatattā tapassino;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃsayaṃ tepi {note:te (sī. pī.)} jānanti, paṭṭhabhūtā {note:vaddhabhūtā (sī. pī.)} yasassino.
::

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ viditvā vidū sabbadhammaṃ, viddhaṃsanaṃ cavanaṃ jīvitassa;
::

::gathalast
Na cīyatī tassa narassa pāpaṃ, sace na ceteti vadhāya tassa.
::

::hangnum
20\.
::

::gatha1
Isipūgasamaññāte, evaṃ lokyā viditā sati {note:pati (ka. syā. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Anariyaparisambhāse, pāpakammaṃ jigīsasi {note:jigiṃsasi (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
21\.
::

::gatha1
Sace ahaṃ marissāmi, tīre te puthusussoṇi;
::

::gathalast
Asaṃsayaṃ taṃ asiloko, mayi pete āgamissati.
::

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā {pb:M:1.0360} hi pāpakaṃ kammaṃ, rakkhasseva {note:rakkhassu ca (syā.)} sumajjhime;
::

::gathalast
Mā taṃ sabbo jano pacchā, pakuṭṭhāyi {note:pakatthāsi (sī. pī.), patvakkhāsi (syā.)} mayi mate.
::

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
Aññātametaṃ avisayhasāhi, attānamambañca dadāmi te taṃ;
::

::gathalast
So duccaje kāmaguṇe pahāya, santiñca dhammañca adhiṭṭhitosi.
::

::hangnum
24\.
::

::gatha1
Yo hitvā pubbasaññogaṃ, pacchā saṃyojane ṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Adhammañceva carati, pāpañcassa pavaḍḍhati.
::

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi {pb:V:1.0267} taṃ pāpayissāmi, kāmaṃ appossuko bhava;
::

::gathalast
Upānayāmi sītasmiṃ, viharāhi anussuko.
::

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0477} puppharasamattebhi, vakkaṅgehi arindama;
::

::gathalast
Koñcā mayūrā diviyā, kolaṭṭhimadhusāḷikā;
::

::gathalast
Kūjitā haṃsapūgehi, kokilettha pabodhare.
::

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
Ambettha vippasākhaggā {note:vippasūnaggā (sī. syā. pī.), vippaonaggā (ka.)}, palālakhalasannibhā;
::

::gathalast
Kosambasaḷalā {note:kosumbhasalalā (sī. syā. pī.)} nīpā, pakkatālavilambino.
::

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
Mālī tiriṭī kāyūrī, aṅgadī candanussado {note:candanassado (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Rattiṃ tvaṃ paricāresi, divā vedesi vedanaṃ.
::

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
Soḷasitthisahassāni, yā temā paricārikā;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ mahānubhāvosi, abbhuto lomahaṃsano.
::

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ kammamakarī pubbe, pāpaṃ attadukhāvahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ karitvā manussesu, piṭṭhimaṃsāni khādasi.
::

::hangnum
31\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjhenāni paṭiggayha, kāmesu gadhito {note:gathito (sī. pī.), giddhito (syā. ka.), giddhiko (ka. aṭṭha.)} ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Acariṃ dīghamaddhānaṃ, paresaṃ ahitāyahaṃ.
::

::hangnum
32\.
::

::gatha1
Yo piṭṭhimaṃsiko hoti, evaṃ ukkacca khādati;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhaṃ ajja khādāmi, piṭṭhimaṃsāni attanoti.
::

::centre
Kiṃchandajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.
::

#### 512. Kumbhajātakaṃ (2)

::hangnum
33\.
::

::gatha1
Ko {pb:M:1.0361} pāturāsī tidivā nabhamhi, obhāsayaṃ saṃvariṃ candimāva;
::

::gathalast
Gattehi {pb:T:1.0478} te rasmiyo niccharanti, sateratā {note:sateritā (sī. syā. ka.)} vijjurivantalikkhe.
::

::hangnum
34\.
::

::gatha1
So chinnavātaṃ kamasī aghamhi, vehāyasaṃ gacchasi tiṭṭhasī ca;
::

::gathalast
Iddhī nu te vatthukatā subhāvitā, anaddhagūnaṃ api devatānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
35\.
::

::gatha1
Vehāyasaṃ gammamāgamma {note:kamamāgamma (sī. syā.)} tiṭṭhasi, kumbhaṃ kiṇāthāti yametamatthaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ko vā tuvaṃ kissa vā tāya kumbho, akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ.
::

::hangnum
36\.
::

::gatha1
Na sappikumbho napi telakumbho, na phāṇitassa na madhussa kumbho;
::

::gathalast
Kumbhassa vajjāni anappakāni, dose bahū kumbhagate suṇātha.
::

::hangnum
37\.
::

::gatha1
Gaḷeyya {pb:V:1.0268} yaṃ pitvā {note:pītvā (sī. pī.)} pate papātaṃ, sobbhaṃ guhaṃ candaniyoḷigallaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bahumpi bhuñjeyya abhojaneyyaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
38\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ pitvā {note:yaṃ ve pītvā (sī.)} cittasmimanesamāno, āhiṇḍatī goriva bhakkhasārī {note:bhakkhasādī (sī. syā. aṭṭha.)};
::

::gathalast
Anāthamāno {pb:T:1.0479} upagāyati naccati ca, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
39\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:M:1.0362} ve pivitvā acelova naggo, careyya gāme visikhantarāni;
::

::gathalast
Sammūḷhacitto ativelasāyī, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
40\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ pitvā uṭṭhāya pavedhamāno, sīsañca bāhuñca {note:bāhañca (pī.)} pacālayanto;
::

::gathalast
So naccatī dārukaṭallakova, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
41\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pivitvā aggidaḍḍhā sayanti, atho sigālehipi khāditāse;
::

::gathalast
Bandhaṃ vadhaṃ bhogajāniñcupenti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ pitvā bhāseyya ābhāsaneyyaṃ, sabhāyamāsīno apetavattho;
::

::gathalast
Sammakkhito {note:samakkhito (sī.)} vantagato byasanno, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pivitvā ukkaṭṭho āvilakkho, mameva sabbā pathavīti maññe {note:maññati (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:1.0480} me samo cāturantopi rājā, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
Mānātimānā kalahāni pesuṇī, dubbaṇṇinī naggayinī palāyinī;
::

::gathalast
Corāna dhuttāna gatī niketo, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
Iddhāni phītāni kulāni assu, anekasāhassadhanāni loke;
::

::gathalast
Ucchinnadāyajjakatānimāya, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
Dhaññaṃ {pb:M:1.0363} dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ, khettaṃ gavaṃ yattha vināsayanti;
::

::gathalast
Ucchedanī vittavataṃ {note:ucchedanī vittagataṃ (syā.), ucchedanivittagataṃ (ka.)} kulānaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā dittarūpova {note:duṭṭharūpova (sī.)} poso, akkosati mātaraṃ pitarañca;
::

::gathalast
Sassumpi gaṇheyya athopi suṇhaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā dittarūpāva nārī, akkosati sasuraṃ sāmikañca;
::

::gathalast
Dāsampi {pb:T:1.0481} gaṇhe paricārakampi, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pivitvāna {note:yañce pītvāna (pī.)} haneyya poso, dhamme ṭhitaṃ samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Gacche apāyampi tatonidānaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pivitvā duccaritaṃ caranti, kāyena vācāya ca cetasā ca;
::

::gathalast
Nirayaṃ vajanti duccaritaṃ caritvā, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0269} yācamānā na labhanti pubbe, bahuṃ hiraññampi pariccajantā;
::

::gathalast
So taṃ pivitvā alikaṃ bhaṇāti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā pesane pesiyanto, accāyike karaṇīyamhi jāte;
::

::gathalast
Atthampi so nappajānāti vutto, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
Hirīmanāpi {pb:M:1.0364} ahirīkabhāvaṃ, pātuṃ karonti madanāya {note:madirāya (pī.)} mattā;
::

::gathalast
Dhīrāpi {pb:T:1.0482} santā bahukaṃ bhaṇanti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā ekathūpā sayanti, anāsakā thaṇḍiladukkhaseyyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dubbaṇṇiyaṃ āyasakyañcupenti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā pattakhandhā sayanti, gāvo kuṭahatāva na hi vāruṇiyā;
::

::gathalast
{note:yaṃ ve pitvā pattakkhandhā, sayanti gāvo kūṭahatāriva; na hi vāruṇiyā vego, narena sussahoriva; (sī.)} Vego narena susahoriva {note:yaṃ ve pitvā pattakkhandhā, sayanti gāvo kūṭahatāriva; na hi vāruṇiyā vego, narena sussahoriva; (sī.)}, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ manussā vivajjenti, sappaṃ ghoravisaṃ miva {note:visamiva (syā.), visaṃ iva (ka.), visāmiva (?)};
::

::gathalast
Taṃ loke visasamānaṃ, ko naro pātumarahati.
::

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā andhakaveṇḍaputtā, samuddatīre paricārayantā {note:andhakaveṇhuputtā (sī. pī.), aṇḍakaveṇḍaputtā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Upakkamuṃ musalehaññamaññaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
::

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ ve pitvā pubbadevā pamattā, tidivā cutā sassatiyā samāya;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0483} tādisaṃ majjamimaṃ niratthakaṃ, jānaṃ mahārāja kathaṃ piveyya.
::

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
Nayimasmiṃ kumbhasmiṃ dadhi vā madhu vā, evaṃ abhiññāya kiṇāhi rāja;
::

::gathalast
Evañhimaṃ kumbhagatā mayā te, akkhātarūpaṃ tava sabbamitta.
::

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0365} me pitā vā athavāpi mātā, etādisā yādisako tuvaṃsi;
::

::gathalast
Hitānukampī paramatthakāmo, sohaṃ karissaṃ vacanaṃ tavajja.
::

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
Dadāmi te gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃ satāni;
::

::gathalast
Ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime, ācariyo hosi mamatthakāmo.
::

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
Taveva dāsīsatamatthu rāja, gāmā ca gāvo ca taveva hontu;
::

::gathalast
Ājaññayuttā ca rathā taveva, sakkohamasmī tidasānamindo.
::

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
Maṃsodanaṃ sappipāyāsaṃ {note:sappipāyañca (sī.)} bhuñja, khādassu ca tvaṃ madhumāsapūve;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0484} tuvaṃ dhammarato janinda, anindito saggamupehi ṭhānanti.
::

::centre
Kumbhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.
::

#### 513. Jayaddisajātakaṃ (3)

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
Cirassaṃ {pb:V:1.0270} vata me udapādi ajja, bhakkho mahā sattamibhattakāle;
::

::gathalast
Kutosi ko vāsi tadiṅgha brūhi, ācikkha jātiṃ vidito yathāsi.
::

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
Pañcālarājā migavaṃ paviṭṭho, jayaddiso nāma yadissuto te;
::

::gathalast
Carāmi kacchāni vanāni cāhaṃ, pasadaṃ imaṃ khāda mamajja muñca.
::

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
Seneva {pb:M:1.0366} tvaṃ paṇasi sassamāno {note:sayhamāno (syā. ka.)}, mamesa bhakkho pasado yaṃ vadesi;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ khādiyāna pasadaṃ jighaññaṃ {note:jighacchaṃ (?)}, khādissaṃ pacchā na vilāpakālo.
::

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
Na catthi mokkho mama nikkayena {note:vikkayena (sī.)}, gantvāna paccāgamanāya paṇhe;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0485} saṅkaraṃ {note:saṅgaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ kammajātaṃ anutappate tvaṃ {note:anutappatī taṃ (sī. pī.)}, pattaṃ samīpaṃ maraṇassa rāja;
::

::gathalast
Ācikkha me taṃ api sakkuṇemu, anujānituṃ āgamanāya paṇhe.
::

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
Katā mayā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsā, taṃ saṅkaraṃ paṭimukkaṃ na muttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
Yā te katā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsā, taṃ saṅkaraṃ paṭimukkaṃ na muttaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajassu.
::

::hangnum
71\.
::

::gatha1
Mutto ca so porisādassa {note:purisādassa (pī.)} hatthā, gantvā sakaṃ mandiraṃ kāmakāmī;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, āmantayī puttamalīnasattaṃ {note:sattuṃ (syā. pī. ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
Ajjeva {pb:M:1.0367} rajjaṃ abhisiñcayassu, dhammaṃ cara sesu paresu cāpi;
::

::gathalast
Adhammakāro {pb:T:1.0486} ca te māhu raṭṭhe, gacchāmahaṃ porisādassa ñatte {note:ñante (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ kamma kubbaṃ tava deva pāva {note:devapāde (sī. syā. pī.)}, nārādhayī taṃ tadicchāmi sotuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yamajja rajjamhi udassaye tuvaṃ, rajjampi niccheyyaṃ tayā vināhaṃ.
::

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
Na kammunā vā vacasā va tāta, aparādhitohaṃ tuviyaṃ sarāmi;
::

::gathalast
Sandhiñca {note:saddhiṃ ca (ka.)} katvā purisādakena, saccānurakkhī punāhaṃ gamissaṃ.
::

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ gamissāmi idheva hohi, natthi tato jīvato vippamokkho;
::

::gathalast
Sace tuvaṃ gacchasiyeva rāja, ahampi gacchāmi ubho na homa.
::

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
Addhā hi tāta satānesa dhammo, maraṇā ca me dukkhataraṃ tadassa;
::

::gathalast
Kammāsapādo taṃ yadā pacitvā, pasayha khāde bhidā rukkhasūle.
::

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
Pāṇena te pāṇamahaṃ nimissaṃ, mā tvaṃ agā porisādassa ñatte;
::

::gathalast
Etañca {pb:T:1.0487} te pāṇamahaṃ nimissaṃ, tasmā mataṃ jīvitassa vaṇṇemi {note:varemi (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
Tato {pb:V:1.0271} have dhitimā rājaputto, vanditvā mātu ca pitu ca {note:vandittha mātucca pitucca (sī. pī.)} pāde;
::

::gathalast
Dukhinissa mātā nipatā {note:nipatī (sī. pī.)} pathabyā, pitāssa paggayha bhujāni kandati.
::

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:M:1.0368} gacchantaṃ tāva pitā viditvā, parammukho vandati pañjalīko;
::

::gatha2
Somo ca rājā varuṇo ca rājā, pajāpatī candimā sūriyo ca;
::

::gathalast
Etehi gutto purisādakamhā, anuññāto sotthi paccehi tāta.
::

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ daṇḍakirañño gatassa {note:yaṃ daṇḍakāraññagatassa (pī.)} mātā, rāmassakāsi sotthānaṃ suguttā;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ te ahaṃ sotthānaṃ karomi, etena saccena sarantu devā;
::

::gathalast
Anuññāto sotthi paccehi putta.
::

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
Āvī raho vāpī manopadosaṃ, nāhaṃ sare jātu malīnasatte;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena sarantu devā, anuññāto sotthi paccehi bhātika {note:bhāta (sī.), bhātā (syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
82\.
::

::gatha1
Yasmā ca me anadhimanosi sāmi, na cāpi me manasā appiyosi;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccena sarantu devā, anuññāto {pb:T:1.0488} sotthi paccehi sāmi.
::

::hangnum
83\.
::

::gatha1
Brahā ujū cārumukho kutosi, na maṃ pajānāsi vane vasantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Luddaṃ maṃ ñatvā ‘‘purisādako’’ti, ko sotthi mājānamidhā’vajeyya.
::

::hangnum
84\.
::

::gatha1
Jānāmi ludda purisādako tvaṃ, na taṃ na jānāmi vane vasantaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca puttosmi jayaddisassa, mamajja khāda pituno pamokkhā.
::

::hangnum
85\.
::

::gatha1
Jānāmi {pb:M:1.0369} puttoti {note:puttosi (syā. ka.)} jayaddisassa, tathā hi vo mukhavaṇṇo ubhinnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sudukkaraññeva {note:sudukkarañceva (syā. pī. ka.)} kataṃ tavedaṃ, yo mattumicche pituno pamokkhā.
::

::hangnum
86\.
::

::gatha1
Na dukkaraṃ kiñci mahettha maññe, yo mattumicche pituno pamokkhā;
::

::gathalast
Mātu ca {note:mātucca (sī.)} hetu paraloka gantvā {note:gamyā (sī. syā.), gamya (pī.)}, sukhena {pb:T:1.0489} saggena ca sampayutto.
::

::hangnum
87\.
::

::gatha1
Ahañca kho attano pāpakiriyaṃ, āvī raho vāpi sare na jātu;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhātajātīmaraṇohamasmi, yatheva me idha tathā parattha.
::

::hangnum
88\.
::

::gatha1
Khādajja maṃ dāni mahānubhāva, karassu kiccāni imaṃ sarīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rukkhassa vā te papatāmi aggā, chādayamāno mayhaṃ tvamadesi maṃsaṃ.
::

::hangnum
89\.
::

::gatha1
Idañca te ruccati rājaputta, cajesi {note:cajāsi (sī. pī.)} pāṇaṃ pituno pamokkhā;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā hi so {note:tasmātiha (sī. syā.)} tvaṃ taramānarūpo, sambhañja kaṭṭhāni jalehi aggiṃ.
::

::hangnum
90\.
::

::gatha1
Tato have dhitimā rājaputto, dāruṃ samāhatvā mahantamaggiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sandīpayitvā paṭivedayittha, ādīpito dāni mahāyamaggi {note:mayā yakkhamaggi (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
91\.
::

::gatha1
Khādajja {pb:V:1.0272}{pb:M:1.0370} maṃ dāni pasayhakārī, kiṃ maṃ muhuṃ pekkhasi haṭṭhalomo;
::

::gathalast
Tathā tathā tuyhamahaṃ karomi, yathā {pb:T:1.0490} yathā maṃ chādayamāno adesi.
::

::hangnum
92\.
::

::gatha1
Ko tādisaṃ arahati khāditāye, dhamme ṭhitaṃ saccavādiṃ vadaññuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Muddhāpi tassa viphaleyya sattadhā, yo tādisaṃ saccavādiṃ adeyya.
::

::hangnum
93\.
::

::gatha1
Idañhi so brāhmaṇaṃ maññamāno, saso avāsesi sake sarīre;
::

::gathalast
Teneva so candimā devaputto, sasatthuto {note:sasaṭṭhako (syā.)} kāmaduhajja {note:kāmaruhajja (ka.)} yakkha.
::

::hangnum
94\.
::

::gatha1
Cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutto, virocate pannaraseva bhāṇumā {note:bhānumā (sī. pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Evaṃ tuvaṃ porisādā pamutto, viroca kapile {note:kampilla (sī. pī.), kapille (syā.)} mahānubhāva;
::

::gathalast
Āmodayaṃ pitaraṃ mātarañca, sabbo ca te nandatu ñātipakkho.
::

::hangnum
95\.
::

::gatha1
Tato have dhitimā rājaputto, katañjalī pariyāya {note:pariyagā (sī.), paggayha (syā. pī.)} porisādaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anuññāto sotthi sukhī arogo, paccāgamā {note:paccāga (pī.)} kapilamalīnasattā {note:kampilla’malīnasatto (sī. pī.), kapila’malīnasattā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
96\.
::

::gatha1
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0491} negamā jānapadā ca sabbe, hatthārohā rathikā pattikā ca;
::

::gathalast
Namassamānā pañjalikā upāgamuṃ, namatthu te dukkarakārakosīti.
::

::centre
Jayaddisajātakaṃ {note:jayadisajātakaṃ (ka.)} tatiyaṃ.
::

#### 514. Chaddantajātakaṃ (4)

::hangnum
97\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ {pb:M:1.0371} nu socasinuccaṅgi, paṇḍūsi varavaṇṇini;
::

::gathalast
Milāyasi visālakkhi, mālāva parimadditā.
::

::hangnum
98\.
::

::gatha1
Dohaḷo me mahārāja, supinantenupajjhagā {note:nu’paccagā (sī. syā. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Na so sulabharūpova, yādiso mama dohaḷo.
::

::hangnum
99\.
::

::gatha1
Ye keci mānusā kāmā, idha lokasmi nandane;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe te pacurā mayhaṃ, ahaṃ te dammi dohaḷaṃ.
::

::hangnum
100\.
::

::gatha1
Luddā deva samāyantu, ye keci vijite tava;
::

::gathalast
Etesaṃ ahamakkhissaṃ, yādiso mama dohaḷo.
::

::hangnum
101\.
::

::gatha1
Ime te luddakā devi, katahatthā visāradā;
::

::gathalast
Vanaññū ca migaññū ca, mamatthe {note:mama te (pī.)} cattajīvitā.
::

::hangnum
102\.
::

::gatha1
Luddaputtā nisāmetha, yāvantettha samāgatā;
::

::gatha2
Chabbisāṇaṃ gajaṃ setaṃ, addasaṃ supine ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa dantehi me attho, alābhe natthi jīvitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
103\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:T:1.0492}{pb:V:1.0273} no pitūnaṃ na pitāmahānaṃ, diṭṭho suto kuñjaro chabbisāṇo;
::

::gathalast
Yamaddasā supine rājaputtī, akkhāhi no yādiso hatthināgo.
::

::hangnum
104\.
::

::gatha1
Disā catasso vidisā catasso, uddhaṃ adho dasa disā imāyo;
::

::gathalast
Katamaṃ disaṃ tiṭṭhati nāgarājā, yamaddasā supine chabbisāṇaṃ.
::

::hangnum
105\.
::

::gatha1
Ito ujuṃ uttariyaṃ disāyaṃ, atikkamma so sattagirī brahante;
::

::gathalast
Suvaṇṇapasso nāma girī uḷāro, supupphito {note:sampupphito (syā.)} kimpurisānuciṇṇo.
::

::hangnum
106\.
::

::gatha1
Āruyha {pb:M:1.0372} selaṃ bhavanaṃ kinnarānaṃ, olokaya pabbatapādamūlaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha dakkhasī meghasamānavaṇṇaṃ, nigrodharājaṃ atha sahassapādaṃ {note:poraṃ (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
107\.
::

::gatha1
Tatthacchatī kuñjaro chabbisāṇo, sabbaseto duppasaho parebhi;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhanti naṃ aṭṭhasahassanāgā, īsādantā vātajavappahārino.
::

::hangnum
108\.
::

::gatha1
Tiṭṭhanti {pb:T:1.0493} te tumūlaṃ {note:tumūla (syā.), bhimūla (pī. ka.)} passasantā, kuppanti vātassapi eritassa;
::

::gathalast
Manussabhūtaṃ pana tattha disvā, bhasmaṃ kareyyuṃ nāssa rajopi tassa.
::

::hangnum
109\.
::

::gatha1
Bahū hime rājakulamhi santi, piḷandhanā jātarūpassa devī;
::

::gatha2
Muttāmaṇīveḷuriyāmayā ca, kiṃ kāhasi dantapiḷandhanena;
::

::gathalast
Māretukāmā kuñjaraṃ chabbisāṇaṃ, udāhu ghātessasi luddaputte.
::

::hangnum
110\.
::

::gatha1
Sā issitā dukkhitā casmi ludda, uddhañca sussāmi anussarantī;
::

::gathalast
Karohi me luddaka etamatthaṃ, dassāmi te gāmavarāni pañca.
::

::hangnum
111\.
::

::gatha1
Katthacchatī katthamupeti ṭhānaṃ, vīthissa kā nhāna {note:nahāna (sī. pī.)} gatassa hoti;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi so nhāyati {note:nahāyati (sī. pī.)} nāgarājā, kathaṃ vijānemu gatiṃ gajassa.
::

::hangnum
112\.
::

::gatha1
Tattheva {pb:M:1.0373} sā pokkharaṇī adūre {note:avidūre (syā. ka.)}, rammā sutitthā ca mahodikā {note:mahodakā (syā. ka.)} ca;
::

::gathalast
Sampupphitā {pb:T:1.0494} bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇā {note:kiṇṇā (katthaci)}, ettha hi so nhāyati nāgarājā.
::

::hangnum
113\.
::

::gatha1
Sīsaṃ nahātuppala {note:nahāto uppala (sī. syā. pī.)} mālabhārī, sabbaseto puṇḍarīkattacaṅgī;
::

::gathalast
Āmodamāno gacchati sanniketaṃ, purakkhatvā mahesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ.
::

::hangnum
114\.
::

::gatha1
Tattheva so uggahetvāna vākyaṃ, ādāya tūṇiñca dhanuñca luddo;
::

::gathalast
Vituriyati {note:vituriya so (sī. aṭṭha.)} sattagirī brahante, suvaṇṇapassaṃ nāma giriṃ uḷāraṃ.
::

::hangnum
115\.
::

::gatha1
Āruyha selaṃ bhavanaṃ kinnarānaṃ, olokayī pabbatapādamūlaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tatthaddasā meghasamānavaṇṇaṃ, nigrodharājaṃ aṭṭhasahassapādaṃ.
::

::hangnum
116\.
::

::gatha1
Tatthaddasā kuñjaraṃ chabbisāṇaṃ, sabbasetaṃ duppasahaṃ parebhi;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhanti naṃ aṭṭhasahassanāgā, īsādantā vātajavappahārino.
::

::hangnum
117\.
::

::gatha1
Tatthaddasā {pb:V:1.0274} pokkharaṇiṃ adūre, rammaṃ sutitthañca mahodikañca;
::

::gathalast
Sampupphitaṃ {pb:T:1.0495} bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇaṃ, yattha hi so nhāyati nāgarājā.
::

::hangnum
118\.
::

::gatha1
Disvāna nāgassa gatiṃ ṭhitiñca, vīthissa yā nhānagatassa hoti;
::

::gathalast
Opātamāgacchi anariyarūpo, payojito cittavasānugāya.
::

::hangnum
119\.
::

::gatha1
Khaṇitvāna {pb:M:1.0374} kāsuṃ phalakehi chādayi, attānamodhāya dhanuñca luddo;
::

::gathalast
Passāgataṃ puthusallena nāgaṃ, samappayī dukkaṭakammakārī.
::

::hangnum
120\.
::

::gatha1
Viddho ca nāgo koñcamanādi ghoraṃ, sabbe ca {note:sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)} nāgā ninnaduṃ {note:ninnādu (syā.), ninnādaṃ (ka.)} ghorarūpaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tiṇañca kaṭṭhañca raṇaṃ {note:cuṇṇaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)} karontā, dhāviṃsu te aṭṭhadisā samantato.
::

::hangnum
121\.
::

::gatha1
Vadhissametanti {note:vadhissamenanti (syā.)} parāmasanto, kāsāvamaddakkhi dhajaṃ isīnaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhena phuṭṭhassudapādi saññā, arahaddhajo sabbhi avajjharūpo.
::

::hangnum
122\.
::

::gatha1
Anikkasāvo kāsāvaṃ, yo vatthaṃ paridahissati {note:paridahessati (sī. pī.), paridhassati (katthaci)};
::

::gathalast
Apeto damasaccena, na so kāsāvamarahati.
::

::hangnum
123\.
::

::gatha1
Yo {pb:T:1.0496} ca vantakasāvassa, sīlesu susamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Upeto damasaccena, sa ve kāsāvamarahati.
::

::hangnum
124\.
::

::gatha1
Samappito puthusallena nāgo, aduṭṭhacitto luddakamajjhabhāsi;
::

::gathalast
Kimatthayaṃ kissa vā samma hetu, mamaṃ vadhī kassa vāyaṃ payogo.
::

::hangnum
125\.
::

::gatha1
Kāsissa rañño mahesī bhadante, sā pūjitā rājakule subhaddā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ addasā sā ca mamaṃ asaṃsi, dantehi atthoti ca maṃ {note:atthoti mamaṃ (syā. ka.)} avoca.
::

::hangnum
126\.
::

::gatha1
Bahū {pb:M:1.0375} hi me dantayugā uḷārā, ye me pitūnañca {note:pitunnampi (pī.)} pitāmahānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jānāti sā kodhanā rājaputtī, vadhatthikā veramakāsi bālā.
::

::hangnum
127\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhehi tvaṃ ludda kharaṃ gahetvā, dante ime chinda purā marāmi;
::

::gathalast
Vajjāsi taṃ kodhanaṃ rājaputtiṃ, ‘‘nāgo hato handa imassa dantā’’.
::

::hangnum
128\.
::

::gatha1
Uṭṭhāya so luddo kharaṃ gahetvā, chetvāna {pb:T:1.0497} dantāni gajuttamassa;
::

::gathalast
Vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā, ādāya pakkāmi tato hi khippaṃ.
::

::hangnum
129\.
::

::gatha1
Bhayaṭṭitā {note:bhayadditā (sī. pī.)} nāgavadhena aṭṭā, ye te nāgā aṭṭha disā vidhāvuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adisvāna {note:adisva (sī. pī.)} posaṃ gajapaccamittaṃ, paccāgamuṃ yena so nāgarājā.
::

::hangnum
130\.
::

::gatha1
Te tattha kanditvā roditvāna {note:roditva (sī. pī.)} nāgā, sīse sake paṃsukaṃ okiritvā;
::

::gathalast
Agamaṃsu te sabbe sakaṃ niketaṃ, purakkhatvā mahesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ.
::

::hangnum
131\.
::

::gatha1
Ādāya {pb:V:1.0275} dantāni gajuttamassa, vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā;
::

::gatha2
Suvaṇṇarājīhi samantamodare, so luddako kāsipuraṃ upāgami;
::

::gathalast
Upanesi so rājakaññāya dante, nāgo hato handa imassa dantā.
::

::hangnum
132\.
::

::gatha1
Disvāna {pb:M:1.0376} dantāni gajuttamassa, bhattuppiyassa purimāya jātiyā;
::

::gathalast
Tattheva tassā hadayaṃ aphāli, teneva {pb:T:1.0498} sā kālamakāsi bālā.
::

::hangnum
133\.
::

::gatha1
Sambodhipatto sa {note:ca (sī. syā.), va (pī.)} mahānubhāvo, sitaṃ akāsi parisāya majjhe;
::

::gathalast
Pucchiṃsu bhikkhū suvimuttacittā, nākāraṇe pātukaronti buddhā.
::

::hangnum
134\.
::

::gatha1
Yamaddasātha dahariṃ kumāriṃ, kāsāyavatthaṃ anagāriyaṃ carantiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā kho tadā rājakaññā ahosi, ahaṃ tadā nāgarājā ahosiṃ.
::

::hangnum
135\.
::

::gatha1
Ādāya dantāni gajuttamassa, vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā;
::

::gathalast
Yo luddako kāsipuraṃ upāgami, so kho tadā devadatto ahosi.
::

::hangnum
136\.
::

::gatha1
Anāvasūraṃ cirarattasaṃsitaṃ, uccāvacaṃ {note:ucaṃ nīcaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} caritamidaṃ purāṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vītaddaro vītasoko visallo, sayaṃ abhiññāya abhāsi buddho.
::

::hangnum
137\.
::

::gatha1
Ahaṃ vo tena kālena, ahosiṃ tattha bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Nāgarājā tadā homi {note:hosiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)}, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
::

::centre
Chaddantajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.
::

#### 515. Sambhavajātakaṃ (5)

::hangnum
138\.
::

::gatha1
Rajjañca {pb:T:1.0499} paṭipannāsma, ādhipaccaṃ sucīrata;
::

::gathalast
Mahattaṃ pattumicchāmi, vijetuṃ pathaviṃ imaṃ.
::

::hangnum
139\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena no adhammena, adhammo me na ruccati;
::

::gathalast
Kiccova dhammo carito, rañño hoti sucīrata.
::

::hangnum
140\.
::

::gatha1
Idha {pb:M:1.0377} cevāninditā yena, pecca yena aninditā;
::

::gathalast
Yasaṃ devamanussesu, yena pappomu {note:pappemu (sī. aṭṭha.)} brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
141\.
::

::gatha1
Yohaṃ atthañca dhammañca, kattumicchāmi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, brāhmaṇakkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
142\.
::

::gatha1
Nāññatra vidhurā rāja, etadakkhātumarahati;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, kattumicchasi khattiya.
::

::hangnum
143\.
::

::gatha1
Ehi {pb:V:1.0276} kho pahito gaccha, vidhurassa upantikaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Nikkhañcimaṃ {note:nikkhaṃ ratta (sī.), nikkhamimaṃ (pī.)} suvaṇṇassa, haraṃ gaccha sucīrata;
::

::gathalast
Abhihāraṃ imaṃ dajjā, atthadhammānusiṭṭhiyā.
::

::hangnum
144\.
::

::gatha1
Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo, vidhurassa upantikaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tamaddasa mahābrahmā, asamānaṃ sake ghare.
::

::hangnum
145\.
::

::gatha1
Raññohaṃ pahito dūto, korabyassa yasassino;
::

::gatha2
‘‘Atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi’’, iccabravi yudhiṭṭhilo;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, vidhurakkhāhi pucchito.
::

::hangnum
146\.
::

::gatha1
Gaṅgaṃ me pidahissanti, na taṃ sakkomi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Apidhetuṃ {pb:T:1.0500} mahāsindhuṃ, taṃ kathaṃ so bhavissati.
::

::hangnum
147\.
::

::gatha1
Na te sakkomi akkhātuṃ, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito;
::

::gatha2
Bhadrakāro ca me putto, oraso mama atrajo;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, gantvā pucchassu brāhmaṇa.
::

::hangnum
148\.
::

::gatha1

#### 516. Mahākapijātakaṃ (6)

::hangnum
178\.
::

::gatha1
Bārāṇasyaṃ {note:bārāṇassaṃ (sī. pī.)} ahū rājā, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
::

::gathalast
Mittāmaccaparibyūḷho, agamāsi migājinaṃ {note:migājiraṃ (sī.), migāciraṃ (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
179\.
::

::gatha1
Tattha {pb:V:1.0279} brāhmaṇamaddakkhi, setaṃ citraṃ kilāsinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Viddhastaṃ koviḷāraṃva, kisaṃ dhamanisanthataṃ.
::

::hangnum
180\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
181\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hatthapādā ca te setā, tato setataraṃ {note:setataro (pī.)} siro;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
182\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaṭṭanāvaḷi {note:vaṭṭhanāvali (pī.)} saṅkāsā, piṭṭhi te ninnatunnatā;
::

::gathalast
Kāḷapabbāva {note:kāḷapabbā ca (syā.), kāḷā pabbā ca (pī.)} te aṅgā, nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ.
::

::hangnum
183\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ugghaṭṭapādo {pb:M:1.0381} tasito, kiso dhamanisanthato;
::

::gathalast
Chāto ātattarūposi {note:ādittarūposi (ka.), atittarūposi (syā. ka. aṭṭha.)}, kutosi kattha gacchasi.
::

::hangnum
184\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duddasī appakārosi, dubbaṇṇo bhīmadassano;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
185\.
::

::gatha1

::gatha1

::gathalast

221\.

::gatha1

222\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
223\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Kāyassa bhedā mittaddu {note:mittadubbhī (syā. ka.)}, nirayaṃ sopapajjatīti {note:so upapajjatīti (sī. syā. pī.)}.

::centre

#### 517. Dakarakkhasajātakaṃ (7)

::hangnum
224\.
::

::gatha1
Sace vo vuyhamānānaṃ, sattannaṃ udakaṇṇave;
::

::gatha2
Manussabalimesāno, nāvaṃ gaṇheyya rakkhaso;
::

::gathalast
Anupubbaṃ kathaṃ datvā, muñcesi dakarakkhasā {note:dakarakkhato (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
225\.
::

::gatha1
Mātaraṃ paṭhamaṃ dajjaṃ, bhariyaṃ datvāna bhātaraṃ;
::

::gatha2

#### 518. Paṇḍaranāgarājajātakaṃ (8)

::hangnum
258\.
::

::gatha1
Vikiṇṇavācaṃ aniguyha {note:anigūḷha (pī.)} mantaṃ, asaññataṃ aparicakkhitāraṃ {note:aparirakkhitāraṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhayaṃ tamanveti sayaṃ abodhaṃ, nāgaṃ yathā paṇḍarakaṃ supaṇṇo {note:suvaṇṇo (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
259\.
::

::gatha1
Yo guyhamantaṃ parirakkhaneyyaṃ, mohā naro saṃsati hāsamāno {note:bhāsamāno (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Taṃ bhinnamantaṃ bhayamanveti khippaṃ, nāgaṃ yathā paṇḍarakaṃ supaṇṇo.
::

::hangnum
260\.
::

::gatha1
Nānumitto {pb:V:1.0285} garuṃ atthaṃ, guyhaṃ veditumarahati;
::

::gathalast
Sumitto ca asambuddhaṃ, sambuddhaṃ vā anattha vā.
::

::hangnum
261\.
::

::gatha1
Vissāsamāpajjimahaṃ {pb:M:1.0388} acelaṃ {note:acelo (sī. pī.)}, samaṇo {pb:T:1.0513} ayaṃ sammato bhāvitatto;
::

::gathalast
Tassāhamakkhiṃ vivariṃ {note:vivaraṃ (sī.)} guyhamatthaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ {note:kapaṇo (pī.)} rudāmi.
::

::hangnum
262\.
::

::gatha1
Tassāhaṃ paramaṃ {note:purimaṃ (sī.)} brahme guyhaṃ, vācañhi maṃ nāsakkhiṃ {note:nāsakkhi (pī.)} saṃyametuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tappakkhato hi bhayamāgataṃ mamaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi.
::

::hangnum
263\.
::

::gatha1
Yo ve naro suhadaṃ maññamāno, guyhamatthaṃ saṃsati dukkulīne;
::

::gathalast
Dosā bhayā athavā rāgarattā {note:rāgaratto (sī. syā. pī.)}, pallatthito {note:pallittho (pī.), pallattito (ka.)} bālo asaṃsayaṃ so.
::

::hangnum
264\.
::

::gatha1
Tirokkhavāco asataṃ paviṭṭho, yo saṅgatīsu mudīreti vākyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āsīviso dummukhotyāhu taṃ naraṃ, ārā ārā {note:ārā arā (pī.)} saṃyame tādisamhā.
::

::hangnum
265\.
::

::gatha1
Annaṃ pānaṃ kāsika {note:kāsikaṃ (pī.)} candanañca, manāpitthiyo mālamucchādanañca;
::

::gathalast
Ohāya gacchāmase sabbakāme, supaṇṇa pāṇūpagatāva tyamhā.
::

::hangnum
266\.
::

::gatha1
Ko nīdha tiṇṇaṃ garahaṃ upeti, asmiṃdha {pb:T:1.0514} loke pāṇabhū nāgarāja;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇo supaṇṇo atha vā tvameva, kiṃ kāraṇā paṇḍarakaggahīto.
::

::hangnum
267\.
::

::gatha1
Samaṇoti {pb:M:1.0389} me sammatatto ahosi, piyo ca me manasā bhāvitatto;
::

::gathalast
Tassāhamakkhiṃ vivariṃ guyhamatthaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi.
::

::hangnum
268\.
::

::gatha1
Na catthi satto amaro pathabyā, paññāvidhā natthi na ninditabbā;
::

Saccena dhammena dhitiyā {note:dhiyā (sī. pī.)} damena, alabbhamabyāharatī naro idha.

::hangnum
269\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
270\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
272\.

::gathalast

::hangnum
273\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
274\.

::hangnum
275\.

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
276\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
277\.
::

::gatha1
Yathāpi assa {note:ayo (syā.), aya (ka.)} nagaraṃ mahantaṃ, advārakaṃ {note:āḷārakaṃ (pī.)} āyasaṃ bhaddasālaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
278\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
279\.
::

::gatha1
Hitvā gharaṃ pabbajito acelo, naggo muṇḍo carati ghāsahetu;
::

::gathalast
Tamhi {note:tamhī (pī.)} nu kho vivariṃ guyhamatthaṃ, atthā ca dhammā ca apaggatamhā {note:apāgatamhā (sī.), apagatamhā (syā.), avāgatamhā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
280\.
::

::gatha1
Kathaṃkaro hoti supaṇṇarāja, kiṃsīlo kena vatena vattaṃ;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
281\.
::

::gatha1
Hiriyā titikkhāya damenupeto {note:damena khantiyā (sī. syā. pī.)}, akkodhano pesuṇiyaṃ pahāya;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇo caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni, evaṃkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ.
::

::hangnum
282\.
::

::gatha1
Mātāva {pb:M:1.0391} puttaṃ taruṇaṃ tanujjaṃ {note:tanūjaṃ (sī.)}, samphassatā {note:sampassa taṃ (sī. pī.)} sabbagattaṃ phareti;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
283\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
284\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
285\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
286\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
287\.
::

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
288\.

::gatha1

::gathalast

::hangnum
289\.
::

::gatha1
Vissāsaye {pb:V:1.0287} na ca taṃ {note:naṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} vissayeyya, asaṅkito saṅkito ca {note:asaṅkito ca saṅkito (sī. pī.)} bhaveyya;
::

::gathalast

::hangnum
290\.
::

::gatha1
Te {pb:M:1.0392} devavaṇṇā {note:devavaṇṇī (pī.)} sukhumālarūpā, ubho samā sujayā {note:sujayo (sī. syā. pī.)} puññakhandhā {note:puññagandhā (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Upāgamuṃ karampiyaṃ {note:kādambiyaṃ (sī.), kārambiyaṃ (pī.)} acelaṃ, missībhūtā assavāhāva nāgā.

::hangnum
291\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
292\.
::

::gatha1
Piyo hi me āsi supaṇṇarājā, asaṃsayaṃ paṇḍarakena saccaṃ;
::

::gathalast
So rāgarattova akāsimetaṃ, pāpakammaṃ {note:pāpaṃ kammaṃ (sī. pī.)} sampajāno na mohā.
::

::hangnum
293\.
::

::gatha1
Na me piyaṃ appiyaṃ vāpi hoti, sampassato lokamimaṃ parañca;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
294\.
::

::gatha1
Ariyāvakāsosi anariyovāsi {note:anariyo cāsi (sī. pī.)}, asaññato saññatasannikāso;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
295\.
::

::gatha1
Aduṭṭhassa tuvaṃ dubbhi, dubbhī {note:dūbhi, dūbhī (pī.)} ca pisuṇo casi;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccavajjena, muddhā te phalatu sattadhā.
::

::hangnum
296\.
::

::gatha1
Tasmā hi mittānaṃ na dubbhitabbaṃ, mittadubbhā {note:mittadubbhā hi (syā.)} pāpiyo natthi añño;
::

::gathalast
Āsittasatto nihato pathabyā, indassa vākyena hi saṃvaro hatoti.

#### 519. Sambulājātakaṃ (9)

::hangnum
297\.
::

::gatha1
Kā {pb:M:1.0393} vedhamānā girikandarāyaṃ, ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi saṃhitūru {note:saññatūra (sī. pī.), sañcitūru (syā.)};
::

::gathalast
Puṭṭhāsi me pāṇipameyyamajjhe, akkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca.
::

::hangnum
298\.
::

::gatha1
Obhāsayaṃ vanaṃ rammaṃ, sīhabyagghanisevitaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kā vā tvamasi kalyāṇi, kassa vā tvaṃ sumajjhime;
::

::gathalast
Abhivādemi taṃ bhadde, dānavāhaṃ namatthu te.
::

::hangnum
299\.
::

::gatha1
Yo putto kāsirājassa, sotthisenoti taṃ vidū;
::

::gatha2
Tassāhaṃ sambulā bhariyā, evaṃ jānāhi dānava;
::

::gathalast
Abhivādemi {pb:T:1.0520} taṃ bhante {note:bhaddante (sī. syā.)}, sambulāhaṃ namatthu te.
::

::hangnum
300\.
::

::gatha1
Vedehaputto {pb:V:1.0288} bhaddante, vane vasati āturo;
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ rogasammattaṃ, ekā ekaṃ upaṭṭhahaṃ {note:upaṭṭhahiṃ (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
301\.
::

::gatha1
Ahañca vanamuñchāya, madhumaṃsaṃ migābilaṃ {note:migāvilaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yadā harāmi taṃ bhakkho, tassa nūnajja nādhati {note:nāthati (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
302\.
::

::gatha1
Kiṃ vane rājaputtena, āturena karissasi;
::

::gathalast
Sambule pariciṇṇena, ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi te.
::

::hangnum
303\.
::

::gatha1
Sokaṭṭāya durattāya, kiṃ rūpaṃ vijjate mama;
::

::gathalast
Aññaṃ pariyesa bhaddante, abhirūpataraṃ mayā.
::

::hangnum
304\.
::

::gatha1
Ehimaṃ girimāruyha, bhariyā me {note:mayhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} catussatā;
::

::gathalast
Tāsaṃ tvaṃ pavarā hohi, sabbakāmasamiddhinī.
::

::hangnum
305\.
::

::gatha1
Nūna {note:nanu (sī. syā. pī. ka.)} tārakavaṇṇābhe {note:hāṭakavaṇṇābhe (pī.)}, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ taṃ pacuraṃ mayhaṃ, ramassvajja {note:ramasujja (sī. syā.)} mayā saha.
::

::hangnum
306\.
::

::gatha1
No ce tuvaṃ maheseyyaṃ, sambule kārayissasi;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ tvaṃ pātarāsāya, paṇhe {note:maññe (sī. pī.)} bhakkhā bhavissasi.
::

::hangnum
307\.
::

::gatha1
Tañca {pb:M:1.0394} sattajaṭo luddo, kaḷāro purisādako;
::

::gathalast
Vane nāthaṃ apassantiṃ, sambulaṃ aggahī bhuje.
::

::hangnum
308\.
::

::gatha1
Adhipannā pisācena, luddenāmisacakkhunā;
::

::gathalast
Sā ca sattuvasampattā, patimevānusocati.
::

::hangnum
309\.
::

::gatha1
Na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ, yaṃ maṃ khādeyya rakkhaso;
::

::gathalast
Yañca {pb:T:1.0521} me ayyaputtassa, mano hessati aññathā.
::

::hangnum
310\.
::

::gatha1
Na santi devā pavasanti nūna, na hi nūna santi idha lokapālā;
::

::gathalast
Sahasā karontānamasaññatānaṃ, na hi nūna santi paṭisedhitāro.
::

::hangnum
311\.
::

::gatha1
Itthīnamesā pavarā yasassinī, santā samā aggirivuggatejā;
::

::gatha2
Tañce tuvaṃ rakkhasādesi kaññaṃ, muddhā ca hi sattadhā te phaleyya;
::

::gathalast
Mā tvaṃ dahī {note:jahī (pī.)} muñca patibbatāya {note:patibbatā sā (sī.), patibbatā yā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
312\.
::

::gatha1
Sā ca assamamāgacchi, pamuttā purisādakā;
::

::gathalast
Nīḷaṃ {note:niḍḍaṃ (syā. ka.)} paḷinaṃ sakuṇīva {note:phalinasakuṇīva (sī. syā. pī.)}, gatasiṅgaṃva ālayaṃ.
::

::hangnum
313\.
::

::gatha1
Sā tattha paridevesi, rājaputtī yasassinī;
::

::gathalast
Sambulā utumattakkhā, vane nāthaṃ apassantī {note:apassatī (sī.)}.
::

::hangnum
314\.
::

::gatha1

::

::gathalast
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi {note:tumhaṃ hi (pī.)} saraṇaṃ gatā.
::

::hangnum
315\.
::

::gatha1
Vande sīhe ca byagghe ca, ye ca aññe vane migā;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum

::gatha1

::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
317\.

::hangnum

::gatha1

::hangnum
320\.
::

::gatha1
Atisāyaṃ vatāgacchi, rājaputti yasassini;
::

::gathalast
Kena nujja samāgacchi {note:samāgacchi (sī. pī.)}, ko te piyataro mayā.
::

::hangnum
321\.
::

::gatha1
Idaṃ khohaṃ tadāvocaṃ {note:tadavocaṃ (sī. syā.)}, gahitā tena sattunā;
::

::gatha2

::

::gathalast

::hangnum
322\.
::

::gatha1
Corīnaṃ bahubuddhīnaṃ, yāsu saccaṃ sudullabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Thīnaṃ bhāvo durājāno, macchassevodake gataṃ.
::

::hangnum
323\.
::

::gatha1
Tathā maṃ saccaṃ pāletu, pālayissati ce mamaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yathāhaṃ nābhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā;
::

::gathalast
Etena saccavajjena, byādhi te vūpasammatu.
::

::hangnum
324\.
::

::gatha1
Ye kuñjarā sattasatā uḷārā, rakkhanti rattindivamuyyutāvudhā;
::

::gathalast
Dhanuggahānañca satāni soḷasa, kathaṃvidhe passasi bhadde sattavo.
::

::hangnum
325\.
::

::gatha1
Alaṅkatāyo {pb:T:1.0523} padumuttarattacā, virāgitā passati haṃsagaggarā;
::

::gathalast
Tāsaṃ suṇitvā mitagītavāditaṃ {note:mitagītavādinaṃ (pī.)}, na dāni me tāta tathā yathā pure.
::

::hangnum
326\.
::

::gatha1
Suvaṇṇasaṃkaccadharā {pb:M:1.0396} suviggahā, alaṅkatā mānusiyaccharūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Senopiyā {note:senūpiyā (pī.)} tāta aninditaṅgiyo, khattiyakaññā paṭilobhayanti {note:paṭilābhayanti (pī.)} naṃ.
::

::hangnum
327\.
::

::gatha1
Sace ahaṃ tāta tathā yathā pure, patiṃ tamuñchāya punā vane bhare;
::

::gathalast
Sammānaye maṃ na ca maṃ vimānaye, itopi me tāta tato varaṃ siyā.
::

::hangnum
328\.
::

::gatha1
Yamannapāne {pb:V:1.0290} vipulasmi ohite, nārī vimaṭṭhābharaṇā alaṅkatā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṅgupetā {note:pañcaṅgupetā (sī. syā. pī.)} patino ca appiyā, abajjha {note:avajjha (syā.), ābajjha (pī.)} tassā maraṇaṃ tato varaṃ.
::

::hangnum
329\.
::

::gatha1
Api ce daliddā kapaṇā anāḷhiyā, kaṭādutīyā patino ca sā piyā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṅgupetāyapi appiyāya, ayameva {pb:T:1.0524} seyyā {note:seyyo (syā. ka.)} kapaṇāpi yā piyā {note:kapaṇāpi yā (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
330\.
::

::gatha1
Sudullabhitthī purisassa yā hitā, bhattitthiyā dullabho yo hito ca;
::

::gathalast
Hitā ca te sīlavatī ca bhariyā, janinda dhammaṃ cara sambulāya.
::

::hangnum
331\.
::

::gatha1
Sace tuvaṃ vipule laddhabhoge, issāvatiṇṇā maraṇaṃ upesi;
::

::gathalast
Ahañca te bhadde imā rājakaññā {note:imā ca kaññā (pī.)}, sabbe {note:sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)} te vacanakarā bhavāmāti.
::

::centre
Sambulājātakaṃ navamaṃ.
::

#### 520. Gandhatindukajātakaṃ (10)

::hangnum
332\.
::

::gatha1
Appamādo {pb:M:1.0397} amataṃ padaṃ {note:amatapadaṃ (sī. pī.)}, pamādo maccuno padaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appamattā na mīyanti, ye pamattā yathā matā.
::

::hangnum
333\.
::

::gatha1
Madā pamādo jāyetha, pamādā jāyate khayo;
::

::gathalast
Khayā padosā {note:khayā ca dosā (sī.)} jāyanti, mā pamādo {note:mā mado (sī. syā. pī.)} bharatūsabha {note:bhāradhūsabha (ka.)}.
::

::hangnum
334\.
::

::gatha1
Bahū hi khattiyā jīnā, atthaṃ raṭṭhaṃ pamādino;
::

::gathalast
Athopi gāmino gāmā, anagārā agārino.
::

::hangnum
335\.
::

::gatha1
Khattiyassa pamattassa, raṭṭhasmiṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhogā vinassanti, rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ.
::

::hangnum
336\.
::

::gatha1
Nesa {pb:T:1.0525} dhammo mahārāja, ativelaṃ pamajjasi;
::

::gathalast
Iddhaṃ phītaṃ janapadaṃ, corā viddhaṃsayanti naṃ.
::

::hangnum
337\.
::

::gatha1
Na te puttā bhavissanti, na hiraññaṃ na dhāniyaṃ {note:na hiraññanidhāniyā (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhe viluppamānamhi, sabbabhogehi jiyyasi.
::

::hangnum
338\.
::

::gatha1
Sabbabhogā parijiṇṇaṃ, rājānaṃ vāpi khattiyaṃ {note:khattiya (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Ñātimittā suhajjā ca, na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ {note:mantiyaṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
339\.
::

::gatha1
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
::

::gathalast
Tamevamupajīvantā, na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ.
::

::hangnum
340\.
::

::gatha1
Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ, bālaṃ dummantimantinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sirī jahati dummedhaṃ, jiṇṇaṃva urago tacaṃ.
::

::hangnum
341\.
::

::gatha1
Susaṃvihitakammantaṃ{pb:V:1.0291}, kāluṭṭhāyiṃ atanditaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe bhogābhivaḍḍhanti, gāvo sausabhāmiva.
::

::hangnum
342\.
::

::gatha1
Upassutiṃ mahārāja, raṭṭhe janapade cara;
::

::gathalast
Tattha disvā ca sutvā ca, tato taṃ {note:tvaṃ (ka.)} paṭipajjasi.
::

::hangnum
343\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ vedetu pañcālo, saṅgāme saramappito {note:samappito (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja vedemi, kaṇṭakena samappito.
::

::hangnum
344\.
::

::gatha1
Jiṇṇo {pb:M:1.0398} dubbalacakkhūsi, na rūpaṃ sādhu passasi;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ tattha brahmadattassa, yaṃ taṃ maggeyya {note:maggheyya (pī.)} kaṇṭako {note:kaṇḍako (sī. syā. pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
345\.
::

::gatha1
Bahvettha brahmadattassa, sohaṃ {note:yohaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)} maggasmi {note:maggosmi (pī.)} brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Arakkhitā {pb:T:1.0526} jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
::

::hangnum
346\.
::

::gatha1
Rattiñhi {note:rattiñca (sī.)} corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.
::

::hangnum
347\.
::

::gatha1
Etādise bhaye jāte {note:tāta (sī. pī.)}, bhayaṭṭā tāta {note:tāva (sī. pī.)} māṇavā;
::

::gathalast
Nillenakāni kubbanti, vane āhatva kaṇṭakaṃ.
::

::hangnum
348\.
::

::gatha1
Kadāssu nāmayaṃ rājā, brahmadatto marissati;
::

::gathalast
Yassa raṭṭhamhi jiyyanti, appatikā kumārikā.
::

::hangnum
349\.
::

::gatha1
Dubbhāsitañhi te jammi, anatthapadakovide;
::

::gathalast
Kuhiṃ rājā kumārīnaṃ, bhattāraṃ pariyesati.
::

::hangnum
350\.
::

::gatha1
Na me dubbhāsitaṃ brahme, kovidatthapadā ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
::

::hangnum
351\.
::

::gatha1
Rattiñhi {pb:T:1.0527} corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
::

::gatha2
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano;
::

::gathalast

::

::hangnum
352\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ sayatu pañcālo, saṅgāme sattiyā hato;
::

::gathalast
Yathāyaṃ kapaṇo seti, hato phālena sāliyo.
::

::hangnum
353\.
::

::gatha1
Adhammena tuvaṃ jamma, brahmadattassa kujjhasi;
::

::gathalast
Yo tvaṃ sapasi rājānaṃ, aparajjhitvāna attano {note:attanā (pī.)}.
::

::hangnum
354\.
::

::gatha1
Dhammena brahmadattassa, ahaṃ kujjhāmi brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
::

::hangnum
355\.
::

::gatha1
Rattiñhi {pb:V:1.0292} corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.

::hangnum
356\.
::

::gatha1
Sā {pb:M:1.0399} nūna puna re pakkā, vikāle bhattamāhari;
::

::gathalast
Bhattahāriṃ apekkhanto, hato phālena sāliyo.
::

::hangnum
357\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ haññatu pañcālo, saṅgāme asinā hato {note:daḷhaṃ (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja pahato, khīrañca me pavaṭṭitaṃ.
::

::hangnum
358\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ pasu khīraṃ chaḍḍeti, pasupālaṃ vihiṃsati {note:pasupālañca hiṃsati (sī.), pasu phālañca hiṃsati (pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ tattha brahmadattassa, yaṃ no garahate {note:garahato (pī.)} bhavaṃ.
::

::hangnum
359\.
::

::gatha1
Gārayho brahme pañcālo, brahmadattassa rājino;
::

::gathalast
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
::

::hangnum
360\.
::

::gatha1
Rattiñhi {pb:T:1.0528} corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
::

::gathalast
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.
::

::hangnum
361\.
::

::gatha1
Caṇḍā aṭanakā {note:aṭanaka (pī.), akaṭanā (ka.)} gāvī, yaṃ pure na duhāmase;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ dāni ajja dohāma, khīrakāmehupaddutā.
::

::hangnum
362\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ kandatu pañcālo, viputto vippasukkhatu;
::

::gathalast
Yathāyaṃ kapaṇā gāvī, viputtā paridhāvati.
::

::hangnum
363\.
::

::gatha1
Yaṃ pasu pasupālassa, sambhameyya {note:pabbhameyya (sī. pī.)} raveyya vā;
::

::gathalast
Ko nīdha aparādhatthi, brahmadattassa rājino.
::

::hangnum
364\.
::

::gatha1
Aparādho mahābrahme, brahmadattassa rājino;
::

::gathalast
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
::

::hangnum
365\.
::

::gatha1
Rattiñhi corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
::

::gatha2
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ no asikosatthā, khīrapā haññate pajā.
::

::hangnum
366\.
::

::gatha1
Evaṃ khajjatu pañcālo, hato yuddhe saputtako;
::

::gathalast
Yathāhamajja khajjāmi, gāmikehi {note:gāmakehi (sī. pī.)} araññajo.
::

::hangnum
367\.
::

::gatha1
Na {pb:M:1.0400} sabbabhūtesu vidhenti {note:vidhanti (ka.)} rakkhaṃ, rājāno maṇḍūka manussaloke;
::

::gathalast
Nettāvatā rājā adhammacārī, yaṃ tādisaṃ jīvamadeyyu dhaṅkā.
::

::hangnum
368\.
::

::gatha1
Adhammarūpo vata brahmacārī, anuppiyaṃ bhāsasi khattiyassa;
::

::gathalast
Viluppamānāya puthuppajāya, pūjesi rājaṃ paramappamādaṃ {note:rājaṃ paramappavādaṃ (sī.), rājā paramappavādiṃ (syā.)}.
::

::hangnum
369\.
::

::gatha1
Sace {pb:V:1.0293} imaṃ brahme surajjakaṃ siyā, phītaṃ raṭṭhaṃ muditaṃ {note:pūritaṃ (ka.)} vippasannaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvā baliṃ aggapiṇḍañca kākā, na mādisaṃ jīvamadeyyu dhaṅkāti.
::

::centre
Gandhatindukajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kiṃchanda {pb:T:1.0529} kumbha jayaddisa chaddanta, atha paṇḍitasambhava sirakapi;
::

::gathalast
Dakarakkhasa paṇḍaranāgavaro, atha sambula tindukadevasutoti.
::

::centre
Tiṃsanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::centre
Jātakapāḷiyā paṭhamo bhāgo niṭṭhito.
::
